namaḥ ādityānām ca pataye vasūnām pataye namaḥ namaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pataye ākāśa pataye namaḥ dhyānine dhyāyamānāya dhyānibhiḥ saṃstutāya ca mṛtyave kāladaṇḍāya yamāya ca mahātmane yajñāya vasu dānāya svargāya a janma dāya ca savitre sarva devānām dharmāya aneka rūpiṇe umā deha ardha rūpāya lalāṭa nayanāya ca mahiṣa andhaka bhettāya sraṣṭre vai parameṣṭhine haline muṣala ghnāya mahā hāsāya vai namaḥ mṛtyu pāśa ugra hastāya takṣaka brahmasūtriṇe sarva bhūta a sama jñāya sarva bhūta anukampine antarbhūta adhibhūtāya prāṇinām jīva dāya ca budhyamānāya buddhāya draṣṭre vai cakṣuṣe namaḥ namaḥ ghrāṇāya ghrātre ca śrotre śrotrāya ca eva hi sūkṣmāya ca eva sthūlāya sattvāya rajase namaḥ namaḥ ca tamase nityam kṣetrajñāya ajitāya ca viṣṇave lokatantrāya prajānām pataye namaḥ manave sapta ṛṣaye tapyamānāya tāpine brahmaṇyāya atha śuddhāya tathā durvāsase namaḥ śilpine śilpa nāthāya viduṣe viśvakarmaṇe bhūtāya bhūtanāthāya kuṣmāṇḍa pataye namaḥ avaśyāya api avadhyāya ajarāya amarāya ca akṣayāya avyayāya eva tathā apratihatāya ca anāveśyāya sarveṣām dṛśyāya adṛśya rūpiṇe sūkṣmebhyaḥ ca api sūkṣmāya sarvagāya mahātmane na viṣṇu tvena deveśa na api indra tvena bhūtapa icchāmi aham tava īśāna gaṇa tvam nityam avyayam nityam tvām sa gaṇam sa ambam prasannam sa paricchadam draṣṭum icchāmi deveśaḥ eṣa me dīyatām varaḥ tvam naḥ gatiḥ purā deva tvam ca eva ārta ayanam prabhuḥ śaraṇam ca tvam eva atha na anyam paśyāmi karhicit tvayā tyaktasya ca eva āśu vināśaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ anyām gatim na paśyāmi yasyāḥ ātyantikam śubham pratīccha mām sadā devaḥ eṣa me dīyatām varaḥ yaḥ imam prātar utthāya paṭhet avimanāḥ naraḥ yaḥ ca imam śṛṇuyāt nityam śrāvayet vā dvijātiṣu śrutvā sakṛt api hi etam stavam pāpa praṇāśanam iti skandapurāṇe ekaviṃśatimaḥ a adhyāyaḥ dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ aśru pūrṇa īkṣaṇam dīnam pādayoḥ śirasā natam karābhyām su sukhābhyām tu saṃgṛhya parama ārti hā utthāpya nayane somaḥ aśrupūrṇe mamārja ha uvāca ca enam tuṣṭa ātmā vacasā āpyāyayan iva nirīkṣya gaṇapān sarvān devyā saha tadā prabhuḥ jāne bhaktim tava mayi jāne ca ārtim tava anagha tasya sarvasya śailāde udarkam saṃniśāmaya akṣayaḥ ca avyayaḥ ca eva sa pitā sa suhṛd janaḥ mama iṣṭaḥ gaṇapaḥ ca eva mad vīryaḥ mad parākramaḥ iṣṭaḥ mama sadā ca eva mama pārśva gataḥ sadā mad rūpaḥ ca eva bhavitā mahā yoga bala anvitaḥ ṛddhimat ca eva te dvīpam kṣīrodam amṛta ākaram kuśeśaya mayīm mālām avamucya ātmanaḥ tatas ābabandha mahā tejāḥ nandine divya rūpiṇīm sa tayā mālayā nandī babhau kaṇṭha avasaktayā tryakṣaḥ daśa bhujaḥ śrīmān dvitīyaḥ iva śaṃkaraḥ āśramaḥ ca ayam atyartham tapasā tava bhāvitaḥ samantāt yojanam kṣetram divyam deva gaṇaiḥ vṛtam siddha cāraṇa saṃkīrṇam apsaraḥ gaṇa sevitam siddhikṣetram param guhyam bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā yat kiṃcid kurute naraḥ śubham vā api aśubham vā atra sarvam bhavitṛ tat śubham jāpyam mānasam tulyam vai rudrāṇām tat bhaviṣyati tatas jaṭā srutam vāri gṛhītvā hāra nirmalam sā tatas divya toyā ca puṇyā maṇijalā śubhā haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇā cakravāka upaśobhitā strī rūpa dhāriṇī ca eva prāñjaliḥ śirasā natā mahādevam upasthitā yasmāt jaṭā udakāt devi pravṛttā tvam śubha ānane tasmāt jaṭodā nāmnā tvam bhaviṣyasi sarit varā tvayi snānam tu yaḥ kuryāt śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ sā tam āghrāya śirasi pāṇibhyām parimārjatī payasā śaṅkha gaureṇa devī devam nirīkṣatī tāni srotāṃsi trīṇi asyāḥ srutāni oghavatī nadī nadīm trisrotasīm puṇya trisrotasam nadīm dṛṣṭvā vṛṣaḥ parama harṣitaḥ yasmāt vṛṣabha nādena pravṛttā sā mahā nadī tasmāt ḍhitkirikām tām vai uvāca vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ jāmbūnada mayam citram svam devaḥ parama adbhutam mukuṭam ca ābabandha asmai kuṇḍale ca amṛta udbhave tam tathā abhyarcitam vyomni dṛṣṭvā meghaḥ prabhā karaḥ deva upavāhyaḥ siṣice sa nādaḥ sa taḍit guṇaḥ tasya abhiṣiktasya tadā pravṛtte srotasī bhṛśam svarṇodakā iti nāmnā tām mahādevaḥ jāmbūnada mayāt yasmāt dvitīyā mukuṭāt śubhāt prāvartata nadī puṇyā ūcuḥ jambūnadī iti tām vyākhyātam phalam etāsām jaṭodāyām mahātmanā tri rātra upoṣitaḥ gatvā snātvā abhyarcya ca śūlinam brāhmaṇān ca tarpayitvā yatra tatra mṛtaḥ naraḥ bhavet mama pārśvāt anapagaḥ priyaḥ saṃmataḥ eva ca sa me sadā syāt gaṇapaḥ variṣṭhaḥ tvayā samaḥ kānti vapuḥ ca nityam iti skandapurāṇe dvāviṃśatimaḥ a adhyāyaḥ trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ devīm uvāca vāgīśaḥ umām giri vara ātmajām devi nandīśvaram devam abhiṣekṣyāmi bhūtapam gaṇān āvāhayiṣyāmi kim vā tvam manyase a avyaye sapta loka ādhipatyam ca gaṇeśānām tathā eva ca tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ sura śatru niṣūdanaḥ prāc mukhaḥ sa gaṇeśānām āhvānam akarot tadā tatas sahasraśas tatra gaṇādhyakṣāḥ mudā yutāḥ samprāptāḥ sarva loka īśāḥ tat śṛṇuṣva mahā mune tatas karāla daśanaḥ bhṛkuṭī bhūṣita ānanaḥ śaṅkha hāra ambu gauraḥ ca daṃṣṭrī sragmī tri locanaḥ jaṭā sahasra ūrdhva śirāḥ jvālā keśaḥ mahā hanuḥ aṭṭahāsān sṛjānaḥ ca aśanīpāta saṃnibhān diṇḍiḥ iti eva vikhyātaḥ gaṇapaḥ samadṛśyata ātmanaḥ sadṛśānām ca koṭībhiḥ daśabhiḥ vṛtaḥ gaṇapānām sura īśānām yoginām dīpta tejasām tryakṣaḥ a anala śata prakhyaḥ aśanīpāta nardanaḥ nṛtyan gāyan ca citrāṇi kurvan nāṭyāni anekaśas jvalat daṃṣṭraḥ mahā hāsaḥ bṛhat skandhaḥ pinākadhṛk koṭībhiḥ daśabhiḥ sārdham dviguṇābhiḥ mahātmanām gaṇānām citra rūpāṇām yugapad sampradṛśyata siṃha āsya gaja koka āsyaiḥ dvīpi śārdūlaka ānanaiḥ saḥ aaṣāḍhiḥ nāma gaṇapaḥ vyāsa tatra samāgataḥ śata yojana bāhuḥ ca digvāsāḥ ca ūrdhva mehanaḥ atidīrghaḥ aatimeḍhraḥ ca lamba bhrūḥ sthūla nāsikaḥ vṛtta āsyaḥ ca mahā akṣaḥ ca bhṛkuṭī saṃhata ānanaḥ daṃṣṭrāḥ catasraḥ vaktreṇa bibhrat śaṅkha indu pāṇḍarāḥ vṛtaḥ koṭī śatena eva sadṛśānām adṛśyata bhārabhūti iti vikhyātaḥ mahā yoga bala anvitaḥ tatas kunda indu śaṅkha ābham himarāśi ambu saṃnibham mṛṇāla sphaṭika ābham ca bhasma kakṣa avalambanam gṛhītvā ca aśanī hāsam tri pādam cīra vāsasam jvālā mālā agra keśam ca vyāghra carma ajina ambaram vāyu vegam mahā hāsam bhujaga ābaddha mekhalam mahā uraga kṛta āpīḍam śaṅku karṇa ūrdhva mehanam bhasma praharaṇam ca eva mahā daṃṣṭram mahā hanum mahāgaṇapatim vīram jvaraḥ iti eva viśrutam koṭī śata vṛtam tam ca gaṇapam saḥ triśūla pāṇiḥ digvāsāḥ mahā yoga bala anvitaḥ bahu veṣa dharaḥ ca eva dhyāna yoga parāyaṇaḥ somavarṇaḥ iti khyātaḥ koṭī śata vṛtaḥ prabhuḥ tādṛśānām gaṇādhyakṣaḥ devena āhūtaḥ āgataḥ atha aparaḥ mahā kāyaḥ śūla pāṇiḥ mahā balaḥ eka pādaiḥ mahā kāyaiḥ tri akṣaiḥ taiḥ śūla pāṇibhiḥ vṛtaḥ koṭī śatena eva sthāṇuḥ tatra abhyavartata tatas aaparaḥ paṭṭisena hrasva pāda udaraḥ śuciḥ sahasra bāhu caraṇaḥ sahasra akṣaḥ pratāpavān karāla daśanaḥ ca eva kṛṣṇa sarpa ambara chadaḥ tryakṣaḥ candra kṛta āpīḍaḥ kaṇṭha mālā vibhūṣitaḥ ugrasenaḥ iti khyātaḥ koṭī śata vṛtaḥ sa ca āgāt samīpam devasya āhūtaḥ svayam īśvaraḥ caturvaktraḥ mahā tejāḥ caturviṃśa īkṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ karāla daśanaḥ ca eva śaṅku karṇaḥ mahā nakhaḥ asi pāṇiḥ mahā tejāḥ śata pādaḥ śata udaraḥ ajaikapād iti khyātaḥ vṛtaḥ koṭī śatena saḥ kāñcana upala vṛkṣa āḍhyaḥ sa meghaḥ iva parvataḥ āgāt tatas aaparaḥ vyāsa gaṇapaḥ su mahā balaḥ sarvatas vadanaḥ śrīmān sarvatas pāṇi pādadhṛk hrasva bāhu ūru pādaḥ ca aśanim dhārayan śubham śataiḥ vṛtaḥ ca koṭīnām aṣṭābhiḥ tu ātmanaḥ samaiḥ nikumbhaḥ iti vikhyātaḥ śata pāda udara ānanaḥ āgāt tatas vidyutkeśaḥ mahā balaḥ gaṇa koṭī śata vṛtaḥ paramam para tāpanaḥ tatas sahasreṇa koṭīnām gaṇapaḥ vṛtaḥ sūrya mālā srajam bibhrat ājagāma mahā tapāḥ dhanuṣpāṇiḥ mahā tejāḥ viśrutaḥ sa mahā dyutiḥ tathā anyaḥ sarpa mālaḥ ca cakra ābharaṇaḥ eva ca gaṇa koṭi śataiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ vṛtaḥ samanudhāvata śaṅkukarṇaḥ gaṇa koṭyā mahā balaḥ nandikaḥ ca api daśabhiḥ piṅgākṣaḥ ca vināyakaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā kuṣmāṇḍaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ hiraṇya varṇaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ca eka pādaḥ tathā eva ca dhūmrakeśaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ patākī daśabhiḥ tathā sahasraghaṇṭaḥ a aṣṭādaśabhiḥ tapaḥ pañcabhiḥ eva ca sahasra śīrṣaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ca bhavaḥ koṭi śata āvṛtaḥ varaḥ daśabhiḥ abhyāgāt kumbhakarṇaḥ tathā aṣṭabhiḥ āveśanī tathā aṣṭābhiḥ saptabhiḥ ca pravartanaḥ mahā ravaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnām gaṇapaḥ vṛtaḥ caturmukhaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ tathā bāhu upahārakaḥ mahākālaḥ śatena eva tathā agni śikharaḥ gaṇaḥ ādityamūrdhā koṭyā ca tathā ca eva dhana āvahaḥ saṃnāmaḥ ca śatena eva kukkuṭaḥ ca kundaḥ ca pañcadaśabhiḥ tathā saṃkoṭakaḥ eka pādaḥ ṣaṣṭyā tathā sapta mahābalaḥ ca navabhiḥ apasmāraḥ ca viśrutaḥ nīlaḥ navatyā deveśaḥ pūrṇabhadraḥ tathā eva ca nirṛtiḥ ca eva saptatyā koṭīnām abhyagāt saha koṭī koṭī sahasrāṇām śataiḥ viṃśatibhiḥ vṛtāḥ ītayaḥ tatra ca ājagmuḥ mahā yoga bala anvitāḥ bhūtāḥ koṭi sahasreṇa pramathāḥ koṭibhiḥ tribhiḥ vīrabhadraḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā vṛṣabhaḥ ca mahā balaḥ meghaḥ saudāmanī mālaḥ navatyā saṃvṛtaḥ prabhākaraḥ ca viṃśatyā viṭpatiḥ ca mahā balaḥ kāṣṭhakarṇaḥ ca divya ātmā bilva rūpaḥ ca viśrutaḥ śatamanyuḥ tathā ca eva pañcākṣaḥ ca eva vīryavān tālaketuḥ ca ṣaṇḍaḥ ca kāpālī gajanāśanaḥ loka antakaḥ ca dīpta ātmā hema kuṇḍalaḥ eva ca mṛtyuḥ ca eva yamaḥ ca eva kālaḥ viṣa haraḥ tathā śata māyaḥ mahā māyaḥ sarvatra aśaraṇaḥ tathā ekaśṛṅgī ca vikhyātaḥ tathā bhṛṅgiriṭiḥ ca yaḥ ete ca anye ca gaṇapāḥ guhyāḥ ye ca mahā balāḥ gāyantaḥ ca dravantaḥ ca nṛtyantaḥ ca mahā balāḥ rathaiḥ nāgaiḥ hayaiḥ ca eva vāyu markaṭa vāhanāḥ vyāghra siṃha biḍālaiḥ ca sarpaiḥ pakṣibhiḥ eva ca bherī śaṅkha mṛdaṅgaiḥ ca paṇava ānaka gomukhaiḥ bherī jharjhara saṃnādaiḥ āḍambaraka ḍiṇḍimaiḥ maḍḍukaiḥ veṇu vīṇābhiḥ vivṛṣaiḥ tuṇavaiḥ api vādyamānaiḥ mahā yogāḥ ājagmuḥ deva saṃsadam te viśvakarmāṇam amitra sāhāḥ viśveśam eka akṣaram avyayam ca trayoviṃśatimaḥ a adhyāyaḥ channam kṛtvā tathā ākāśam kiṃnara uraga cāraṇāḥ nānā vimānam ārūḍhāḥ koṭiśas tatra ca apare caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ te gaṇeśāḥ mahāsattvāḥ sarve deva īśvara īśvarāḥ kim artham vayam āhūtāḥ ājñāpaya kṛtam hi tat kim sāgarān śoṣayāmaḥ yamam vā saha kiṃkaraiḥ baddhvā indram saha devaiḥ ca sa viṣṇum saha vāyunā ānayāmaḥ su saṃkruddhāḥ daityān vā saha dānavaiḥ kasya adya vyasanam ghoram kariṣyāmaḥ tava ājñayā tān tathāvādinaḥ sarvān namataḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ uvāca devaḥ sampūjya gaṇān gaṇapatiḥ bhavaḥ śṛṇudhvam yatkṛte yūyam iha āhūtāḥ jagat hitāḥ śrutvā ca prayata ātmānaḥ kurudhvam tat aśaṅkitāḥ nandīśvaraḥ putraḥ naḥ sarveṣām īśvara īśvaraḥ priyaḥ senānīḥ vaḥ samāhitaḥ tam imam mama saṃdeśāt yūyam sarve senānyam abhiṣiñcadhvam mahā yoga patim patim adya prabhṛti yuṣmākam ayam nandī īśvaraḥ śubhaḥ tasya rūpāśrayam divyam jāmbūnada mayam śubham āsanam meru saṃkāśam manoramam atha aharan śātakumbha mayam ca api cāru cāmīkara prabham muktā dāma avalambam ca maṇi ratna avabhāsitam stambhaiḥ ca vaiḍūrya mayaiḥ kiṅkiṇī jāla saṃvṛtam cāru ratnaka saṃyuktam maṇḍapam viśvatomukham tasya agratas pāda pīṭham nīlam vajra avabhāsitam cakruḥ pāda pratiṣṭhā artham kalaśau ca asya pārśva gau sampūrṇau parama ambhobhiḥ aravinda āvṛta ānanau agratas a agnim samādhāya vṛṣabham ca api pārśvatas sa vatsām surabhim ca api tasya pārśve a atha dakṣiṇe chattram śata śalākam ca jāmbūnada mayam śubham śaṅkha hāra ambu gaureṇa pṛṣṭhena abhivirājitam vyajanam candra śubhram ca hema daṇḍam sucārumat mālām kuśeśayānām ca bhramara āvali sevitām āninyuḥ tatra gaṇapāḥ nandyāvartān ca kāñcanān svastikam vardhamānam ca śrīvatsam ca eva kāñcanam kīcakāḥ veṇavaḥ ca eva kanyā ca eva abhipūjitā airāvatam supratīkam gajau etau ca pūjitau dhvajam ca pūjitam divyam śaṅkham ca eva indu varcasam kalaśānām sahasram ca kāñcanānām suvarcasām rājatānām sahasram ca pārthivānām tathā eva ca tāmrāṇām atha divyānām sahasram anala tviṣām vāsaḥ yugam vṛkṣa jam ca virajaḥ sūkṣmam eva ca mukuṭam kāñcanam ca eva su kṛtam viśvakarmaṇā paṭṭisam ca mahat divyam śūlam ca aśanim eva ca jāmbūnada mayam sūtram keyūra dvayam eva ca hāram ca maṇi citra aṅgam rocana rucakam tathā darbhān ca divyām samidham ājyam dhūpam atha api ca samantāt ninyuḥ avyagrāḥ gaṇapāḥ deva saṃmatāḥ tatas diśaḥ samudrāḥ ca varuṇaḥ sa dhaneśvaraḥ tārā rūpāṇi sarvāṇi nakṣatrāṇi dhruvaḥ tathā rudrāḥ rakṣāṃsi yakṣāḥ ca aśvinau daitya dānavāḥ pṛthivī ca samudrāḥ ca varṣāṇi girayaḥ tathā vṛkṣāḥ ca vīrudhaḥ ca eva oṣadhyaḥ ca mahā balāḥ nadyaḥ sarvāḥ samājagmuḥ paśavaḥ ca eva sarvaśas bhūtāni prakṛtiḥ ca eva indriyāṇi ca sarvaśas tīrthāni ca eva sarvāṇi dānāni vividhāni ca ṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni atharva aṅgirasau api yajñāḥ ca kratavaḥ ca eva iṣṭayaḥ niyamāḥ tathā chandāṃsi ca eva sarvāṇi piśācāḥ devayonayaḥ brahmā ca ṛṣayaḥ ca eva viṣṇuḥ sa anucaraḥ tathā teṣu āgateṣu sarveṣu bhagavān go vṛṣa dhvajaḥ kṛtvā adbhiḥ pūrayitvā ca kuśeśaya mukha āvṛtam jayām ca vijayām ca eva siṃhīm vyāghrīm tathā eva ca suvarcalām śaṅkhapuṣpīm viṣṇukrāntām punarnavām kumārīm candrakāntām ca mṛtasaṃjīvanīm api ādityavarcasam ca eva amṛtām śrīniketanām tathā kumudvatīm ca eva prākṣipan teṣu atha auṣadhīḥ pārthiveṣu tadā vyāsa sarveṣu eva gaṇeśvarāḥ sauvarṇeṣu tu sarveṣu tīrthāni vividhāni ca dānāni ca eva sarvāṇi bhagavān saṃnyaveśayat rājateṣu ca kumbheṣu mantrān chandāṃsi ca eva ha kratūn anyān ca vividhāḥ iṣṭīḥ kāmyān tathā itarān audumbareṣu sarveṣu saritaḥ sāgarān tathā veṣṭayitvā ca sūtreṇa devebhyaḥ pradadau vibhuḥ sa jagrāha tadā brahmā ekam kalaśam ātmanā gaṇapebhyaḥ tathā ca anyān ṛṣibhyaḥ ca pitāmahaḥ tatas viṣṇuḥ tatas śakro ṛṣayaḥ ca saha amaraiḥ gaṇa adhipāḥ ca sarve te abhyaṣiñcanta nandinam keyūre kuṇḍale ca eva mukuṭam hāram eva ca paṭṭisam śūla vajre ca aśanīm ca dadau svayam ṛṣayaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca eva pitāmaha purogamāḥ viṣṇuḥ uvāca namaḥ kuṣmāṇḍa rājāya vajra udyata karāya ca śālaṅkāyana pautrāya halamārga utthitāya ca gaṇānām pataye ca eva bhūtānām pataye namaḥ umā putrāya devāya paṭṭisa āyudha dhāriṇe namaḥ daṃṣṭrā karālāya lalāṭa nayanāya ca pramathāya vareṇyāya īśānāya arpitāya ca dvāra adhyakṣāya śūrāya suyaśā pataye namaḥ namaḥ pravara mālāya kṣīroda nilayāya ca mahā gaṇādhipataye mahā yogeśvarāya ca diṇḍi muṇḍāya caṇḍāya eka akṣara ratāya ca akṣayāya amṛtāya eva ajarāya amarāya ca namaḥ pavana vegāya sarvajñāya ajitāya ca kirīṭine kuṇḍaline mahā parigha bāhave sarvān devān gaṇān ca eva pāhi deva namaḥ a astu te prāñjaliḥ prayataḥ bhūtvā jaya śabdam cakāra ha tatas gaṇāḥ jaya iti ūcuḥ tatas devāḥ tatas aasurāḥ tatas sarvāṇi bhūtāni brahmā śakraḥ tathā eva ca tatas śaṅkhān ca bherīn ca paṭaha āḍambarān tathā vaṃśān ca paṇavān ca eva kṛkavān goviṣāṇikān diṇḍimān veṇukān ca eva mardalān ca eva sarvaśas avādayanta gaṇapāḥ harṣayantaḥ mudā yutāḥ namaḥ nandīśvarāya iti kṛtvā yaḥ svapnam ācaret yatra ayam sthāpyate nityam stavaḥ parama pūjitaḥ te devadevasya sahādri putryāḥ iṣṭāḥ variṣṭhāḥ ca gaṇāḥ bhavanti iti skandapurāṇe caturviṃśatimaḥ a adhyāyaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ āmantrya nāmnā tān īśaḥ sa śakraḥ sa pitāmahaḥ yuṣmākam suyaśā kanyā subhagā divya rūpiṇī dātum arhatha tām subhrūm snuṣām mahyam mahā balāḥ marutaḥ ūcuḥ mā naḥ parān iva īśāna yācanena vibhāvaya pitā naḥ kaśyapaḥ śrīmān marīciḥ ca pitāmahaḥ pitāmaha pitā brahmā tasya api tvam pitāmahaḥ suyaśām marutām kanyām ānayāmāsa tad kṣaṇāt svayam hotā asya tatra āsīt brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ kaśyapaḥ ca tathā udgātā atriḥ sāma svayam jagau nāradaḥ parvataḥ ca eva citrasenaḥ ca gāyanaḥ ruciḥ ca eva hāhāḥ hūhū tathā eva ca tathā śāliśirāḥ yaḥ ca viśrutaḥ gaṇḍamaṇḍakaḥ ītiḥ ca eva indravāhaḥ ca yajñavāhaḥ a atha dakṣiṇaḥ urvaśī ca eva rambhā ca ghṛtācī pūrvacittī api tilottamā ca viśvācī anyāḥ ca apsarasaḥ śubhāḥ anṛtyanta mahābhāgāḥ nṛttam sura manoharam tatas sa tu kṛta udvāhaḥ nandī gatvā mahāmanāḥ śilādasya ca lokeśaḥ śriyā paramayā yutaḥ varam vṛṇīṣva putra tvam snuṣā ca iyam tava priyā sadā ca tuṣṭaḥ bhava me sa ambaḥ saha gaṇeśvaraiḥ sadā aham tava nandīśa su tuṣṭaḥ sa gaṇa īśvaraḥ pārvatyā sahitaḥ dhīman idam ca śṛṇu me vacaḥ sadā iṣṭaḥ ca variṣṭhaḥ ca parama aiśvarya saṃyutaḥ parvatam ca asya vaibhrājam kāmagam sarva kāñcanam sthānam śrīparvate ca asya bhaviṣyati su pūjitam bhṛgau tasmin ca yaḥ prāṇān tyakṣyate vai su dhārmikaḥ sa kāma cārī vaibhrāje gaṇapaḥ aasya bhaviṣyati tatas devī mahābhāgā śailādeḥ adadat varam varam vṛṇu yathā iṣṭam vai tau idam pratyuvāca ha ūcatuḥ muditau devau snuṣām tām varavarṇinīm varam daduḥ mahāsattvāḥ sa vavre kāñcana prabhaḥ yuṣmāsu mama bhaktiḥ ca aiśvaryam ca api saṃmatam vaśyāḥ ca yūyam sarve me priyaḥ yuṣmākam eva ca gaṇāḥ ūcuḥ asmākam īśaḥ sarveṣām devānām api ca īśvaraḥ kuṣmāṇḍānām variṣṭhaḥ ca rudrāṇām tvam mahā balaḥ ītīnām dvāra pālaḥ ca pramathānām tathā eva ca mahā balaḥ mahā yogī sa inānīḥ tvam hi naḥ mataḥ tvam bhūtaḥ bhūta netā ca nāyakaḥ aatha vināyakaḥ grahāṇām adhipaḥ ca eva ugra daṇḍa dharaḥ tathā mahā anubhāvaḥ tvam ca eva kṣīroda nilayaḥ ca ha bhāvanaḥ sarva bhūtānām vara daḥ vara da arcitaḥ saḥ evam gaṇapaiḥ sarvaiḥ stutaḥ nandīśvaraḥ vibhuḥ uvāca praṇataḥ sarvān brūta kim karavāṇi vaḥ te evam uktāḥ gaṇapāḥ sarve eva mahā balāḥ ūcuḥ tam divya bhāva jñāḥ devadevasya saṃnidhau tvam asmākam gaṇādhyakṣaḥ kṛtaḥ devena śambhunā asmābhiḥ ca abhiṣiktaḥ tvam nāyakaḥ dharma dāyakaḥ sa tvam śivaḥ ca saumyaḥ ca guṇavān aguṇeṣu api kṣamā śauca dama upetaḥ bhava naḥ priya kṛt sadā śirasi añjalim ādhāya gaṇapān astuvat tadā deva asura manuṣyāṇām āpyāyibhyaḥ namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ vaḥ sarva bhūtānām namaḥ vaḥ sarvatas śubhāḥ mama saumyāḥ śivāḥ ca eva bhavantu gaṇanāyakāḥ iti stutāḥ gaṇapatayaḥ mahā balāḥ śubhaiḥ vacobhiḥ sura śatru nāśanāḥ tapaḥ aakṣayam sthānam atha atulām gatim yaśaḥ tathā agryam bahu dharma nityatām diśantu sarvam manasā īpsitam ca me sura īśvarāḥ puṣṭim anuttamām tathā imau nandi gaṇa indrāṇām stavau yaḥ a adhyeti nityaśas sandhyāyām aparasyām tu japan pāpam divākṛtam pūrvasyām saṃtyajet vā api sarva rātri kṛtam japan tatas te gaṇapāḥ sarve saṃstutāḥ tena dhīmatā nisṛṣṭāḥ ca tadā jagmuḥ praṇipatya vṛṣadhvajam devāḥ ca sarva lokāḥ ca tatas devaḥ svayam prabhuḥ sṛṣṭvā nandīśvara gṛham pradāya ca mahāmanāḥ abhiṣekam vivāham ca paṭhet vā śrāvayīta vā brāhmaṇaḥ sa mṛtaḥ yāti nandīśvara salokatām pañcaviṃśatimaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca devyā saha atha bhagavān āsīnaḥ tatra kāma daḥ bhagavān himavat śṛṅge śarvaḥ devyāḥ priya īpsayā gaṇeśaiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ hāsam saṃjanayan muhur mahā anubhāvaiḥ sarvajñaiḥ kāma rūpa dharaiḥ śubhaiḥ atha devī āsasāda ekā mātaram parameśvarī āsīnām kāñcane śubhre āsane parama arcite atha dṛṣṭvā satīm devīm āgatām tu surūpiṇīm āsīnām tām ca sā uvāca menā himavataḥ priyā daridra krīḍanaiḥ tvam hi bhartrā krīḍasi saṃgatā ume te evam krīḍanti yathā tava patiḥ śubhe sā evam uktā tu mātrā atha na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ bhavat mahatyā akṣamayā yuktā na kiṃcid tām uvāca ha visṛṣṭā sā tadā mātrā gatvā devam uvāca ha anyam vṛṇu mama āvāsam bhuvaneśa mahā dyute sadā tvam ucyamānā vai mayā vāsa artham īśvari idānīm svayam eva tvam vāsam anyatra śobhane gṛham gatā aham deveśa pituḥ adya mahātmanaḥ dṛṣṭā ca me tatra mātā vijane loka bhāvanī āsana ādibhiḥ abhyarcya sā mām evam abhāṣata ume tava sadā bhartā daridra krīḍanaiḥ śubhe krīḍate na hi devānām krīḍā bhavati tādṛśī yat kila tvam mahādeva gaṇeśaiḥ vividhaiḥ śubhaiḥ ramase tat aniṣṭam hi mama mātuḥ vṛṣadhvaja tatas devaḥ prahasya āha devīm hāsayitum prabhuḥ kṛttivāsāḥ hi avāsāḥ vā śmaśānanilayaḥ ca ha aniketaḥ hi araṇyeṣu parvatānām guhāsu ca pārśva stham gaṇapam prāha nikumbham nāma viśrutam gaṇeśvara nikumbha tvam gatvā vārāṇasīm śubhām śūnyām kuru mahā bāho upāyena eva mā balāt tatra rājā nivasati divodāsaḥ pratāpavān dhārmikaḥ mama bhaktaḥ ca mahā yogī mahā balaḥ sa tvam tathā gataḥ kuryāḥ yathā asmai na aparādhyase tasya eva ca aparādhena śūnyā vārāṇasī bhavet uvāca devam praṇataḥ prāñjaliḥ hṛṣita ānanaḥ tathā kariṣye deveśa yathā sa hi narādhipaḥ bhaviṣyati apara adhīśa tvam ca tuṣṭaḥ bhaviṣyasi śūnyā vārāṇasī ca eva bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ jagāma puṇyām lokeṣu purīm vārāṇasīm prabhuḥ tatra asau darśanam svapne nāpitāya dadau gaṇaḥ maṇḍūka akṣāya rūpam ca svam tasya adarśayat tadā maṇḍūka akṣa nikumbhaḥ a aham gaṇapaḥ śoka nāśanaḥ divodāsa gṛha dvāri kuruṣva tvam mama ālayam sthāpayasva ca tatra arcām mad rūpa sadṛśīm śubhām nāpitaḥ uvāca svāmin tava gṛha dvāri kariṣye gaṇa pālayam sthāpayiṣye gaṇeśam ca tat me a anujñātum arhasi pratyasthāpayat arcām ca yādṛśīm dṛṣṭavān asau tasya pūjām ca mahatīm prāvartayata śobhanām gaṇeśasya mahā sattvaḥ sa ca tām pratyagṛhṇata paśūn ca eva hi putrān ca saubhāgyam ca adadat prabhuḥ tasya tām vṛddhim atulām nāpitasya abhivīkṣya tu ārirādhayiṣuḥ lokaḥ tasya pūjām cakāra ha cakruḥ yātrāḥ tathā kecid upavāsān tathā apare homam japyam tathā eva anye pūjām ca anye vara arthinaḥ upahārān tathā eva anye gīta nṛttam tathā apare dadau sarvān abhiprāyān ye ye teṣām abhīpsitāḥ evam tam kāma dam jñātvā divodāsaḥ nṛpaḥ tadā uvāca mahiṣīm vyāsa kadācid putra lipsayā sā evam uktā tadā gatvā gaṇeśam prāpya śobhanā upavāsam kariṣyāmi tava deva abhirādhane jāte ca putre dāsyāmi śatānām daśatīḥ daśa tvām uddiśya dvijātibhyaḥ go dhenūnām gaṇa īśvara brāhmaṇānām sahasrāṇām śatam ca api su pūjitam purastāt bhojayiṣye te putre jāte na saṃśayaḥ bahūn dāsyati rājā ca grāmān dāsyaḥ tathā eva ca sadā sattram ca pūjām ca kariṣyati tava prabho sa upavāsā tadā pūjām mahatīm tasya kurvatī tām tathā tiṣṭhatīm devaḥ provāca sa gaṇeśvaraḥ uttiṣṭha na asti te putraḥ mā khedam tvam vṛthā kṛthāḥ asakṛt procyamānā sā niyamāt virarāma ha evam mahiṣyā sa proktaḥ svayam eva narādhipaḥ sadā sa niyamaḥ tasthau gaṇeśasya agratas nṛpaḥ mā sthāḥ vṛthā iha nṛpate na te putram dadāmi aham krodha rakta īkṣaṇaḥ prāha tam utthāya gaṇeśvaram rājā uvāca gaṇaḥ vā tvam piśācaḥ vā bhūtaḥ vā rākṣasaḥ vā kṛtaghnaḥ tvam na saṃdehaḥ na tvam pūjām iha arhasi pūjā arhaḥ na bhavān tasmāt mattaḥ daṇḍam tvam arhasi nṛśaṃsaḥ ca avaliptaḥ ca niṣṭhuraḥ matsara anvitaḥ sthaṇḍilam ca babhañja āśu dadāha arcām ca su prabhām nikumbhaḥ a api kṛtārthaḥ san ākāśe saṃsthitaḥ prabhuḥ yasmāt mama ālayaḥ bhagnaḥ tvayā nirapakāriṇaḥ tasmāt varṣa sahasram te purī śūnyā bhaviṣyati saḥ evam uktvā rājānam nikumbhaḥ parama ātmavān deveśāya nivedya evam tasthau pārśva gataḥ prabhoḥ vrīḍām parām samāsādya gṛhān abhyagamat tadā atha sā tena śāpena purī vārāṇasī tadā śūnyā samabhavat kṣipram viśuddhā mṛga sevitā tām tu śūnyām sa vijñāya devyā saha pinākadhṛk sa gaṇaḥ nandinā sārdham ājagāma mahā dyutiḥ sa tatra mānasam divyam vimānam sūrya varcasam na me prabhavati prajñā kṛtsnaśas tad nirūpaṇe deva udyānāni ramyāṇi nandana ādyāni yāni tu tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamam śrīmat udyānam asṛjat prabhuḥ ṣaḍviṃśatimaḥ a adhyāyaḥ saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ āsane kāñcane divye nānā ratna upaśobhite athā acalasutā devī sukha āsīnā vibhāvarī saḥ evam umayā proktaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca kim tat sa bhagavān devaḥ prīyamāṇaḥ mahā tapāḥ praṇayāt sa tadā devyā pṛṣṭaḥ aakathayat avyayaḥ mayā api etat purā vyāsa pṛṣṭaḥ nandīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ gaṇeśānam mahābhāgam sūrya ayuta sama prabham īśena yat purā devyāḥ kathitam gaṇa sattama nandīśvarā uvāca śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi pṛcchataḥ te mahā mune śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi yat mām pṛcchasi suvrate hitāya devi bhaktānām pṛṣṭaḥ te kathayāmi te prāsādam yaḥ tu me devi śubhram kuryāt anindite carate sa mayā sārdham nityam aṣṭaguṇa anvitaḥ kāñcanam tuṭi mātram vā yaḥ dadyāt bahu vā mama yaḥ me gāḥ tu hiraṇyam vā dadyāt avimanāḥ priye vṛṣabham yaḥ prayaccheta śvetam nīlam atha api vā sa me puram samāsādya gaṇeśaiḥ saha modate yaḥ me puṇya phalam dadyāt ātmanā pūrvam arjitam yaḥ ā anuyānam caturdaśyām kṛṣṇasya kurute mama sa tayā śraddhayā pūtaḥ vimuktaḥ sarva pātakaiḥ snātvā yaḥ pūrvasaṃdhyāyām sadā mām upagacchati sa mitram yakṣa rājasya yakṣaḥ bhavati vīryavān saṃmārjanam pañcaśatam sahasram upalepanam gandhāḥ ca daśa sāhasrāḥ ānantyam ca arcanam smṛtam abhyaṅgaḥ ca eva snapanam tri śatam bhavet kṣamāmi devi ca asya iha aparādhān bahūn api agarum daśa sāhasram ṣaṣ sahasram tu candanam caturdaśa sahasrāṇi dhūpaḥ kālāgaruḥ smṛtaḥ akṣatāḥ taṇḍula yavāḥ śālayaḥ dviśatāḥ smṛtāḥ dve sahasre palānām tu mahiṣākṣasya yaḥ dahet ubhe pakṣe trayodaśyām aṣṭamyām ca upavāsikaḥ upatiṣṭheta mām bhaktyā sa upahāram anindite dadāni asya svakam lokam tuṣṭaḥ a aham devi śāśvatam eka rātram ca yaḥ martyaḥ dīpam dhārayati sthitaḥ mayā eva mohitāḥ sarve lokāḥ sa jaḍa paṇḍitāḥ na mām paśyanti rāga andhāḥ tamasā bahulīkṛtāḥ dhyāninaḥ nitya yuktāḥ ye satya dharma parāyaṇāḥ ekāgra manasaḥ dāntāḥ te mām paśyanti nityadā ye me bhaktāḥ sadā ca eva sāṃkhya yoga viśāradāḥ dhyāninaḥ nitya yuktāḥ ca devi paśyanti mām budhāḥ yāni lokeṣu tīrthāni devatāyatanāni ca pādayoḥ tāni suśroṇi sadā saṃnihitāni me sarva avasthaḥ a api pāpa ātmā jñāna niṣṭhena cetasā praviśeta sa mām kṣipram atra nā asti vicāraṇā iti skandapurāṇe saptaviṃśatitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas vyāsa punar devī patim vratapatim śubhā vratānām phalam alpam vā mahat vā yat trilokapa vratam bhavati yādṛś vā tat prabrūhi maheśvara vratam yādṛś ca yat proktam tat śṛṇuṣva anindite caturdaśyām tathā aṣṭamyām ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ śuciḥ saṃvatsaram a bhuñjānaḥ śāntaḥ dāntaḥ jita indriyaḥ sattra yāji phalam yat ca satya vāc ṛtu gāminām sa tapyati ā nakha agrebhyaḥ nityam yaḥ mām samāśritaḥ lokāḥ tasya akṣayāḥ devi yadi api syāt su pāpa kṛt navamī aṣṭamī ca eva paurṇamāsī trayodaśī bhūtānām dayitaḥ ca eva divyam rūpam bibharti ca śrīvatsam yaḥ ca piṣṭena dadyāt hema phalam śubham kiret kṛṣṇa tilān ca atra taṇḍula akṣatam eva ca sa vai varṣa sahasrāṇi dviṣaṣṭim divi modate divya rūpa dharaḥ śrīmān devataiḥ saha nityaśas haribera mayīm yaḥ me dadyāt pratikṛtim svakām sarvagandha rasaiḥ yuktām niryāsaiḥ ca susaṃskṛtām pārśveṣu haritālam ca kṛṣṇa agaru manaḥśilām tasya puṇya phalam devi śṛṇu yat mattakāśini varṣa koṭi śatāni aṣṭau divi bhuktvā mahat sukham ratnāvalim tu yaḥ dadyāt brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ viś śūdraḥ strī vā sa me loke mad saukhyam prāpnute param ṛṣīn ca sarva devān ca rūpam ca āpnoti puṣkalam sarve devāḥ tathā viṣṇuḥ brahmā ṛṣayaḥ eva ca prajñā rūpa guṇaiḥ yuktaḥ saṃvatsara śata ayutam kṣīreṇa yaḥ mām satatam snāpayeta tris udyataḥ aparādha sahasram tu kṣame tasya aham antaśas saṃvatsaram tu yaḥ kuryāt kṣīreṇa snapanam śuciḥ sarpiṣā yaḥ mama abhyaṅgam karoti avimanāḥ naraḥ niṣkāṇām ca suvarṇasya sahasrasya phalam labhet saṃmārjanam ca yaḥ kuryāt saṃvatsaram anuvrataḥ vitarāmi śubham lokam nityam tasya dhruvam śivam liṅga pūjām tu yaḥ kuryāt mama devi dṛḍha vrataḥ śatam varṣa sahasrāṇi divyāni divi modate caturṇām puṣpa jātīnām gandham āghrāti śaṃkaraḥ nirmālyam yaḥ hi me nityam śirasā dhārayiṣyati brahmacārī śuciḥ bhūtvā nirmālyam yaḥ tu dhārayet tasya pāpam aham śīghram nāśayāmi mahāvrate dīpa mālām tu yaḥ kuryāt kārttike māsi vai mama avasāne ca dīpānām brāhmaṇān tarpayet śuciḥ dadyāt kṛṣṇa tilān ca eva saha siddhārthakān ca ha ye hi siddhārthakāḥ proktāḥ tathā kṛṣṇa tilāḥ ca ye tyaktvā sarvāṇi duḥkhāni mām eva pratipadyate na tuṣyāmi arcitaḥ tathā devi naga ātmaje tyaktvā sarvāṇi pāpāni nirdvandvaḥ dagdha kilbiṣaḥ apṛcchat puṣpyamāṇa āsyā kena tvam deva tuṣyasi tatas prahasamāna āsyaḥ sarva loka īśvara īśvaraḥ vacaḥ provāca bhagavā lokānām hita kāmyayā śṛṇu devi yathātattvam yena yānti śubhām gatim na ca prakāśayet guhyam nāma te kīrtayet naraḥ sadā sarva sahā iti evam prātar prāñjaliḥ utthitaḥ yaśaḥ kīrtim ca samprāpya rudra loke mahīyate sarva mālyāni yaḥ dadyāt sarva mūrtiṣu nityaśas somāya bhūtanāthāya bhāvanāya bhavāya ca kaṭaṃkaṭāya eva svāhā svāhā devāya śuṣmiṇe atha añjalim amāvāsyām su sampūrṇām samāhitaḥ tilānām ca eva kṛṣṇānām sarṣapāṇām ca pārvati arcayitvā yathānyāyam yathālābham prayacchati arcayitvā ca mām devi brāhmaṇān na ca tarpayet arcayitvā dvijān mām ca yaḥ me nāmāni kīrtayet caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamyām pakṣayoḥ ubhayoḥ api umāpate nīlakaṇṭha śānta śrīkaṇṭha gopate eteṣām ekam api yaḥ kathayet vā paṭheta vā amāvāsyām tu yaḥ nityam sa ghṛtam guggulam dahet kṣīreṇa ca eva saṃmiśram guhyam etat mama priye saḥ a acyutam sthānam āpnoti mad prasādāt na saṃśayaḥ arka parṇa puṭam pūrṇam ghṛtasya madhunā saha imāni ca mahābhāge yaḥ me nāmāni kīrtayet śmaśānanilayaḥ nagnaḥ bhasma śāyī yata vrataḥ vāmadevaḥ praśāntaḥ ca stabdha śephaḥ trilocanaḥ purāṇaḥ puruhūtaḥ ca mṛtyoḥ mṛtyuḥ jita indriyaḥ saṃsāra cakrī yoga ātmā kāpālī diṇḍiḥ eva ca japet etat niyamavān śṛṇuyāt vā api nityaśas na aśubhāya na pāpāya na anṛtāya kadācana śrāvayet bhaktimān puṇyam na apetāya kadācana dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam śānti vṛddhi karam śubham pūtam pavitram paramam maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam iti skandapurāṇe īśvarapūjā nāma aṣṭāviṃśatitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ūnatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca evam kālena samprāpya vārāṇasyām niketanam tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ devīm himavataḥ sutām uvāca devi paśyāmaḥ udyānam yadi rocate evam bhavatu deveśa yathā āttha tvam vṛṣadhvaja saha devyā tatas vyāsa vārāṇasyām vṛṣadhvajaḥ deva udyāna didṛkṣā artham vicacāra samantataḥ pūrvasmin sa diśā bhāge devyāḥ devaḥ pinākadhṛk udyānam darśayāmāsa nānā kusuma śobhitam campaka aśoka puṃnāga priyaṅgū cūta saṃkulam ramyaiḥ surabhi puṣpaiḥ ca ṣaṭpada vrāta sevitaiḥ saṃyuktam sarvatas śrīmat vanam vaibhrāja saṃnibham sa tat udyānam āsādya devīm āha jagatpatiḥ ūrdhvam go loka saṃsthānām gavām vatsaiḥ svayaṃbhuvaiḥ pīyatīnām payaḥ vegāt phenam mūrdhni samāpatat tatas mayā ūrdhvam dṛṣṭāḥ tu gāvaḥ tāḥ soma pārśva gāḥ tatas tāḥ prekṣitāḥ tatra mayāḥ gāvaḥ tadā abhavan tejasā dahyamānāḥ tu na eka varṇāḥ bhṛśa arditāḥ gāvaḥ pūrvam imāḥ devi āsan kapila varṇa jāḥ na eka varṇāḥ tadā abhūvan yadā samprekṣitāḥ mayā tāsām śaraṇya tām yātvā tābhiḥ mām eva śailaje goprekṣeśvaram āgatya dṛṣṭvā ca arcya ca mānavaḥ atrā api svayam eva aham vṛṣadhvajaḥ iti śrutaḥ sāṃnidhyam kṛtavān devi sa ca ayam dṛśyatām sthitaḥ kapilāhrada tīrthe snātvā na anya manāḥ naraḥ vṛṣadhvajam imam dṛṣṭvā sarva yajña phalam labhet salokatām mṛtaḥ ca api arcayitvā tu mām iha śānti artham sarva lokānām sarvāḥ dugdhāḥ payaḥ mṛtam tāsām kṣīreṇa saṃjātam hradam etat manoharam gaccha upaśamam īśa iti upaśānta śivaḥ tatas dṛṣṭvā enam prayataḥ martyaḥ svarga lokam avāpnuyāt atra aham brahmaṇā ānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā brahmaṇaḥ ca api saṃgṛhya viṣṇunā sthāpitaḥ punar brahmaṇā sa tatas viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvigna cetasā mayā ānītam idam liṅgam kasmāt sthāpitavān asi tam uvāca punar viṣṇuḥ brahmāṇam kupita ānanam dṛṣṭvā enam api deveśam mama lokam vrajet naraḥ punar ca api tatas brahmā mama liṅgam imam śubhe sthāpayāmāsa vidhivat bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ tasmāt svarlīnaḥ iti evam guhyam kṣetram mama smṛtam ānantyā sā gatiḥ tasya yoginām ca eva sā smṛtā vyāghra rūpam samāsthāya nihataḥ darpitaḥ balī vyāghreśvaraḥ tatas khyātaḥ nityam atra aham āsthitaḥ na punar durgatim yāti dṛṣṭvā enam amara īśvaram sa avajñam geṇḍukena atra tasya idam cihnam āsthitam ādau atra aham āgatya āsthitaḥ gaṇapaiḥ saha jyeṣṭham sthānam idam tasmāt etat me puṇya darśanam dṛṣṭvā imam mama liṅgam tu jyeṣṭhasthāna samāśritam kṣetram vārāṇasī puṇyā mukti dam sambhaviṣyati avimukta īśvaram mām vai yaḥ a atra drakṣyati mānavaḥ prāṇān iha tu saṃnyasya yāsyate muktim uttamām mama priyam idam sthānam jñātvā liṅgam pratiṣṭhitam śaileśvaram iti khyātam dṛśyatām idam āsthitam nadī vārāṇasī ca iyam puṇyā pāpa pramocanī kṣetram etat alaṃkṛtya jāhnavyā saha saṃgatā sthāpitam saṃgame ca asmin brahmaṇā liṅgam uttamam saṃgameśvaram iti evam khyātam jagati dṛśyatām saṃgame deva nadyoḥ tu yaḥ snātvā manujaḥ śuciḥ arcayet saṃgameśānam tasya janma bhayam kutas idam anyat bṛhat kṣetram nivāsam yoginām param kṣetra madhye ca yatra aham svayam bhūtvā samāsthitaḥ siddhānām sthānam etat hi madīya vrata cāriṇām yoginām mokṣa lipsūnām janma mṛtyu jita ātmanām dṛṣṭvā idam madhyameśānam janma prati na śocati sthāpitam liṅgam etat ca śukreṇa tava sūnunā nāmnā śukreśvaram nāma sarva siddha amara arcitam dṛṣṭvā idam mānavaḥ sadyas muktaḥ syāt sarva kilbiṣaiḥ purā jambuka rūpeṇa asurāḥ deva kaṇṭakāḥ brahmaṇaḥ a atha varam labdhvā gomāyu vadha śaṅkitāḥ abhavam jagati khyātaḥ sura asura namaskṛtaḥ dṛṣṭvā enam api deveśam sarva kāmān avāpnuyāt grahaiḥ śukra purogaiḥ ca etāni sthāpitāni hi paśya liṅgāni puṇyāni sarva kāma pradāni tu evam etāni puṇyāni mad nivāsāni pārvati kathitāni tava kṣetre guhyam ca anyat idam śṛṇu krośam krośam catur dikṣu kṣetram etat prakīrtitam gaṇa tvam labhate dṛṣṭvā kṣetre aasmin mokṣa āpyate gāṇapatya padāt tasmāt yatas sā muktiḥ uttamā tatas mahālayāt tasmāt kedārāt madhyamāt api smṛtam puṇyatamam kṣetram avimuktam idam śubhe mama puṇyāni bhūrloke tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamam tu idam yatas sṛṣṭāni lokāni tatas kṣetram idam śubham avimukteśvaram liṅgam mama dṛṣṭvā iha mānavaḥ sadyas pāpa vinirmuktaḥ paśu pāśaiḥ vimucyate śaileśam saṃgameśam ca svarlīnam madhyameśvaram hiraṇyagarbham īśānam goprekṣam sa vṛṣadhvajam upaśānta śivam ca eva jyeṣṭhasthāna nivāsinam śukreśvaram ca vikhyātam vyāghreśam jambukeśvaram dṛṣṭvā na jāyate martyaḥ saṃsāre duḥkha sāgare sa vidyut stanita ghoṣam sūrya ayuta śata uditam tatas pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasma abhyaṅga sita prabhāḥ yogi īśvarāḥ mahātmānaḥ tathā vaitānika vratāḥ punar nirīkṣya deveśam dhyāna yogam ca kṛtsnaśas tasthuḥ ātmānam ādhāya līyamānāḥ iva īśvare sthitānām sa tathā teṣām devadevaḥ umāpatiḥ saṃcintya paramām mūrtim babhūva puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ tasya tām paramām mūrtim āsthitasya jagatprabhoḥ na śaśāka vapuḥ draṣṭum hṛṣṭa romā girīndrajā tatas tat sṛṣṭam ātmānam buddhvā sā prakṛti sthitam prakṛteḥ mūrtim āsthāya yogena parama ātmikā tam śaśāka vapuḥ draṣṭum puruṣasya parātmanaḥ viviśuḥ hṛdayam sarve dagdha saṃsāra bījinaḥ anugṛhya tatas sarvān tān siddhān yati puṃgavān tam dṛṣṭvā śailajā prāha hṛṣṭa sarva tanūruhā tām uvāca suraśreṣṭhaḥ tadā devīm girīndrajām kṣetrasya asya prabhāveṇa bhaktyā ca mama bhāvataḥ pratimāsam atha aṣṭamyām pratimāsam caturdaśīm ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ devi vārāṇasyām mama āspade śaśi bhānu uparāge ca kārttikyām tu viśeṣataḥ pṛthivyām sarva tīrthāni vārāṇasyām tu jāhnavīm uttara pravahām puṇyām mama mauli vinirgatām pituḥ te girirājāt ca srutām himavataḥ śubhām saṃnihityā kurukṣetram sārdham tīrtha śataiḥ tathā puṣkaram naimiśam ca eva prayāgam sa pṛthūdakam sandhyā saptaṛcam ca eva sarvāḥ nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca samudrāḥ sapta ca eva atra deva tīrthāni kṛtsnaśas bhāgīrathīm sameṣyanti sarva parvasu kāśi gām avimukteśvaram mām ca kāśī stham acala ātmaje pṛthivyām yāni puṇyāni mahyam āyatanāni ca kedāre ca eva yat liṅgam yat ca liṅgam mahālaye madhyameśvara saṃstham ca tathā paśupatīśvaram śaṅkukarṇeśvaram ca eva gokarṇe ca tathā hi ubhau sthāneśvaram atha aikāmram kāleśvaram ajeśvaram bhairaveśvaram īśānam tathā ka ārohaṇa āsthitam yāni ca anyāni puṇyāni sthānāni mama bhū tale tāni sarvāṇi aśeṣeṇa kāśi puryām viśanti mām snātasya ca eva gaṅgāyām dṛṣṭena ca mayā śubhe sarva yajña phalaiḥ tulyam iṣṭaiḥ śata sahasraśas sarva āyatana mukhyānām divi bhūmau giriṣu api na atas parataram devi budhyasva asti iti kṛtsnaśas sthānam mama idam himaśaila putri guhyam sadā kṣetram idam su puṇyam kṣetre a asmin nivasanti ye sukṛtinaḥ bhaktāḥ sadā mām narāḥ evam etat su vistīrṇam nānā druma latā ākulam jāhnavyā alaṃkṛtam puṇyam kṣetram guhyatamam mama bhāgīrathīm iha āsādya vārāṇasyām mama āspade na atas puṇyatamam devi na atas guhyatamam kvacid na atas śubhataram kiṃcid na atas priyataram mama kṣetram mama idam sura siddha juṣṭam samprāpya martyaḥ sukṛta prabhāvāt khyātaḥ bhavet sarva sura asurāṇām mṛtaḥ ca yāyāt paramam padam tam triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavan piṅgalaḥ kena gaṇa tvam samupāgataḥ anna da tvam ca samprāptaḥ vārāṇasyām mahā dyutiḥ kṣetrapālaḥ katham jātaḥ priya tvam ca katham gataḥ śṛṇu vyāsa yathā lebhe gaṇeśa tvam sa piṅgalaḥ anna da tvam ca lokānām sthānam vārāṇasīm ca hi pūrṇabhadra sutaḥ śrīmān āsīt yakṣaḥ pratāpavān tad āśīḥ tad namaskāraḥ tad niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ āsīnaḥ ca śayānaḥ ca gacchan tiṣṭhan anuvrajan tam evam yukta manasam pūrṇabhadraḥ pitā bravīt na hi yakṣa kulīnānām etat vṛttam bhavati uta guhyakāḥ vata yūyam vai svabhāvāt krūra cetasaḥ kravyādāḥ ca eva kiṃbhakṣāḥ hiṃsā śīlāḥ ca putraka mā evam kārṣīḥ na naḥ vṛttiḥ evam dṛṣṭā mahātmanām svayambhuvā yathā sṛṣṭā sā eva vṛttiḥ praśasyate harikeśaḥ uvāca duṣṭā ca eva apraśastā ca garhitā sādhubhiḥ sadā vṛttiḥ svayambhuvā sṛṣṭā tyaktavyā yadi no bhavet āśrama antara jam karma na kuryuḥ gṛhiṇaḥ tatas deva tvam naḥ vimārgeyuḥ mānuṣyām jātim eva ca atha ced vihitam teṣām karma tad prāpti saṃśritam mama api vihitam paśya karma etat na atra saṃśayaḥ saḥ evam uktaḥ putreṇa pūrṇabhadraḥ pratāpavān vārāṇasīm samāsādya tapaḥ tepe su duścaram sthāṇu bhūtaḥ hi animiṣaḥ śuṣka kāṣṭha upala upamaḥ saṃniyamya indriya grāmam avātiṣṭhata niścalaḥ atha tasya evam aniśam tad parasya tad āśiṣaḥ sahasram ekam varṣāṇām divyam abhyativartata valmīkena samākrāntaḥ bhakṣyamāṇaḥ pipīlikaiḥ udyānam punar evā idam draṣṭum icchāmi sarva da kṣetrasya ca eva māhātmyam śrotum kautūhalam hi me iti vijñāpitaḥ devaḥ pārvatyā bhuvaneśvaraḥ sarvam pṛṣṭam yathānyāyam ākhyātum upacakrame nirjagāma ca deveśaḥ pārvatyā saha śaṃkaraḥ udyānam darśayāmāsa devyāḥ devaḥ pinākadhṛk virūḍha puṣpaiḥ paritas priyaṅgubhiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiḥ ca ketakaiḥ aśoka puṃnāga vanaiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ dvirepha mālā ākula puṣpa saṃcayaiḥ kvacid praphulla ambuja reṇu rūṣitaiḥ vihaṃgamaiḥ cāru kala praṇādibhiḥ vināditam sārasa haṃsa nādibhiḥ pramatta dātyūha rutaiḥ ca valgubhiḥ kvacid ca kāraṇḍava nāda nāditam kvacid ca matta ali kula ākulīkṛtam mada ākulābhiḥ bhramara aṅganābhiḥ niṣevitam cāru sugandhi puṣpam kvacid su puṣpaiḥ sahakāra vṛkṣaiḥ latā upagūḍhaiḥ tilakaiḥ ca gūḍham pragīta vidyādhara siddha cāraṇam pranṛtta nitya anugata apsaraḥ gaṇam prahṛṣṭa nānāvidha pakṣi sevitam pramatta hārīta kula upanāditam nibiḍa nicula nīlam nīlakaṇṭha abhirāmam kvacid vilāsa alasa gāminībhiḥ niṣevitam kiṃpuruṣa aṅganābhiḥ pārāvata dhvani nikūjita cāru śṛṅgaiḥ abhraṃkaṣaiḥ sita manohara cāru rūpaiḥ haṃsānām pakṣapāta pracalita kamala svaccha vistīrṇa toyam sāraṅgaiḥ kvacid upasevita pradeśam saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacid upalipta kīrṇa puṣpaiḥ puṣpa utkara anila vighūrṇita pādapa agram candra aṃśu jāla dhavalaiḥ tilakaiḥ manojñaiḥ kvacid añjana cūrṇa ābhaiḥ kvacid vidruma saṃnibhaiḥ kvacid kāñcana saṃkāśaiḥ puṣpaiḥ ācita bhū talam udyānam darśitam deva śobhayā parayā yutam idam guhyatamam kṣetram sadā vārāṇasī mama sarveṣām eva jantūnām hetuḥ mokṣasya sarvadā asmin siddhāḥ sadā devi madīyam vratam āśritāḥ nānā liṅga dharāḥ nityam mama loka abhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ nānā vṛkṣa samākīrṇe nānā vihaga sevite kamala utpala puṣpa āḍhyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛte rocate me sadā āvāsaḥ yena kāryeṇa tat śṛṇu vimuktam na mayā yasmāt mokṣyate vā kadācana snānāt saṃsevanāt vā api na mokṣaḥ prāpyate yatas prayāgāt api tīrtha agryāt idam eva mahat smṛtam jaigīṣavyaḥ parām siddhim yaḥ gataḥ sa mahā tapāḥ asya kṣetrasya māhātmyāt bhaktyā ca mama bhāvataḥ jaigīṣavya guhā śreṣṭhā yoginām sthānam iṣyate dhyāyataḥ tatra mām nityam yoga agniḥ dīpyate bhṛśam ātmanaḥ ca eva sāyujyam īpsitam sthānam eva ca kuberaḥ sa mahā yakṣaḥ tathā sarva arpita kriyaḥ kṣetra saṃsevanāt devi gaṇeśa tvam avāpa ha iha eva ārādhya mām devi siddhim yāsyati vṛṣabha yāyī sarva duḥkhānta kārī samara vṛṣabha ketuḥ candramauliḥ jagāma iti skandapurāṇe vārāṇasī avalokane jaigīṣavya dhanada pañcadūḍānām varapradāna nāmā triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ triṃśaḥ o adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavan piṅgalaḥ kena gaṇa tvam samupāgataḥ anna da tvam ca samprāptaḥ vārāṇasyām mahā dyutiḥ kṣetrapālaḥ katham jātaḥ priya tvam ca katham gataḥ śṛṇu vyāsa yathā lebhe gaṇeśa tvam sa piṅgalaḥ anna da tvam ca lokānām sthānam vārāṇasīm ca hi pūrṇabhadra sutaḥ śrīmān āsīt yakṣaḥ pratāpavān tad āśīḥ tad namaskāraḥ tad niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ āsīnaḥ ca śayānaḥ ca gacchan tiṣṭhan anuvrajan tam evam yukta manasam pūrṇabhadraḥ pitā bravīt na hi yakṣa kulīnānām etat vṛttam bhavati uta guhyakāḥ vata yūyam vai svabhāvāt krūra cetasaḥ kravyādāḥ ca eva kiṃbhakṣāḥ hiṃsā śīlāḥ ca putraka mā evam kārṣīḥ na naḥ vṛttiḥ evam dṛṣṭā mahātmanām svayambhuvā yathā sṛṣṭā sā eva vṛttiḥ praśasyate harikeśaḥ uvāca sṛṣṭā ca eva apraśastā ca garhitā sādhubhiḥ sadā āśrama antara jam karma na kuryuḥ gṛhiṇaḥ tatas deva tvam naḥ vimārgeyuḥ mānuṣyam jātim eva ca atha ced vihitam teṣām karma tad prāpti saṃsṛtam mama api vihitam paśya karma tat na atra saṃśayaḥ saḥ evam uktaḥ putreṇa pūrṇabhadraḥ pratāpavān vārāṇasī samāsādya tapaḥ tepe su duścaram sthāṇu bhūtaḥ hi animiṣaḥ śuṣka kāṣṭha upala upamaḥ saṃniyamya indriya grāmam avātiṣṭhata niścalaḥ atha tasya evam aniśam tad parasya tad āśiṣaḥ sahasram ekam varṣāṇām divyam atyativartata valmīkena samākrāntaḥ bhakṣyamāṇaḥ pipīlikaiḥ udyānam punar evā idam draṣṭum icchāmi sarva da kṣetrasya ca eva māhātmyam śrotum kautūhalam hi me iti vijñāpitaḥ devaḥ pārvatyā bhuvaneśvaraḥ sarvam pṛṣṭam yathānyāyam ākhyātum upacakrame nirjagāma ca deveśaḥ pārvatyā saha śaṃkaraḥ udyānam darśayāmāsa devyāḥ devaḥ pinākadhṛk virūḍha puṣpaiḥ paritas priyaṅgubhiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiḥ ca ketakaiḥ aśoka puṃnāga vanaiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ dvirepha mālā ākula puṣpa saṃcayaiḥ kvacid praphulla ambuja reṇu rūṣitaiḥ vihaṃgamaiḥ cāru kala praṇādibhiḥ kvacid ca kāraṇḍava nāda nāditam kvacid ca matta ali kula ākulīkṛtam mada ākulābhiḥ bhramara aṅganābhiḥ niṣevitam cāru sugandhi puṣpam kvacid su puṣpaiḥ sahakāra vṛkṣaiḥ latā upagūḍhaiḥ tilakaiḥ ca gūḍham pragīta vidyādhara siddha cāraṇam pranṛtta nitya anugata apsaraḥ gaṇam prahṛṣṭa nānāvidha pakṣi sevitam pramatta hārīta kula upanāditam nibiḍa nicula līna ā nīlakaṇṭha abhirāmam nava kiśalaya śobhā śobhita prānta śākham kvacid vilāsa alasa gāminībhiḥ niṣevitam kiṃpuruṣa aṅganābhiḥ pārāvata dhvani vikūjita cāru śṛṅgaiḥ abhraṃkaṣaiḥ sita manohara cāru rūpaiḥ haṃsānām pakṣa vāta pracalita kamala svaccha vistīrṇa toyam toyānām tīra jāta pravikaca kadalī vāṭa nṛtta mayūram māyūraiḥ pakṣa candraiḥ kvacid api patitaiḥ rañjita kṣmā pradeśam sāraṅgaiḥ kvacid upasevita pradeśam hṛṣṭābhiḥ kvacid api kiṃnara aṅganābhiḥ kṣībābhiḥ sumadhura gītavṛkṣa ṣaṇḍam saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacid upari prakīrṇa puṣpaiḥ āvāsaiḥ parivṛta pādapam munīnām ā mūlāt phala nicitaiḥ kvacid viśālaiḥ siddha aṅganā kanaka nūpura rāva ramyam bhṛṅga āvali śabali tāmra kadamba puṣpam puṣpa utkara anila vighūrṇita pāda apagram gulma antara prasṛta bhīta mṛgī samūham ūhāvatām tanubhṛtām apavarega dātṛ candra aṃśu jāla dhavalaiḥ tilakaiḥ manojñaiḥ puṣpa utkaraiḥ upacitam su viśāla śākhaiḥ kvacid añjana cūrṇa ābhaiḥ kvacid vidruma saṃnibhaiḥ kvacid kāñcana saṃkāśaiḥ puṣpaiḥ ācita bhū talam tuhinaśikhari putryā sārdham iṣṭaiḥ gaṇeśaiḥ vividha taru viśālam matta hṛṣṭa anyapuṣṭam upavanam ati ramyam darśayāmāsa devyāḥ udyānam darśitam deva śobhayā parayā yutam idam guhyatamam kṣetram sadā vārāṇasī mama sarveṣām eva jantūnām hetuḥ mokṣasya sarvadā asmin siddhāḥ sadā devi madīyam vratam āsthitāḥ nānā liṅga dharāḥ nityam mama loka abhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ nānā vṛkṣa latā ākīrṇe nānā vihaga sevite kamala utpala puṣpa āḍhyaiḥ sarobhiḥ rocate me iha āvāsaḥ yena kāryeṇa tat śṛṇu japa dhyāna udyatānām ca jñāneṣu ārakta cetasām tamaḥ moha hatānām ca vārāṇasyām gatiḥ nṛṇām vimuktam na mayā yasmāt mokṣyate vā kadā ca na snānāt saṃsevanāt ca api na mokṣaḥ prāpyate yatas prayāgāt api tīrtha agryāt idam eva mahat smṛtam jaigīṣavyaḥ parām siddhim yaḥ gataḥ sa mahā tapāḥ asya kṣetrasya māhātmyāt bhaktyā ca mama bhāvataḥ jaigīṣavya guhā preṣṭhā yoginām sthānam iṣyate dhyāyataḥ tatra mām nityam yoga agniḥ dīpyate bhṛśam atra siddhim parām prāptaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ mahā tapāḥ ātreyāḥ bhārgavāḥ siddhāḥ asmin kṣetre su durlabhe ātmanaḥ ca eva sāyujyam īpsitam sthānam eva ca iha eva ārādhya mām devi siddhim yāsyati anuttamām parāśara sutaḥ yogī ṛṣiḥ vyāsaḥ mahā tapāḥ brahmā api ṛṣibhiḥ sārdham viṣṇuḥ vāyuḥ divākaraḥ devarājaḥ tathā śakraḥ api ca anye divaukasaḥ ālarkaḥ ca purīm etām mad prasādāt avāpsyati sa ca enām pūrvavat kṛtvā catur varṇa samākulām sphītām janapada ākīrṇām bhuktvā ca su ciram tadā tatas prabhṛti cārvāṅgi ye a api kṣetra nivāsinaḥ gṛhiṇaḥ liṅginaḥ vā api mad bhaktāḥ mad parāyaṇāḥ iha kṣetre mṛtaḥ ca api saṃsāram na punar viśet ye punar nirmamāḥ dhīrāḥ siddhāḥ syuḥ vijita indriyāḥ vratinaḥ sarvatas mayi bhāvitāḥ dehabhedam samāsādya dhīmantaḥ sarga varjitāḥ saṃsāra bhūta dṛḍha pāśa vimukta śokaḥ vārāṇasīm mama purīm samupaiti lokaḥ atas parataram nā asti siddham guhyam adhīśvari vārāṇasī tu bhuvanatraya sāra bhūtā yatra āgatāḥ vividha duṣkṛta kāriṇaḥ pāpa kṣayāt virajasaḥ yānti muktim yaḥ āgacchet kathaṃcid ca purīm vārāṇasīm naraḥ kāśī puryām tyajet deham yadi icchet paramam padam etat smṛtam mama devi viśvam mokṣa ākhyam na saṃśayaḥ iti skandapurāṇe vārāṇasīmāhātmyam nāma triṃśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ etasmin eva kāle tu vyāsa dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ ayajat saḥ a aśvamedhena rājā prācetasa ātmajaḥ tatra devanikāyānām bhāgadheyāni sarvaśas anusmarantī tad vairam śāpa kāraṇam eva ca śliṣṭam madhurayā vācā kāraṇena samanvitam tvam devaḥ sarva devānām gatiḥ ca śaraṇam tathā devānām bhāgadheyāni vahati agniḥ ayam bhava na ayam tava maheśāna kim kāraṇam ati dyute ayam mūḍhaḥ aavaliptaḥ ca rājā prācetasa ātmajaḥ anusmaran pūrva vairam nā eva dāsyati aśāsitaḥ tasya ayam āgataḥ kālaḥ tad arthena vidhīyatām evam uktaḥ tadā vyāsa bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ pūrva janmani suśroṇi prajāpati sutaḥ śubhe mama tvam bhāva vijñānam kurvatī devi bhāṣase lalāṭe bhṛkuṭīm kṛtvā tatas devī āyata īkṣaṇā krodhāt kareṇa nāsā agram saṃmamarda śuci smitā tasyām saṃmṛdyamānāyām nāsikāyām ati prabhā jajñe strī bhṛkuṭī vaktrā catur daṃṣṭrā tri locanā sa khaṅgā sa dhanuṣkā ca sa tūṇīrā patākinī svādaśa āsyā daśa bhujā tanu madhyā tamaḥ nibhā ghana stanī pṛthu kaṭī nāga nāsā ūruḥ avyayā bhadrakālī iti tām prāha devīm devī śubha ānanā tatas aabravīt tadā devam eṣā sṛṣṭā mayā prabho bhṛkuṭī bhūṣita āsyaḥ ca baddha godhā aṃgulitravān kavacī baddha tūṇīraḥ śarī khaṅgī śarāsanī sa sṛṣṭaḥ praṇataḥ bhūtvā hariḥ nāmnā gaṇeśvaraḥ uvāca prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā devadevam saha umayā ājñāpaya sureśāna yat kartavyam mayā vibho tatas sa bhagavān aha harim tam gaṇanāyakam prācetasa sutasya asya yajñam gaccha vināśaya bhadrakālyā saha āśu tvam etat kṛtyam gaṇeśvara tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ gaṇeśān kāmarūpiṇaḥ sva gātrebhyaḥ aasṛjat dhīmān nānā rūpa dharān gaṇān pasparśa bāhum samyak ca tasmāt jātāḥ mahā balāḥ koṭyaḥ tāḥ navatiḥ ca eva śatam ca eva tadā prabhoḥ sa tān ca uvāca bhagavān yajñam pramathata anaghāḥ jagmatuḥ sāgara unnāda megha aśani nināda taiḥ devaḥ saha pārvatyā raibhya āśrama samīpataḥ sthitvā apaśyat gaṇeśānām karma tad yajña nāśanam vṛkṣāḥ kanakhaleyāḥ tu gaṅgādvāra samīpa gāḥ suvarṇa śṛṅgaḥ ca giriḥ meru parvata sannibhaḥ gaṇeśvara balam ca agāt bhīmam kālī purogamam tam saṃprāpya mahābhāgāḥ sarve dīpta anala prabhāḥ ūcuḥ tam yajamānam ca ṛtvijaḥ a atha munīn surān vayam hi anucarāḥ sarve śarvasya paramātmanaḥ iha abhilipsavaḥ prāptāḥ bhāgān yacchadhvam īpsitān tapasā yajña bhāga arhāḥ balena niyamena vā sarvam ca asmāsu api hi tat vayam api aṃśa bhāginaḥ atha ced svāminaḥ devāḥ tena bhāga arha tām gatāḥ svāmi tve ca balam hetuḥ tapaḥ vā na atra saṃśayaḥ tam brūta yaḥ jñāpayati vetsyāmaḥ hi vayam tatas evam uktāḥ tu hariṇā sarve deva puraḥsarāḥ ūcuḥ mantrāḥ pramāṇam vaḥ bhāgam prati gaṇeśvarāḥ ūcuḥ surān yūyam tama upahata cetasaḥ tadā yātāḥ tatas mantrāḥ brahma lokam sanātanam tatas śakra ādayaḥ devāḥ sarve ūcuḥ gaṇeśvarān teṣām sa garvam tat vākyam śrutvā hariḥ amitra jit mantrāḥ pramāṇam na kṛtāḥ yuṣmābhiḥ bala garvitaiḥ yeṣām ca lavattā vaḥ tān sarvān nāśayāmi aham gaṇeśvarāḥ ca saṃkruddhāḥ yūpān utpāṭya cikṣipuḥ prasthātrā saha hotāram aśvam ca eva gaṇeśvarāḥ gṛhītvā kupitāḥ sarve gaṅgā srotasi cikṣipuḥ vyanāśayan cikṣipuḥ ca śālāḥ ca anye aabhyadīpayan vyaṣṭaṃbhayat adīna ātmā tathā anyeṣām divaukasām bhagasya netre pūṣṇaḥ ca daśanān ruṣita ānanaḥ dhanuṣkoṭyā samāhatya miṣatām saṃnyapātayat viṣṇoḥ cakram ca tat ghoram yuga anta āditya varcasam vyaṣṭambhayat adīna ātmā kara stham na cacāla ha tuṣitān ca tathā devān udyuktān yuddha lālasān vāyavya astreṇa saṃhatya pṛthivyām tān nyapātayat anyān ca devān devaḥ sarvān yuddhāya saṃsthitān rājānaḥ ca api ye kecid tatra āyātāḥ didṛkṣavaḥ tān sarvān astra vīryeṇa sva gṛhān anayat balāt pradīpita mahā śālam dṛṣṭvā yajñaḥ tam tadā mṛga rūpeṇa dhāvantam gaganam prati hariḥ śaram sa sandhāya viśiraskam atha akarot śaram ca aparam ādāya vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān palāyamānam tam yajñam sasāra mṛga rūpiṇam nakṣatra sama tām yātum dvābaddham vītam abhyagāt evam te nikṛtāḥ vyāsa gaṇaiḥ kāltyā tathā eva ca hariṇā ca eva devena sarve śaraṇam āgatāḥ tān prapannān tadā sarvān devān sa muni lokapān deveśam tatas vaḥ bhavitā śamaḥ prasādayitum avyagrāḥ duḥkha śoka samanvitāḥ tatas te na atidūre tu sa ambam sa gaṇam īśvaram apaśyanta mahātmānaḥ sarve tad gata mānasāḥ te tam dṛṣṭvā praṇamya uccais tuṣṭuvuḥ dīpta tejasam vāgbhiḥ āhavanīyābhiḥ kṛtvā brahmāṇam agratas devāḥ ūcuḥ śipiviṣṭa kṛte viṣṇoḥ narasiṃha abhighātine mahā vimāna yānāya ṛtu vighna karāya ca pūṣṇaḥ danta vināśāya bhagna netra harāya ca viṣṭambhanāya śakrasya viṣṇoḥ cakrasya ca eva hi vyāghra carma bhṛte tubhyam kṛṣṇa carma ambarāya ca utpādakāya viṣṇoḥ ca jayāya vijayāya ca namaḥ harṣāya kopāya gaṇeśvara namaḥ namaḥ deva anutāpāya mṛga bāṇa arpaṇāya ca tvayā sṛṣṭam idam viśvam yajñaḥ devāḥ ca yajña han prasīda mā krudhaḥ a asmākam mā naḥ kṛtvā vināśaya uvāca prahasan vākyam sarva ātmā sarva bhāvanaḥ kruddhe hi mayi yuṣmākam na syāt jīvam kṣaṇa antare evam uktvā tadā devaḥ surāṇām hita kāmyayā prāveśayat surān sarvān tatas tān yoga māyayā te praviṣṭāḥ tadā deham īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ te paribhramya tān lokān kṛtsnān sarve bhaya anvitāḥ pañcākṣam gaṇapam vīram tatra apaśyan samāgatāḥ tena te sura śārdūlāḥ sarve hi ūrdhvam atandritāḥ ākṣiptāḥ tad muhūrtena lokam anyam upāgatāḥ apaśyan te mahābhāgāḥ nagaram sūrya sannibham sphāṭikena ati mahatā prākāreṇa abhisaṃvṛtam śṛṅgaiḥ ca vividhiḥ citraiḥ maṇi hema ujjvalaiḥ śubhaiḥ sapta yojana koṭīkam samantāt nagaram śubham rājatena āvṛtam divyam prākāreṇa indu varcasā tasya madhye ca ūrdhvam ṣaṣ koṭyā vistṛtam puram jāmbūnada mayena eva prākāreṇa su saṃvṛtam tasya madhye tatas ca anyat pañca koṭī pramāṇataḥ indranīla upalena eva prākāreṇa samāvṛtam catur yojana koṭīkam vistāra āyāmataḥ samam vaidūrya upala yuktena prākāreṇa abhisaṃvṛtam sarva ratna vicitreṇa prākāreṇa abhisaṃvṛtam teṣām madhye janapadāḥ sarva duḥkha vivarjitāḥ kṣudh pisā vinirmuktāḥ roga śoka vivarjitāḥ amarāḥ jarayā tyaktāḥ nityam mudita mānasāḥ dīrghikābhiḥ vicitrābhiḥ vāpībhiḥ ca api alaṃkṛtāḥ vṛkṣaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ citraiḥ sadā puṣpa phala upagaiḥ sarva bhakṣān prasūyante vṛkṣāḥ tatra apare śubhāḥ apare ca api alaṃkārān sarva vāsāṃsi ca apare sarva bhāvān tathā ca anye madhu ca amākṣikam śubham apare kṣīriṇaḥ tatra vṛkṣāḥ vyāsa mahā prabhāḥ kṣīram kṣaranti te nityam sarve gavyam samanvitāḥ sarvā maṇi mayī bhūmiḥ śubhā kāñcana vālukā tasya madhye puram ca anyat dvi koṭī vistṛtam śubham padmarāga mayena eva prākāreṇa pariṣkṛtam īdṛśāni purāṇi sma vyatikramya surāḥ tatas koṭī yojana vistīrṇam samantāt vahninā āvṛtam saṃvartaka anala ākāram durnirīkṣyam puram mahat advāram dadṛśuḥ divyam anantam te sura uttamāḥ dṛṣṭvā jagmuḥ puram ca eva vismayam bhayam eva ca tān bhīta vadanān vyāsa vepamānān sura īśvarān pañcākṣaḥ gaṇapaḥ prāha mā bhīḥ bhavatu vaḥ surāḥ idam tat su mahat ghoram puram ghora anala āvṛtam draṣṭvyam vaḥ mahātmanaḥ yad kṛte ca āgatāḥ tu iha evam uktvā sa pañcākṣaḥ śūlena anala varcasā paśyatām sura saṃghānām dvāram cakre mahā balaḥ te praviṣṭāḥ mahātmānaḥ pañca akṣa sahitāḥ surāḥ divyam dadṛśire pūrṇam siṃhānām tat puram mahat meru mandara kalpānām nakha daṃṣṭrāvatām tathā ghorāṇām agni varṇānām kruddhānām ati tejasām teṣām ekaḥ tadā siṃhaḥ chittvā bandhanam ūrjitaḥ viṣaṇṇa vadanāḥ sarve pañcākṣam śaraṇam yayuḥ pañcākṣaḥ uvāca na bhetavyam surāḥ devam darśayāmi adhunā hi vaḥ iti uktāḥ dadṛśuḥ śarvam sahasā te saha umayā na ca eva tat puram vyāsa na siṃham na api kiṃcana vepamānāḥ bhayena īśam śaraṇam paryupāgatāḥ tān śaraṇyaḥ sa bhagavān uvāca prahasan tadā dṛṣṭāḥ hi vaḥ mama krodhāḥ siṃha rūpāḥ bhayānakāḥ ekena teṣām raudreṇa yūyam sarve tarjitāḥ yadi sarvān aham krodhāt visṛjeyam kadācana na bhaveta na sandehaḥ sarve yūyam kṣaṇa antare iyam tu devī yuṣmākam kupitā parvatātmajā etām prasādayata vai na aham kupyāmi vaḥ surāḥ devī devīm mukhāt ghorām sasṛje bhaya vardhanīm daṃṣṭrā karāla vadanām bahu pāda kara aṅgulim dhanuḥ paraśu khaḍga ugra cakra śūla iṣu dhāriṇīm jvalardaka sahasra aṃśu tejasam viśva rūpiṇīm daśa yojana sāhasraḥ tasyāḥ dehaḥ pramāṇataḥ tayā abhibhūtāḥ te devāḥ vadhyamānāḥ ca sarvaśas na śekuḥ puratas sthātum vyāghrān mṛga gaṇāḥ iva tatas vyathita cittāḥ te kālakarṇī bhayāt surāḥ bhasma rāśim sthitam pārśve devasya viviśuḥ bhayāt tān dṛṣṭvā bhasma kūṭam tu praviṣṭān śaraṇa arthinaḥ surān bhasma vilipta aṅgān devī devīm nyaṣedhayat kālakarṇi nivartasva mā vadhīḥ sura sattamān ete pāśupatībhūtāḥ bhasmanā digdha mūrtayaḥ etat paśupati proktam vratam pāśupatam purā ete bhagavataḥ vaśyam anugrāhyāḥ sura uttamāḥ bhasma yena praviṣṭāḥ tu tasmāt mā etān vināśaya raudrāḥ paśavaḥ ete hi praveśāt bhasmasaḥ jātāḥ ca gaṇapāḥ sarve hantavyāḥ na tvayā īśvari na eṣām mṛtyuḥ prabhavati śaṅkara arpita cetasām mayā hi etat vratam śarvam caritam sārvakāmikam iti uktā kālakarṇī tu devyāḥ bhairava rūpiṇī kālakarṇīm nivṛttām tu dṛṣṭvā te surāḥ tatas śāntam ca bhayam ati ugram tuṣṭuvuḥ himavat sutām devāḥ ūcuḥ hara vara mahiṣīm mahādeva patnīm priyām tryambakasya ambikām vācam eka akṣarām loka saṃhāra kartrīm umām devadevasya pātnīm śubhām śaṃkha kunda indu hāra ambu gaura ugra daṃṣṭrām jayām āhaveḥ durnirīkṣyām acintya ugra dṛṣṭim viśāla īkṣaṇām pītakośeya vastrām mahā śūla ghaṇṭā patākā dhvajām divya gandha ājya dhūpa priyām kāla daṇḍa asi carma ugra hastām vapā śoṇita antra vasā pūrṇa bhāṇḍām diśām dakṣiṇām cāru cāmīkara ābaddha paṭṭām yugānta anala ābha īkṣaṇām aṭṭahāsān sṛjantīm yathā kāma kartrīm anaṅga āyudha avikṣatām śūrasenām nadīm viśrutām mandara āvāsa nityām diviṣṭhām prapadyāmahe kānasī iṣṭim asura mahiṣa daraṇīm dāraṇīm sundubheḥ sunda mārīm niśumbhasya mṛtyum vibhām soma mūrya agni bhāsām sṛjat kāntim iṣṭa pradām śoka duḥkha ārti hartrīm viśekām aghorām ghanām antakasya anta kartrīm rāja rājñīm manojñām karālām kṣapām daṇḍanītim sthiti siddhim iṣṭām śubhām kālarātrīm aparṇām samādhim śaraṇyām naga indra adhivāsa priyām kṣīroda nityām śubhām mahā kiṃkiṇīkām prakīrṇa ūrdhva keśīm pradīpta agni sandhyā abhra rāga tviṣam baddha godhā aṅgulitrām tri netrām jaṭā keśa rakta ambuja ābaddha mālām viśalyām an aṅgāri netra ulkā jām hema mālā nibaddha srajām dīrgha veṇīm su veṇīm yaśaḥ kīrti yuktām mayūra aṅgajā baddha citra dhvajām rājasām śānti kartrīm prapadye ā aham ekām sadā bhujaṅga śata kṛta aṅgadām mahā dānava prāṇa śauṇḍām citā bhasma rūkṣa aṅga keśīm mahā jānu lamba udarām sarpa yajñopavīta ṛddha vaktra uddhṛta akṣa ardha pāda ārdra hasta avataṃsām gīta hāsya pralāpa pramoda priyām jāpya homa upavāsa ādavāsā pravāsa adhivāsa atiriktām mahā yoga vijñāta sāra anusāra ugra sārām dhṛtim jyānu ghaṇṭā avabaddha ugra śabdām mahā megha vajra prapāta udadhi prakya tīvra ugra ghoṣām kriyām dīkṣitānām ca dīkṣām virūpākṣa bhāryām harasya ardha deha adhivāsām prapadye mukholykā udbhavām devīm ādyām parām pārvatīm sarva vidyā adhidevīm gatim yama niyama dama ātma bhūtām pitR̥ṇām ca kanyām śubhām parvata indra ātmajām dakṣa yajña anta kartrīm viṣṇu keśa apahartrīm mahā siṃha yukta ativāhām mahā bhairavām bhīṣitām skanda candra araṇīm mātaram hastivaktrasya ca agryām viśākhasya janma araṇīm nandinaḥ naigameṣasya ca utpādanīm sarva lokasya ca adya araṇīm pūjyām mātaram yoginām yoginīm dhyāyamānām dhṛtim deva vipraiḥ mahā yoga tarkaiḥ agamyām viśiṣṭa iṣṭa śiṣṭa adhivāsām ca lakṣmīm bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar janaḥ satya vairāja māhātmya loka araṇīm kāraṇīm indriyāṇām ahaṅkāra tanmātra kartrīm tamaḥ satva rāga pravṛttim parām ca pravṛttim maheśasya śaktim tathā cetanām prapadyāma devīm umām mātaram diśa tvam sukham mātar asmāsu tuṣṭā mahādeva patnīm śubhām yām vayam cintyām aikayā saṃvidā dhyāyamānāḥ sadā dāruṇam ca api sarvam kṛtam yat tvayā tat ca naḥ jāti koṭī sahasreṣu pūrvam kṛtam yat kariṣyāma yat kurma tat sarvam evam ca dadyāḥ ca naḥ sarvam artham sa kāmam tathā ārogyam ūrjām śriyam jñāna vijñāna nedhāḥ tathā dhāraṇām tarkam ūhām apoham dhṛtim ca artha bhāvam gatim ca eva divyām tathā dharma nitya tvam etān ca ye ca api atas aanye guṇāḥ tān ca sarvān juṣasva adya devi tubhyam namaḥ evam sā saṃstutā devī devaiḥ hṛṣṭena cetasā tryambaka anugrahāt ca eva devān tuṣṭā abravīt idam gacchadhvam vijvarāḥ sarve tuṣṭā aham vaḥ na saṃśayaḥ mā evam kārṣṭa punar devāḥ mā vināśaḥ hi vaḥ bhavet prakṛti sthān surān sarvān cakāra sura śatru hā uvāca ca etān deveśaḥ gacchadhvam vigata jvarāḥ yajñaḥ ca eva yadā kṛtyam tadā ayam bhavitā hi vaḥ sa śiraskaḥ diteḥ putrāḥ mantreṇa anena sandhitaḥ dadau ātharvaṇam devaḥ provāca idam ca susvaram nakṣatra sama tām yātu yajñaḥ aayam sura sattamāḥ bhadrakālī hariḥ ca eva gaṇāḥ ca ime mahā balāḥ sarve bhadrāḥ bhaviṣyanti yuṣmākam amarāḥ sadā evam uktāḥ bhagavatā devāḥ te brahmāṇā saha śirobhiḥ praṇatāḥ sarve śarvam ūcuḥ idam vacaḥ bhāgānām sarva yajñeṣu tubhyam sarvam dadāmahe cakāra rūpam paramam sarva deva mayam śubham sva ātmānam te tadā devāḥ hi apaśyanta maheśvare śiraḥ bāhu ūru pādeṣu vasti hasta udara ādiṣu avasthitān mahātmānaḥ munīn ca eva tapodhanān sa tat rūpam tadā kṛtvā devān provāca śaṃkaraḥ sarve yūyam mahātmānaḥ mad śarīra samudbhavāḥ yuṣmākam ca śarīrāṇi mad mayāni prapaśyata ātmānam ca api apaśyanta vismaya āpanna cetasaḥ evam sa teṣām deveśaḥ darśayitvā ātmanaḥ balam uvāca sura śārdūlān dṛṣṭāḥ hi etāḥ vibhūtayaḥ yaḥ yām pūjayate mūrtim bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ tasya tām mūrtim āsthāya pūjām gṛhṇāmi aham surāḥ na bhāgadheyaiḥ kṛtyam me bhāgadheyāni vaḥ surāḥ sarvāṇi eva dadāmi adya yāta sarve gata jvarāḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ sādhayitvā carum ca eva bhojayet brāhmaṇān śuciḥ parityakṣyati yaḥ ca atra kaścid prāṇān nara uttamaḥ jagāma bhagavān śarvaḥ sa umaḥ gaṇa śatiḥ vṛtaḥ devāḥ api rājñā sahitāḥ tasmin sthāne yathāsukham tasthuḥ brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca jagmatuḥ deva pṛṣṭhatas sa gatvā stokam adhvānam ubhābhyām sahitaḥ prabhuḥ na atidūre tatas prāha tiṣṭha viṣṇo mahā bala nirīkṣamāṇaḥ deveśam deśaḥ tasmāt abhūt asau kubjāmrakaḥ iti khyātaḥ viṣṇoḥ kṣetram samṛddhimat na ati dūram tatas gatvā bhūvaḥ devaḥ pitāmaham pradakṣiṇam samāvṛtya praṇamya prayayau tatas āvarttaḥ sva śarīrasya prakṛtaḥ puṇya karmaṇā aśvamedha phalam tatra snātaḥ prāpnoti mānavaḥ sādhayitvā carum ca atra bhojayitvā tathā dvijān tatas a abhyetya suraiḥ sārrdham brahmā viṣṇu puraḥsaraiḥ sa liṅgam tatra saṃsthāpya pūjām kṛtvā ati bhāsvaram tam prayāntam tadā dakṣaḥ brahmāṇam idam ūcivān pitāmahaḥ uvāca prasādaya mahā iṣvāsam śarvam ugram kapardinam tatas yajña samāptim ca lokān ca prāpsyase tasya saṃvatsara śate pūrṇe divye prajāpateḥ tatas dṛṣṭvā mahādevī vāyubhakṣam avasthitam liṅge paramayā bhaktyā pūjayantam maheśvaram uvāca hṛṣitā devī devam sarva sura arcitam kṛta añjali puṭāḥ vyāsa sarva deva patim patim kṣudraḥ duṣṭa cetāḥ ca stabdhaḥ mānī ca durmatiḥ diṣṭyā tvayā vinikṛtaḥ tvām eva śaraṇam gataḥ anujñātā mayā subhru tvam eva asya varam diśa ūcatuḥ paśya dakṣāvām tuṣṭau divyena cakṣuṣā kāma rūpa dharaḥ śrīmān gaṇeśaḥ ca bhavasva me akṣayaḥ ca amaraḥ ca eva duḥkha śoka vivarjitaḥ śṛṇuṣva bhūyas kim ca anyat prayacchatu maheśvaraḥ prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ bhūtvā idam āha mahāmatiḥ dakṣaḥ uvāca bhaktānām aśubha haram pinākapāṇim tam devam śaraṇa gatāḥ vayam sa bhāryam yaḥ a ajñānāt asura tayā ati māna mohāt na asmābhiḥ saha khalu pūjitaḥ aadri putryā yaḥ śāpam mama ruṣitaḥ dadau sureśaḥ tam devam śaraṇa gatāḥ vayam sa bhāryam yaḥ sraṣṭā sura gaṇa yakṣa rākṣasānām siddhānām ditisuta dānava indra nR̥ṇām bhūtānām paśu mṛga pakṣi patta gānām tam devam śaraṇa gatāḥ vayam sa bhāryam yaḥ kodhāt mahat asṛjat gaṇeśvara īśam siṃha indram harim amita prabhāva rūpam patnīm ca api abhita guṇa prabhāva yuktām tam devam śaraṇa gatāḥ vayam sa bhāryam yaḥ devān saha varuṇān sa vitta gopān sa brahmān sa śata makhān sa viṣṇu vāyūn indra agryān sa muni mahā āyudhān vijigye tam devam śaraṇa gatāḥ vayam sa bhāryam yat kiṃcid tvayi kaluṣam kṛtam ca duṣṭam hi ajñānāt api ca hi rāga doṣa mohāt tat sarvam mama saha bhāryayā adya śarvaḥ viśvātmā kṣamatu mahā anubhāva bhāvāt tatas evam sa deveśam stutvā sa asra āvila īkṣaṇaḥ prasārya bāhū sarveṇa śarīreṇa apatat bhuvi tam prapannam tadā devaḥ dakṣam sa asra āvila īkṣaṇam tasya aśrūṇi apatan carum kṛtvā nivedya ca gavām lokam mahā tejāḥ na ca tasmāt patiṣyati evam sa sṛṣṭvā saritam kṛtvā ca eva api anugraham tam āśvāsya sureśaḥ tu dakṣam prāha nṛpam tadā brūhi kim te punar sādho dadāni caran tṛptaḥ tṛṣ arditaḥ jagāma sāgaram pātum vṛṣa rāj surabhīsutaḥ saḥ mahā grāsaḥ sāgarasya tadā mahat madhyam vyādāya vadanam sa jhaṣam sa timiṃgalam tasmin pibati daitya indrāḥ sannaddhāḥ sa asi mārgaṇāḥ sa dhanuṣpāṇayaḥ sarve sahasrāṇi caturdaśa niṣpetuḥ śakra saṃkāśāḥ yama kāla anala upamāḥ maya putrāḥ mahā satvāḥ vṛṣabham prati vegitāḥ tān tathā ruṣitān daityān sa asi mudgara tomarān tān pītān pīyamānān ca dṛṣṭvā hi arṇava vāsinaḥ vitresuḥ sahasā sarve vineduḥ ca api duḥkhitāḥ tatas samudraḥ bhagavān pīyamānaḥ su duḥkhitaḥ vaḍavāmukham āgatya saṃvartam śaraṇam yayau sa ca analaḥ su saṃrabdhaḥ dattvā tasya mahā balaḥ abhayam vṛṣam āgatya provāca idam kṛtāñjaliḥ sarva bhūta śaraṇyaḥ daityānām ca ālayaḥ śubhaḥ na enam hīnam bhavān adbhiḥ kartum arhati vīryavān vṛṣabhaḥ uvāca tat me darśaya havya īśa pibāmi enam tava agratas evam uktvā vṛṣa indraḥ tu vaḍavāmukha vāsinam saṃrambhāt sāgaram pātum niḥśeṣam upacakrame aham tvām vārayiṣyāmi surabhīsuta katthana yat pītam chardayāmāsa tat toyam dānavaiḥ vinā visṛjya uvāca gaccha iti na tvām hanmi vṛṣa īśvara tathā api aham na garjāmi garjitaiḥ kim balīyasām visṛjya vṛṣabham vahniḥ āśu yātaḥ svam ālayam vṛṣabhaḥ jagāma eva duḥkha śoka abhisaṃvṛtaḥ saḥ a avamānena tejasvī mahā ukṣaḥ surabhī sutaḥ abalaḥ balī vahniḥ yena aham nikṛtaḥ tathā jīvita īśena bhūtvā ca na aham prāṇaiḥ viyojitaḥ adya prāṇān aham tyakṣye niyataḥ vratam āthitaḥ śatruṇā nigṛhītasya durbalasya durātmanaḥ jīvitāt maraṇam manye viśiṣṭam jīvitena kim saḥ evam cintayan ukṣā vācam śuśrāva khāt śubhām sa sraṣṭā sarva bhūtānām brahma ādīnām na saṃśayaḥ sa te duḥkham idam sarvam vyapaneṣyati bho vṛṣa etat śrutvā mahā tejāḥ sādhyasya su mahātmanaḥ himavantam girim prāpya tatāpa vipulam tapaḥ tasya vartṣa sahasreṇa tad parasya tad āśiṣaḥ bhagavān sarva bhūta īśaḥ sa ambaḥ sa gaṇaḥ ūcivān iṣṭān brūhi varān vatsa dāsye tān su bahūn api tatas sa devam saṃdṛśya sa ambam sa gaṇam īśvaram praṇamya śirasā pādau prāñjaliḥ su samāhitaḥ bhūyas bhūyas nirīkṣya enam nigṛhītam tvayā avyaya vāmam pārśvam tathā mṛjya rudram ekam sasarja ha kirīṭamālinam tri akṣam kuṇḍala aṅgada bhūṣaṇam baddha godhā aṅgulitram ca khaṅga divya astra dhāriṇam jagāma sāgaram vegāt dadarśa ca hutāśanam saṃvarttaka analam baddhvā devapārśvam upānayat vyāsaḥ uvāca etat icchāmi vijñātum vada tvam vadatām vara gaṇapaḥ uvāca svāmī sarvasya jagataḥ devaḥ candra ardha būṣaṇaḥ ājñāpayati vahne tvām vṛṣam enam prasādaya praṇataḥ a asmi iti tam brūhi vṛṣabham sa suhṛd janaḥ uvāca na tisaṃhṛṣṭaḥ tu idam vacanam arthavat yadi mām vakṣyati punar kariṣye tatas tathā gaṇeśvaraḥ uvāca bāliśāḥ vata ye prājñāḥ bala jñāna bahiṣkṛtāḥ te evam uktāḥ gacchanti yathā mām tvam prabhāṣase sakṛt ājñā balavatām sakṛt prabhavatām api dūtaḥ ca api sa vai śreṣṭhaḥ yaḥ bhavet artha sādhakaḥ visphurantam mahā pāśaiḥ neṣyāmi dyubhṛtaḥ saḥ evam uktaḥ tejasvī krodha dīpta anala īkṣaṇaḥ gaṇapam prati dudrāva tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tāḍayāmāsa balavān sa prajajvāla vegavān jvalantam tam tadā abhyāsam āgatam krodha mūrcchitam visphurantam mahā vahnim gaṇapaḥ krodha mūrcchitaḥ tam baddham pāśa varyeṇa patitam vīkṣya ca eva hi tasya putra suhṛd vargāḥ vividha āyudha pāṇayaḥ dudruvuḥ gaṇapam kruddhāḥ śataśas a atha sahasraśas upaninye harāya āśu paśum medhyam iva adhvare tam ānītam mahādevaḥ samprekṣya arṇava bhojanam uvāca vṛṣabham brūhi kim asya kriyatām iti sa tam kṛpaṇam ālakṣya mahā ukṣāḥ dīna cetasam praṇamya śirasā pādau idam āha kṛtāñjaliḥ dṛṣṭam etat tava vibho māhātmyam sadasatpate dṛṣṭaḥ a ayam kṛpaṇaḥ ca api hi abalaḥ ca mahā bala visṛjyatām suraśreṣṭha hataḥ eṣa na saṃśayaḥ putrāḥ hi asya hatāḥ sarve suhṛdaḥ ca eva sarvaśas etat vacaḥ maheśaḥ vai vṛṣabhasya āmi bhāṣitam śrutvā tuṣṭaḥ prahasya enam dahanam vyasṛjat tadā gaṇeśvara patim kṛtvā dvīpam asmai dadat prabhuḥ jāmbūnada mayaiḥ śubhraiḥ sarva kāma samanvitaiḥ tasmin kāle tadā devyāḥ sarve brahma puraḥsarāḥ tvayā hi adhyāsitaḥ pūrvam nādena apūrayat balī vegena ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ vimānaiḥ saha bhūtapa bhrāmayan tridaśān nādāt gagane saṃcacāra ha tvam naḥ gatiḥ ca deveśa śaraṇam ca eva bhūtapa sadā bhaya abhibhūtānām tvam trātā sarvaśas prabho yathā bhayam na bhavati yathā svasthāḥ ca nityaśas asṛjat vara dānāt ca gaṇeśam cāru kuṇḍalam ākarṇāt dārita āsyam ca mahā kāyam mahā balam mahā parigha bāhum ca vajra saṃhananam dṛḍham mahā daṃṣṭram mahā uraskam mahā khaḍga dhanuḥ dharam graha nakṣatra citreṇa taḍit sūrya avabhāsitā uttarīyeṇa viyatā bhāsvantam meru kūṭa vat abravīt sarva devānām samakṣam tam prabhākaram prabhākara mayā ājñaptaḥ tvam devānām guṇa ākara parama aiśvarya saṃyuktaḥ vṛṣavegam nivāraya jyotsnā bhavitrī patnī te tathā ca eva ajara amaraḥ tatas tam devatāḥ sarvāḥ praṇamya brahmaṇā saha jagmuḥ svāni kṣayāni sma devaḥ a api vṛṣavān babhau cakṣuṣī candra sūryau ca brahmā mūrdhānam āśritaḥ jihvāyām tasya varuṇaḥ vāyuḥ antar caraḥ svayam pādān viṣṇuḥ bhagaḥ ca eva pūṣā śakraḥ ca saṃsthitāḥ jaṃghāḥ śeṣāḥ tathā divyāḥ ūrūḥ ca eva samāśritāḥ rudrāḥ karṇau ca nāsām ca grīvā uṣṭhau hanum eva ca āyudhāni khurāḥ tasya cakra vajrau ca śṛṅgayoḥ apāne ca svayam mitraḥ puccham dānāni sarvaśas asthīni parvatāḥ sarve purīṣam śrīḥ abhūt śubhā mūtram ca asya abhavat divyam amṛtam vyāsa pāvanam romāṇi ṛṣayaḥ sarve nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvaśas grahāḥ tasya abhavan vyāsa sandhayaḥ śubha darśanāḥ iṣṭayaḥ veda yajñāḥ ca mantrāḥ stotrāḥ phalāni ca abhavan tasya māṃsāni rudhiram sarit arṇavāḥ mantra bhūtāḥ ca paśavaḥ sakṛt snāyuḥ ca vīrudhaḥ ballyaḥ vṛkṣa gulmāḥ ca tathā eva anye nagāḥ śubhāḥ nāgāḥ tasya abhavan nāḍyaḥ vasavaḥ śukra saṃcayaḥ āma pakvāśayau tasya tau devau aśvinau smṛtau meghāḥ tasya abhavan tvac ca taḍit mālā mānuṣāḥ mātaraḥ ca eva bhūtāni vividhāni ca romakūpāṇi tasya āsan vṛṣabhasya mahātmanaḥ evam sa bhagavān devaḥ parama aiśvarya saṃyutaḥ akhilam ca eva śṛṇuyāt vā paṭheta vā nityam śuciḥ adīna ātmā sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate mṛtaḥ ca kāle kāle vā rudra lokam avāpnuyāt na idam śaṭhāya dātavyam śrāvyam vā api kathaṃcana na nāstikāya duṣṭāya tathā vā pāpa karmaṇe idam śiṣyāya dhārmikāya mahātmane deyam śrāvyam ca śucaye guhyam etat sanātanam vṛṣotpattimāhātmyam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ a adhyāyaḥ catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vṛṣa vāhaḥ samabhavat yathā te kathitam mayā vyāsaḥ uvāca katham bhagavatī devī kṛṣṇā gaura tvam āgatā kāraṇam tatra kim ca api hi etat icchāmi veditum āsīnau mandaraprasthe umā kāma aṅga nāśanau remāte pramathaiḥ sārdham nānā rūpa dharaiḥ tadā atha devena tatrasthā krīḍatā sā kathā antare kṛṣṇa iti uktā bhagavatī sā cukopa manasvinī kupitām tām mahādevaḥ pariṣvajya mahā dyutiḥ uvāca asakṛt avyagraḥ sāntvayan madhuram vacaḥ hāsyam prakṛtam etat me kṛṣṇa iti samudāhṛtam adya prabhṛti na anena vacasā aham śubha ānane vakṣyāmi tvām tyaja krodham tām uvāca pinākadhṛk pañcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ sukeśam gaṇapam punar cakāra brāhmaṇam vyāsa tapaḥ satya parāyaṇam vyāsaḥ uvāca katham sa brāhmaṇaḥ pūrvam gaṇeśa tvam upāgataḥ kena asya tapasā tuṣṭaḥ gaṇeśa tvam dadau prabhuḥ āsīt vasiṣṭha kula jaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ satya vāc śuciḥ tīrtha yātrāsu abhirataḥ upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ vyāghram vyātta ānanam ghoram nakha daṃṣṭra āyudham tadā dṛṣṭvā tam sa tadā vipraḥ tyaktvā panthānam āśu gaḥ viveśa mahatīm ghorām aṭavīm prāṇi varjitām tatra apaśyat sa puratas vīraṇa stambam āśritān puruṣān lambamānān ca krandamānān su duḥkhitān tān avākśirasaḥ dṛṣṭvā lambamānān tadā dvijān pitaraḥ ūcuḥ narakāt iti sa tvam naḥ pātayiṣyasi duḥkhitān janma prabhṛti yat ca api mayā kiṃcid kṛtam śubham tena yūyam itas garttāt uddharadhvam pitāmahāḥ pitaraḥ ūcuḥ na vayam tapasā śakyāḥ na yajñaiḥ na api atas aanyathā na dārān āhariṣyāmi tārayiṣye ca vai pitR̥n tatas sa tān tathā utsṛjya duḥkhena mahatā vṛtaḥ jagāma rudram śaraṇam pitaraḥ a antarhitāḥ tatas pitṛṣu antarhiteṣu evam vāyubhakṣaḥ tadā dvijaḥ kāṣṭha loṣṭha upalībhūtaḥ nirucchvāsaḥ aavatiṣṭhata sandhāya mānasam rudre niścalaḥ su samāhitaḥ hṛdayena japan rudrān ākāśe samatiṣṭhata tasya pūrṇe tadā māsi vāta varṣam abhūt mahat duḥkham vā api athavā bhaṅgaḥ samyak evā avatasthivān viṣṇu rūpa dharaḥ bhūtvā provāca dvijasattamam sukeśaḥ tu tatas dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇam upāgatam viṣṇuḥ uvāca devaiḥ api na śakyaḥ a asau draṣṭum kim uta mānuṣaiḥ sukeśaḥ uvāca draṣṭum śakyaḥ na vā śakyaḥ kim ebhiḥ vaḥ vicāritaiḥ kugrahaḥ sugrahaḥ vā aham tathā api īśe śaṃkarāt eva cakra īśa śubham vā yadi vā aśubham varam kāṃkṣe na ca tvattaḥ na ca anyasmāt kathaṃcana tasya tam niścayam jñātvā saṃtuṣṭaḥ bhagavān haraḥ viṣṇu rūpam parityajya svam rūpam pratyapadyata uvāca ca enam vipra indra gaṇapaḥ me bhava akṣayaḥ aiśvaryeṇa ca saṃyuktaḥ priyaḥ mama puraḥsaraḥ imam ca mad kṛtam divyam trikūṭam nāma parvatam bhavanaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ yuktam kāmagam te dadāmi aham yeṣām kṛte ca putra tvam mām toṣayitum udyataḥ tāritāḥ narakāt ghorāt gaṇeśam tvām upasthitāḥ kiṃkarāḥ te bhaviṣyanti nityam duḥkha vivarjitāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ tava eva ime bhaviṣyanti vaśa anugāḥ sadā ca aṣṭaguṇa aiśvarya samāyuktaḥ cariṣyasi tatas sa dṛṣṭvā atha pitR̥t narakāt sa suhṛd janān tīrṇān gaṇeśvara tvena punar pūjyena saṃyutān maheśvaram hṛṣṭa manāḥ śirasā prāñjaliḥ nataḥ uvāca hṛṣyamāṇa āsyaḥ tadā vacana kovidaḥ sukeśaḥ uvāca amara tvam tathā akṣayyam tathā eva ajara tā varā pitaraḥ tāritāḥ ca ime gaṇapāḥ ca eva me kṛtāḥ icchāmi tvām mahādeva somam sa pravara īśvaram sadā su mukham atyartham su dṛśyam ca eva kāma da uvāca evam idam sarvam bhaviṣyati gaṇeśvara gaccha sva iṣṭām gatim vatsa devān viprān ca pālaya visṛjya tam tatas devaḥ sukeśam gaṇanāyakam jagāma adarśanam somaḥ sarveṣām eva paśyatām narakāṇām sa tattva artham pitR̥n papraccha yatnataḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca etat vistaraśaḥ tāta saṃkṣepāt vā yathātatham sūtaḥ uvāca jagāda vākyam sura loka vardhanaḥ purā kṛtam suṣkṛta sarva nāśanam iti skandapurāṇe sukeśavarapradānam nāma pañcatriṃśaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ āsīnaḥ kāñcane divye vimāne strī samākule pitR̥n sarvān samāhūya saṃpūjya vidhivat tadā sukha upaviṣṭān tān dṛṣṭvā idam vacanam abravīt sukeśaḥ uvāca yuṣmākam tejasā sarvam idam aiśvaryam īdṛśam bhavadbhiḥ tat kṛtam devāḥ yena asmni sukha bhāj kṛtaḥ pitaraḥ ūcuḥ na asmad prasādāt aiśvaryam tava putra kadācana vayam tu niraye ghore yātyamānāḥ su dāruṇe tvayā vayam su putreṇa tāritāḥ nirayāt yathā tathā na anyam prapaśyāmaḥ dhanyaḥ hi tvam sutaḥ hi naḥ bahavaḥ prāṇinaḥ putra yātyante tātra saṃyatāḥ sukeśaḥ uvāca pitaraḥ na ukta pūrvam me mṛṣā na ca vadāmi vai yathā prabhāvāt yuṣmākam aiśvaryam mama tat tadā śṛṇudhvam vadataḥ samyak mā avamadhvam vacaḥ mama nityam ca āśāsate ca eva prajāḥ naḥ santu puṣkalāḥ dhārmikāḥ ca kṛtajñāḥ ca sat karma ratayaḥ tathā teṣām tad kārya karaṇāt svadharma acyavanena ca sa dharmaḥ a anuṣṭhitaḥ samyak prajāḥ janayate śubhāḥ dhārmikāḥ ca vadanyāḥ ca kṛtajñāḥ sat pathe sthitāḥ pitṛ bhaktāḥ ca sarvatra pitR̥ṇām tāraṇe ratāḥ devam ārādhya narakāt pitR̥n tāritavān punar eṣa prabhāvaḥ yuṣmākam tapaḥ su caritam ca ha mama atra kim mahā prajñā anṛtam vā atra kim vacaḥ iyam ca vaidikī śubhrā śritiḥ veda vidām varāḥ pramāṇam yadi manyadhve ātmanā kṛtam iti uta aṅgāt aṅgāt saṃbhavasi hṛdayāt adhijāyase ātmā vai putra nāmā asi sa jīva śaradām śatam aṅgebhyaḥ a aham samutpannaḥ yuṣmākam hṛdayāt ca ha ātmanā aham tathā ātmānam yuṣmān tāritavān tatas tasmāt hi ghorāt narakāt tāritāḥ svena karmaṇā sva karmaṇā hi jantūnām phala pākaḥ vidhīyate harṣeṇa sa aśru nayanāḥ idam ūcuḥ tadā vacaḥ pitaraḥ ūcuḥ tvad anyaḥ kaḥ vadet evam yaḥ na syāt īśa saṃmataḥ yaḥ na syāt īdṛśaḥ putra katham tam sarva deva paḥ iṣṭaiḥ tu yojayet samyak yathā tvām go vṛṣa dhvajaḥ tvam dhātā tvam hi naḥ bandhuḥ tvam janetā mahāmate pitā tvam eva putrāḥ hi vayam tava na saṃśayaḥ atra te tarpayiṣyāmaḥ purāvṛttam mahāmate pitaraḥ ūcuḥ putrāḥ hi brahmaṇā sṛṣṭāḥ devāḥ yajata mām iti te yajanta tadā ātmānam teṣām brahmā cukopa ha uvāca ca enān saṃrabdhaḥ naṣṭa saṃjñāḥ bhaviṣyatha duḥkha śoka samāyuktāḥ dīnāḥ tam tuṣṭuvuḥ tadā prasannam tam samālakṣya te ūcuḥ śirasā natāḥ naṣṭa saṃjñāḥ vayam deva tān naḥ yaccha punar prabho tat kṣamasva ca deveśa ajñānāt yat kṛtam hi naḥ uvāca praṇatān devān sa anukrośam idam vacaḥ prāyaścittam mahāsattvāḥ caradhvam niyamena ha vyabhicāra kṛtam sarvam tatas pāpam prahāsyatha devāḥ ūcuḥ yayā jñāsyāmahe tāni prāyaścittāni lokapa svān putrān paripṛcchadhvam tatas śreyam avāpsyatha punar saṃjñām ca dharma jñāḥ mā kurudhvam atas pitaraḥ ūcuḥ tatas te sura śārdūlāḥ papracchuḥ svān sutān tadā prāyaścittāni dharmān ca vedān sa aṅgān sa vistarān te ca tebhyaḥ tadā putrāḥ ācakhyuḥ prayatāḥ śubhāḥ yātātahyena tat sarvam parameṇa samādhinā svān putrān abhyabhāṣanta prīyamāṇāḥ mudā yutāḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ putrāḥ na yūyam asmākam vayam putrāḥ hi vaḥ sutāḥ yaiḥ jñānam naṣṭa saṃjñānām kṛtam asmākam avyayam uvāca ca idam tān devān sarvān eva mahā yaśāḥ vadanti na anṛtam devāḥ satyam deveṣu vartate sutāḥ ca uktāḥ hi vaḥ sarve pitaraḥ na anṛtam hi tat tasmāt pitṛ tvam yuṣmākam putrāṇām nityam avyayam bhaviṣyati na sandehaḥ yūyam putrāḥ ca sarvaśas eka arthau putra śiṣyau ca tasmāt putrāḥ stha sarvaśas taranti putraiḥ pitaraḥ putrān tān tārayanti ca tārayitvā pitṛ tvam ca karmaṇā tena yānti te yūyam ca tāritāḥ putraiḥ ajñānāt narakāt tathā tasmāt ime hi pitaraḥ yūyam putrāḥ ca sarvaśas pāti yasmāt pitā tasmāt janayati api vā pitā pitaraḥ tān varaiḥ iṣṭaiḥ chandayāmāsuḥ avyathāḥ yathāgatam tatas jagmuḥ brahmaṇā saha sarvaśas pitaraḥ ūcuḥ yathā vayam tvayā putra narakāt naṣṭa cetasaḥ tāritāḥ cetanāvantaḥ punar ca pravarīkṛtāḥ pitā tatas bhavān pūjyaḥ yaḥ mahā praṇataḥ prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā pitR̥n vacanam abravīt evam etat yathā uktam vaḥ na anṛtam vaḥ vacaḥ śubham paraspara pitṛ tvam hi sarveṣām samudāhṛtam varam bhūyas imam mahyam prayacchata gaṇeśvarāḥ pitaraḥ ūcuḥ bhavān asmad pramāṇa artham vyākhyā tattvam iha icchasi śrutam vā api anubhūtam yathāśakti yathātatham sukeśaḥ uvāca bhavantaḥ narake ghore parikliṣṭāḥ su dāruṇe atas śruti jñāḥ sarveṣām narakāṇām asaṃśayam teṣām sa tattvam yogam ca kāla bhedam tathā kramam kiyantaḥ narakāḥ te ca kimpramāṇāḥ kimāśrayāḥ kiṃrūpāḥ ke kathayāmāsuḥ avyayāḥ pitaraḥ ūcuḥ ayam te janakaḥ putra suśarmā loka viśrutaḥ tatas suśarmā viprarṣe tam āmantrya mahāmanāḥ uvāca idam mahā sattvam sukeśam gaṇa sattamam suśarmā uvāca sukeśa na vayam sākṣāt patitāḥ naraka arṇave kim tu tad yātanā bhītāḥ cintayāmaḥ tu aharniśam kīdṛśāḥ te mahā ghorāḥ narakāḥ śruti dāruṇāḥ tatas te kathayiṣyāma yathāprajñam yathāśrutam gaṇeśvara īśa śṛnu me narakāḥ ye prakīrtitāḥ durāsadāḥ mahā durgāḥ sarva prāṇi bhayaṃkarāḥ dvitīyaḥ śālmalaḥ nāma tṛtīyaḥ kālasūtrakaḥ tathā vaitaraṇī ṣaṣṭhaḥ saptamaḥ ca api ayodhanaḥ aṣṭamaḥ padmaḥ iti eva mahāpadmaḥ tathā aparaḥ ete mahāntaḥ narakāḥ ucchrāyāḥ ca tathā apare ekaikasya ucchrayāḥ hi aṣṭau narakāḥ te kīrtitāḥ ucchrayeṣu sa viśrāmā yātanā bhavati īśvara itareṣu tu aviśrāmaḥ viśeṣaḥ hi eṣa kīrtitaḥ teṣām satata duḥkham tu nR̥ṇām pāpena karmaṇā bhedaḥ kṣayāt ca pāpasya kramaḥ teṣām pravakṣyate pramāṇam tu gaṇeśa iha na śakyam vaktum ekaśas kṣīṇa pāpāḥ prapaśyanti yathā tat śṛṇu me aavyaya yātyamānaḥ diśam ekām prapadyate sa gatvā śīghram adhvānam bahu yojana vistṛtam bahūn anyān an āsādya tasya antam vinivartate evam sarvāḥ diśaḥ gatvā hi antam a prāpya duḥkhitaḥ yātanā ante tu akaruṇam pāpasya ante tatas punar evam hi narakāḥ sarve hi anantāḥ ca akṣaya avyayāḥ na teṣām parisaṃkhyānam yojanaiḥ saṃvidhīyate kṛtvā pāpāni karmāṇi kṣaya ante duṣṭa cetanaḥ vyādhi ādhi yuktaḥ kleśena tyajati svān tanūn tatas yama dūtaiḥ mahā pāśaiḥ baddhvā duḥkha samīritaḥ viṣameṇa pathā deva nīyate vikṛta ākṛtiḥ keśa majja asthi paṅkaiḥ ca dihyamānaḥ samantataḥ tatra bhinna śiraḥ jānu pāda bāhu ūru bandhanaḥ kṛṣyate yamadūtaiḥ ca punar kaṇṭakibhiḥ drumaiḥ nīyamānaḥ vaśaḥ kleśān prāpnoti yama sādanam sa tatas yamam a prāpya dūrāt eva yama ājñayā somaḥ a agniḥ varuṇaḥ vāyuḥ sūryaḥ ca iti tadā naram sākṣiṇaḥ tatra jantūnām bruvate yat kṛta akṛtam narake pātyate ārttaḥ ūrdhva pādaḥ hi adhaḥśirāḥ tomaraiḥ ca ati tīkṣṇa agraiḥ śaraiḥ ca atha paraśvadhaiḥ kīlaiḥ ca muśalaiḥ ca eva kṣāra piṣṭena ca eva hi hanyamānaḥ divārātram vinadan karuṇam bahu varṣāṇām tu sahasreṇa narakam prāpnute a aśubham sa tatra patitaḥ bhūyas yātyamānaḥ su duḥkhitaḥ varṣa koṭim aviśrāntam niraya antam prapadyate mahā naraka muktaḥ ca ucchraya antaram āśritaḥ śītena vāyunā spṛṣṭaḥ sukham tatra sa vindati sa tam viśrāmam āsādya vismṛtaḥ yātanām tadā muhūrtam āhṛte svapne rākṣasena apakṛṣyate sa tena kṛṣyamāṇaḥ ca bhūyas duḥkha śucā arditaḥ karuṇam bahudhā atīva pravilapya avatiṣṭhate tatas bhūyas samākṛṣya yātanāyām sa rākṣasaḥ yātayati eva tam jantum sa viśrāmam sa cetanam evam saḥ ucchrayān prāpya aṣṭau pāpena karmaṇā saṃsāre kṛmi kīṭa ādi jantuḥ sampratipadyate ye tu gacchanti tān ghorān narakān puruṣa adhamāḥ tān aham sampravakṣyāmi tava putra samāsatas yātyante tatra puruṣāḥ mahāniraya gāminaḥ pakṣibhiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ puruṣaiḥ ca udyata āyudhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ aparṇaiḥ saṃyuktau sucībhiḥ vajrakaṇṭakaiḥ tayoḥ antaram ekam vai samam sūcībhiḥ āvṛtam anyatas puruṣaiḥ ghoraiḥ śastra pāṇibhiḥ āvṛtau ākāśe ca api lauhena tau jālena samāvṛtau ākramanti parakyām vai kanyā dūṣake eva ca nyāsa apahārakaḥ ca eva tathā māṃsa apahārakaḥ rasa apahārakaḥ ca eva yaḥ ca api para dūṣakaḥ indriya grāma ghātī ca mithyā liṅgī tathā eva ca mṛga śva apada hantā ca pṛṣṭha māṃsa āśinaḥ ca ye vṛthāmāṃsa āśinaḥ ye ca hiṃsām ye ca prakurvate yamaleṣu ca jāteṣu yaḥ na kuryāt nara adhamaḥ tatra vyāghraiḥ ca kupitaiḥ śarabhaiḥ ca tarakṣubhiḥ sarpaiḥ viḍālaiḥ patagaiḥ ayaḥ tuṇḍaiḥ ca bhakṣyate taiḥ bhakṣyamāṇaḥ yadi ca vṛkṣam samadhirohati tatra taiḥ kaṇṭakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bhidyate pakṣibhiḥ ca atha ced kandarām tasya guhām vā yātum icchati samāgamamya acalau kṣipram pīḍayetām atīva hi pīḍyamānaḥ sa yantreṇa ikṣu vat āturaḥ karuṇam krandamānaḥ tu yātanām tām samaśnute dagdhasya ca navam bhūyaḥ śarīram abhijāyate evam sa yātyamānaḥ vai bahūn abdān su duḥkhitaḥ dvāram labdhvā viniryātaḥ ucchrāyeṣu nipātyate śṛṇuyāt yaḥ aabhīkṣṇaśas sa na yāti eva tam ugra pāpa yogam yamalācalakathanam nāma saptatriṃśaḥ a adhyāyaḥ aṣṭatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ suśarmā uvāca atas param pravakṣyāmi śālmalīnarakam punar yātyante tatra puruṣāḥ su bhṛśam pāpa karmiṇaḥ śālmalīnām sahasrāṇi bahūni pravara īśvara uccāḥ sarvāḥ ca tāḥ ghorāḥ bahu yojana vistṛtāḥ mahā śākhāḥ mahā patrāḥ mahā kaṇṭaka saṃyutāḥ lauhena mahatā ca eva prākārena abhisaṃvṛtāḥ jālena mahatā sarvāḥ upariṣṭāt samāvṛtāḥ puruṣāḥ tatra tiṣṭhanti bahavaḥ ruṣita ānanāḥ vajra daṇḍa upala dharāḥ asi mudgara dhāriṇaḥ anyaiḥ ca vividha ākāraiḥ āyudhaiḥ vṛta pāṇayaḥ yātayanti bhṛśam jantūn avaśāḥ te su dāruṇāḥ chidyamānaḥ ca tatra api rākṣasaiḥ krūra karmabhiḥ diśaḥ prapadyate sarvāḥ vedanā ārtaḥ su duḥkhitaḥ garteṣu ca eva rākṣasāḥ sarvaśas śastraiḥ ca vividha ākāraiḥ nikṛntanti ati dāruṇāḥ śrāvayantaḥ purā anena kṛtam pāpam durātmanā tatas utthāya bhinna aṅgaḥ saḥ aanubaddhaḥ ca rākṣasaiḥ sūcī kaṇṭaka saṃyuktam deśam anyam prapadyate tatra sūcībhiḥ ugrābhiḥ kaṇṭakaiḥ ca āyasaiḥ punar tatra api enam samāsādya vividha āyudha pāṇayaḥ rākṣasa abhidravanti eva vairiṇaḥ vairiṇam yathā patraiḥ ca vividha ākāraiḥ ayaḥ tuṇḍaiḥ ca pakṣibhiḥ hṛta karṇa akṣi nāsā uṣṭhaḥ patitaḥ dharaṇī tale evam bahuvidha ākārāḥ yātanāḥ tatra duḥkhitāḥ prāpnivanti durācārāḥ ye tān nigadataḥ śṛṇu puṃsi yaḥ vā ucchṛjet śukram viṣa daḥ māṃsa vikrayī samudra yāyī duṣṭa ātmā yaḥ ca ekaḥ miṣṭam aśnute ghaṇṭikaḥ grāma yājī ca śūdra adhyāpakaḥ eva ca ete gacchanti durvṛttāḥ kūṭaśālmali saṃjñakam koṭī dvayena tu uttirṇāḥ varṣāṇām vai punar ca te ucchraye pātitāḥ stokam kālam viśrāmya vai punar pātyante narake tasmin yāvat kṣīṇam tad enasam eṣa eva vidhiḥ anyeṣām narakāṇām mune smṛtaḥ yaḥ imam bṛśa duḥkhita upalambham su kṛtīnām ati durgama acalam śṛṇuyāt prayataḥ kutūhala ātmā na sa gacchet nirayam hi śālmalam kūṭaśālmalikarthanam nāma aṣṭatriṃśaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ūnacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ suśarmā uvāca atas param pravakṣyāmi narakam kālasūtrakam samantāt mahatā uccena prākāreṇa su saṃvṛtam loha jālena ca tathā ākāśe yathā ekaḥ ca tathā sarve narakāḥ abhisaṃvṛtāḥ sa ucchrayāḥ ca eva vijñeyāḥ na vakṣye tān aham punar loka druhaḥ janāḥ tatra yātyante puruṣa adhamāḥ dharmasya ca ātmanaḥ ca eva brāhmaṇānām ca nindakaḥ chadmanā yaḥ ca śāstrāṇi punar gurum nindati yaḥ ca api pitaram mātaram tathā śvaśuram bhrātaram jyeṣṭham tathā ca anyān garīyasaḥ āśramāṇām tathā bhettā rahasyānām ca sarvaśas tisraḥ koṭīḥ tu saṃpūrṇāḥ varṣāṇām tu nara adhamāḥ yātyante mṛtyu vacanāt krandamānāḥ vicetasaḥ kālasūtreṇa mahatā mitvā mitvā tu duṣkṛtam chindanti aṅgāni jantūnām kuṇṭha agraiḥ āyudhaiḥ bhṛśam kiṃkaraiḥ taiḥ aviśrāntam divārātram atandritaiḥ viśrāmya sa tadā jantuḥ
