āhatya saṃghaśas yatra āste kauśikī devī tam śailam abhitas a asurāḥ atha dānava siṃhānām dhvajāḥ petuḥ yiyāsatām aśivam ca śivāḥ neduḥ dīptāyām diśi saṃsthitāḥ papāta nabhāsaḥ reṇuḥ kapota udara dhūsaraḥ upariṣṭāt ca senāyāḥ babhramuḥ gṛdhra vāyasāḥ pratīpam ca vavau teṣām rajaḥ garbhaḥ samīraṇaḥ parājaya nimittāni budhyamānāḥ suradviṣaḥ abhijagmuḥ kṛtāntena kṛṣyamāṇāḥ iva avaśāḥ ādideśa atha daitya indraḥ mūkam ārakṣikam tadā gṛhāṇa śulkam iti tām brūhi gatvā sumadhyamām sa gatvā vacanāt tasya praṇamya uvāca kauśikīm śulkam kila gṛhāṇa ārye dīyamānam suradviṣā vyavardhata mahā yogā yogam āsthāya kauśikī baddha godhā aṃguli trāṇāḥ sa āyudhāḥ bhīma darśanāḥ vāyasī vāyasa āsyānām strīṇām koṭyā samāvṛtā upakā kokila āsyābhiḥ tāvatībhiḥ mahā balā pracaṇḍā siṃha vaktrābhiḥ devībhiḥ abhisaṃvṛtā ugrā vyāghra mukhābhiḥ ca paritas parirakṣitā devībhiḥ śikhi vaktrābhiḥ ameyābhiḥ vṛtā anaghā jayamānā śva vaktrābhiḥ haṃsya āsyābhiḥ prabhā vṛtā prabhāvatī ca cakrāhva vadanābhiḥ mahā balā śivāḥ gomāyu vaktrābhiḥ aśivāḥ vidviṣām raṇe saramā śva mukhībhiḥ ca vṛtā parama durjayā vijayā śyena vaktrābhiḥ sarvatas parirakṣitā kaṃka āsyābhiḥ vṛtāḥ mṛtyuḥ hantrībhiḥ samare ripūn aśaniḥ kukkuṭa āsyābhiḥ bahvībhiḥ abhināditā revatī vṛṣadaṃśā ca pūtanā kaṭapūtanā alakṣmīḥ adhṛtiḥ lakṣmīḥ potakī vānarī spṛhā etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca kauśikyāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ mahā balāḥ nānā veṣa dharābhiḥ ca bahvībhiḥ paritas vṛtā biṃbhratībhiḥ vicitrāṇi kavacāni āyudhāni ca sasarja kauśikī tūrṇam haimān sāṃgrāmikān rathān vājinaḥ sa upakaraṇān mada unmattān mataṅga jān āyudhāni tanutrāṇi tūryāṇi vividhāni ca uvāca ca mahā yogā tāḥ devīḥ puratas sthitāḥ devyaḥ śuṃbhaḥ niśuṃbhaḥ ca bhrātarau deva kaṇṭakau netum mām kila saṃgrāme vijitya raṇa mūrdhani tau aham vinihaṃsyāmi śeṣān hata suradviṣaḥ ajarāḥ ca amarāḥ ca eva bhaviṣyatha mahā balāḥ iti tābhyaḥ varam dattvā samādiśya ca tāḥ tadā devīḥ devī mahābhāgā yuddhāya kṛta niścayā puratas samavekṣya kauśikī su kṛtam hema mayam nabhaścaram vividha āyudha varma saṃyutam pracalat piṅga saṭā kalāpibhiḥ nṛtyat mayūreṇa vikīrṇa bhāsā samucchritena atitarām dṛḍhena jagrāha vijayā chatram siṃhī sūtā tadā abhavat jayantī ca jayā ca asyāḥ dadhatuḥ cāmarāṇi atha tatas sā baddha kavacā vividha āyudha dhāriṇī āruroha ratham divyam kṛta āśīḥ jaya maṅgalā saṃbījyamānā ca vicitra daṇḍaiḥ su cāmaraiḥ indu marīci gauraiḥ tatas tāḥ tūryam āhatya neduḥ nādān pṛthagvidhān devyāḥ devyaḥ su saṃyuktāḥ babhūvuḥ ca purassarāḥ tena nādena daityānām hṛdayāni cakampire visasarja śakṛt mūtram hasti aśvam ca asure bale cakampe iva bhūrlokaḥ cukṣubhuḥ sāgarāḥ iva tadā tad devatā anīkam patākā dhvaja śobhitam balākā paṃkti śabalam sa indracāpam mahā svanam javena devatā anīkam saṃkṣipya iva diśaḥ daśa sainyavarṇanam nāma catuḥṣaṣṭitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ pañcaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha tāḥ devatāḥ kruddhāḥ daityān agrasarān tadā daityāḥ nānā āyudha upetāḥ devīḥ jaghnuḥ tadā raṇe abalāḥ balinaḥ vīrāḥ samare a amara dviṣaḥ turaṅginaḥ turaṅga sthāḥ padātīn ca padātayaḥ rathāḥ nāgāḥ turaṅgāḥ ca rathān nāgān turaṅgamān padātīḥ sādinaḥ śūrāḥ sādinīḥ ca padātayaḥ nirjaghnuḥ dānava indrāṇām prāsa śakti paraśvadhaiḥ pādaiḥ ca pipiṣuḥ śūrān nipātya bhuvi dānavān vibhiduḥ muṣṭibhiḥ kāścid śirāṃsi sura vidviṣām vidārya uraḥsthalam kāścid samare darpa śālinām papuḥ ca rudhiram devyaḥ prāṇaiḥ saha suradviṣām chinān ca khaṇḍaśas kecid hetīn utthāya vegitāḥ kecid mada ambu nisyanda śyāma gaṇḍa sthalāḥ gajāḥ pipiṣuḥ parama kruddhāḥ samare devatā rathān kapola bhitti saṃlīna matta ṣaṭpada paṃktayaḥ varmiṇaḥ kecid udbhrānta śita nistriṃśa pāṇayaḥ cicchiduḥ devatā anīkam devatāḥ dānavān api mattāḥ praticchinna mukhān ca kecid gandhena vijñāya gajān gaja indrāḥ ghrātvā tu gandham sahasā abhijaghnuḥ ādhoraṇaiḥ api abhisaṃgṛhītāḥ visphāryamāṇāni mahā dhanūṃsi mahā balaiḥ dāna kyodha mukhyaiḥ tāram viresuḥ samara ajireṣu krauñcāḥ iva vyomni śarad niśāsu tūrya svanaiḥ jyā tala sannipātaiḥ nāga aśva nādaiḥ ratha nemi ghoṣaiḥ devyaḥ samutsārya raṇe ripūṇām uccais vineduḥ prasabham balāni neduḥ ca nādān parihṛṣṭa cittāḥ protsārya devīḥ yudhi daitya yodhāḥ mahā vanāni iva samīraṇena samīritāni udgata pallavāni chinnāni vaktrāṇi purassarāṇām vicitra haima ābharaṇa ujjvalāni devībhiḥ ājau patitāni rejuḥ nikṛtta nālāni yathā ambujāni pratyāhatā vidruta bhīta nāgā sā devatābhiḥ nitahata aśva yodhā hatāḥ nipetuḥ samare nadantaḥ deva dviṣām añjana śaila kalpāḥ devībhiḥ ābaddha vicitra ghaṇṭāḥ marma atigaiḥ vāṇa varaiḥ gaja indrāḥ balāni teṣām abhisṛtya vegāt abhyāhatāni āśva paseru rājau mahā udadhim prāpya vivṛddhi kāle pratyāhatāni iva sarit jalāni devyaḥ ca daityāḥ ca mahā samāje virejire a anyonya visakta vāṇāḥ saṃsakta bhāsa upagame ghanānām abhre samūhāḥ iva tārakāṇām udghṛṣya nāmāni atha dānava indrāḥ nirjagmuḥ āśu sva balāt ratha sthāḥ kruddhāḥ su yattāḥ rathinām variṣṭhāḥ visphārya citrāṇi śarāsanāni megha svanam pratyudiyāya ṣaṣṭhī kārtasvaram mṛtyuḥ udīrṇa kopā drumeṇa lakṣmīḥ atha saṃyuga sthā mayena kāntiḥ saramā mureṇa ghanena caṇḍā niyatiḥ khareṇa prabhāvatī dhundhum ayāt sa roṣā daityāḥ yuyutsā utsuka mānasāḥ te devīḥ sa māyāḥ sa bhujaiḥ sa śastraiḥ abhyāyayuḥ śīghram a mṛṣyamāṇāḥ khyāta avalepāḥ sva rathaiḥ su yattāḥ jyotiḥ prakāśān tapanīya puṃkhān ākarṇapūrṇa āyata cāpa muktān saṃpreṣayāmāsuḥ adīna sattvāḥ bāṇa pravekān yudhi devatānām devyaḥ a atha teṣām niśitān su puṃkhān marma chidaḥ dūra gamān su patrān āgacchatām dānava yūthapānām bāṇān anantān sasṛjuḥ tathā eva te bāṇa mukhyāḥ vividhāḥ virejuḥ anyonya muktāḥ vyatiṣajyamānāḥ te pūrṇamāsyām vighane dina ante bhāsaḥ samūḍhāḥ iva cāndra saurāḥ chinnāḥ nipetuḥ yudhi devatābhiḥ bhujāḥ sa śastrāḥ ditija adhipānām nirasta bhogāḥ nibiḍāḥ bṛhantaḥ nigīrṇa jihvāḥ iva pannaga indrāḥ meghasvanasya atha raṇe tadānīm kruddhā śara oghān visasarja ṣaṣṭhī āgacchataḥ tān abhitas pṛṣatkaiḥ ciccheda daityaḥ śataśas bāṇān athā udvīkṣya tadā nikṛttān laghīyasaḥ a anyān visasarja tūrṇam daityaḥ tān āpatataḥ pṛṣatkān vrātaiḥ śarāṇām bahuśas cakartta nikṛttya bāṇān ditijaḥ punar tān cikṣepa ṣaṣṭhyā daśa rukma puṃkhān tān āśu ṣaṣṭhī prativārya daityam vivyādha ṣaṣṭhyā tapanīya puṃkhaiḥ kārtasvanaḥ kāñcana citra puṃkhān sasarja devyāḥ samare pṛṣatkān ciccheda tān mṛtyuḥ udāra puṃkhaiḥ anāgatān eva śarān śara oghaiḥ chittvā śarān tasya śaraiḥ vicitraiḥ vivyādha tam vakṣasi pañca ṣaṣṭhyā aśvān ca tasya āśu jaghāna mṛtyuḥ pṛthak pṛṣatkaiḥ tapanīya puṃkhaiḥ tat carma tasya āpatataḥ śara oghaiḥ cakartta mṛtyuḥ śataśas śita agraiḥ sa kṛtta carma āvaraṇaḥ sura indraḥ nistriṃśam udyamya niśāta dhāram abhyadravat mṛtyum abhūt tadānīm khe rohiṇīm meghaḥ iva abhividyut tam āpatantam yudhi kāla kalpam mṛtyuḥ śaraiḥ ugra bhujaṅga kalpaiḥ lakṣmīḥ drumam bāṇa varaiḥ ajayyā samākirat vāraṇa rāja līlam karṇa anta muktaiḥ niśitaiḥ ajihmaiḥ raṇa ajire cāru suvarṇa puṃkhaiḥ sa taiḥ vicitraiḥ śuśubhe viṣaktaiḥ mahā drumaḥ pakṣi gaṇeḥ iva āśriteḥ lakṣmīm tatas kiṃpuruṣa adhipaḥ vivyādha vrāṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ su puṃkhaiḥ vaktre sa pūrṇa indu samāna vaktrām bāhvoḥ pṛthak ca aṣṭaśatena dhīraḥ a cintayantīṣu varān vara asyāḥ mukhe ā asya tīkṣṇān nicakhāna bāṇān anyān asaṃkhyān ca pṛthak śarīre su patritān hāṭaka mṛṣṭa puṃkhān aśvān ca tasyāḥ caturaḥ caturbhiḥ sūtam ca vivyādha śareṇa tūrṇam nārācam ādāya tatas lakṣmīḥ jaghāna sūtam yudhi devaśatroḥ vivyādha vāhān ca pṛthak pṛṣatkaiḥ dhvajam ca ciccheda rathasya tūrṇam yantrā vinā tasya ratham tadānīm te sāyakaiḥ apratimaiḥ prataptāḥ saṃgrāma bhūmeḥ apaninyuḥ aśvāḥ prāṇān iva svān parirakṣamāṇāḥ kāntiḥ mayam bāṇa śataiḥ avākirat mayaḥ kāntim niśitaiḥ śara oghaiḥ nīhāra pātaiḥ iva sa andhakāram tadā tayoḥ antaram āsa tatra ādāna sandhāna vikarṣaṇeṣu sthāna krama pragraha tejaneṣu śikṣā guṇaiḥ tau aparaspareṇa viśeṣayāmāsatuḥ rāji madhye kāntiḥ mayāḥ tān nicakarta bāṇān mayaḥ ca kāntyāḥ viśikhān visṛṣṭān aśveṣu sūte sa rathe dhvaje ca sarveṣu gātra avayaveṣu sa asya a jihma gān hāṭaka mṛṣṭa puṃkhān mayasya kāntiḥ nicakhāna bāṇān mayaḥ ca kāntim sa rathām sa sūtām sa cāru citra dhvaja vāji mukhyām saṃcchādayāmāsa śitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ vana sthalīm meghaḥ iva ambu varṣaiḥ sūtam jaghāna āśu ripoḥ tadānīm aṣṭābhiḥ aṣṭau turagān ca bāṇaiḥ hata aśva sūtaḥ virathaḥ mayaḥ aatha nistriṃśam ādāya niśāta dhāram jñātvā eva kāntyāḥ samare prabhāvam vihāya yuddham viyut utpapāta vivyādha tīkṣṇaiḥ saramā raṇa ajire bāṇaiḥ muram dānava daitya yūthapam anyat dhanuḥ saḥ a atha tadā gṛhītvā vivyādha devyāḥ caturaḥ turaṅgān te vihvalāḥ śoṇitam udvamantaḥ daitya indra bāṇa abhihatāḥ turaṅgāḥ bhūmau nipetuḥ samare śvasantaḥ prāṇān jahuḥ ca āśu samam samastāḥ utpatya kham tasya tadā jaghāna yantāram aśvān ca mahā pramāṇān vivyādha devīm daśabhiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ śaraiḥ urasi ugra bhujaṅga kalpaiḥ vivyādha caṇḍā ghanam āpatantam śaraiḥ śita agraiḥ yudhi rukma puṃkaiḥ abhyadravat tān a vicintya vāṇān caṇḍām ghanaḥ sāyaka jāla varṣī āgacchataḥ tasya śaraiḥ su patraiḥ vivyādha caṇḍā ratha vāji mukhyān ciccheda daityaḥ samucchrita agram dhvajam turaṅgān ca jaghāna devyāḥ viceratuḥ maṇḍalam āji madhye bhūmim tadā agra aṅgulibhiḥ spṛśantau tān tān ca mārgān laghu pāda cārau chidram na ca anyonyam avāpatuḥ tau abhipluta uccapluta siṃhapātān nivṛttaka ākrīḍitaka ūrdhvabāhūn khaga apayāta abhihata apayātān niṣaṇṇaka āviddha śiraḥ abhighātān utplutya vegena tathā atha tasya śirodharām āśu cakarta caṇḍā sa kṛtta mūrdhā nipapāta tasyām saṃgrāma bhūmau urasā āśu daityaḥ sa śoṇita ādigdha vapuḥ tadānīm ghanaḥ parāsuḥ patitaḥ dharaṇyām vivyādha tīkṣṇaiḥ niryatiḥ su patraiḥ kharam śaraiḥ vakṣasi hema puṃkhaiḥ gurvī gadām ca āśu tadā gṛhītvā cikṣepa devyāḥ rudhira akta mūrttiḥ sā dānava agryeṇa gadā pramuktā vicitra hema ujjvala cāru ghaṇṭā saṃcūrṇayāmāsa ratham niyatyāḥ sūtam dhvajam ca āśu samucchrita agram vajreṇa bhinnaḥ śikhara agra deśe giriḥ yathā dhātu rasa pravāhī urasi udārāḥ daśabhiḥ śita agraiḥ ghanāghana vrāta samāna varṇaiḥ jaghāna sā ṣoḍaśa devatā areḥ turaṅgamān ṣoḍaśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ dhundhuḥ gadām bhāra sahasra gurvīm cikṣepa kārtasvara cāru ghaṇṭām tām āpatantīm śataśas cakartta prabhāvatī daitya pati pramuktām ādāya daityaḥ parigham mahāntam āplutya vāhāt abhitas sasāra devīm asau añjana śaila nīlaḥ raṇa ajire kālaḥ iva ātta daṇḍaḥ devyā samastān a vicintya bāṇān abhyetya tām āhava mūrdhni roṣāt acūrṇayat tam ratham āśu devyāḥ sa aśvam sa sūta dhvaja hema cakram dṛṣṭvā sa tām tatra tadā apayātām tam eva lauham parigham gṛhītvā tam marma gaiḥ marmasu bāṇa mukhyaiḥ saṃtāḍayat dānavam āśu devī iti skandapurāṇe śumbha niśumbha saṃgrāme devīyuddhām nāma pañcaṣaṣṭitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ devyaḥ teṣām vidita prayatnāḥ gaja uttamān āruruhuḥ sa yatnāḥ śucīn mada ambu sravataḥ su dantān praśasta gātra ambara hasta pakṣān su puṣkarān unnata vṛtta kumbhān su bāla dhīn añcita cāru karṇān su danta veṣṭān kalaviṅka netrān su vakṣasaḥ su āsana pṛṣṭhavaṃśān sāṅgrāmikān agrajavān vayaḥsthān su śikṣitān unnata pūrvakāyān tāsām patākā dhvaja śobhitāni vicitra nānā āyudha bhūṣaṇāni mātaṅga vṛndāni tadā babhūvuḥ vane vanāni iva samāgatāni daitya api te vāraṇa mūrdhni ṣannāḥ visphārayantaḥ vibabhuḥ dhanūṃṣi sa indrāyudhāḥ sa aśani śabda garbhāḥ śaileṣu meghāḥ iva sannilīnāḥ sainyāni tāni āhanane gajānām ādhoraṇaiḥ āśu abhicoditāni anyonyam āpetuḥ abhīritāni vātena vṛndāni yathā ghanānām vegena nāgān abhisṛtya nāgāḥ madān mada śyāma mukhān viṣāṇaiḥ loha abhinaddhaiḥ visakāṇḍa gauraiḥ śambūka deśeṣu abhijaghnuḥ ājau ādhoraṇaiḥ aṅkuśa pāśa vāgbhiḥ a vidhyamāna api mada abhidṛptāḥ chinnāni petuḥ niśitaiḥ kṣurapraiḥ samucchritāni ātapa vāraṇāni citrāḥ patākāḥ vividhāḥ dhvajāḥ ca paraspareṇa āhanane gajebhyaḥ yodhāḥ nipetuḥ pariniṣṭanantaḥ viddhāḥ śaraiḥ marmasu devatābhiḥ sa phenam āsyaiḥ rudhiram vamantaḥ dhanūṃṣi sajjāni karaiḥ dadhānāḥ devībhiḥ ājau ditija adhipānām vāta abhinunnāḥ iva gaṇḍaśailāḥ mātaṅga mukhyān patitān parāsūn raṇa ajire nīlagiri indra kalpān chinnāni vaktrāṇi sa kuṇḍalāni bhujāḥ sa śtrāḥ ca su candana aktāḥ petuḥ gajebhyaḥ a asura yūthapānām devībhiḥ ājau niśitaiḥ kṣurapraiḥ cukūjuḥ uccais paritas dhanūṃṣi vineduḥ āhatya surāri mukhyāḥ vipusphuruḥ jyāḥ parikṛṣya muktāḥ śara abhividdhāḥ ca gajāḥ niṣeduḥ nāgaiḥ patadbhiḥ viśikha abhividdhaiḥ samucchrita ūru dhvaja cāru pṛṣṭhaiḥ āstīryate bhūḥ anila pranunnaiḥ sa tālavṛkṣaiḥ iva śaila pādaiḥ nāgāḥ gajān āhanane a abhijaghnuḥ daityāḥ ca devīḥ ditijān ca devyaḥ daityān gaja indrāḥ dviradān ca daityāḥ kruddhāḥ sa roṣān abhisṛtya tatra śastra abhitaptaiḥ patitaiḥ samantāt mātaṅga vṛndaiḥ giri sānu kalpaiḥ saṃcāra yogyā na babhūva bhūmiḥ āyaḥ ghane daivata dānavānām abhyarditāni sva balāni dṛṣṭvā devībhiḥ ājau nihata dvipāni jñātvā tayoḥ āgamanam tadānīm devī calat piṅgala keśara āḍhyāt saṃcodayāmāsa rathasya siṃhān visphārayantī samare dhanūṃṣi jyānim javasya atha turaṅgamāṇām mada pramoṣam ca mahā dvipānām ājau samāsthāya param prayatnam śarāḥ surāṇām ripubhiḥ samastāḥ a prāpya devīm patitāḥ pṛthivyām parājayam prāhuḥ iva asurāṇām tadvat śara oghaiḥ ditija adhipānām raṇa ajire vyāpa balāni devī nipetuḥ āśu vyasavaḥ turaṅgamāḥ vicaskhaluḥ matta gajāḥ kṣarat madāḥ cakampire yodha varāḥ suradviṣām samam samastāḥ samare śara āhatāḥ arcirbhiḥ iddhaiḥ jvalitaḥ yathā analaḥ kakṣāṇi śuṣkāṇi dahati a vāritaḥ dīptaiḥ śara oghaiḥ samare sainyāni tadvat pradadāha kauśikī chāyām yathā sthāvara jaṃgamānām madhyandine a alpām kurute vivasvān devī tathā tām dhvajinīm ripūṇām alpa avaśiṣṭām samare cakāra āhūya devīm atha dānava adhipau visphārya cāpe mahatī bhiseratuḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ su patraiḥ viśikhaiḥ ca kauśikīm saṃchādayāmāsatuḥ āhava ajire daityau api iṣūn a vicintya śūrau gade pragṛhya ujjvala cāru ghaṇṭe udbhrāmya yatna atiśayena devyāḥ raṇa ajire cikṣipatuḥ bṛhatyau te vyomni bāṇaiḥ śataśas nikṛtya su parvabhiḥ hāṭaka cāru puṃkhaiḥ cakhāna ca anyān api sat pṛṣatkān suradviṣoḥ marmasu hema puṃkhān śuṃbhaḥ niśuṃbhaḥ ca rathau apāsya daitya īśvarau bāṇa vara abhitaptau ādāya nistriṃśa varau tadānīm utpetatuḥ vyoma śita asi nīlam dititanaya patī tau niṣpipeṣa āśu devī vigata bhaya viṣādaiḥ stūyamānā muni indraiḥ iti skandapurāṇe śumbhaniśumbhanipātanam nāma ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ saptaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ājagmuḥ kauśikīm draṣṭum atha vindhyam divaukasaḥ dharma aṅgirā uśanaḥ dakṣa vasiṣṭha bhṛgu kaśyapāḥ apsaraḥ yakṣa gandharvāḥ siddhāḥ nāgāḥ mahā uragāḥ upavedāḥ ca yajñāḥ ca vedāḥ vidyāḥ sarasvatī samudrāḥ saritaḥ śailāḥ tīrthāni vividhāni ca mātaraḥ lokapālāḥ ca nakṣatrāṇi dhruvaḥ grahāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ hṛṣṭa manasām āsīnām asura dviṣaḥ nighnatyāḥ devi lokānām duḥkha śalyam apākṛtam ṛṣayaḥ pāvanam devi haviḥ juhvati sāmpratam uṭajeṣu ca viśvastāḥ munayaḥ śerate sukham āsate nirbhayāḥ devi santaḥ sat mārgam āśritāḥ lokapālāḥ śirāṃsi uccais tvad prasādāt ca bibhrati pṛktaḥ puṣpa rajobhiḥ ca sukhaḥ vāti samīraṇaḥ jalāni devi saritaḥ svacchāni śiśirāṇi ca idānīm ca punar jātāḥ girayaḥ girija ātmaje vijvarāḥ śiśira svādu nirjhara udaka vāhinaḥ udanvantaḥ ca viśvāsāt idānīm sukham āsate siddha aṅganāḥ ca sevante viśvastāḥ devi sāṃpratam śikhareṣu mahīdhrāṇām utphullān candana drumān svabhāvāt madhu pānāt ca raktotpala vilocanāḥ vicaranti adhunā yakṣāḥ gandhamādana sānuṣu sukham bibharti vasudhām idānīm vigata klamaḥ śeṣaḥ phaṇaiḥ sva ratna aṃśu vitāna pariveṣibhiḥ mātā tvam asi lokānām bhītānām abhaya pradā vṛṇu devi varān iṣṭān abhiṣicyasva ca acyute su prasannam prasannām ca jananīm ca śaila nandanām pitṛbhyām ca api anujñātām abhiṣekṣyatha mām tatas tejasām iva sarveṣām saṃghātam puratas sthitam jaṭānām prānta babhrūṇām śirasā bhāram unnatam bibhrāṇam jvalitam vahnim dīptānām arciṣām iva karpūra bhaṅga gaureṇa snānam puṇyena bhasmanā madhyandine pradīpānām arcīṃsi iva divākaram sudhā ambu syandinīm tanvīm ekatas pariveṣiṇīm dadhānam maulinā kiṃcid kuṭilām aindavīm kalām vijihmām ujjvalām gurvīm dhūsarām bhasma reṇunā saiṃhīm vasānam ālambām īṣat bhaṅgavatīm tvacam mahatā bhogapatinā vakṣaḥsthalavisarpiṇā bhavānīm ca asya pārśva sthām dīpyamānām sva tejasā vasānām aṃśukam raktam kalpapādapa sambhavam mandāra mālām utphullām matta ali kula sevitām dadhānām uttamāṅgena sva reṇu utkara piñjarām svar śilpi ghaṭitaiḥ citraiḥ ratna aṃśu pariveṣibhiḥ śātakuṃbha mayaiḥ ślāghyaiḥ bhūṣitām bhūṣaṇa uttamaiḥ bibhratīm rucirām śuddhām śarad candra aṃśu nirmalām śirodhareṇa amahatīm eka āvalim anuttamām athā utthāya surāḥ sarve kauśikī ca ānata ānanā tayoḥ caraṇa padmeṣu nipetuḥ tuṣṭa mānasāḥ atha udvīkṣya mahādevaḥ kauśikīm idam abravīt ajeyā sarva bhūtānām mahā yogā mahā dyutiḥ vicariṣyasi lokān tvam sarvatra apratighātinī imāḥ ca devatāḥ sarvāḥ tvad prasādāt anindite bhaktyā bali upahāraḥ ca eva pūjayiṣyanti mānavāḥ vara dā ca api bhaktānām bhaviṣyasi sadā anaghe kṛtsnam rakṣa ca bhūrlokam pūjyamānā sadā avyaye śarvāṇī ca pariṣvajya mūrdhni ca āghrāya kauśikīm prāha prītā mahābhāgā mad prabhāvāt bhaviṣyasi arcayanti yathā mām ca surāḥ yakṣāḥ mahā uragāḥ atha indraḥ viśvakarmāṇām ādideśa tadā prabhuḥ ṛtūn ca sarvān tatra ittham ādideśa śatakratuḥ nānā puṣpa utkaraiḥ kṣipram bhūmiḥ samyak vibhūṣyatām kṣupa gulma latā vṛkṣa puṣpa reṇu sugandhayaḥ ākṣipantaḥ manāṃsi atra sukhāḥ vāntu samīraṇāḥ tāram nadantu śikhinaḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ sarvatodiśam nṛtyantu paritas citrān darśayantaḥ pṛthagvidhān rasān bhāvān vilāsān ca sarve gaṇāḥ suvīṇāḥ ca gandharvāḥ madhura svaram āhanyatām samantāt ca deva dundubhayaḥ bhṛśam pāṇibhiḥ kaṭhinaiḥ tūrṇam citra rūpāḥ mahā svanāḥ manda anila samuddhūtāḥ līna ali kula paṃktayaḥ patantu asmin pradeśe ca divyāḥ kusuma vṛṣṭayaḥ ucchriyantām samantāt ca patākāḥ citra mūrtayaḥ dhvajāḥ ca vividha ākārāḥ hema daṇḍāḥ susaṃskṛtāḥ atha āśu nirmame tatra viśvakarmā mahā dyutiḥ vajra sphaṭika niryūhām jāmbūnada mayīm śubhām indranīla ūru sopānām muktā dāma avalambinīm sa dhvajām sa patākām ca ghaṇṭā svana nināditām tapaḥ niyama yajñānām sākṣāt siddhim iva udgatām bhinna kālāni puṣpāṇi dadṛśuḥ devatāḥ tadā samam su puṇya gandhīni vicitrāṇi bahūni ca puṣpa kiñjalka garbhāḥ ca sukha sparśāḥ sugandhayaḥ nādayantaḥ muhur ghaṇṭāḥ vavuḥ tatra samīraṇāḥ prajaguḥ sura gandharvāḥ nanṛtuḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ gībhiḥ puṇyābhiḥ kauśikīm tadā sarva ratna auṣadhaiḥ gandhaiḥ pūrṇāḥ puṇyaiḥ ca vāribhiḥ ānītāḥ tatra kalaśāḥ hema ratna mayāḥ śubhāḥ kalpayāmāsa devyāḥ ca viśvakarmā varāsanam ṛṣibhiḥ devatābhiḥ ca devadeva sutā tatas tasmin siṃhāsane divye niṣasāda atha kauśikī muktā dāma avabaddha aṅgī śukla sraj anulepanā tatas saptarṣayaḥ viṣṇuḥ dharmaḥ yajñaḥ prajāpatiḥ ādityāḥ kaśyapaḥ rudrāḥ lokapālāḥ hutāśanāḥ pṛthivī gaṅgā candramāḥ marutaḥ samudrāḥ vasavaḥ lakṣmīḥ sandhyā kīrtiḥ sarasvatī nāga indrāḥ vihaga īśāḥ ca vividhāḥ ca sarit varāḥ ādāya kalaśān sarvān abhyaṣiñcanta kauśikīm pūrṇa indu bimba pratimam ratna daṇḍam mahā dyutim cāmaraiḥ hema daṇḍaiḥ ca dīrghaiḥ candra aṃśu nirmalaiḥ bījayāmāsuḥ āyastaiḥ lokapālāḥ tadā avyayām uvāca sa tatas śrīmān kauśikīm pākaśāsanaḥ pāhi kṛtsnām bhuvam devaḥ bhaginī tvam mama avyaye bhaktān anugṛhāṇa īśe jahi ca amara kaṇṭakān vicarasva samastān ca lokān siddha gaṇa arcitā iti vacanam atha uktvā kauśikīm devarājaḥ tridaśa gaṇa sametaḥ śubhra lola uru hāraḥ yaḥ imam śṛṇuyāt nityam paṭhet vā sat samāgame saptaṣaṣṭitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha tāḥ devatāḥ devī kauśikī deha saṃbhavāḥ nyaveśayan mahābhāgāḥ deśeṣu nagareṣu ca bahuputrām pralambām ca laṅkāyām sannyaveśayat lamba oṣṭhīm vṛṣadaṃśām ca kinnarīm ca eva siṃhale gokarṇe revatīm devīm pāṇḍyeṣu mukhamaṇḍikām ābhīreṣu aśivām ca eva śāntim ca varaṇā taṭe vatsagulme prabhām devīm lakṣmīm kolagirau api upakām pārasīkeṣu vāyasīm yavaneṣu ca pracaṇḍām ca tuṣāreṣu kośaleṣu ca lambikām jayām ca vijayām ca eva sva pure saṃnyaveśayat prabhāvatīm kaliṅgeṣu jayantīm nāgasāhvaye kāśmīreṣu ca sā ṣaṣṭhīm saramām malayeṣu ca pūtanām ca supīreṣu mṛtyum pṛṣṭapure tathā koṭīvarṣe bāhumāṃsām pauṇḍreṣu kaṭapūtanām a spṛṣṭām madhyadeśe tu kinnarīm barbareṣu ca vārāṇasyām nirāyāsyām citraghaṇṭām ca kauśikīm mahākālīm mahākāle vānarīm śabareṣu ca śeṣāḥ ca devatāḥ sarvāḥ grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca karvaṭeṣu mahīdhreṣu kauśikī saṃnyaveśayat kasyacid tu atha kālasya svarṇa akṣe hi mahā tapāḥ yatra viṣṇuḥ varam lebhe devam ārādhya śaṅkaram cakram sudarśanam nāma dviṣatām antaka upamam ṛṣiḥ āste mahābhāgaḥ śaradvān nāma gautamaḥ tasya yajñam jagāma atha devī tena nimantritā tasyāḥ tatra āgamam jñātvā sūnuḥ śumbhasya vīryavān ājagāma āśu tam deśam mahiṣaḥ nāma dānavaḥ su saṃhataḥ pṛthu uraskaḥ mahā grīvaḥ su bāladhiḥ vakra śṛṅgaḥ pṛthu khuraḥ viśāla ucchrita mastakaḥ vajra niṣpeṣa paruṣam nardamānaḥ mahā svanaḥ devyāḥ panthānam āvarya dānava indra sutaḥ sthitaḥ vijñāya tasya āgamanam yoga īśāḥ vindhyavāsinī jagāma tvaritā tatra yatra asau dānava adhamaḥ atha dṛṣṭvā sa tām devīm krodhāt raktatara īkṣaṇaḥ abhyājagāma vegena yatnam āsthāya dānavaḥ udbāladhiḥ tīkṣṇa viṣāṇa koṭiḥ su pīna vakṣāḥ kaṭhina ūrdhva karṇaḥ tam kauśikī vīkṣya tadā āpatantam daitya indra putram mahiṣam sa roṣam abhyetya tām dānava rāja sūnuḥ balena mattaḥ parameṇa devīm abhyāhanat vakṣasi lola hāre śṛṅgeṇa śakrāyudha karkaśena viṣahya tam tasya tadā prahāram jagrāha śṛṅge mahiṣam kareṇa udgṛhya sā bāladhim indra śatroḥ kṛtvā ca pādam śirasi prasahya triśūlam ādāya bibheda pṛṣṭhe vyayojayat ca asubhiḥ āśu daityam kuliśa kaṭhina śṛṅgam nīla jīmūta kalpam mahiṣam atha nihatya prauḍha darpam tadānīm vividha kusuma vṛṣṭyā sarvatas kīryamāṇā dharaṇidharam agacchat kauśikī sannivāsam mahiṣāsuravadhaḥ nāma aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tapaḥ kṛtvā tadā devī puṣkalam himavat sutā somanandī ca śārdūlaḥ kim avāpa varam śubham namaskṛtya mahādevam paramam brahma śāśvatam yam paṭhanti sadā sāṃkhyāḥ puruṣam paṃcaviṃsakam yoginaḥ ca eva ṣaḍviṃśam brahma ādyāḥ ca divaukasaḥ praṇamya parayā bhaktyā śirasā tam trilocanam gauryā samāgamaḥ vyāsa śaṅkarasya yathā bhavat tat pravakṣyāmi te sarvam śṛṇu yoga vidām vara tasmin himavataḥ śṛṅge tapaḥ kṛtvā su duṣkaram gaura aṅgī sā tadā bhūtvā śuddha hema sama prabhā darśane śaṅkarasya atha śarvāṇī matim ādadhe nandinam gaṇapam devī dīpta paṭṭiśa dhāriṇam tatas nandīśvaram dṛṣṭvā bhaktam premṇā girīndrajā ehi vatsa cirāt dṛṣṭaḥ tvam iti uktavatī tadā nandī saṃprekṣya tām ca api gaura aṅgīm hema saprabhām harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaḥ pādayoḥ apatat bhṛśam praṇamya sa tadā dhīmān astuvat parvatātmajām tvam kriyā kāraṇam tvam ca prakṛtiḥ muktiḥ eva ca āntiḥ dyutiḥ tathā tuṣṭiḥ śāntiḥ svastyayanam param dakṣiṇā niyatiḥ mṛtyuḥ sandhyā vidyut ahar kṣapā pṛthivī kauśikī śrīḥ ca śarvāṇī śarva vallabhā gaṇamātā ditiḥ ca eva pavitrā vindhyavāsinī atha devī tadā dṛṣṭvā nandinam pādayoḥ natam evam astu iti sā procya praviveśa āyata īkṣaṇā agratas yayau nandī somanandī ca pṛṣṭhatas ājagāma mahā tejāḥ saṃbhrama utphulla locanaḥ atha devaḥ tadā āyātām devīm giri vara ātmajām samuvāca suraśreṣṭhaḥ samālokya muhur muhur diṣṭyā asi prīta vadanā diṣṭyā ca saphalam tapaḥ diṣṭyā ca idam varam varṇam gauram kanaka saprabham priyam naḥ sarvathā devi paramam yat tvam āgatā pratijñām pūrayitvā iha śārdūlaḥ a ayam kutas ca te evam uktā tadā devī bhartrā praṇaya peśalam kathayāmāsa devāya sarvam caritam ātmanaḥ prāk aham yat tvayā deva kṛṣṇa varṇā iti bhāṣitā tadā manyu parīta aṅgī gaura varṇa samīpsayā tasmin eva eṣa śārdūlaḥ somanandī mama agratas vyatiṣṭhata mahādeva bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ tāvantam kālam eṣaḥ mama atiṣṭhat samīpatas stabdha lāṅgūla netra āsyaḥ nirāhāraḥ vilokayan tam aham pūrvam asya arthe varam saṃprārthayam vibho mama eva anucaraḥ pārśve kṛtaḥ yogī ca śaṅkara varṇam ca idam adāt mahyam tava ādeśāt pitāmahaḥ mṛgendraḥ gaṇa śreṣṭhaḥ soma nandī mahā balaḥ yādṛśaḥ mama nandīśaḥ tādṛśaḥ te bhaviṣyati tam bhūyas a api tvayā sārdham draṣṭum icchāmi śaṅkara evam uktaḥ sa pārvatyā provāca parameśvaraḥ nandinam sa tadā āhūya gaṇapān ca sahasraśas vandyamānaḥ aasakṛt devaḥ stūyamānaḥ ca sarvaśas nandinaḥ pṛṣṭham ārūḍhaḥ prakrīḍita gaṇa īśvaraḥ sa tam śikharam āsādya ramya dhātu vibhūṣitam āgatam tam atho dṛṣṭvā mūrimān acalaḥ tadā upatasthe mahādevam praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ vara dānena śaila indram anvagṛhṇāt pinākadhṛk puṇyaḥ tvam acala śreṣṭha bhavitā pāpa mocanaḥ dūrāt eva naga śreṣṭha dṛṣṭvā tvām ucchritam janāḥ dṛṣṭvā gaurīm atha abhyarcya tarpayiṣyati nārī vā atha naraḥ vā api lokam gauryāḥ sa yāsyati yaḥ ca iha tyakṣyate prāṇān niyamena samāhitaḥ sa gāṇapatyam samprāpya mayā sārdham cariṣyati gauryāḥ ca atrā eva sānnidhyam sarvadā te bhaviṣyati iti uktvā tam naga śreṣṭham devadevaḥ trilocanaḥ athā apaśyat śilām vyāsa sauvarṇām maṇi bhūṣitām kathayāmāsa tām devyai śilām paśya iti a prabhuḥ tam āha devī deveśam iha taptam mayā tapaḥ atha tām anujagrāha śilām prītyā bhavaḥ tadā śuciḥ asyām nirāhāram tri rātram yaḥ kariṣyati eka pādena yaḥ martyaḥ tiṣṭhet ekam ahar śuciḥ prāṇān parityajet yaḥ ca śilāyām iha dustyajān athā apṛcchat punar devaḥ pārvatīm vicaran prabhuḥ katham etāni kuṇḍāni babhūvuḥ iha śailaje evam pṛṣṭā punar devī vākyam etat jagāda ha ete tābhyām kṛte kuṇḍe sita toye mahā plave tapaḥ taptum alaṅkārān aham tyaktavatī yadā tayā ca idam apām kuṇḍam dvitīyam me kṛtam śubham śarīrāt me tadā deva kṛṣṇā kośī viniṣkramat tasyām kośyām samutpannam etat kuṇḍam tṛtīyakam idam kṛṣṇājinam śubhram sthāpitam tat purā mayā atha śrutvā mahādevaḥ pārvatyāḥ vacanam prabhuḥ pratyuvāca tadā devīm prītyā paramayā yutaḥ stana toyena yat pūrṇe tava kuṇḍe śaśiprabhe upavāsī nataḥ yaḥ snātvā abhyarcya ca devatāḥ alaṃkārāt srutā dhārā yā iyam tava varānane eṣā alaṃkāradhārā iti nāmnā khyātim gamiṣyati asyām snātvā naraḥ yaḥ tu pitR̥n saṃtarpayiṣyati nīla toyam idam yat te mahat kuṇḍam śubha udakam agni kāryam iha snātvā yaḥ kuryāt brāhmaṇaḥ śuciḥ agnihotram hutam tena bhavet svādaśa vārṣikam gṛhītvā pādapa sthāni valkalāni tadā prabhuḥ tāni abhūvan tadā vyāsa nadī svaccha jalā śubhā taṭa jaiḥ vividhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ haṃsa cakra āhva śobhitā tām uvāca sura śreṣṭhaḥ puṇya toyām mahā nadīm cīrebhyaḥ nissṛtā yasmāt tvam atra saritām varā loke puṇyatamā tasmāt niścīrā iti bhaviṣyasi kapilām ca atra yaḥ dadyāt brāhmaṇāya samāhitaḥ mahā phalam mahā puṇyam sarva siddhi pradam śubham iha upoṣya śuciḥ snātvā bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ kṛṣṇājinam mahā puṇyam sarva pāpa haram tava tat eva labhate devi dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇājinam dvijaḥ āvayoḥ gaṇapaḥ bhūtvā jagat sarvam cariṣyati evam naga indram sa tadā anugṛhya muni indra sārdham girirāja putryā kośī śilā stana kuṇḍa ajina gaurīśikhara vara pradānam nāma vyāsaḥ uvāca cāru sopāna saṃkīrṇe citra paṭṭa śilā tale sahasrākṣaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ ca vāyuḥ ca eva tadā gatāḥ samāgamya pura dvāram dṛṣṭvā te nandinam sthitam ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ bhūtvā śaṅkaram saṃdidṛkṣavaḥ atha nandī samāgatya dvāra mūle samāsthitaḥ śambhoḥ nivedayāmāsa trīn devān tu samāgatān viviśuḥ te trayaḥ devāḥ śaṅkarasya antikam tadā atha tān prāha lokeśaḥ śirobhiḥ praṇatān sthitān kā vaḥ kartavyatā devāḥ kimartham yūyam āgatāḥ brūta dāsyāmi tat sarvam yat yat mṛgayatha amarāḥ atha devaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ vacaḥ provāca śaṅkaram yat cakāra vapuḥ viṣṇuḥ nārasiṃham bhayānakam tam hatvā api sa daitya indram viṣṇuḥ para bala ardanaḥ tena rūpeṇa deveśa krūreṇa api hita īpsunā na vayam nirvṛtāḥ bhūtvā trāsāt tiṣṭhāma śaṅkara sa yathā siṃha rūpam tat parityajati mādhavaḥ atha provāca tam śakram devadevaḥ pinākadhṛk siṃha rūpam yathā śakra viṣṇuḥ tyakṣyati bhīṣaṇam kariṣyāmi tathā śakra vyetu te mānasaḥ jvaraḥ atha vāyuḥ tadā devam vyajñāpayata śaṃkaram aśarīraḥ yathā na syām tathā me kartum arhasi śarīram su mahat prādāt yena asau mūrtimān abhūt vijñāpitam śaśāṅkena tatas vyāsa mahātmanā dakṣeṇa aham purā śaptaḥ yakṣma dehaḥ bhaviṣyasi sa yathā yakṣma hīnaḥ syām prasādam me tathā kuru vijñaptim śaśinaḥ śrutvā devaḥ tasmai vacaḥ prabhuḥ idam prāha mahā tejāḥ śaśine praṇatāya tu tapaḥ kṛtvā prabhāse tvam yakṣma hīnaḥ bhaviṣyasi vāyu soma sahasra akṣāḥ svāni veśmāni bhejire vyāsaḥ uvāca kim vīryam kim tapaḥ ca asya śaṃsa etat pṛcchataḥ mama ditiḥ nāma abhavat patnī kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ hiraṇya kaśipum jyeṣṭham hiraṇya akṣam kanīyasam abhiṣiktaḥ sa daityānām rājā abhūt brahmaṇā purā atha teṣām tadā vyāsa trailokyam saṃpraśāsatām hiraṇyakaśipuḥ daityaḥ śakra rājya jihīrṣayā sa gatvā dakṣiṇām āśām śrīparvata samāsthitaḥ sva raktena juhāva agnau saṃmiśrāḥ samidhaḥ carūn ūrdhvabāhuḥ nirālambaḥ divā sūrya arpita īkṣaṇaḥ ekapādaḥ aanimeṣaḥ ca saḥ aatiṣṭhat kṛta niścayaḥ dve sahasre tadā abdānām divyānām sthitavān balī athā abhyetya sura śreṣṭhaḥ brahmā kamala vāhanaḥ iṣṭam vṛṇu varam rājan iti provāca sādaram tam dṛṣṭvā daitya rājaḥ tu brahmāṇam vara dam prabhum varam prārthitavān vyāsa śṛṇu yādṛśam īpsitam amaraḥ syām avadhyaḥ ca jarā hīnaḥ mahā balaḥ na śatreṇa na ca astreṇa na rātrau na divā tathā na eva ārdreṇa na śuṣkeṇa na puṃsā na ca yoṣitā jagāma ātma puram kṣipram śāntaḥ prītaḥ pitāmahaḥ saḥ sarva asura śreṣṭhaḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ tadā jitvā śakram svayam rājyam cakāra diti nandanaḥ trailokyam ātmasātkṛtvā jitvā sarvān divaukasaḥ ātmanā eva abhavat śakraḥ svayam vāyuḥ svayam yamaḥ praṇamadhvam yajadhvam mām brahmā aham sa purandaraḥ iti prāha ṛṣīn sarvān siddhān viprān ca saḥ a asuraḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca katham śrīparvataḥ a asau vai kim puṇyam tatra kim phalam tapaḥ siddhān mahā yogān jvalana āditya varcasaḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇām śambhoḥ sa praṇāmam mahā mune ke ete deva saṃsiddhāḥ yogi īśāḥ tvām praṇemire yoga siddhāḥ mahātmānaḥ yoge pāśupate sthitāḥ ye iha ārādhya mām devi jahuḥ prāṇān nara uttamāḥ mokṣa siddheḥ parām niṣṭhām gantāraḥ paramam padam devam provāca śarvāṇī vacaḥ parama pūjitam yathā aham api deveśa prāpnuyām siddhim īdṛśīm kariṣyāmi tathā yatnam eṣā ca asmi gatā vibho tatas kṛtvā śriyaḥ rūpam devī parama śobhanā devaḥ ca asyāḥ varam prādāt taiḥ samānam mahā dyutiḥ mahā yoga īśvarī siddhā para artha jñā bhaviṣyasi ayam ca parvataḥ śrīmān nāmnā tava bhaviṣyasi śrīparvataḥ iti khyātaḥ citra rūpa vibhūṣitaḥ samantāt yojana śatam mahā puṇyaḥ bhaviṣyasi śuciḥ snātvā arcayet martyaḥ sa lokam mama yāsyati yaḥ tu iha tyakṣyate prāṇān śrīgirau acala uttame trinetraḥ kāmagaḥ bhūtvā gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt iha āgatya ca ye śailam kariṣyanti pradakṣiṇam śarvāyatana saṃyuktam bhaviṣyanti ca te gaṇāḥ śrīgiri vara pradānam nāma agāt kālaḥ mahān vyāsa trailokyam sa carācaram darpeṇa mahatā āviṣṭaḥ śrī mada udvṛtta cetanaḥ sa devān sahitān sarvān śakra ādyān krodha mūrchitaḥ cālitān api rājye sve kṛcchram āpādayat bhṛśam santāpyamānāḥ te sarve brahmāṇam śaraṇam yayuḥ trailokyam kṛtsnam ākramya rājyam naḥ hṛtavān divaḥ aniśam ca avamānan naḥ prayuṅkte vaira yātanam tena vidrāvitāḥ sarve śaraṇam vayam āgatāḥ prasādam kuru deveśa sa na syāt naḥ yathā ripuḥ provāca idam mahā prajña devānām prita kṛt vacaḥ kṣīṇam tat daitya rājasya tapaḥ tasya durātmanaḥ kṛcchram gamitavān yaḥ vaḥ rājyam ca hṛtavān ripuḥ tena aham prārthitaḥ pūrvam sarva avadhya tvam uttamam antaram bhāṣitaḥ ca asau mayā saṃjñā vimohitaḥ tadā eva manasā toṣam aham āgām mahā balāḥ tam brūta sahitāḥ sarve tasya nāśa artham acyutam narasiṃha vapuḥ kṛtvā sakṛt āhatya haṃsyati hiraṇyakaśipum daityam tatas nivṛtim eṣyatha ājagmuḥ sahitāḥ devāḥ viṣṇoḥ bhavanam ādṛtāḥ atha dṛṣṭvā mahā tejāḥ viṣṇuḥ devān upasthitān uvāca ślakṣṇayā vācā vacaḥ ca ukti manoharam svāgatam bhavatām astu kimartham yūyam āgatāḥ pūjyāḥ bhavantaḥ sarve me suhṛdaḥ yat vaḥ manaḥ gatam kiṃcid mayā kāryam divaukasaḥ kṣipram tat brūta saṃkṣiptam kartāham avicāritam viṣṇunā evam tadā proktāḥ devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ ūcuḥ prahṛṣṭa vadanāḥ saṃstuvantaḥ janārdanam bhayam naḥ su mahat jātam rājyam ca apahṛtam divaḥ tathā kuru hṛṣīkeśa varaḥ aayam naḥ pradīyatām tatas viṣṇuḥ ciram dhyātvā vadha upāyam pracintya ca prāha devān suraśreṣṭhaḥ vacasā āpyāyayan iva evam astu suraśreṣṭhaḥ sarvam kartāsmi vaḥ vacaḥ āviśantu bhavantaḥ śarīram mama suvratāḥ sarva deva mayaḥ bhūtvā dṛptam haṃsyāmi vaḥ ripum tatas devāḥ tadā sarve viviśuḥ vaiṣṇavīm tanum sa ca api balavān bhūtvā rūpam kṛtvā bhayānakam nārasiṃham mahā tejāḥ nakha daṃṣṭrā vibhūṣaṇam jagāma vilasat viṣṇuḥ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ puram nṛsiṃhaḥ daitya siṃhasya dṛsṭvā tasthau su vismitaḥ vṛkṣaiḥ kāma phalaiḥ ca eva vaibhrāja sadṛśam vanam tat babhañja nṛsiṃhaḥ tu khela gāmī mahā utkaṭaḥ sarāṃsi kṣobhayāmāsa karī iva sa mada ulvaṇaḥ athā abhyetya nṛsiṃham tam vanapālāḥ ruṣā anvitāḥ balinaḥ vārayāmāsuḥ tān ca eva abhyahanat balī hata śeṣāḥ tatas tatra pravilīnāḥ tu ye a asurāḥ te gatvā kathayāmāsuḥ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ tadā teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā daitya rājaḥ mahā balaḥ prahlādam ca anuhlādam ca namucim bāṣkalim balim vipracitti pradhānān ca sarvān āhūya dānavān provāca tvaritam gatvā baddhvā siṃham mama antikam krīḍaṇam siṃha potaḥ devyāḥ mama bhaviṣyati iti śrutvā asurāḥ sarve vipracitti purogamāḥ udyānam sahitāḥ gatvā nṛsiṃham dadṛśuḥ sthitam dūra sthāḥ cikṣipuḥ pāśān tān sa ciccheda mādhavaḥ atha vidrāvayāmāsa dānavān keśarī bhṛśam pārśvam dānava rājasya sarvam ca akathayan tadā atha kruddhaḥ svayam rājā hiraṇyakaśipuḥ balī ratham āsthāya sannaddhā nṛsiṃham prādravat ruṣā sa rathaḥ siṃha rājena sa āyudhaḥ parvata upamaḥ sambhrāmya pātitaḥ tūrṇam cūrṇam āgāt mahī tale vṛkṣam utpāṭya vegena nṛsiṃhāya vyasarjayat atha asau patitaḥ gātre siṃha rājasya pādapaḥ mṛd khaṇḍaḥ iva pāṣāṇe kṣiptaḥ cūrṇam jagāma ha gṛhītvā sa tadā siṃhaḥ hiraṇyakaśipum sakṛt divaḥ rājyam punar śakraḥ lebhe niṣkaṇṭakam mahat athā gatya tatas devaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ viṣṇoḥ tyājayitum rūpam saiṃham adbhuta karmaṇaḥ śarabhaḥ sa tadā bhūtvā himavat śikhara upamaḥ caturbhiḥ pṛṣṭha jaiḥ pādaiḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭraḥ mahā balaḥ narasiṃha samīpam tu gatvā agarjat samāhitaḥ atha siṃhaḥ tadā dṛṣṭvā śarabham samupasthitam ātmanā eva agamat kṛcchram sparśāt tasya mahātmanaḥ tatas viṣṇuḥ ciram dhyātvā jñātvā śaṃkaram āgatam namaḥ śarvāya rudrāya senānye śarma dāya ca kālāya yama rūpāya kāla daṇḍāya vai namaḥ namaḥ kāla anta kartre ca kālekāla harāya ca namaḥ pinākahastāya raudra bāṇa dharāya ca caṇḍāya vāmadevāya sarva yoga īśvarāya ca nara nārāyaṇa īśāya nara nārāyaṇa ātmane śarabhāya su rūpāya vyāghra carma su vāsase nandi īśvara gaṇa īśāya gaṇānām pataye namaḥ indriyāṇām atha īśāya manasaspataye namaḥ namaḥ pradhāna pataye surāṇām pataye namaḥ carācarāṇām pataye bhūtānām pataye namaḥ bhagavan tvad pratiṣṭhaḥ tvad niṣṭhaḥ tvad parāyaṇaḥ śaraṇam tvām prapannaḥ a aham prasīda mama sarvadā yaḥ imam śṛṇuyāt nityam śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam svargyam pāpa praṇāśanam śrāvaṇam śravaṇam ca asya tathā anusmaraṇam sadā saḥ evam stūyamānaḥ tu viṣṇunā bhuvaneśvaraḥ hṛṣīkeśam uvāca idam vacaḥ parama pūjitam tubhyam viṣṇo mayā dattaḥ puṇyaḥ hi eṣa varaḥ śubhaḥ sa tvam viṣṇuḥ mahā tejāḥ mattaḥ labdha varaḥ sadā velāyām tvām samudraḥ tu tiryagyonim asūta yaḥ kṛtam kāryam tvayā sarvam hiraṇyakaśipuḥ hataḥ ehi gaccha śubhām yonim ātmanaḥ parama adbhutām tatas tam ākramat pādaiḥ siṃham śarabha sattamaḥ viṣṇave a atha varam dattvā daitya ghnam sa vṛṣadhvajaḥ iti skandapurāṇe hiraṇyakaśipu upakhyāne śarabha kṛta narasiṃha uddhāra ākhyānam nāma vyāsaḥ uvāca apanīya tadā viṣṇoḥ siṃha rūpam vṛṣadhvajaḥ sva yonim viṣṇum ānīya devadevaḥ bhavaḥ tadā ramyān sa kānana uddeśān gireḥ prasravaṇāni ca vana prekṣā ratam devam jñātvā śaṃkaram avyayam tatas mahīruhāḥ sarve sarāṃsi ca samantataḥ nānāvidhāni puṣpāṇi mumucuḥ sahasā samam kamala utpala saṃchannāḥ ṣaṭpada vrāta sevitāḥ haṃsa sārasa saṃvāsāḥ vāpyaḥ tatra manoharāḥ gandha āḍhyāḥ jātayaḥ kṣipram babhūvuḥ saha campakaiḥ aśokāḥ gandhapuṣpāḥ ca tathā ca eva atimuktakāḥ sarva ṛtu kusuma ākīrṇam dṛṣṭvā tat vanam uttamam puṣpāṇi ādāya deveśaḥ svayam eva jagatpatiḥ alaṃcakāra hṛṣṭa ātmā devīm himagireḥ sutām nandīśvaram ca pārśva stham ātmānam ca sureśvaraḥ tatas praṇamya deveśam pārvatī praṇayāt idam provāca idam mahā tejāḥ devyāḥ priya cikīrṣayā evam bhavatu deveśe vijñaptim saphalām imām śreṣṭhaḥ sarva sura īśānām mahā yoga bala anvitaḥ prārthitaḥ hi eṣa putra artham tena avaśyam dadāmi te nandīśena tadā sārdham vicarantau jagadgurū darī kandara saṃkīrṇam nānā nirjhara saṃyutam sa taḍit megha saṃghāta ghanīkṛta śilā uccayam nānā vṛkṣa śilā upetam nānā kusuma saṃyutam mānasam tasya madhye tu puram sṛṣṭvā mahā ṛddhimat nandinam ca tatas devī samājñāpayat avyayā vatsa nandin tathā dvāre tiṣṭheḥ tvam gaṇapa īśvara viśet na iha yathā kaścid sūkṣmaḥ vāyuḥ api sthitaḥ kṛtvā śirasi tām ājñām nandīśaḥ gaṇapa adhipaḥ tasthatuḥ su ciram kālam tanaya artham mahā dyutī sa na śakyaḥ mayā vaktum brahmaṇā vā mahā mune brahmaṇaḥ madvidhānām ca śreṣṭhaḥ a asau parameśvaraḥ avaśyam tu āgame vācyam yathāvṛttam yathāśrutam atas vakṣyāmi te vyāsa priyaḥ śiṣyaḥ ca me bhavān atītam sthitayoḥ divyam sahasram śaradām abhūt cacāla pṛthivī kṛtsnā sa śaila vana kānanā nadyaḥ śoṣam tadā jagmuḥ cukṣubhe saritām patiḥ tapanaḥ niṣprabhaḥ ca āsīt vavāv uṣṇaḥ samīraṇaḥ petuḥ ulkāḥ mahā ghorāḥ diśaḥ ca āsan su dāruṇāḥ jagāma śaraṇam viṣṇum gatvā ca ārtim nyavedayat utpātāḥ dāruṇāḥ deva babhūvuḥ bahavaḥ bhṛśam tena atīva samudvignā tvām adya śaraṇam gatā atha viṣṇuḥ surān sarvān idam aśrāvayat prabhuḥ ekatra saṃgatāḥ bhūtvā cakruḥ bahuvidhāḥ kathāḥ mahā buddhiḥ atha āha idam vākyam aṅgirasaḥ sutaḥ śrīkaṇṭhaḥ bhagavān eṣa devadevaḥ trilocanaḥ divyam varṣa sahasram tu yogena parameṣṭhinaḥ aga ādi uktasya pārvatyāḥ babhūvuḥ dāruṇāḥ tatas utpātāḥ jagataḥ trāsāḥ cintyate kim iha aparam gacchāma sahitāḥ sarve stotum bhaktyā vṛṣadhvajam yathā ca deha jaḥ putraḥ bhavet devyāḥ sura īśvarāḥ vijñāpayāmāsa deveśam tathā śīghram iha amarāḥ utpatsyati na ca drogdhā tatas kṣaṃsyāma tam surāḥ tatas enam aham baddhvā kāla pāśena bālakam āneṣye sva vaśam krūram mṛtyunā sahitaḥ dvidhā yena kṛtaḥ mūḍhaḥ prāṇān tyakṣyati dustyajān viṣṇuḥ provāca dharma ātmā vacāṃsi parama artha vid tanayaḥ kila yaḥ śambhoḥ girijāyām bhaviṣyati sa mūḍhaḥ iva yaḥ kaścid bhavitā vaśagaḥ tava kālena aparipūrṇena mānavasya api bhānuja na tvam nāśayitā nāma kimu putrasya śūlinaḥ sa katham vadhya tām yāyāt tava śakrasya vā vibho prayāma sahitāḥ sarve tam prasādayitum haram yaḥ naḥ svayaṃvare dattaḥ varaḥ tiṣṭhati śaṃkare na asmākam ahitam śambhuḥ putram utpādayiṣyati vayam eva sutāḥ sarve śaṃkarasya agrajāḥ vibhoḥ na śakyaḥ tapasā draṣṭum na jñānena sura īśvarāḥ bhaktyā paramayā draṣṭum śakyaḥ syāt sa vṛṣadhvajaḥ āgacchadhvam gamiṣyāmaḥ yatra tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ parām bhaktim samāsthāya yathā paśyeya śaṃkaram sarveṣām eva vijñaptyā surāṇām sura sattamāḥ bṛhaspati purogāḥ te hṛṣṭa ātmānaḥ divaukasaḥ sādhu sādhu iti santuṣṭāḥ vacāṃsi ūcuḥ sura uttamāḥ tatas viṣṇu sahāyāḥ te gatvā tad śṛṅgam uttamam ūcuḥ hutāśanam devam vacaḥ stuti puraḥsaram praviśya trāhi naḥ sarvān śaṃkarāya nivedaya tathā kuryāḥ suraśreṣṭha yena nirgamya śaṃkaraḥ asmān nirīkṣate devaḥ prahvān bhaktimataḥ sthitān iti uktaḥ sa suraiḥ sarvaiḥ pratyuvāca hutāśanaḥ pārvatyā saha saṃyuktam devadeveśvaram param na me śaktiḥ haram draṣṭum bhavantaḥ ca ākulāḥ bhṛśam pravekṣye dūta vat devāḥ kariṣye sāhasam mahat iti uktvā sa jagāma āśu bhavanam tat kapardinaḥ dvāram ākramya tiṣṭhantam dīpta paṭṭiśa dhāriṇam tam dṛṣṭvā sa tadā vahniḥ samālokya samantataḥ na asti kaścid iha upāyaḥ sūkṣma jantoḥ api sthite praveṣṭum iti saṃcintya tam eva śaraṇam yayau nandinam hutabhuj devaḥ tuṣṭāva ca kṛtāñjaliḥ namaḥ gaṇādhipataye namaḥ caṇḍāya śūline namaḥ senā adhipataye namaḥ śarva ātmane sadā hālāhalāya rudrāya nīla rudrāya vai namaḥ namaḥ śmaśānarudrāya koṭīrudrāya te namaḥ virūpākṣāya rudrāya śvetarudrāya te namaḥ vara daḥ bhava nandīśa mā naḥ krodham kṛthāḥ prabho brūhi kim te priyam deva karavāṇi hutāśana deva kāryeṇa deveśa praveṣṭum dīyatām mama na tam śakṣyasi deveśam draṣṭum tvam yogam āsthitam saha devyāḥ maheśānam sraṣṭāram jagataḥ aavyayam gaccha sūkṣmataraḥ bhūtvā durālakṣyaḥ hutāśana praviśya niṣkrama kṣipram avijñāta āgama kriyaḥ sa nandinā abhyanujñātaḥ jātavedāḥ mudā yutaḥ jyotiḥ sūkṣmataraḥ bhūtvā bhāskarasya aṃśunā saha vāhneya maṇi madhya stham stambham tam bhāsayan muhur saḥ aapaśyat tatra deveśam devīm ca bhuvaneśvarīm tuṣṭāva manasā devau tatas havyavāhanaḥ tathā saṃstūyamānaḥ ca prītim devyāḥ ca darśayan vīkṣya stambham haraḥ devīm vākyam etat abhāṣata saṃstauti mām tvayā sārdham dadāni asmai varam śubham brūhi kāryam yathā iṣṭam tvam tat sarvam te baviṣyati devāḥ tvām draṣṭum icchanti bahiṣthāḥ bhuvana īśvara dadāmi darśanam vahne bhavataḥ priya kāmyayā atha dṛṣṭvā mahādevam devāḥ sarve vṛṣadhvajam praṇemuḥ mūrdhabhiḥ hṛṣṭāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca mudā yutāḥ mahatām pataye nityam devānām pataye namaḥ namaḥ śmaśāna rataye vyāghra carma su vāsase namaḥ nīlaśikhaṇḍāya sa patnīkāya vai namaḥ namaḥ kāmeṣu asaktāya kāma saktāya vai namaḥ namaḥ sarvāya śarvāya daṇḍine jaṭine namaḥ pratyuvāca mahādevaḥ tān surān praṇatān sthitān parituṣṭaḥ aasmi bho devāḥ brūta kim pradadāni vaḥ aśubhāni nimittāni dṛśyante su mahā dyute pṛthivī duḥsthitā deva vayam ca bhṛśam ākulāḥ tena eṣa na yathā devyāḥ dehe saṃjāyate sutaḥ teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā devadevaḥ aabravīt vacaḥ mahān eṣa varaḥ sarvaiḥ prārthitaḥ sura puṅgavaiḥ tathā api ca prayacchāmi yuṣmad priya cikīrṣayā mahāntam kim tu idam kālam tejaḥ sandhāritam mayā babhūvuḥ sahitāḥ tūṣṇīm surāḥ brahma purogamāḥ teṣām madhye tadā vahniḥ provāca bhuvaneśvaram juhāva agnau tatas tejaḥ tadā svīyam param bhavaḥ hutvā tasmin tatas kṛtsnam tuṣṭaḥ aabhūt parameśvaraḥ varam vṛṇu hutāśa tvam iti provāca śaṃkaraḥ śāpasya aham agamyaḥ syām paśyeyam tvām ca nityaśas dhārayeyam sukhena etat utsṛjeyam ca śaṃkara mayi devāḥ ca yajñāḥ ca pratiṣṭhām yāntu śūla dhṛk aham bhūteśvaraḥ ca syām aham paśupatiḥ ca ha aham tava tanuḥ syām ca tvad mūrtiḥ tvad upāśrayaḥ varam icchāmi deveśa dīyamānam imam tvayā kva gatvā tvam iha āyātaḥ kṣipram tribhuvana īśvara tatas provāca deveśaḥ pārvatīm ruṣita ānanām katham tvam āgatān deva bahiḥsthān tridivaukasaḥ jñātavān asi santrastān kena ākhyātam ca te vibho tatas bhagavatī kruddhā nandinam prāha pārvatī tatas sā asya bhṛśam kruddhā śravaṇa nyastam utpalam gṛhītvā vajra saṃkāśam nandīśāya vyasarjayat dvādaśa āditya saṃkāśam prajvalat tat tadā utpalam hataḥ nandīśvaraḥ iti procya utthāya ca śaṃkaraḥ aho bata mahat kaṣṭam kṛtam krodha vaśāt mayā kathaṃcid na hataḥ nandī mahā gaṇapa nāyakaḥ tat gṛhītvā tatas hastāt devasya śravaṇa utpalam haṃsa sārasa saṃkīrṇam cakravāka upaśobhitam nāmnā bhadrotpalam iti hemaśṛṅga samīpataḥ tatra snātvā naraḥ kṣipram sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate tatra akṣayam sadā dānam pitṛ tarpaṇam eva ca mṛtaḥ ca atra naraḥ yāti nandīśvara salokatām tatas devam punar devī vākyam āha gireḥ sutā kim ūcuḥ tvām surāḥ deva kīdṛśam ca arthayan varam kathayāmāsa deveśaḥ tatas devyai vṛṣadhvajaḥ aśubhāni atra dṛśyante dāruṇāni sahasraśas santrastā pṛthivī kṛtsnā vayam ca bhṛśam ākulāḥ tena eṣa na yathā devyāḥ garbhe saṃjāyate sutaḥ bhavet ca tanayaḥ ślāghyaḥ varaḥ eṣa pradīyatām sutaḥ te bhavitā śrīmān ṣaṣ śirāḥ dvādaśa īkṣaṇaḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā śaśāpa girijā amarān svāsu tasmāt te na prāpsyanti surāḥ sutam pṛthivī ca api saṃmūḍhā mad śāpa upahata indriyā virarāma tatas devī śaptvā devān sa vāsavān kaiṭabhā nāma nāmnā ca puṇyā nā eka vara pradā puṇyam āyatanam tat hi śilām ca ramaṇāhvayām athā ājagmuḥ surāḥ sarve sārdham tatra havirbhujā vivarṇāḥ kaśmala upetāḥ sa garbhāḥ lajjayā anvitāḥ tān dvāḥsthān āgatān nandī śaṃkarāya nyavedayat praviśya samanujñātāḥ devam ūcuḥ divaukasaḥ trāhi naḥ sura loka īśa yathā syāma gata jvarāḥ yuṣmad arthe parākrāntam hirāṇyākṣa sutam varam nāmnā śaravaṇam nāma puṇyam dvādaśa yojanam yuṣmākam tatra sambhidya kukṣīn daivata puṅgavāḥ suvarṇa tvam ca yāsyanti kukṣayaḥ vaḥ sura uttamāḥ śrīmantam merum ājagmuḥ śara dhānam ca tat śubham yatra teṣām tadā bhittvā kukṣīn teṣām nirakramīt yugānta anala saṃkāśam durnirīkṣyam sura asuraiḥ meruḥ ca eva bhavat kṣipram śrīmān ati manoharaḥ sarvam hiraṇmayam cakre tejaḥ māheśvaram param teṣām ca kukṣi bhedāḥ te suvarṇa tvam param yayuḥ puṣpāṇām vṛṣṭayaḥ petuḥ sugandhīnām anekaśas namaskāraiḥ ca bhūtānām adṛśyānām abhūt svanaḥ evamādīni paśyantaḥ śṛṇvantaḥ ca sura uttamāḥ gatvā pinākine hṛṣṭāḥ sarvam āvedya suvrata preṣitāḥ sthāṇunā jagmuḥ svān lokān hṛṣita ānanāḥ jñātvā tasthau vibudha vara dā yogamātā vidhātrī tuṣṭim ca agāt hṛdi sura śiraḥ spṛṣṭa pāda aravindā vyāsaḥ uvāca andhakaḥ kasya putraḥ a asau kiṃvīryaḥ kiṃparākramaḥ śṛṇu vyāsa mahābuddhe sarvam etat yathā bhavat hiraṇyakaśipuḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ tatas aanujaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ tatra abhavat rājā hiraṇyakaśipuḥ tadā hiraṇyākṣaḥ abhavat rājā sarva daitya namaskṛtaḥ sa śaṃkukarṇam samprāpya sindhu sāgara saṃgame tapaḥ tepe diteḥ putraḥ devam draṣṭum pinākinam vyāsaḥ uvāca śaṃkukarṇam maheśasya kṣetram sarva artha sādhakam purā hi bhagavān devaḥ kapardī nīlalohitaḥ daśasu api tatas dikṣu rakṣaṇa artham jagatpatiḥ sthāpayāmāsa gaṇapān nikumbha ādīn sahasraśas śaṃku karṇam mahā daṃṣṭram sthūla akṣam sthūla nāsikam hrasva pāda karam ca eva dārita āsyam vibhīṣaṇam śaṃkukarṇam iti khyātam gaṇeśam su mahā balam samāhūya samīpam tu bhagavān idam abravīt svaiḥ tvam gaṇeśvaraiḥ sārdham na viśeyuḥ yathā surāḥ evam sa kṛtvā rakṣām tu mahādevaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ atha ājagmuḥ surāḥ tatra sarve śakra purogamāḥ niruddhāḥ śaṃku karṇena na celuḥ padam agratas devāḥ ūcuḥ bho gaṇeśāḥ vayam devam śarvam ugram kapardinam draṣṭum kāryeṇa samprāptāḥ tat naḥ darśayata anaghāḥ ākulāḥ tam a paśyantaḥ naśyāma pramatha īśvarāḥ śaṃkukarṇaḥ uvāca na yuṣmābhiḥ surāḥ śakyaḥ devaḥ draṣṭum kathaṃcana devāḥ ūcuḥ mā lokānām vināśaḥ syāt gaṇeśvara mahā dyute śaṃkukarṇaḥ uvāca lokāḥ naśyantu yūyam vā na praveśaḥ pradīyate vinaṣṭān punar eva īśaḥ srakṣyate bhuvaneśvaraḥ sraṣṭā saḥ eva bhūtānām sa vināśayitā tathā tam vinā kaḥ surāḥ śaktaḥ lokān nāśayitum vibhum yacchāma na vayam dvāram ājñā naḥ pārameśvarī atha brahmā surān āha mayā saha punar surāḥ gacchadhvam gaṇapān yāvat pratyāpattim nayāmi vaḥ tatas te brahmaṇā sārdham viṣṇunā ca divaukasaḥ tam eva punar ājagmuḥ tiṣṭhate yatra śaṃkaraḥ śaṃku karṇaḥ gaṇādhyakṣaḥ tejasā prajvalan iva gaṇeśvara na devānām dauṣṭyam kiṃcid hi vidyate tava prasādāt paśyantu devāḥ devam vṛṣadhvajam śirasā praṇatāḥ tubhyam devāḥ ca indra purogamāḥ aham ca viṣṇunā sārdham prayācema gaṇeśvara tasya tat vacanam śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ sa gaṇeśvaraḥ kruddhaḥ paṭṭiśam udyamya vacaḥ provāca niṣṭhuram na me gurutaraḥ devāḥ praṇāmaḥ bhavatām nu ayam ājñā garīyasī śambhoḥ na praveśaḥ kaścana pratiṣiddhān katham brahman niyuktāḥ rakṣaṇāya ca īśa ājñām samatikramya prayacchāma praveśanam tasya tat vacanam śrutvā gaṇeśasya mahātmanaḥ ekāntam prayayau brahmā lajjayā parayā anvitaḥ devāḥ sarve tatas dṛṣṭvā vrīḍā yuktam pitāmaham kruddhāḥ manyu parīta aṅgāḥ vākyam ūcuḥ gaṇeśvaram na evam tvām vibruvantam hi kṣaṃsyate vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ avamānam punar mā evam tvam asmākam kṛthāḥ gaṇa mā adya te vayam udyuktāḥ nāśayiṣyāma jīvitam teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā śaṃkukarṇaḥ ruṣā anvitaḥ guravaḥ kim bhavantaḥ me yena śaṃke aamara adhipāḥ prasādya śaṃkaram yūyam gatāḥ deva tvam uttamam gaṇa bhūtāḥ sureśasya yūyam api amara uttamāḥ vayam api atiyogi īśāḥ gaṇapāḥ tasya śūlinaḥ samānāḥ yūyam asmākam hīnāḥ vā tridivaukasaḥ yasmāt vayam sureśānam paśyāmaḥ ca sarvaiḥ eva suraiḥ tasmāt vayam pūjyāḥ sadā adhikāḥ paśyāmaḥ nirbhayāḥ yūyam praveśam kuruta amarāḥ yāvat adya gaṇeśānām balam drakṣyatha dāruṇam yat vā balam ca yogaḥ ca yat tapaḥ yaḥ ca vaḥ śramaḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā sarve devāḥ su garvitāḥ pragṛhīta āyudhāḥ kṣipram śaṃkukarṇam vidudruvuḥ teṣām āpatatām vyāsa surāṇām śūra māninām balam jagrāha yogena śaṃkukarṇaḥ mahā balaḥ na aśaknuvan padam dātum tasthuḥ stambhāḥ iva acalāḥ nigṛhīteṣu deveṣu viṣṇuḥ praharatām varaḥ abhidudrāva vegena śaṃkukarṇam gaṇeśvaram sa yogam punar āsthāya viṣṇuḥ aiśvarya saṃyutaḥ vinigṛhya sa tam viṣṇum gaṇeśaḥ śarva vallabhaḥ sa sūkṣmam yogam āsthāya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ sa bhūtāni samutsṛjya tanmātrāṇi āviśat prabhuḥ indriyāṇi atha tattvāni bhāvān ca eva pitāmahaḥ apaśyat sthūla śirasam śaṃku karṇam mahā balam samāptam ca abhavat vyāsa vratam tasya mahātmanaḥ avaikṣata diśaḥ sarvāḥ jīvayan iva śaṃkaraḥ saḥ aapaśyat nigṛhītān tān sarvān eva divaukasaḥ sāmnā eva sa tadā devaḥ śaṃkukarṇam nyavārayat samyak ājñā kṛtā vatsa tvayā me gaṇapa īśvara muñca devān imān sarvān mā avamaṃsthāḥ gaṇeśvara evam devena samproktaḥ śaṃkukarṇaḥ gaṇādhipaḥ surāḥ api tadā sarve vrīḍayā parayā yutāḥ tān tadā vrīḍitān devaḥ prahasya vidita ātmavān uvāca brahmaṇā sārdham viṣṇum ābhāṣya su svaram gaṇeśvaraḥ deva īśāḥ mad śāsana paraḥ sadā yat anena kṛtam kiṃcid vyetu tat vaḥ sura uttamāḥ kartavyam yat ca tat brūta yad artham yūyam āgatāḥ śaṃkukarṇaḥ hi ayam śrīmān gaṇeśaḥ yena naḥ balam asmabhyam paratas dadyāḥ sadā darśanam ātmanaḥ śaṃkukarṇam iti khyātam tathā sthūleśvaram śubham yaḥ a atra āgatya carum kṛtvā mām yatnena arcayiṣyati sa yogam paramam prāpya śaṃku karṇa samaḥ bhavet yaḥ ca prāṇān iha kṣetre tyajet niyamam āsthitaḥ pitR̥ṇām akṣayam śrāddham iha dattam bhaviṣyati yūyam ca aiśvarya sampannāḥ tapaḥ yoga bala anvitāḥ nityam drakṣyatha mām devāḥ prayāta vigata jvarāḥ prakāmam darśanam nityam tatra eva antaradhīyata tatra liṅgam pratiṣṭhāpya cakre tīrthāni anekaśas daśāśvamedhikam tīrtham puṇyam pañcāśvamedhikam surāṇām ca eva tīrthāni kṛtvā sva bhavanam yayau siddha cāraṇa saṃkīrṇam apsaraḥ gaṇa sevitam tasmin gatvā vane vyāsa hiraṇākṣaḥ pratāpavān atha devaḥ tadā gatvā sa gaṇaḥ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ramyam himagireḥ śṛṅgam mainākam iti viśrutam tasya āgatya tadā devīm saṃsthitā pṛṣṭhatas śanais karābhyām padma tulyābhyām netre śambhoḥ nyamīlayat jānīte nā iti saṃcintya krīḍā artham himavat sutā apradṛśyam hi tamasā tathābhūtam purā yathā atha devaḥ tadā dṛṣṭvā tṛtīyam netram avyayam lalāṭe asṛjat ūrdhva stham yuga anta agni sama prabham pārvatī pitaram dṛṣṭvā tathā dagdham pinākinā apanīya karau tasthau viṣaṇnā pati pārśvataḥ atha devaḥ tadā dṛṣṭvā viṣaṇṇa vadanām umām sa tathā dṛṣṭa mātraḥ tu punar paurāṇikaḥ abhavat prakṛti stham punar dṛṣṭvā devī pitaram avyayam praṇamya uvāca bhartāram hṛṣita āsyā girīndrajā śailaḥ eṣa tvayā deva kimartham bhasmasātkṛtaḥ tasyāḥ tat vacanam śrutvā provāca parameśvaraḥ andhāḥ samabhavat lokāḥ tadā sarve tamaḥ vṛtāḥ prakāśa artham tatas devi netram etat mayā kṛtam tvām ca dīnām pitṛ vadhāt upalakṣya tatas śubhe praiya artham tava suśroṇi prakṛti sthaḥ punar kṛtaḥ asmin ca tamasā graste loke tīvreṇa sarvatas tapyamānāya dāsyāmi hiraṇyākṣāya tam sutam evam uktvā sa bhagavān pragṛhya andham gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ sindhu sāgaram āgamya hiraṇyākṣam uvāca ha paśya mām tvam diteḥ putra cakṣuḥ divyam dadāmi te sa protthāya hiraṇyākṣaḥ praṇamya śirasā bhavam tam uvāca suraśreṣṭhaḥ śirasā pādayoḥ natam ayam te a asura śārdūla putraḥ putra śata agrajaḥ bhavitā ye mahān eṣa tapaḥ vīrya bala anvitaḥ jagāma śikharam ramyam mainākam punar eva tu ādāya andham punar saḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahā asuraḥ svam aśmakapuram yātvā bhāryām āha manasvinīm saṃvarddhaya enam yogena mā pramādam kṛthāḥ kvacid tasyāḥ snehena tam dṛṣṭvā stanābhyām prasnutam payaḥ dhanyāḥ te puruṣāḥ loke ye svayam yānti aviklavāḥ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā mukhān bandhūn ābhāṣya hi yathāsukham kāryam bhavet ca loṣṭena tṛṇena atha śavena vā na mayā anugṛhītena dhik mām aśubha kāriṇam suta snehāt ayam daityaḥ sadā mām rakṣate pitā hantavyam na vihanti eṣa koṣa kṣaya karam hi mām na ayam snehena saṃmūḍhaḥ jānāti imām mama vyathām āmantrya sahitam mātrā pitaram tam praṇamya ca jagāma tapase dhīmān saṃkalpya kṛta niścayaḥ pitrā śoka paripluta īkṣaṇa mukhena āyāsa khinna ātmanā tad tīvra ādhṛti kheda dṛṣṭi viraha prakṣveḍitaḥ śvasan tapaḥprayāṇam nāma gaṅgādvāram śubha dvāram tapovanam anuttamam divyam kanakhalam nāma yatra hairaṇvatī nadī vṛkṣāḥ kanakhalāḥ yatra sarve eva hi kāñcanāḥ sarvān tān śaraṇam yāmi tapaḥ siddhim diśantu me varān yena āpnuyām iṣṭān mṛtyum vā prāṇa nāśanam saḥ evam uktvā tu tatas pārāśarya mahā balaḥ tathā triṣavaṇa snāyī juhvānaḥ a agnīn tathā eva ca varṣe varṣe tu sampūrṇe sva aṅgāt utkṛṣya kārṣikam piśitasya tadā bhāgam juhāva agnau mahā asuraḥ juhvataḥ svāni māṃsāni varṣāṇām pratyaham tadā saḥ a asuraḥ śaṃkha hāra ambu sudhā kunda indu pāṇḍaraḥ babhūva asthi sirā śeṣaḥ kevalam tapasi sthitaḥ sa tena tapasā yuktaḥ bhāskaram niṣprabham tadā somam ca graha tārābhiḥ saha cakre a amita ātmavān aśoṣayat palvalāni nadī kūpa sarāṃsi ca tasya tat tapasaḥ rūpam dṛṣṭvā vighna śatāni uta tuṣṭaḥ aasmi te mahā bāho cakṣuṣmān bhava suvrata śarīram prakṛtim yātu yathāpūrvam ca te a asura brūhi ca anyam varam bhūyas yaḥ te manasi saṃsthitaḥ sa cakṣuṣmān tadā bhūtvā śarīreṇa akṣatena ca uvāca praṇataḥ sākṣāt brahmāṇam loka bhāvanam mahā bala tvam māyāḥ ca tathā ca amara tām api hiraṇyākṣa sutam prāha punar eva vacaḥ śubham yā strī syāt loka mātā vai praṇameyam na tām yadi jagāma svam tadā āvāsam virarāma andhakaḥ ca saḥ sa gaṅgā ambhobhiḥ āplutya devam iṣṭvā yathāvidhi sa hṛṣṭa cetāḥ tapasā mahā balaḥ vivṛddha kāmaḥ sura śatru toṣaṇaḥ pituḥ sakāśam punar eva dīptimān agacchat hūta balāhaka upamaḥ saḥ a aṣṭābhiḥ dānavaiḥ sārdham gatvā tat puram antike nivedayāmāsa pituḥ kṛtārthaḥ a andhakaḥ āgataḥ priya ākhyātuḥ tatas vyāsa hiraṇyākṣaḥ a asura īśvaraḥ dadau ratnāni anekāni tathā kāmān abhīpsitān svayam rājā tadā sarvaiḥ suhṛdbhiḥ saha vāhanaiḥ saha strībhiḥ yayau tūrṇam somaḥ tārā gaṇaiḥ iva āsasāda sutam śrīmān somaḥ budham iva aparam kṛtārtham sa sutam dṛṣṭvā tuṣṭaḥ aabhūt dānava īśvaraḥ snehāt sa tam pariṣvajya mūrdhni upāghrāya ca asakṛt pṛṣṭhaḥ sa kathayāmāsa yathāvṛttam aśeṣatas śrutvā te a asura śārdūlāḥ praṇeduḥ sāgarāḥ iva sa putra sahitaḥ bhāti daityaḥ sampūrṇa mānasaḥ caran rāśim iva ādityaḥ yathā saha śanaiscaraḥ adhvaryuḥ iva sānnāyye yathā anyān ṛtvijaḥ sthitān hiraṇyākṣaḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam yat idānīm me kṛtyam hṛdi cira sthitam mayā manīṣitam pūrvam kṛtakṛtyaḥ iha āgate kariṣyāmi iti tat sarvam kriyatām aviśaṅkayā ghuṣyatām nagara hi asmin catvareṣu sabhāsu ca kaumudī divasān aṣṭau sapta ca eva mama ājñayā suhṛdaḥ ye ca daitya indrāḥ dānavāḥ ca mahā balāḥ asmad pakṣe ca ye viprāḥ śukra prabhṛtayaḥ śubhāḥ nāgāḥ rakṣāṃsi yakṣāḥ ca gandharvāḥ manujāḥ tathā te evam uktāḥ daitya indrāḥ hiraṇyākṣeṇa dhīmatā dūtān sampraiṣayan kṣipram daityānām dānavaiḥ saha tathā anyeṣām ca pakṣāṇām ātmanaḥ śakti nandana nimantrayati vaḥ rājā hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahā balaḥ suhṛd vargaiḥ tu sahitāḥ gacchadhvam tam didṛkṣavaḥ ghaṇṭikaḥ ca ahataiḥ vastraiḥ veṣṭitaḥ su vibhūṣitaḥ ārūḍhaḥ pāṇḍaram mattam gajam samavaghoṣayat rājā jayati daitya indraḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān hatāḥ daitya dviṣaḥ sarve danavānām ca śatravaḥ jayāya diti putrāṇām ādityānām bhayāya ca prātar prabhṛti rājā vaḥ ājñāpayati kaumudīm su saṃmṛṣṭa upaliptābhiḥ rathyābhiḥ kriyatām puram sragviṇaḥ sa śiraḥsnātāḥ datta bhuktāḥ yathākramam gāyantu gāyanāḥ ca eva nṛtyantu naṭa nartakāḥ ucchriyantām patākāḥ ca gṛha vīthi āpaṇeṣu ca puṣpa prakara juṣṭāni dhūpaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ api sragdāmavanti sarvāṇi vanamālā ākulāni ca brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva bhojyantām kriyantām vācāni ca brahmaghoṣāḥ ca sarvatra puṇya aha udīraṇāni ca dīpa rātrau ca sarvatra rājamārge gṛheṣu ca taruṇāḥ saha yoṣidbhiḥ samantāt paryaṭantu ca ramamāṇāḥ hasantaḥ ca gāyantaḥ nṛtta sevinaḥ bhāṇḍa vādyāni vādyantām nṛtyantām daitya yoṣitaḥ mahādevasya pūjām ca gandha puṣpa ādikīm śubhām upahārān ca vividhān snapanāni mahānti ca valayaḥ puṣkalāḥ ca eva bhakṣya bhojyaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ dīpān ca vividha ākārān pānāni ca rasān tathā phalāni ca vicitrāṇi māṃsa pakvam anūpakam suvarṇa maṇi ctrāṇi īśvarāya prayacchata vaddhyantām paśavaḥ ca atra bhojyantām dvijasattamāḥ yaḥ na kuryāt idam sarvam pura vāsī janaḥ kvacid pātayet tasya śārīram rājā daṇḍam mahā yaśāḥ evam sa ghoṣayitvā tu ghāṇṭikaḥ hasti pṛṣṭhatas jagāma sva gṛham bhūyas kaumudī ca abhyavartata rājā api saṃyataḥ snātaḥ śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ kṣīreṇa sarpiṣā dadhnā rasaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ śubhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ ca bījaiḥ ca ratnaiḥ ca adbhiḥ samanvitaiḥ ekaikasya svayam rājā ghaṭānām daśabhiḥ śataiḥ pūjayitvā tatas rājā viprān anyān abhojayat bali śayyā āsana ādyaiḥ ca stūyamānaḥ gṛhān yayau cakruḥ sarve muni śreṣṭha yathā rājā tathā eva te andhakam sa gṛhītvā tu hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān eṣa devaḥ sadā putra tava astu sumukhaḥ prabhuḥ asmin bhaktiḥ tvayā kāryā bhāvitā parameśvare eṣa vandyaḥ ca pūjyaḥ ca atas na asti paraḥ guruḥ saḥ evam uktvā praṇipatya śaṃkaram mahā asuraḥ saḥ a asura dānava īśvaraḥ ṣaṭsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha tasyām saha strībhiḥ kaumudyām daitya dānavāḥ tatra kācid śubha apāṅgī padmam divyam mukha upari mukha aravinda trāṇa artham dadau soma bhayāt iva aparā caraṇena etya priyam matā abhyatāḍayat śītāṃśuḥ iva pādena vikacam śarad ambujam aparāḥ rājamārgāṇām anabhijñāḥ kulastriyaḥ sphāṭika upacitām bhūmim dṛṣṭvā muñcanti pādukām utkṛṣya vasanam ca anyā vipra indra jala śaṅkayā rājamārgeṣu gacchanti dṛṣṭvā maṇi citām bhuvam gṛhāt candra aṃśubhiḥ spṛṣṭā papāta madana alasā patitā eva ca sā somam uvāca idam kula aṅganā bhūyas mām tvam karaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ dahase nalinīm iva sūryeṇa kila dagdhāni jīvayasi auṣadhāni ha madanena katham dagdhām na jīvayasi mām dṛḍham jala candre iva ābhānti vīci cañcala mūrtayaḥ kecid gāyanti sahitāḥ strībhiḥ daityāḥ mahā balāḥ rājamārgaḥ kvacid bhāti strībhiḥ bahvībhiḥ āvṛtaḥ kvacid nūpura kāñcīnām kokilānām ca nisvanaḥ babhau śrotra sukhaḥ śrotuḥ kalā madana dīpanaḥ kvacid ramaṇa raktānām strīṇām vyāsa priyaiḥ saha hṛdaya vyākula karaḥ śrūyate madhuraḥ svaraḥ dānavānām tadā prīti saukhya viśrambha vardhanaḥ prakṛti sthe jane vyāsa dānavāḥ te samāgatāḥ viviśuḥ bhīma saṃhlādāḥ sabhām divyām manoramām muktā dāma avalamba ādhyām sraj dāma uttama bhūṣitām divya jāla upasannaddhām kiṅkiṇī citra śobhitām upetām dīrghikābhiḥ ca bahu śayyā āsanām śubhām aklamām bahu nisyandām sarva duḥkha vivarjitām sarva kāma samṛddhām ca bahu strī puruṣa ākulām viviśuḥ tām sabhām divyām daityāḥ darpa samāvṛtāḥ prahlādaḥ ca anuhlādaḥ ca siniḥ vāṣkalaḥ eva ca virocanaḥ baliḥ ca eva bali putrāḥ ca viśrutāḥ sahasrāṇi daśa dve ca yeṣām śreṣṭhaḥ mahā balaḥ bāṇaḥ nāma mahā māyaḥ rājā bāhu sahasradhṛk bāṇasya putrāḥ ye ca anye sahasrāṇi daśa eva ca muraḥ dhamuṣumuṇḍaḥ ca vipracittiḥ ca dānavaḥ kālaḥ hayaśirāḥ ca eva sambaraḥ kālasambaraḥ viśrutaḥ ca indradamanaḥ kālanemī ca dānavaḥ rāhuḥ ca śataketuḥ ca dhvajaḥ tāraḥ sa tārakaḥ mahiṣaḥ dundubhiḥ ca eva kālakaḥ ca mahā balaḥ andhakaḥ ca tathā aṭiḥ ca bakaḥ śarabhaḥ eva ca svarbhānuḥ vṛṣaparvā ca madhuḥ kaiṭabhaḥ eva ca mahākāyaḥ śatānandaḥ śatadundubhiḥ eva ca kaṇḍalaḥ ca eva mīḍhaḥ ca durlomā ca eva viśrutaḥ dhundhuḥ ca śatamāyaḥ ca śatavārttaḥ a atha duḥsahaḥ mayaḥ ca dānava śreṣṭhaḥ maya putrāḥ ca viśrutāḥ teṣām aṣṭau sahasrāṇi sarve ca kṛta niśacayāḥ vṛtraḥ ca dānava śreṣṭhaḥ namuciḥ bhajahaḥ tathā śatodaraḥ ca vyaṃsaḥ ca tāthāyaḥ ca hradodaraḥ hālaḥ gārgyaśirāḥ ca eva kuśaḥ śambhuḥ tathā eva ca tathā gaganamūrdhā ca sālukaḥ śālvaḥ eva ca kharaḥ khararomā ca sūcīlomā ca dānavaḥ parighaḥ aaparighaḥ ca eva daṇḍaḥ kāśyapaḥ eva ca dundubhiḥ ca mahā kāyaḥ saiṃhikeyaḥ ca yaḥ gaṇaḥ paulomāḥ ṣaṣṭi sāhasrāḥ kālakeyāḥ ca viśrutāḥ kālakañjāḥ sahasrāṇi aṣṭau te devakaṇṭakāḥ nivāta kavacānām ca tisraḥ koṭyaḥ mahā balāḥ tāḥ eva gaṇitāḥ sarvāḥ koṭyaḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ suradviṣām tad pakṣān varjayitvā tu manuṣyān pannagān api rākṣasān ca piśācān ca yakṣān pakṣinaḥ eva ca teṣām api tadā vyāsa koṭyaḥ viṃśati saṃmitāḥ te tām sabhām samāviśya sarve darpāt suradviṣaḥ sa vidyut ulkāḥ bhānti sma prāvṛṣ jaladharāḥ iva te svanantaḥ iva ambhodāḥ sa dhūmāḥ iva parvatāḥ utpātāḥ iva nirmuktāḥ sa viṣāḥ iva pannagāḥ gajāḥ iva ca saṃmattāḥ pavanāḥ iva vegitāḥ surāṇām viprakāra artham tasthuḥ āpūrya tām sabhām atha gatvā sabhāpālaḥ rājānam idam abravīt sukha āsīnam tadā vyāsa siṃhāsana gatam yuvā praṇamya śirasā pūrvam jānubhyām avanim gataḥ baddhāñjali puṭaḥ samyak vācā ślakṣaṇa pada akṣaram svāmī jayatu sarveṣām asurāṇām jaya āvahaḥ prahlāda ādyāḥ sabhām sarve vipracitti purogamāḥ tatas suradviṣaḥ śrutvā sarvān prāptān sabhām tadā sa kirīṭī mahā daṃṣṭraḥ muñja keśaḥ mahā hanuḥ ākarṇāt dārita āsyaḥ ca mahā chatra śirāḥ tathā ājānu bāhuḥ vṛtta akṣaḥ piṅga akṣaḥ ca ūrddhva romavān hāra varya aṅkita uraskaḥ sa balākaḥ iva ambudaḥ sa tām tadā dānava rāja sattamaḥ vicitra ratna aṃśu parīta kuṇḍalaḥ sabhām viveśa asura daitya puṅgavaiḥ samāvṛtām dyām uditaiḥ grahaiḥ iva hiraṇyākṣasya sabhāpraveśaḥ nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamaḥ ṣaṭsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sa gatvā tām sabhām vyāsa apaśyat daitya dānavān prāvṛṣ kāle mattān yathā indraḥ samupasthitān mā uttiṣṭhata iti tān sarvān avocat asura adhipaḥ māyā pañcakam āsādya bhogī vāyudharān iva sa teṣām agratas bhāti hiraṇya akṣaḥ mahā asuraḥ madhye kalabha vṛndānām yathā mattaḥ mahā gajaḥ bhāti siṃhāsana āsīnaḥ sa rājā sura vidviṣām meru śṛṅgam iva āsādya sa balākaḥ mahā ambudaḥ babhūvuḥ upaviṣṭāḥ ca tūṣṇīm eva asurāḥ tadā sisṛkṣavaḥ jalam kāle nīla ambhodāḥ iva unnatāḥ sa teṣām iṅgita jñā kāla ca sura tāpana hiraṇyākṣaḥ svayam rājā tān uvāca suradviṣaḥ yūyam sarve mahā māyāḥ śṛṇudhvam saṃyatāḥ samam kāla prāptam ca pathyam ca śiṣyāḥ iva guroḥ vacaḥ mama bhrātā priyaḥ hi āsīt jyeṣṭhaḥ pūjyaḥ yathā pitā rājā mahātmā satya saṃgaraḥ dhārmikaḥ ca vadānyaḥ ca yajvā dātā tapaḥ nvitaḥ āhitāgniḥ catur vedaḥ sarva bhūta sukha āvahaḥ rājya arthe sa hataḥ devaiḥ vikṛtyā mūḍha mānasaiḥ tasya duḥkhena tapyāmi śuṣyāmi ca mahā asurāḥ salilāt uddhṛtam grīṣme padmam kusumitam yathā teṣām kartum aham daṇḍam śaktaḥ bhavatām tatra bālānām rakṣā artham na udyataḥ hi aham saḥ aaham daṇḍam svayam kartum ekākī asura vidviṣām gamiṣyāmi na saṃdehaḥ mā bhīḥ bhavatu vaḥ a asurāḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā dānavāḥ te mudā anvitāḥ parasparam udaikṣanta vrīḍayā parayā anvitāḥ yadi yuddhe na tiṣṭhanti māyām kāṃcid vinā āśritāḥ bālaiḥ api hiraṇyākṣa su upapattyā prasādhitam hiraṇya kaśipuu rājā bhrātā naḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ uttamaḥ ākrandantam vinā rājan atas vijñāpayāmi te bhavataḥ tu vayam bālāḥ na teṣām asura īśvara śaktāḥ vayam su yuddhe na tān hantum kula pāṃsanān tapaḥ yoga bala upetāḥ māyābhiḥ ca samanvitāḥ tathā asmākam mahā rāja mā naḥ bālān yathā cara tariṣyāmaḥ vayam tat vai bāla matsyāḥ iva arṇavam prahlādaḥ a ayam saha bhrātā sa sutaḥ sa suhṛd janaḥ ekaḥ eva āhvayet sarvān yathā siṃhaḥ mahā dvipān surān sayama vitta īśān śaktaḥ sarvān prabādhitum ayam bāṇaḥ ca tad putraḥ rājā bāhu sahasradhṛk ayam mayaḥ ca vikrāntaḥ sārakaḥ tāraḥ eva ca anye ca dānavāḥ śūrāḥ śaktāḥ devān prabādhitum badhiṣyāmaḥ surān sarvān vyādhāḥ iva mṛgān vane śūraḥ aayam andhakaḥ śrīmān brahmadatta varaḥ tadā kariṣyāmaḥ mahat yuddham devatānām bhayaṃkaram pūrvam devāḥ vayam sarve paścāt te devatāḥ abhavan katham bibhīma teṣām vai siṃhānām śarabhāḥ iva uvāca vacanam tatra harṣayan dānava īśvarān mahā balāḥ vayam rājan bala hīnāḥ surāḥ tu te adya tam rāja hantāram durātmānam kula adhamam adya mātā ditiḥ teṣām duḥkham tiṣṭhadhvam dānavāḥ sarve paryāptaḥ a aham durātmanām asmākam rāja hantR̥ṇām mṛtyuḥ asmi samāgataḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān uvāca dānavān vyāsa jaya īpsuḥ sura vidviṣām adya puṣyam ca nakṣatram asmākam bala kāraṇam adya eva daṃśitāḥ sarve drutam niryātu dānavāḥ atha te dānavāḥ śīghram vāhanāni mudā yutāḥ prāvārayanta saṃgrāme yogyāni ripu bādhane śīghram kurudhvam sajjāni gacchāmaḥ daivatān prati teṣām su tumulaḥ śabdaḥ vāhanānām babhūva ha mama aśvaḥ tava siṃhaḥ mama ayam gaja yūthapaḥ niryāntu daitya indrāḥ yāsyāmaḥ pṛṣṭhatas vayam āroha svam ratham vīra kim rathena mama adya vai padātiḥ eva saṃgrāme haṃsyāmi adya suradviṣaḥ evam teṣām abhūt śabdaḥ su manojñaḥ suradviṣām vaṃśa vīṇā svana unmiśraḥ pralāpaḥ iva yoṣitām atha śukraḥ tadā abhyetya bhṛgoḥ putraḥ mahā tapāḥ hiraṇyākṣam uvāca idam harṣayan dānava īśvaram mayā śāntiḥ kṛtā te a adya rakṣā ca saha dānavaiḥ aham tvā svena tapasā sahabhṛtyam sa bāndhavam dhārayiṣyāmi yudhyantam lokān yajñaḥ iva aparaḥ tatas pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā śukram mūrdhnā praṇamya ca bhārgavam puratas kṛtvā nirjagāma sa mandirāt tatas bheryaḥ ca śaṅkhāḥ ca praṇava ānaka gomukhāḥ sāḍastamāḥ diṇḍimāḥ ca bhāṇḍāḥ ca paṭahaiḥ saha kaṭaṃkaṭāḥ pepukāḥ ca tathā ca eva eka puṣkalāḥ pañcākṣāḥ saridhīkāḥ ca mukundāḥ murajāḥ tathā labhakāḥ jala mattāḥ ca avādyanta sahasraśas gāyanaiḥ ca eva gāyadbhiḥ stuvadbhiḥ sūta māgadhaiḥ divyābhiḥ kula vṛddhābhiḥ strībhiḥ ca kṛta maṅgalāḥ dvāri apaśyan ratham kḷptam yathā deva mayam haraḥ śata nalva pramāṇa aṅkam divyam jāmbūnadam dṛḍham yantā rathasya tasya āsīt makaraḥ nāma viśrutaḥ putraḥ garutmanaḥ vyāsa khagaḥ kāma gamaḥ śubhaḥ tam asau rāja śabdena āśīrbhiḥ ca abhipūjitaḥ āruroha ratham rājā eka cakram yathā raviḥ kavacī baddha tūṇīraḥ śarī khaḍgī śarāsanī baddha godhā aṅgulitraḥ ca kaṇṭha trāṇa kṛtaḥ tathā bahvībhiḥ vaijayantībhiḥ sa balākaḥ iva ambudaḥ āviṣkṛta payoda ābhaḥ paurṇamāsyām yathā śaśī tādṛś eva rathaḥ hi āsīt sutasya su mahātmanaḥ tri sāhasrān haya agryān tu yān rathe pratyacūcudat pracoditāḥ tam ūḍhuḥ te javanāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ hayāḥ kāma gamāḥ sapta raveḥ iva mahā ratham tasya agratas tadā śukraḥ rathena ambuda nādinā dakṣiṇe tasya pārśve ca abhūt andhaka dānavaḥ dakṣiṇāyanam āsādya yathā lokasya bhāskaraḥ dvitīyam pārśvam āśritya vipracittiḥ abhūt sthitaḥ pṛṣṭhatas ca agratas ca eva yathāprīti yayuḥ tadā apare dānavāḥ śūrāḥ śaśāṅkasya yathā grahāḥ valgita āsphoṭita utkruṣṭam siṃhanāda uddhatam yayau bāhu śabda kucita avanāditaiḥ yāti dānava balam bhaya āvaham hiraṇyākṣaniryāṇam nāma aṣṭasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ uvāca katham antarhitam teṣām kaḥ mantraḥ ceṣṭitam ca kim dhārmikāḥ ca vadānyāḥ ca vidvāṃsaḥ chinna saṃśayāḥ iṣṭāḥ sarvasya lokasya kim akurvata devatāḥ śṛṇu vyāsa yathā devāḥ uttaram pratipedire asurāṇām ca yat yuktam pratyakurvata daṃśitāḥ udyukteṣu eva daityeṣu devānām bhaya sūcakāḥ saṃjajñire a amarāvatyām utpātāḥ dāruṇāḥ bhṛśam piśita āśāḥ khagāḥ tatra bhramanti upari sarvatas mamluḥ mālyāni devānām gandhaḥ ca eva aśubham vavau āyudhāni ca dīpyante sa dhūmam śaktinandana kabandhāḥ ca tathā āditye yuddham ca atra pradṛśyate dvayoḥ puruṣayoḥ vyāsa hāhākāraḥ ca sarvaśas devānām aratim ca eva cittam vā api samaśnute sphuranti vāmanetrāṇi jṛmbhikā ca upajāyate etān ca anyān ca vividhān utpātān bhaya sūcakān dṛṣṭvā prāha gurum śakraḥ bṛhaspatim idam vacaḥ yat ime sūcayanti ugrāḥ utpātāḥ naḥ su dāruṇāḥ na ime niṣkāraṇam manye na ca alpī alpam hi tat hi naḥ yat ime sūcayanti ugrāḥ kalpānte iva dāruṇāḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā devācāryaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ nirīkṣya buddhyā saṃcintya provāca idam tatas vacaḥ yat bhavān āha tat tathyam na ime niṣkāraṇam tathā sa hataḥ narasiṃhena prāptam rājyam ca naḥ punar adya varṣa sahasrāṇi dvādaśa eva su nirvṛtaiḥ daitya adhipāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dānavaiḥ saha śerate pātāle danu putrāḥ ca duḥkha śoka samāhatāḥ andhakaḥ ca asya putraḥ brahmaṇā hi amaraḥ kṛtaḥ tat bhavantaḥ su saṃnaddhāḥ sarve yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ pratīkṣadhvam mahāsattvāḥ yāvat autpātikam sthitam tasya tat vacanam śrutvā śakraḥ sarvān tadā surān uvāca sajjībhavata yuddhāya kṛta niścayāḥ bhayam mahat idam prāptam mā tiṣṭhata nirudyamāḥ mā naḥ samprāpya daitya indrāḥ hanyuḥ mattān iva amarāḥ uvāca prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā devānām eva saṃsadi eṣa daityaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ sarva asura samāvṛtaḥ tat bhavān daṃśitaḥ samyak saha asmābhiḥ mahā balaḥ jayāya uttiṣṭha deva indra vināśāya suradviṣām tatas sa bhagavān vyāsa mahātmā devarāj svayam abhedyam kavacam divyam jāmbūnada vibhūṣitam tatas godhā aṅgulitrāṇi talatram ca eva bhāsuram iṣudhīn akṣayān ca eva khaṅgam ca eva amṛta udbhavam ābabaddha asya mantreṇa yat ajaryam śara ādibhiḥ tatas sa śaram cāpam pañca vajram su dāruṇam maṅgalāni tastastasya darśayāmāsa vīryavān ghaṭam ca pūrṇam astram ca airāvatam atha api ca arcitam dhūpitam ca eva dhūpitam krodha darpaṇaiḥ āruḍhaḥ sa tadā bhāti airāvatagakam vibhuḥ pāṇḍareṇa ātapatreṇa surarāj sambabhau tadā haṃsa saṃvījitam phullam śaradi iva mahā utpalam tasya pārśve jayantaḥ ca putraḥ śakrasya dhārmikaḥ tatas yamaḥ ca puṇḍreṇa mahiṣeṇa mahā balaḥ kāladaṇḍam puraskṛtya koṭībhiḥ daśabhiḥ vṛtaḥ nirjagāma kuberaḥ ca rākṣasaiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtaḥ teṣām dvādaśa koṭyaḥ tāḥ sahasrāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ śatāni ca tathā aśītiḥ tathā eva aṣṭa adhikā punar varuṇaḥ niryayau devaḥ putrāṇām daśabhiḥ śataiḥ yādobhiḥ te vṛtāḥ sarve koṭyaḥ tāḥ ca ekaviṃśatiḥ analaḥ ca tatas devaḥ koṭībhiḥ daśabhiḥ vṛtaḥ tatas vāyuḥ mahā tejāḥ sarva vyāpī mahā javaḥ akṣauhiṇībhiḥ daśabhiḥ nirjagāma mahā balaḥ ādityāḥ niryayuḥ sarve dvādaśa akṣauhiṇī vṛtāḥ tathā rudrāḥ ca nirjagmuḥ mahā māyā mahā balāḥ ekaikaśas tadā sarve ṣoḍaśa akṣauhiṇī vṛtāḥ vasavaḥ daśabhiḥ ca eva aṣṭābhiḥ ca aśvinau ubhau tathā eva aṅgirasaḥ devāḥ sarve te aakṣauhiṇī vṛtāḥ yāmāḥ dāmāḥ ca sādhyāḥ ca lekhāḥ ye ca mahā balāḥ te a api koṭī śataiḥ sarve daśabhiḥ saha saṃgatāḥ abhūvan viṃśatiḥ koṭyaḥ gandharvāṇām mahātmanām pannagānām catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ khagānām ca eva viṃśatiḥ piśācānām ca koṭyaḥ tāḥ pañcāśat tatra saṃgatāḥ rājñām saḥ dṛṣṭvā tat bahu aparyantam devānām balam uttamam uvāca jīvaṃjīvānām rājā parama dharma vid bhagavan kriyatām vyūhaḥ yasmāt teṣām durātmanām adhṛṣyaḥ ca aprameyaḥ ca yat na vetti ca bhārgavaḥ na vetti yasya vā bhedam na kuryāt pākaśāsana uśanāḥ sa tu yat vetti mahā yogī mahā yaśāḥ sa tu tīkṣṇa tayā ca eva mānāt ca eva śacīpate tasmāt te a aham kariṣyāmi vyūham śyenam ati prabham yena tān dānavān saṃkhye kaṃcid kālam vijeṣyatha śyenam nāma mahā yogī devānām hitam ādadhat grīvāyām tasya saṃcakre vitteśam varuṇam tathā śiraḥ cūḍām yamam tasya mṛtyum kālam ca tau ubhau vaktram tasya akarot jīvaḥ candra sūryau ca cakṣuṣī ekam pakṣam cakāra asya rudrān sarvān sa vai dvijaḥ gandharvāḥ pannagāḥ ca eva nakhān tasya samāśritāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ ca mahāsattvāḥ piśācāḥ ca mahā balāḥ rājānaḥ tasya pāda sthāḥ tale bhūtān nyaveśayat mahā balān mahā utsāhān sarvān devān sabhāsadaḥ sa kṛtvā tam khaga vyūham mantreṇa eva abhimantrya ca uvāca devarājam tam bṛhaspatiḥ idam vacaḥ kalpitaḥ mayā vyūhaḥ kṛtvā rākṣasa pārthivam jaya śatrūn raṇe śakra devataiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ bhāgyāt naḥ jaya lābhāya na anyatra sura puṃgava jahi śatrūn mahā bāho mā bhīḥ bhavatu te raṇe tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca paṭahāḥ ḍiṇḍimāḥ tathā āḍambarāḥ ca nambhāḥ ca kṛkavāḥ goviṣāṇakāḥ mardalāḥ pepukāḥ citrāḥ neduḥ tūryāṇi sarvaśas tena śabdena yodhānām yuddha harṣaḥ mahān abhūt siṃhanādān akurvan te vādita āsphoṭitāni ca devāḥ tatas śaṅkha mṛdaṅga vādyaiḥ amogha sarva āyudha dīpta hastāḥ aṣṭasaptatitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ekonāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyūḍhe surāṇām sainye a atha sthite yuddhāya daṃśite dānavānām balam ghoram samadṛśyata bhīṣaṇam tat dānava balam dṛṣṭvā devāḥ sarve sa vāsavāḥ siṃhanādān akurvan te vāditra rava miśritān sa nādaḥ su mahān vyāsa sāgarasya iva mathyataḥ āpūrayat jagat sarvam yugānta ambuda nisvanaḥ tatas dānava śārdūlāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā sura uttamān vyūhya sainyam sthitān samyak vīkṣāṃcakruḥ parasparam tān vīkṣamāṇān saṃdṛśya sthitaḥ dānava yūthapān uvāca bhārgavam vyāsa hiraṇyanayanaḥ svayam ete vyūham imam kṛtvā devāḥ tiṣṭhanti abhīta vat manyante dānavān yuddhe vayam jeṣyāma sarvaśas khagasya tasya yat chettum śiraḥ kāyāt iyeṣa ca cakāra tasya śṛṅge tu prahlāda andhaka dānavau dhārān nivāta kavacān paulomān kālakā sutān pṛṣṭham cakre mahā yogī madhyam rājānam eva ca uvāca ca enam viśrabdhaḥ bhārgavaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ hiraṇyākṣam idam yuktam kāle pathyam ca sarvaśas daivata vyūha bhettā ayam mahā vyūhaḥ hi vaḥ kṛtaḥ yuktam kuruta bhadram vaḥ mayā anuparipālitāḥ mahā māyāḥ surāḥ sarve yathā na eva abhimanyata tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca paṇava ānaka gomukhāḥ āḍambarāḥ ḍiṇḍimāḥ ca paṭahāḥ ca mahā svanāḥ nānāvidhāni ca anyāni prāvādyanta sahasraśas devānām dānavānām ca mada sattva pradāni vai tatas pramathnatā iti uktāḥ dānavāḥ dānava īśvaraiḥ mamarduḥ devatā anīkam prahatāḥ sarvaśas tathā devāḥ te ca saṃyattāḥ tapaḥ yoga bala anvitāḥ dānavān vividhaiḥ śastraiḥ abhijaghnuḥ kṛta āgasaḥ asīnām pātyamānānām śirasām hastinām api āsīt śabdaḥ mahā ghoraḥ vaṃśānām iva pāṭyatām vikṛṣyatām ca dhanuṣām bāṇānām ca vimucyatām āsīt tatra mahān śabdaḥ girīṇām iva bhidyatām ākāśam abhavat sarvam khadyotaiḥ iva saṃvṛtam śirobhiḥ caraṇaiḥ ca eva bāhubhiḥ ca nipātitaiḥ kṣaṇena yuddha bhūmiḥ sā viṣamā samapadyata kabandhaiḥ ca abhinṛtyadbhiḥ durnirīkṣyam abhūt raṇe niṣka sūtraiḥ su mukuṭaiḥ keyūraiḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ api kaṇṭha trāṇaiḥ vicitraiḥ ca dukūlaiḥ maṇibhiḥ ca ha muśalaiḥ śūla daṇḍaiḥ ca ghaṇṭābhiḥ ca aṅkuśaiḥ api kruddhaḥ keśeṣu saṃgṛhya virathaḥ aapi mahā rathaḥ ratham cikṣepa ca vṛtaiḥ kuśa muṣṭim iva adhvare śaraiḥ āśīviṣa ākāraiḥ anayat yama sādanam hatam api eṣa turagaḥ sādinam patitam kṣitau upāste pādataḥ suptam gurum śiṣyaḥ yathā ātmavān vahanti puruṣāḥ kṣīvāḥ jñānavantaḥ iva āgamān bāhubhyām veṣṭayitvā tam prayayau devatā antikam sa tena eva gajena urvyām papāta viniṣūditaḥ ete padātayaḥ ca anye bahavaḥ saṃhatāḥ bhṛśam evam ākāśa gāḥ siddhāḥ ṛṣayaḥ cāraṇāḥ tathā piśācāḥ ca api modante nṛtyanti ca nikumbhilāḥ jaghnuḥ tadā rākṣasa tulya rūpāḥ svārājya hetoḥ jayam īpsamānāḥ devāsurasaṃgrāma nāma ekonāśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ aśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ dānavān vai tadā devāḥ samantān paryavārayan mṛtyuḥ kālaḥ yamaḥ ca eva kṛtāntaḥ kalahaḥ tathā nikṛtiḥ vyādhayaḥ ca eva vairam krodhaḥ ca vīryavān narakāḥ ca eva te sarve yamadūtāḥ ca sarvaśas pretāḥ ca pitaraḥ ca eva catvāraḥ ye gaṇāḥ tu iti vāmanaḥ ca eva yaḥ devāḥ kiṃkarāḥ ca mahā balāḥ niṣṭananti kṣitau daityāḥ nirayeṣu iva pāpinaḥ asi carma viniṣpiṣṭāḥ mṛtyu pāśa uvapāśitāḥ kṛtānta vaśa gāḥ sarve sambhajyanti diteḥ sutāḥ tatas hāhākṛtaḥ śabdaḥ dānavānām bale abhavat sādhu sādhu iti devānām yamam pūjayatām abhūt yamam pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā droṇa meghaḥ iva aparaḥ sa śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ akuṇṭha agraiḥ ayaḥ mayaiḥ varuṇam ca dhaneśam ca vāyum ca eva abhyavarṣata sa saṃchādya tadā bhāsam bhāskarasya śitaiḥ karaiḥ avākirat tadā devān saṃvarttakaḥ iva ambudaḥ te śara arcita sarva aṅgāḥ vadhyamānāḥ punar punar yāntam āyāntam aprāptam prāptam dūra stham eva ca athā evam asyataḥ vyāsa varuṇaḥ kārmukam tadā tam tathā nikṛtam dṛṣṭvā baliḥ bāṇaḥ ca tau ubhau prahlādaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdham lokapālān upādravan teṣām āpatatām eva lokapālāḥ mahā balāḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa ākāraiḥ cakrarakṣān apothayan vāyuḥ bāṇasya viśikhaiḥ kārmukāṇi vikarṣataḥ cikṣepa tāni vegena vāyuḥ anyām diśam punar hayān ca punar eva asya śaraiḥ sannata parvabhiḥ gadām gṛhītvā vegena śvasanam samupādravat śaraiḥ āśīviṣa ākāraiḥ gadām tām samakṛntata sa nikṛtta gadaḥ ca api bāṇaḥ praharatām varaḥ pragṛhya tu gadām anyām cikṣepa ca jahāsa ca tām āpatantīm vegena gadām bāṇasya khecarīm ākṣipya vāyuḥ vyadhamat anyām diśam adīna vat viratham tam atha ālakṣya vāyunā ca bhṛśa arditam sūryācandramasau yadvat pūrṇamāsyām samāgatau atha teṣām ca teṣām ca tat yuddham abhavat tadā tān niruddhān atha ājñāya lokapālaiḥ mahā balaiḥ nivāta kavacāḥ sarve kālakeyāḥ ca daṃśitāḥ paulomāḥ saiṃhikeyāḥ ca śambaraḥ kālaśambaraḥ andhakaḥ ca mahā daityaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ ca viśrutaḥ sarve vyūham a muñcantaḥ dānavāḥ yuddha lālasāḥ cakruḥ vegam mahā vegāḥ sa meghāḥ iva sānavaḥ tān āpatataḥ eva atha yamaḥ daṇḍena vīryavān avārayata te tasthuḥ citra paṭṭe iva arpitāḥ tān yamasya bhayāt daityān dṛṣṭvā sarvān avasthitān yamam lalāṭe daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ vivyādha vīryavān pañcabhiḥ mahiṣam ca asya ṣaḍbhiḥ kālam tathā agratas mṛtyum ca daśabhiḥ ca eva kṛtāntam ca eva saptabhiḥ hiraṇyākṣa sutaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ hi andhakaḥ aham mahā balaḥ tasya evam vadataḥ tūrṇam sūryaputraḥ pratāpavān tasya tām daṇḍa ghātena gadām saḥ śirasi enam punar kruddhaḥ daṇḍena samatāḍayat puras pratihatam dṛṣṭvā jahasuḥ dānava īśvarāḥ siṃhanādān sa vāditrān bāhuśabdān ca su svarān talena āhatya mahiṣāt yamam bhūmau nyapātayat tatas hāhākṛtam devaiḥ gṛhṇa gṛhṇa iti dānavaiḥ atha mṛtyuḥ ca kālaḥ ca kṛtāntaḥ ca iti te trayaḥ andhakam bahubhiḥ pāśaiḥ babandhuḥ krodha mūrcchitāḥ pāśān ca eva sa daitya indraḥ vicchidya su mahā balaḥ bāhu pāśena balavān kṛtāntam avabadhnata sa baddhaḥ bāhu pāśena kṛtāntaḥ krodha mūrcchitaḥ utkṣipya andhakam uddhūtaḥ nināya balavān balāt tam nīyamānam samprekṣya hiraṇāykṣaḥ sutam svakam jaghāna sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kṛtāntam su bhṛśam dṛḍham tasya gātrāṇi sarvāṇi sandhīn ca eva mahā balaḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sa viṣṭabdhaḥ vyatiṣṭhata tam bāṇaiḥ vivṛtam dṛṣṭvā devāḥ sarve sa vāsavāḥ atha ki khara mṛdaṅga veṇu vīṇā paṇava sughoṣaka ḍiṇḍi mānakānām asura sura bale mahān tadānīm samabhavat ugrataraḥ sa tūrya nādaḥ yuddhe a aśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ekāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ tadā āyāntam dṛṣṭvā devendram agratas anayat tam sura indrāya hutam bhāgam yathā analaḥ śarapāte tadā sthitvā provāca asura puṅgavaḥ pūrvadevāḥ vayam ca eva trailokyam ca akhilam hi naḥ jyeṣṭha krama āgatam kṛtvā nyāyena ca surottama te yūyam nyāyam utsṛjya hatvā me bhrātaram punar viśrambheṇa śaṭāḥ bhūtvā paścāt deva tvam āgatāḥ ime vayam pūrvadevāḥ navāḥ yūyam ca devatāḥ yudhyatām vedmi sarveṣām jīvitāni harāmi aham saha anugaiḥ tvām iha adya hatvā kṛtvā balim tathā bhaviṣyāmi anṛṇaḥ bhrātuḥ yaḥ tvayā māyayā hataḥ saḥ evam uktvā balavat dhanuḥ ākṛṣya vīryavān lalāṭe pañcabhiḥ vyāsa vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa viddhaḥ tena devānām lalāṭe pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ rājā babhau yathā meruḥ sūrya pādaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ sa tena su prahāreṇa diśaḥ dīptāḥ hi apaśyataḥ atha śaktim samādāya cikṣepa ruṣitaḥ tadā tām āpatantīm dīpta āsyām ugrām mṛtyoḥ iva svasām gadām anyām samudyamya hiraṇyākṣaḥ tadā śubhām tasya apatata eva āśu gadām hema pariṣkṛtām ciccheda bahudhā rājā dharma arthau iva nāstikaḥ kālanemiḥ ca ṣaṇḍaḥ ca vipākaḥ pākaḥ eva ca ilvalaḥ namuciḥ ca eva vātāpī kālamuñjikaḥ tān āpatataḥ eva atha rudra ādityāḥ pramanyavaḥ rurudhuḥ vijane yadvat gajān siṃhāḥ samūrjitāḥ teṣām teṣām ca saṃgrāmaḥ su ghoraḥ samapadyata araṇye a anyonya sampātāt mattānām dantinām iva tatra aṃśaḥ nāma ādityaḥ rathena ambuda nādinā āyamya kārmukam vyāsa dānavān samupādravat sa vipracittim daśabhiḥ śinim pañcabhiḥ eva ca tribhiḥ ca vāṣkalim saṃkhye mayam pañcabhiḥ eva ca saṃvaram ca eva viṃśatyāḥ asilomānam eva ca tāram ca tārakam ca eva ilvalam namucim tathā vātāpim ca indradamanam vipākam pākam eva ca kālanemim ca ṣaṇḍam ca tathā cāmīsṛ muñjikam etān sarvān sa vivyādha daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ vikarṣatām ca saṃgrāme tatas eṣām punar vāhān sūtān divyān jaya dhvajān te hata aśvāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ hata sūtāḥ ca sarvaśas vegena khaṅginaḥ sarve aṃśam eva abhidudruvuḥ tān mūrttīn iva śaila indrān garjataḥ jaladān iva asambhrāntaḥ tat ādityaḥ jānuṣu eva avapūrayat śara pūrita gulphāḥ te jānuṣu eva ca dānavāḥ aṃśam utsṛjya vegena jagmuḥ anyām diśam tadā siṃhanādān ca vipulān bāhu śabdān ca puṣkalān dānavānām sa daityānām akarot kadanam mahat śirāṃsi dānava indrāṇām aṃśaḥ praharatām varaḥ apātayat phalāni iva pakvāni śvasataḥ yathā dhāvanti kecid aṃśena aśiraskāḥ śaraiḥ kṛtāḥ gatvā vegena saṃgrāmāt patanti ūrvyām gatāsavaḥ apare bāhubhiḥ chinnaiḥ ūrubhiḥ ca mahā balāḥ patitāḥ niṣṭananti ugram niraya sthāḥ yathā narāḥ śara pūrita sarva aṅgāḥ śara sambaddha bandhanāḥ na sa tatra asti daityaḥ vā dānavaḥ vā mahā balaḥ yam śarāḥ na viśanti ugrāḥ aṃśasya su mahātmanaḥ aśoka kiṃśukānām vā tathā daitya balam babhau ayam aṃśaḥ na iti ayam ca ayam iti uta sarvam aṃśa mayam daityāḥ hi apaśyanta bhaya arditāḥ saḥ a api nitya āyata dhanuḥ pariveṣī iva bhāskaraḥ yam yatas paśyate daityam tam tam vivyādha patribhiḥ na ādadānaḥ tadā hi aṃśaḥ sandadhānaḥ tathā api vā maṇḍalīkṛtam eva asya dṛśyante kārmukam mahat sa divya cāpaḥ laghu hastavān balī sadā mahā maṇḍala bhūta kārmukaḥ dadāha śatrūn pavana īritaḥ raṇe vibhāvasuḥ śuṣkam iva indhanam mahat yuddhe ekaśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ dvyaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ tān tathā aṃśena daitya indrān kālyamānān itastatas dṛṣṭvā balaḥ mahā māyaḥ yantāram idam abravīt nayasva mām yatas a aṃśaḥ a ayam durātmā dahate balam yāvat enam śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ nayāmi yama sādanam tasya apatata eva aṃśaḥ tadā praharatām varaḥ dhvajam ciccheda bāṇena hayān ca ekaikaśas tadā bhallena ca śiraḥ kāyāt yantuḥ āśu nyapātayat tasya daityasya te bhānti lalāṭe pañca sāyakāḥ su vṛṣṭim iva jīmūtaḥ iva aśanim karān divākaraḥ yadvat tuṣāram candramāḥ yathā tathā sa dānavaḥ darpāt balaḥ praharatām varaḥ aṃśam eva akirat tīkṣṇaiḥ sāyakaiḥ marma bhedibhiḥ hayān vega hatān kṛtvā sārathim ca api asārathim yathāṃśam sa cakāra ugra sthān yān api daivatān nirudyamān mahā māyaḥ cakāra virarāsa ca kvacid gīṣpati saṃkāśaḥ kvacid bhāskara saṃnibhaḥ kvacid ca ākāśam āviśya adṛśyaḥ saḥ aasṛjat śarān viṣṭabdham mūka vat sarvam devānām balam ābabhau naṣṭa āvāditra ninadam haya heṣita varjitam gaja bṛṃhita vimraṣṭam śrānta yodha ugra nāditam ceṣṭā virahitāḥ ca āsan yathā mokṣa pathi sthitāḥ tān tathā sīdataḥ sarvān dṛṣṭvā bala mahā arṇave vāyuḥ jayantaḥ pūṣā ca bhagaḥ ca su mahā balāḥ vāyuḥ tasya mahābhāga śarān meghāt iva uditān muñcataḥ mucyamānān ca muktān ca eva aharat balī dehatrāṇam tathā pūṣā jayantaḥ ca iṣudhī tathā samārdayan śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ devāḥ ravi sama prabhāḥ saḥ a ardyamānaḥ tadā devaiḥ balī dānava puṅgavaḥ vṛkṣaiḥ kānana jaiḥ vyāsa yuyudhe bhīma vikramaḥ tān drumān te tad ākṣiptān balena bahudhā śubhān gṛhītvā sa mahat śṛṅgam sa mṛga vyāla kinnaram cikṣepa su mahā nādam prakurvāṇaḥ jahāra śṛṅgam tat ca api papāta asura mūrdhani dānavānām tadā koṭim ekām vīryavatām yudhi jaghāna bala muktam tat giri śṛṅgam mahā svanam tān hatān dānavāḥ tena śṛṅgena diti nandanān dṛṣṭvā devān ca tān ugrān abhajyanta sahasraśas utsṛjya vāhanāni anye jīvita abhyarthinaḥ tadā pramuñcantaḥ mahā nādān palāyanta sahasrśas dravataḥ tān tadā abhyetya hiraṇyākṣaḥ
