sa dānavaḥ vipracittiḥ ca danujaḥ prahlādaḥ ca mahā balaḥ ūcire dānavān sarvān daityān ca bhaya vihvalān bho bho dānava śārdūlāḥ daityāḥ ca sura śatravaḥ kim pālayatha tiṣṭhadhvam mā bhayam vaḥ astu dānavāḥ kva gatāḥ dānavāḥ yūyam sukham lapsyatha vā na vā ete balam a jānantaḥ devāḥ pūrvam mahā balāḥ niḥśeṣān pramathiṣyanti pātāle a api kula adhamāḥ mā yāta vinivartadhvam rirakṣiṣata sarvaśas kva ca vairam suraiḥ sārdham kva rājya haraṇam gatam yat ca vaḥ garjitam pūrvam tasya kālaḥ āgataḥ vayam ekaikaśas yogyāḥ devānām na aśane ca nivartadhvam adharma jñāḥ yudhyadhvam kṛta niścayāḥ kaśyapasya sutaḥ śrīmān hiraṇyākṣaḥ a asmi dānavāḥ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ vīryam yat abhūt asura uttamāḥ dviguṇam tat mama api asti vīkṣadhvam tat aśaṅkitāḥ adya ca etān mayā sarvān hatān paśyata dānavāḥ saṃgrāme yadi tiṣṭhanti sarve devāḥ mama agratas vijvarāḥ mokṣyatha sukham mayā indreṇa asura uttamāḥ sa putram mām yudhi yathā vīkṣamāṇāḥ tu tiṣṭhata vinivṛttāḥ punar sarve lajjayā ati samāvṛtāḥ te chatra saṃchādita vaktra padmāḥ lajjā samāviṣṭa virāga vaktrāḥ yuddhe aasurākrośanaḥ nāma dvyaśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ tryaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha te dānavāḥ vyāsa nivṛttāḥ raṇa mūrdhani duṣkaram tam tadā cakruḥ vegam nadyaḥ iva arṇave prahlādaḥ ca anuhlādaḥ ca śiniḥ bāṣakalaḥ eva ca vipracittiḥ ca ṣaṇḍaḥ ca hradaḥ ca sa śatodaraḥ yamaḥ aasuraḥ ca vyaṃsaḥ ca śatāvarttaḥ huta udaraḥ tāraḥ ca tārakaḥ ca eva bakaḥ ca aṭiḥ ca viśrutaḥ ketuḥ ca śataketuḥ ca rāhuḥ svarbhānuḥ eva ca kālanemī vipākaḥ ca pākaḥ duryodhanaḥ tathā vṛṣaparvā śatākrandaḥ śatāvarttaḥ aatha dhenukaḥ saiṃhikeyāḥ ca vikhyātāḥ paulomāḥ kālakā sutāḥ nivāta kavacāḥ ca eva bāleyāḥ ca tathā gaṇāḥ bāṇasya ca sutāḥ sarve kālakhañjāḥ ca viśrutāḥ vṛtraḥ vṛttaḥ ca sa gaṇaḥ tathā anye su mahā balāḥ vegaḥ sa sindhurājasya velām prati yathā mahān vāditra rava saṃmiśraiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ su puṣkalaiḥ ratha nemi hayānām ca gajānām bṛṃhitaiḥ saha devāḥ hi api su saṃyattāḥ sarva udyogena saṃsthitāḥ pratyagṛhṇanta tān daityān krodha tāmra āyata īkṣaṇāḥ asibhiḥ pātyamānaiḥ ca śataghnībhiḥ ca sarvatas śara asi bhinna kṛttāni patanti urvyām śirāṃsi hi mukuṭaiḥ hā keyūraiḥ śroṇī sūtraiḥ ca saprabhaiḥ niṣkaiḥ dukūlaiḥ kaṭakaiḥ aṅgulīyaiḥ sa kuṇḍalaiḥ uracchadaiḥ kaṅkatībhiḥ karapālaiḥ ca dantinām paṭṭaiḥ ca kāñcanaiḥ divyaiḥ kavacaiḥ ca mahā prabhaiḥ tatra yuddha niśā bhāti tārābhiḥ dyauḥ iva aparā tiṣṭha tiṣṭha kva me yāsi na asti mokṣaḥ tava adya vai kim garjasi vṛthā vyomni śaradi iva balāhakāḥ karmaṇā darśaya kṣipram garjitam te aadya niṣphalam na evam prahriyate mūḍha mā vīkṣasva dṛḍhaḥ bhava tiṣṭha tiṣṭha kva gantāsi mama hatvā priyam sutam adya te ratām sarvām deva adhama su duḥsahām nāśayiṣyanti mad bāṇāḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha mama agratas evam vadantaḥ yuyudhuḥ yathā mattāḥ mahā gajāḥ siddhāḥ ca cāraṇāḥ ca eva vyomni sarve vyavasthitāḥ mama ayam dānavaḥ saṃkhye hataḥ bhartā vinirmitaḥ ayam devaḥ tava patiḥ mā pārakye manaḥ kṛthāḥ kim evam lobha yuktā asi śreṣṭham śreṣṭham parīkṣase asaṃtuṣṭam manaḥ kim te saṃtuṣṭā bhava sundari bhāgaḥ a ayam te suraiḥ dattaḥ tam gṛhītvā vraja ālayam mekhalā valaya unmiśram tāsām tat kala bhāṣitam śrutvā śrutvā ca te yodhāḥ yuyudhuḥ bhaya varjitāḥ valgita āsphoṭitaiḥ ca eva diśaḥ sarvāḥ vyanādayan yuddhe tryaśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ caturaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatra yajvā svayam devaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ pratāpavān saha devaiḥ surādhyakṣaḥ kuśāḥ tasya śarāḥ matāḥ āyudhāni vicitrāṇi sruvāḥ yaiḥ hūyate haviḥ haviḥ prāṇāḥ samākhyātāḥ agniḥ mṛtyuḥ mahā prabhā mantrāḥ ca astrāṇi divyāni puroḍāśāḥ śirāṃsi api ādityāḥ bahvṛcaḥ ca āsan hotram ca vasubhiḥ kṛtam śāmitram ca aśvinau tau tu yajñe evam vyavarttata paśuḥ tatra abhavat daityaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ saha anugaḥ evam babhau tadā yajñaḥ daityānām śiśirādhipaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ abhavat yajvā daitya dānava nāyakaḥ vipracittiḥ abhūt hotā prasthātāraḥ ca dānavāḥ udgātā ca eva prahlādaḥ śukraḥ brahmā ca suvrataḥ paśuḥ indraḥ sahasra akṣaḥ evam saḥ aayajat avyayaḥ tasmin tadā mahā yajñe vartamāne mahā bhaye indraḥ samāsadat daityam hiraṇyākṣam mahā balam vāyuḥ abhyāyayau tūrṇam vipracittim mahā balaḥ saktaḥ saṃvareṇa aṃśaḥ balena bhagaḥ eva ca bāṇena varuṇaḥ sārdham andhakena yamaḥ saha ahirbudhnyena rāhuḥ ca kāpālī śataketunā hiraṇyākṣaḥ tadā indrasya dṛḍham āyamya kārmukam ṣaḍbhiḥ lalāṭe vivyādha gajam bhūyas ca saptabhiḥ gaurikā ambu parisrāvī śvetaḥ parvatarāj iva tasya kruddhaḥ tadā śakraḥ vajreṇa śataparvaṇā prahāram adadat vyāsa gaṇḍa veśe nanāda ca a cintayānaḥ sa gajam śakram eva ardayat balī sa vegam mahat āsthāya aṅkuśena ca coditaḥ hiraṇyākṣa ratham tūrṇam jagrāha ratha kūbare gṛhītvā sa tam utkṣipya cikṣepa gaja sattamaḥ meru śṛṅgam iva utkṣipya sa megham śveta kuṇḍalī svarbhānunā hataḥ pūrvam sa rathaḥ bhāskaraḥ yathā tatra samyak sthitam bhūmau hiraṇyākṣa ratham punar ājagāma gajaḥ tūrṇam jighṛkṣuḥ muni sattama tam āpatantam vegena samīkṣya asura sattamaḥ tam tu maṇḍalam āvṛttam gajaḥ tathā eva hi stabdha dṛś karṇa lāṅgūlaḥ prasārita karaḥ hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvam sādhu sādhu iti ca ubhayoḥ balayoḥ deva daityānām mūka vat ca abhavat punar sādhu daitya iti ca anyeṣām hiraṇyākṣa iti ca eva hi hiraṇyākṣaḥ ca daitya indraḥ bhramitvā tris mahā asuraḥ devarājam śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ samantāt paryavārayat sa taiḥ śaraiḥ tadā vyāsa marma saṃdhiṣu tāḍitaḥ vajreṇa śatadhā tasya kavacam pravyaśātayat hayānām ca eva yoktrāṇi sarvāṇi eva tā akṛntata raśmīn ca sūta hasta sthān pratodam ca eva kāñcanam hiraṇyākṣaḥ gadayā samatāḍayat śakṛt mūtram sṛjan vyāsa prādravat balavān tadā asinā abhyāhataḥ ca api devarājaḥ mahā balaḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ prayayau pramāthinā hiraṇyanetreṇa yudhi pramāthitaḥ caturaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vipracittiḥ mahā māyaḥ vāyum bahubhiḥ āśugaiḥ saṃchādayan tadā vyāsa maṇḍalīkṛta kārmukaḥ iṣūn cikṣepa tīkṣṇa agrān śalabhān sāgaraḥ yathā dhārāḥ balāhakāt yadvat jyotsnāḥ candramasaḥ yathā tathā te śara saṃghātāḥ dhanuṣaḥ maṇḍalīkṛtāt bhāskaram chādayānān tān śarān āpatataḥ balī chinnāḥ ca niṣṭananti urvyām niraya sthāḥ yathā narāḥ tān tathā nihatān dṛṣṭvā vipracittiḥ mahā asuraḥ amanyanta surāḥ ca eva nigṛhītam danoḥ sutam athā utpatya tadā vegāt gadayā pavanam dṛḍham atāḍayat hiraṇyākṣaḥ gaṇḍa deśe mahā balaḥ sa tena su prahāreṇa hiraṇyākṣasya parityajya yayau tūrṇam anya deśam mahā balaḥ yuddham samabhavat ghoram draṣṭR̥ṇām tuṣṭi vardhanam aṃśaḥ aasya āpatataḥ tūrṇam saṃvarasya mahā balaḥ dhanuḥ ca pañcadhā kṛtvā hayān ninye yama kṣayam tatas ā asya sāratheḥ kāyāt śiraḥ bhūmau apātayat bhūyas enam catuḥṣaṣṭyā sāyakānām avidhyata sa māyām tāmasīm ghorām samāviśya āśu dānavaḥ kaṃkaṭaiḥ karavālaiḥ ca bhindipālaiḥ ayaḥ ghanaiḥ jaghāna sa ratham devam aṃśam vyāsa raṇa ajire sa saṃdṛśya samantāt ca pātyamānam mahā bhayam aṃśaḥ mūḍhaḥ raṇam tyaktvā prayayau anyatas bhayāt bhagaḥ balam samāsādya rathena ambuda nādinā tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti tam daityam uktvā vivyādha patriṇā sa sāyakam samāsādya balaḥ a asura mahā rathaḥ tasya tat lāghavam śauryam amūḍha tvam sa vīrya tām dṛṣṭvā deva asurāḥ sarve sādhu sādhu iti apūjayan bhagaḥ lajjayā āviṣṭaḥ padā tena āhataḥ tadā nāma śeṣān tadā kṛtvā vinanāda yathā ambudaḥ syandanam tu balaḥ tyaktvā cūrṇitam sa hayam tadā bhagasya kārmukam divyam bhūmi sthaḥ ca ācchinat balī tatas enam pṛṣatkena lalāṭe samatāḍayat gṛhṇataḥ kārmukam ca asya pṛṣṭha deśe balaḥ aacchinat tam āpatantam muśalam balaḥ dānava puṅgavaḥ śaraiḥ viṣṭambhayāmāsa nandī mṛtyum yathā ātmanaḥ atha pratihatam matvā muśalam saḥ a asuraḥ punar dhanuṣkoṭyā bhagam mūrdhni balavān samatāḍayat ratham ca saha sūtena gṛhītvā kūbare punar cikṣepa dakṣiṇasyām sa vāyuḥ girim iva arṇave pūṣā virocanam devaḥ śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ āśugaiḥ kruddhaḥ pūṣā tathā ākṛṣya balavān kārmukam mahat jīvita anta karam ghoram yuga anta āditya varcasam tam āpatantam bahudhā nadantam diśaḥ ca sarvāḥ avabhāsayantam sa ca api avaplutya mahā asura indraḥ dṛṣṭvā tam āditya samāna bhāsam kṛtvā āśu bhasma iva yathā hutāśaḥ jagāma kham divyam adṛśya rūpam yuddhe pañcāśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ṣaḍaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vegena asim viniṣkṛṣya sa pūṣṇaḥ niśitān śarān ciccheda āpatataḥ sarvān kārmukam ca eva vīryavān patitam tam sa daitya indraḥ pragṛhya āśu mahā balaḥ cikṣepa devarājānam nardamānaḥ payoda vat tam sārathiḥ mṛtyu bhayāt viṣaṇṇam samupasthitam apovāha tadā vyāsa tatas daityāḥ vicukruśuḥ bāṇam vivyādha varuṇaḥ pṛṣatkānām śatena ha sa kārmuka śatāni sma pañca bāṇaḥ pratāpavān ākṛṣya yugapad kruddhaḥ śarān cikṣepa tāvataḥ ekaikam pañcadhā kṛtvā bāṇam vivyādha pañcabhiḥ chinnām dṛṣṭvā ca tām bhūyas gadāḥ pañca asṛjat balī saḥ ekasyām tadā saktaḥ tāḥ gadāḥ na abhyavaikṣata avikṣatāḥ ca tāḥ sarvāḥ petuḥ tasya tatas upari kācid ca kārmukam ghoram hasta deśāt nyapātayat kācid dhvajam dṛḍham divyam cikṣepa dharaṇī tale kācid ratham tadā āhatya pāṃsu grāsam cakāra ha urasi ūru udare kaṭyām aparāḥ tasya tāḥ gadāḥ patantyaḥ su mahā ghorāḥ ārtim cakruḥ mahā bhayāḥ evam sa tena virathaḥ kṛtaḥ kṛcchreṇa dhīmatā varuṇaḥ tam samutsṛjya jagāma anyat raṇa ajiram yamaḥ aandhakam samāsādya tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti coditaḥ sa ratham tasya saṃcūrṇam kṛtvā śata sahasraśas andhakaḥ ratham tyaktvā gadā pāṇiḥ mahā balaḥ daṇḍena eva gadām ugrām bhasma sāyujyam ānayat mayā vairam samāsādya kva ante jīvam vimokṣyase adya tvā nihaniṣyāmi su dṛḍham kriyatām jagat agre draṣṭāsi tatra eva sarvān etān suradviṣaḥ uvāca tam yamam kruddham krodhāt dīpta anala īkṣaṇaḥ hiraṇyākṣa sutaḥ dṛptaḥ sura antakaḥ mahā yoga bala upetaḥ na asmi prākṛta dānavaḥ aṅga ādyena samutkṛtya bhāgān māṃsasya kārṣikān saṃvatsara śatāni aṣṭau pañca ca eva hutaḥ tuṣṭaḥ brahmā dadau yasya sadā eva amara tām śubhām saḥ a aham nāmnā mahā sattvaḥ mṛtyu utsedhaḥ na saṃśayaḥ na tvam mama kṛtaḥ mṛtyuḥ siṃhasya iva vane śaśaḥ aham tu bhavitā mṛtyuḥ tava na asti atra saṃśayaḥ adya tvā aham durātmānam sarva loka bhayaṃkaram na tvayā āsāditam pūrvam haratā jīvitāni hi kiṃcid bhūtam mahat bhūtam tena tvam nirbhayaḥ sadā amṛte na tathā prītim kariṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ prāṇaiḥ saha eva dehānte nāśayiṣyāmi sarvaśas daṇḍena asura śārdūlam uttamāṅge aabhyatāḍayat kālaḥ ca tam kareṇa eva hṛdaye samatāḍayat mṛtyuḥ ca aśaninā kṣipram śirasi eva abhyatāḍayat kaṇṭhe ca niyatiḥ tasya pāśam cikṣepa dāruṇam kṛtāntaḥ parighena eva gaṇḍa deśe samāhanat puṣpa vṛṣṭyā yathā kaścid ārtimān abhavat tathā na pāśāḥ tasya līyante daṇḍaḥ vā parighaḥ vā anyāni ca asya tīvrāṇi na duḥkhāya bhavanti uta tatas sarvaiḥ tadā utkruṣṭam dānavaiḥ sarvatodiśam avādyanta ca tūryāṇi mumude ca andhakaḥ bhṛśam sa teṣām tuṣṭi śabdena mada vīrya samīritaḥ ājaghāna mahā vegaḥ muṣṭinā urasi tam yamam jayantaḥ ca ilvalam prāpya vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ hayānām ca eva yoktrāṇi pratodam ca eva kāñcanam avidhyetām tadā yasya kārmuke sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya nedatuḥ sāgarau iva atha śakrasutaḥ śrīmā labdhvā tasya tadā antaram gṛhītvā anyasya patitām gadām hema vibhūṣitām sa yāvat tām gadām ghorām śaraiḥ sannata parvabhiḥ atha yāvat sa nistriṃśam jagrāha aditinandanaḥ tāvat enam padā daityaḥ vāmena urasi atāḍayat tatas hāhākṛtam abhūt asurāṇām bale mahat devānām siṃha nādāḥ ca śaṅkha śabdāḥ ca puṣkalāḥ tūryāṇi ca api avādyanta sādhu sādhu iti ca abhavat jayantaḥ yathā cakram vidhātā balavān tadā kālakeyāḥ ca te daityāḥ paulomāḥ siṃhikā sutāḥ nivāta kavacāḥ ca enam samantāt paryavārayan hiraṇyākṣa pathe kṣiptvā prādravat yena devatāḥ yuddhe ṣaḍaśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ saptāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa ākāraiḥ nardamānaḥ yathāmudar tasya asyataḥ tatas bāṇān candramāḥ prahasan iva ekaikam saptadhā kṛtvā mayam vivyādha pañcabhiḥ sa tasya hasataḥ śīghram lalāṭe kaṅka patriṇā cakrarakṣān ca nistriṃśaiḥ anayat yama sādanam tasya tat cāpalam vīkṣya mayaḥ dānava sattamaḥ māyām divyām samāsthāya rāhuḥ samabhavat tadā sa rāhu bhūtaḥ daitya indraḥ deveśam śaśalakṣaṇam sa tām māyām tadā jñātvā devaḥ hi amṛta sambhavaḥ saḥ daityaḥ mahā māyaḥ tān śarān māyayā eva tu vārayan abhidudrāva śītaraśmim mahā asuraḥ gṛhītvā kūbare daityaḥ cikṣepa ca rarāsa ca tasya utpatya rathāt rāhuḥ gadayā bhīma rūpayā dhanuḥ dhvajam hayān ca eva samacūrṇayat avyayaḥ aśanim śata ghaṇṭām sa dīptām mṛtyoḥ iva snuṣām jagrāha bhṛśam āyastaḥ pāśam mṛtyoḥ iva antakaḥ bhrāmayitvā sa tām ugrām yama daṇḍa nibhām balāt cikṣepa rāhum uddiśya vidyutam megharāj iva papāta rāhoḥ śirasi yathā vajram śiloccaye sa prahasya bhṛśam rāhuḥ vegam cakre mahā balaḥ ahirbudhnam prati kruddhāḥ nāgānām iva pakṣirāj āpatantam sa vīkṣya eva bhagavān deva sattamaḥ śataketuḥ ca tam vīraḥ rathena ambu nādinā abhyadravat raṇe kruddhaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt ādhāvataḥ kāpālī hṛdayam kaṅka patribhiḥ tatas hāhākṛtam daityaiḥ gṛhṇa gṛhṇa iti ca api uta śambaraḥ ca ilvalaḥ ca eva bāṇaḥ baliḥ atha api ca kālakeyāḥ sa paulomāḥ nivāta kavacāḥ ca ye te śaraiḥ ca gadābhiḥ ca muśalaiḥ prāśa tomaraiḥ kālanemiḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ gadām hema pariṣkṛtām śata ghaṇṭā aṭṭahāsām ca mṛtyoḥ jihvām iva adbhutām bhrāmayitvā asakṛt daityaḥ nardamānaḥ yathā vṛṣaḥ śakra muktām iva āyāntīm aśanim parvata upari vidyutam vā mahā śaktām sa rudraḥ bhīma vikramaḥ vañcayāmāsa vegena śvetaḥ mṛtyum iva āgatām tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca api uktvā rudraḥ praharatām varaḥ bhrāmayitvā gadām ghorām daityasya upari apātayat sa tayā gadayā daityaḥ dīptayā bhīma rūpayā hataḥ mūrdhni diśaḥ sarvāḥ hāridrāḥ samapaśyata maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi darśayitvā mahā balaḥ aja eka pādam gadayā skandha deśe vyatāḍayat saṃstabhya gadayā bhūyas rudram kukṣau atāḍayat sa tayā gadayā nunnaḥ yathā vāyu īritaḥ nagaḥ papāta bhūmau vegena śataśṛṅgaḥ yathā purā bhrāmayitvā ca cikṣepa sa ca amṛtyuḥ avasthitaḥ kārtasvanam jvaraḥ ca ugraḥ rudraḥ praharatām varaḥ kārtasvanaḥ ca bāṇena kārmukam tasya dīptimat rudraḥ daṇḍam sarva artha sādhakam tam yuga anta anala prakhyam śata sūrya anala prabham jaghāna śara jālena meghaḥ vṛṣṭyā yathā acalam hanyamānaḥ ca taiḥ daṇḍaḥ haviṣā iddhaḥ iva analaḥ tam a pratihatam daṇḍam jñātvā kārtasvanaḥ sa tu daṇḍaḥ ca ratham abhyetya sa hayam saha yantṛṇā chittvā dhvajam dhanuḥ ca asya tathā yoktrāṇi vājinām viratham tam jvaram kṛtvā asinā mūrdhni atāḍayat asi ghāta parīta ātmā sa rudraḥ śatru saṃsadam yuddhe saptāśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ aṣṭāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ aryamā bahubhiḥ bāṇaiḥ prahlādam daitya puṅgavam ājaghāna ratham ghoram dhvajam ca asya vyaśātayat jaghāna bahubhiḥ bāṇaiḥ vṛṣṭyā meghaḥ yathā acalam śarān a gaṇayan eva hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ gṛhītvā kūbare tasya ratham hema pariṣkṛtam nirjitāḥ tarjitāḥ ca eva yuddhāya ca punar sthitāḥ tatas saṃkulam eva abhūt devānām dānavaiḥ saha paraspara jigīṣūṇām yuddham bhīru bhaya āvaham tatas bheryaḥ ca śaṅkhāḥ ca paṭaha āsekya puṣkalāḥ jharjharyaḥ pepukāḥ ca eva ḍiḍṇimāḥ goviṣāṇakāḥ avādyanta bale vyāse ubhayeṣām sahasraśas keśa śaivāla bahulā dhanuḥ jyā kṛta tantukā niṣṭanat śastra maṇḍūkā dukūla chatra phenilā uṣṇīṣa vara haṃsā ca kara pāda śira upalā hāra keyūra sikatā mukuṭa utphulla paṅkajā medaḥ usra kapha paṅkā ca prāṇa jīvita nāśinī prāvartata nadī ghorā hasti aśva ratha vāhinī tasyām snāyanti rakṣāṃsi pibanti ca ramanti ca nṛtyanti ca api bhaya dāḥ tathā gṛdhrāḥ gomāyavaḥ ca eva śvānaḥ mārjāra vāyasāḥ cakṣūṃṣi kara pāda antram bhakṣayantaḥ mama ayam hastinaḥ pādaḥ mama ayam meda paṭṭakaḥ mama ayam ca karaḥ śukraḥ bāhuḥ ca rudhirasya daḥ mama ayam tava na ayam ca gṛhṇa paśya iti ca eva hi kalaham cakrire tatra krūrāḥ piśita bhojanāḥ tyaktvā anye ca hatān tatra sva dehān su mahā rathāḥ vimānaiḥ strī jana ākīrṇaiḥ prayayuḥ brahmaṇaḥ sadaḥ apare pāpa karmāṇaḥ hanyamānāḥ ruṣā andhitaiḥ kecid ārtta svaram kṛtvā ṣa arditāḥ mriyante puruṣāḥ yuddhe śataśas aatha sahasraśas daśantaḥ ca tṛṇāni anye bhrātar putra iti ca apare krandamānāḥ janāḥ bhītāḥ prāṇān kṛcchreṇa tatyajuḥ saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭāḥ kecid deva asura mahā rathāḥ śara sannata marmāṇaḥ patanti urvyām drumāḥ iva aśivāni śivāḥ neduḥ aṭṭahāsān ca rākṣasāḥ ārtta nādān ca puruṣāḥ tathā eva gaja vājinaḥ siṃhanādāḥ ca śūrāṇām bāhu śabdāḥ ca puṣkalāḥ dhanuṣām kṛṣyamāṇānām śabdāḥ vādya ravāḥ tathā atha indraḥ ca dhaneśaḥ ca yamaḥ kālaḥ ca vīryavān varuṇaḥ marutaḥ ca eva viśvedevāḥ ca sarvaśas mitraḥ ca eva jayantaḥ ca bhagaḥ pūṣā aryamā tathā kāpālī ca api yaḥ rudraḥ vasavaḥ ca mahā balāḥ nāsatyaḥ ca eva dasraḥ ca pṛśnayaḥ ca sura uttamāḥ ete ca anye ca devānām pravarāḥ bāhu śālinaḥ prabhañjanāḥ iva akāle mahāntaḥ iva ca acalāḥ vṛṣabhāḥ iva nardantaḥ bṛṃhantaḥ iva kuñjarāḥ grasantaḥ ca yathā grāhāḥ chindantaḥ makarāḥ iva varṣamāṇāḥ iva ghanāḥ siṃḍāḥ iva ca nardinaḥ dānavānām balam sarve vegena eva abhyavārayan yuddhe aṣṭāśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ teṣām tad vega nunnānām bhagnānām kliśyatām punar trāṇa artham ati dīpta akṣaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ aagrahīt padam andhakaḥ ca mahā māyaḥ bhrātaraḥ ca asya tad samāḥ śatam ratha sahasrāṇām sarveṣām apalāyinām prahlādaḥ ca saha bhrātā hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ teṣām teṣām ca saṃgrāmaḥ su ghoraḥ samapadyata grāhāṇām iva kāṇḍe ca gajānām iva vā vane indraḥ tvaṣṭā ca pūṣā ca hiraṇyākṣam avārayan saṃgatya sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ sarva marmasu atāḍayan teṣām dhanūṃṣi citrāṇi asyatām ca divaukasām tāni viṣṭambhitāni sma tadā daityena māyayā nānamanti yathā pūrvam tatas te hi ākulāḥ abhavan babandha teṣām gātrāṇi samantāt astra māyayā tān baddhān ca samīkṣya evam akarmaṇyān mahā balān yantāraḥ vāhanaiḥ kṣipram jahnu stambhāt raṇa ajirāt pragṛhīta āyudhāḥ kruddhāḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti vādinaḥ teṣām āpatatām saṃkhye sa daityaḥ krodha mūrcchitaḥ sarveṣām sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bibheda kavacān yudhi yamaḥ daṇḍam sasarja asya tathā kālaḥ ca dhaneśaḥ ca aśanim ghoram varuṇaḥ pāśam eva ca bhagaḥ ca muśalam ghoram anye ca anyān tathā amarāḥ vyaṣṭambhayat adīna ātmā śakra hastam yathā bhavaḥ sādhuvādān tatas hṛṣṭāḥ dānavānām mahā rathāḥ samam cakruḥ ca sampūjya hiraṇyākṣam mahā asuram kaśyapena prasūtasya rājñaḥ a asmākam ca svāminaḥ apare siṃhanādān ca bāhuśabdān ca puṣkalān cakruḥ hṛṣṭāḥ ca vādyāni tathā sarvāṇi avādayan evam hi samprahṛṣṭānām dānavānām mahā āhave pārāśarya giraḥ bahvyaḥ śrūyante teṣām praharṣam jñātvā ittham deva bhaṅgam ca tam tadā samantāt dhvaja yuktena patākā śata mālinā javena yantR̥ṇām yatnāt nigṛhītena śabdavān prapūrayan diśaḥ sarvāḥ sahasā pratyadṛśyata sa pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ daitya rājam atha avyayaḥ āhatya yojane tasmāt deśāt kṣipram avāsṛjat andhakam ca tatas ṣaṣṭyā vipracittim ca saptabhiḥ mayam pañcāśatā viddhvā saptabhiḥ saptabhiḥ punar daityān ca dānavān ca eva sarvān vivyādha tad kṣaṇāt punar puloma putrān ca nivāta kavacān api te tena bahubhiḥ viddhāḥ śaraiḥ asura puṅgavāḥ dikṣu sarvāsu vikṣiptāḥ yojana antaritāḥ sthitāḥ yān yān ca te vimuñcanti gadā muśala paṭṭiśān tān sarvān bhagavān vāyuḥ dānava upari apātayat te hatāḥ hanyamānāḥ ca sva muktaiḥ āyudhaiḥ bhṛśam ārta nādān prakurvāṇāḥ prādravanta diśaḥ diśaḥ pāṃśu varṣeṇa ca punar cakṣūṃṣi eṣām apūrayat śastrāṇi ca tathā anyāni puñjaśas ca avatsthire tasya tat karma saṃvīkṣya hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān dhik vaḥ daityāḥ balam sarvam dhik darpāḥ dhik parākramāḥ ye yūyam raṇa madhya sthāḥ jīvite sati bāliśāḥ athavā yat mayā proktam yūyam bālāḥ rati klamāḥ tat tathā nā asti saṃdehaḥ bālaiḥ iva hi vaḥ kṛtam tiṣṭhadhvam bāla vat sarve rakṣantaḥ jīvitam svakam tatas sa parvataḥ bhūtvā diti putraḥ pratāpavān samantāt vāyu vegam tam samavārayat avyayaḥ ro anilam jñātvā parvatena nivāritam sa baddhaḥ bāhu pāśena tadā vāyuḥ pratāpavān sampragṛhya andhakam śīghram utpapāta vihāyasā rāhuḥ gadām mahā raudrām kṣipram mūrdhni nyapātayat jagrāha su mahā grāhaḥ matsyān iva mahā arṇave sa tena su prahāreṇa vihvalaḥ prāṇi gocaraḥ alātam iva saṃdīptam niśāyām muni sattama bhrāmyamāṇam samālakṣya punar devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ vegam cakruḥ mahā vegāḥ gṛhṇa gṛhṇa iti vādinaḥ ālakṣya su bahūn saṃkhye garjamānaḥ payoda vat abhīkṣṇam bhīma saṃhrādam vāyum dānava yūthapaḥ sa ca api tena vikṣiptaḥ labdha saṃjñaḥ mahā balaḥ vidhāya vegam deva indram upatasthe kṛtāñjaliḥ tatas vāyuḥ ca devāḥ ca sarve eva saha anugāḥ teṣām teṣām ca saṃgrāmaḥ su ghoraḥ samapadyata siṃhānām iva dṛptānām vijane śarabhaiḥ saha tatra kecid vinihatāḥ su prahāreṇa mūrcchitāḥ sādhu sādhu iti bhāṣantaḥ prāṇān ūrdhvam vitatyajuḥ apare danu daitya indrāḥ mudā yuktāḥ mahā balāḥ pareṇa abhyāhatam śūram samarakṣan su putra vat a vikṣatāḥ śitaiḥ śastraiḥ ātmānam garhayanti uta aśastram kecid abhyetya deva daityāḥ mahā balāḥ devāḥ ca na āhatāḥ ye vai na abhighnanti kadācana sādinaḥ sādibhiḥ sārdham rathinaḥ rathibhiḥ saha evam teṣām hi saṃgrāmaḥ devānām dānavaiḥ saha āvartata śatāni aṣṭau varṣāṇi su mahā bhayaḥ abhidudrāva deva indram tiṣṭha tisṭha iti ca abravīt tasya apatata eva atha bhagavān pākaśāsanaḥ jatru deśe śaram ghoram nicakhāna rarāsa ca anubhūya prahāram tam sa daityaḥ bhīma vikramaḥ tomareṇa bibheda āśu kumbha deśe mahā balaḥ anaṅkuśaḥ svam balam hi anivāritaḥ te tathā vadhyamānāḥ tu ādityāḥ daitya dānavaiḥ bhaya arditāḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ palāyante sma sarvaśas tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca vādyāni vividhāni api siṃhanādān ca saṃcakruḥ daitya dānava saṃmatāḥ tat deva sainyam saṃdṛśya daitya dānava yūthapaiḥ vadhyamānam bhṛśam vyāsa vyādhaiḥ iva mṛgān vane timirāriḥ mahā tejāḥ somaḥ praharatām varaḥ tigma varṣmā su śīta arciḥ svayam pavana sārathiḥ somaḥ tu daśabhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ sāyakaiḥ marma bhedibhiḥ vivyādha hṛdaye daityam hiraṇyākṣam mahā asuram moham samāviśat vyāsa krauñcaḥ śattyā eva parvataḥ tam tathā abhisamīkṣya eva ratham yantā saha asuram apovāha mahā māyam dhaneśam nidhayaḥ yathā tatas hāhākṛtam daityaiḥ daivataiḥ sādhu sādhu iti gṛhṇa gṛhṇa iti daityaiḥ ca mā gṛhṇa iti ca daivataiḥ tatas bheryaḥ ca śamkhāḥ ca paṇavāḥ goviṣāṇakāḥ avādyanta surāṇām vai harṣa rāga pravartanāḥ atha andhakaḥ ca tāraḥ ca tārakaḥ namuciḥ tathā vipracittiḥ śaṃvaraḥ ca mahā māyaḥ ca dānavaḥ dhundhuḥ kārtasvanaḥ ca eva rāhuḥ ca eva mahā balaḥ śataketuḥ śatāvartaḥ pulomā vilvalaḥ tathā vātāpī kālanemiḥ ca śatāvartaḥ śatodaraḥ mahāpārśva udaraḥ ca eva musuṇḍaḥ suṇḍaḥ eva ca mārīcaḥ ca subāhuḥ ca śvetakuṇḍaliḥ eva ca vṛṣaparvā atikāyaḥ ca śarabhaḥ siṃhaḥ eva ca prahlādaḥ ca anuhlādaḥ ca śiniḥ bāṣkalaḥ eva ca virocanaḥ baliḥ bāṇaḥ vātāśvaḥ ca mahā balaḥ mayaḥ tārakākṣaḥ ca vidyunmālī prabhākaraḥ dundubhiḥ mahiṣaḥ ca eva ariṣṭaḥ riṣṭaḥ eva ca tathā gaganamūrdhā ca asilomā ca dānavaḥ sūcīlomā tuhuṇḍaḥ ca huṇḍaḥ ca paratāpanaḥ aśvagrīvaḥ sambaraḥ ca tathā anyaḥ kālasaṃvaraḥ śālvaḥ śatabhujaḥ ca eva drumaḥ vyāghraḥ ca dānavaḥ chāyāgrahaḥ ca vikhyātaḥ saiṃhikeyāḥ ca viśrutāḥ hālāhalāḥ ca te sarve bali putrāḥ ca viśrutāḥ tathā maya sutāḥ sarve nivāta kavacāḥ ca ye paulomāḥ kālakeyāḥ ca vipracitti sutāḥ ca ye ete ca anye ca bahuśas daitya dānava saṃmatāḥ mahiṣāḥ iva hastinaḥ śarabham yathā vighnāḥ yadvat kāmāḥ mokṣa āśritam yathā indriya arthāḥ yathā yogam anarthāḥ duḥkhitam yathā nāgāḥ iva garutmānam bhramarāḥ iva pādapam tathā te dānavāḥ sarve pragṛhīta vara āyudhāḥ dudruvuḥ śiśiram devam mahā jalada nisvanāḥ teṣām āpatatām vyāsa timirāriḥ hasan iva udyatāni āyudhāni sma śaraiḥ ciccheda sarvaśas tatas sa tān punar devaḥ sarvān eva ruṣā anvitaḥ hṛdayeṣu śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bibheda ca rarāsa ca tuṣāreṇa ca śītena tārādhipatiḥ avyayaḥ ājaghāna asurān sarvān krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ te śaraiḥ ca vinirbhinnāḥ śītena ca bhṛśa arditāḥ sthitāḥ tatra eva daitya indrāḥ citra paṭṭa arpitāḥ iva candraḥ a api devaḥ samare maṇḍalīkṛta kārmukaḥ nicakhāna śarān aṣṭau mukhe tasya api candramāḥ śara nirbhinna sarva aṅgāḥ citra paṭṭa arpitāḥ iva yathā sa bhagavān devaḥ candramāḥ dānava ardanaḥ hanyamāne mahā māyaḥ samāśvasya tadā asuraḥ hiraṇākṣaḥ diteḥ putraḥ idam āha ruṣā anvitaḥ garutmanaḥ sutam vīram ratha yantāram āhave khageśvara na te lajjā bhavati iha raṇa arṇave kim vakṣyanti asurāḥ sarve daityāḥ ca eva mahā balāḥ rājā asmākam jitaḥ saṃkhya śatrubhiḥ śatru tāpanaḥ jīvita eṣī parityajya bālān asmān durātmavān raṇāt apagataḥ kvāpi dhik mām aśubha kāriṇam kaśyapasya sutaḥ bhūtvā bhrātā daityasya saṃmataḥ agratas sarva daityānām dānavānām tathā eva ca rājā svāmī ca śūraḥ ca nirjitaḥ śatrubhiḥ katham tam eva pakṣam bhajase na mām tvam parirakṣase na aham tava na śaktaḥ a adya śiraḥ kāyāt sa kuṇḍalam khaḍgena anena tīkṣṇena chettum khaga kula adhama atas kṛtvā abhirakṣāmi gaccha muktaḥ asi doṣavān uvāca ślakṣṇayā vācā hiraṇyākṣam mahā asuram mā krudhaḥ dānava śreṣṭha na asmi daitya tava ahitaḥ tadā upavāhitaḥ kṣipram raṇāt rakṣā artham eva hi sūtāḥ śāstra vidaḥ ca eva bruvate dānava īśvara rathinā śastra ghātebhyaḥ rakṣyaḥ yantā yathā priyā aśaktaḥ syāt iti iti evam mayā kṣipram apohitaḥ āśvasya balam ādhāya punar yuddhena daṃśitaḥ ripūn jeṣyasi saṃgrāme tu evam tvam apavāhitaḥ ye hi kāle sma kāle ca āyānti daṃśitāḥ teṣām na asulabhaḥ daitya jayaḥ yuddhe mahātmanām mā śaṅkām kuru daitya indra śape satyena sarvatas aham garutmanaḥ putraḥ devān hitvā asurān śritaḥ tava eva daitya snehena mā śaṅkām tvam kṛthāḥ mayi trāhi kṣipram mahā bāho na śokam kartum arhasi māyām atha samāsthāya dhanuṣā vā balena vā jahi śatrūn mahā rāja mā ruṣantu diteḥ sutāḥ tatas sa tam pariṣvajya pakṣirājam mahā asuraḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa ākāraiḥ dhvājam cicchidatuḥ yudhi tatas lalāṭe vidhvā enam tau devau śaśi pāvakau tayoḥ tat lāghavam dṛṣṭvā hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān āgneyena astra mukhyena śiśiram tat vyaśātayat tuṣāra varṣaṇam dagdhvā tatas māyayā punar sa rāhuṇā tadā tena grasyamānaḥ khageśvaraḥ dānavāḥ hi api te sarve naṣṭe tasmin himāśaye te samudra sama nāditāḥ daitya dānava mahā rathāḥ pravara sādinaḥ āśvasantaḥ yuddha kāṃkṣiṇaḥ daṃṣṭriṇaḥ iva mahā gajāḥ vana samāśritāḥ nakṣatra adhipatim dṛṣṭvā bhagavān havyavāhanaḥ sa śaraiḥ dānava ratham sa sūtam saha vājinam tatas aasya kārmukam divyam śareṇa ānata parvaṇā vijyam cakāra saṃkruddhaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt anye ca dānava śreṣṭhāḥ kuśānum paryavārayan saḥ tadā teṣām dhanūṃṣi ca rathān tathā kavacāni vicitrāṇi śirāṃsi ca vasūttamaḥ dadāha vikṛta ākāraḥ nādayan sarvatas diśaḥ hā hā iti nadatām tatra bhagavān havyavāhanaḥ jihvāḥ dahan babhau vyāsa guhāyām dīpta vat sthitaḥ keṣāṃcid pradahan tāni dānavānām mukhāni saḥ paṅkajāni iva phullāni timirāriḥ mahā prabhaḥ keṣāṃcid tu gaja indrāṇām karān kāñcana bhūṣitān śarān śarāsanān ca eva tathā khaḍga paricchadān te hanyamānāḥ daitya indrāḥ viśastrāḥ duḥkhitāḥ bhṛśam teṣām vahni pradīptānām dahyatām sura vidviṣām hiraṇyākṣaḥ svayam rājā parjanyaḥ samapadyata tam praśāntam tadā ālakṣya vidhuram havyavāhanam vipracittiḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ lalāṭe samavākirat mukhe śarān mahā ghorān nicakhāna mahā asuraḥ uttasthau vāyu vat dhūmaḥ śarīrāt añjana upamaḥ tena dhūmena kham ca eva divam bhūḥ ca eva sarvaśas pūritā mahatā vyāsa na prajñāpayata kiṃcana tena śabdena saṃjñābhiḥ nāma viśrāvaṇaiḥ api āṭim daityāḥ prakurvanta vakaḥ iti eva devatāḥ ca surāḥ iti evam tat vyavartata evaṃbhūtam abhūt yuddham varṣāṇām tu sahasrakam jagat vināśāya jagat hita eṣiṇām sura asurāṇām rudhira ogha nisravam vāyunā abhihitaḥ ca eva agacchat vilayam bhṛśam tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca paṭaha āḍambarāḥ tathā su ghoṣakāḥ ḍiṇḍimāḥ ca bhagnāḥ bheryaḥ ca sarvaśas pūṣā bhagaḥ ca dvau etau aryamā mitraḥ eva ca jayantaḥ marutaḥ ca eva rudra ādityāḥ ca sarvaśas tatra cāmīkara ābhāsam pragṛhya balavat dhanuḥ sa pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ viddhvā hiraṇyākṣam mahā balam aśvān ca ekaikaśas sarvān jahāsa ca nanāda ca śarān āśīviṣa ākārān vyasṛjan vikṛta aśanān abhyadhāvat yamam tūrṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tasya vajreṇa deva indraḥ gadām hema pariṣkṛtām tam viśastram vikavacam kṛtvā te deva sattamāḥ yugapad śastra varṣeṇa tāḍayāmāsuḥ āhave yamaḥ daṇḍena tam mūrdhni śakraḥ vajreṇa ca ahanat vitta daḥ ca eva pāśena varuṇaḥ tathā saḥ daityaḥ tatas utpatya puṇḍasya āsthāya pṛṣṭhatas yamam muṣṭi prahāreṇa puṇḍāt bhūmau apātayat bhrāmayitvā akṣipat dūre naṣṭaḥ tvam iti ca abravīt tatas dhaneśasya punar śivikām kāma gāminīm tatas gajaiḥ gajān nighnat padātīn ca padātibhiḥ ratham rathena ca raṇe hayān ca haya sādibhiḥ sarve devāḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ pranaṣṭāḥ jīvita arthinaḥ pūrveṇa bhagavān indraḥ saha ādityaḥ sa lokapaḥ dakṣiṇena tathā rudrāḥ vasavaḥ ca aśvinau api pratīcīm takṣa rakṣāṃsi piśācāḥ pannagaiḥ saha uttareṇa tathā anye ca prapadyanta yathā mṛgāḥ teṣu bhagneṣu daitya indrāḥ pṛṣṭhatas vikṛta āyudhāḥ tatas muhūrtam te gatvā hiraṇyākṣeṇa vāritāḥ nivṛttāḥ samatiṣṭhanta sarve aamarṣa vaśam gatāḥ athā uvāca tatas kruddhān hiraṇyākṣaḥ hasan iva daitya dānava nāthān tān idam vacana kovidaḥ kim ebhiḥ abalaiḥ adya yuṣmākam daitya dānavāḥ avabaddhaiḥ ca ruddhaiḥ ca mṛta saṃjñaiḥ durātmabhiḥ hatāḥ te na atra saṃdehaḥ yeṣām rājyam idam dhṛtam na eṣām jīvitam adya asti mā tvaradhvam su bāliśāḥ abalān api saṃrabdhān nirāśān jīvita eṣiṇaḥ avadhyā iti balāt ca eva durjayāḥ ca na saṃśayaḥ ca iti uvāca sadā uśanāḥ yat etat rājyam iti āhuḥ prāṇāḥ hi ete mahātmanām sa teṣām harati prāṇān yaḥ teṣām rājyam āharet teṣām adya suraiḥ āpūrayāma sthānāni devānām dānava īśvarāḥ tatas te sa hiraṇyākṣāḥ prāviśan amarāvatīm ratnāni jagṛhuḥ vyāsa vijayam ca avaghoṣayan ārakṣam āmanuḥ tatra cakṣuḥ āptaiḥ ca te a asurāḥ āśvāsayanta paurān ca tathā prakṛtayaḥ ca ha āśīrbhiḥ ca asura śreṣṭham hiraṇyākṣam praṇemire kāryāṇi kṛtvā sarveṣām agacchat varuṇālayam te siṃhanādaiḥ vividhaiḥ ca vādyaiḥ pravalgana āsphoṭita kūjitaiḥ ca mahā asurāḥ dānava rāja siṃham jagmuḥ samantāt parivārya sarve dṛṣṭvā varuṇa putrāḥ te pitrā saha vidudruvuḥ daityāḥ ca api hi te sarve prāpya tat varuṇālayam vyūḍha skandhāḥ vyatiṣṭhanta vyasṛjan tat puram prati dūtam vātāpinam ca eva rājñā preṣitam ūrjitam sa gatvā tām purīm ramyām praviśya ca mahā asuraḥ pauraiḥ su pūjitaḥ vyāsa prāha idam tān su garvitaḥ kaśyapasya sutaḥ śrīmān hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān jitvā sarvān surān saṃkhye ājñāpayati vaḥ sadā yūyam śṛṇuta sarve me ājñām kuruta ca eva hi nārada ādyāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ tam samāsādya daityakam ūcuḥ tam asuram vyāsa sāntva yuktam idam tadā rājā bhojaḥ virāj samrāj bhūpatiḥ kṣatriyaḥ nṛpaḥ sa tvam rājā ca bhojaḥ ca virāj samrāj tathā eva ca bhūpatiḥ kṣatriyaḥ ca eva nṛpaḥ sarva sahaḥ tathā nirjitāḥ su mahā vīryāḥ tvayā devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ kaḥ tvayā sadṛśaḥ loke bāhya ekam rudram īśvaram tvam pātā sarva lokānām hartā sraṣṭā tathā eva ca kaḥ tava ājñām mahā rāja pratihanyāt durātmavān vara daḥ tvam hi bhūtānām asmākam vara daḥ bhava teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā vara daḥ asmi iti saḥ aabravīt ūcuḥ te daitya rājānam tadā vacana kovidāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ na tathā tat bhavet daityaḥ eṣ sa naḥ dīyatām varaḥ mama pratijñā vipra indrāḥ pūrvam eva tapodhanāḥ lokānām sukham edheyam rājā lokasya yadi aham na tathā tat kariṣyāmi yadi aham muni sattamāḥ mithyāpratijñaḥ syām ca aham asatyaḥ ca durātmavān kartāsmi tam tathā sarvam yāce a aham śirasā hi vaḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā ṛṣayaḥ sarve eva te hiraṇyākṣam idam vyāsa punar eva abruvan vibhum ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ pratijñā prabhavet sā yat lokānām suḥkha varjanam tat ca tasmāt na naśyeta brahmaṇaḥ kṛtiḥ avyayā evam tvayā anṛṇa tvam ca brahmaṇaḥ adya kṛtam bhavet teṣām sa vacanam śrutvā ṛṣīn niścitya daitya rāj ye drohāḥ śakra pāśāḥ ca mama ājñā bhaṅga kāriṇaḥ teṣām eva bhavet mṛtyuḥ narakeṣu ca yātanāḥ etat āha tadā rājā te ca api ūcuḥ narādhipam evam astu iti tān ca uktvā yātanā mokṣam ādiśat sa muktvā nārakān sarvān dadau sthānasya rakṣaṇam tatas sa jayam pūjayitvā tu tān dvijān jagāma dhanada āvāsam hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahā balaḥ te tām dhaneśasya purīm mahā balāḥ vinādayantaḥ a andhaka pālitāḥ tadā tathā laṅkām samāsādya dhaneśasya purīm śubhām adūre tasthuḥ uddhūtāḥ sannaddha kavaca āyudhāḥ avasthitān tathā dṛṣṭvā dānavān bala darpitān laṅkā nivāsinaḥ sarve nidhi pālāḥ tathā eva ca nidhayaḥ śaṃkha padma ādyāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ argham ratnāni ca ādāya dānavāya nyavedayan ūcuḥ ca tava daitya indra vayam vaśyāḥ na saṃśayaḥ kiṃkarāḥ ca praśādhi asamān yathāvat dānava īśvara hiraṇyākṣaḥ uvāca mā bhīḥ bhavatu vaḥ yakṣāḥ mama yūyam na saṃśayaḥ ayam rājā hi vaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ prahlādaḥ deva saṃghānām sarveṣām viprabādhanaḥ anyeṣām deva saṃghānām sthānāni āpūrayat punar saṃsthāpya sarva sthāneṣu sthāninaḥ dānava īśvarān bhūrlokam ca akhilam daityaḥ svayam eva anvaśāsata bhūyas ca dhanuḥ ādāya sa śaram sūrya sannibhaḥ daitya indraḥ medinīm prāha mama ātmānam vidarśaya sā bhītā tasya daityasya vepamānā kṛtāñjaliḥ jaya iti uktvā agratas tasthau viṣṇoḥ lakṣmīḥ iva aparā tām mṛgīm iva śārdūlaḥ bhujaṅgīm iva pakṣirāj śārdūlīm siṃhaḥ iva ca siṃhīm śarabha rāj iva haṃsīm kākaḥ iva kṣudraḥ mayūrīm madgu rāj iva tathā tām sa diteḥ putraḥ jagrāha ruṣita ānanaḥ uvāca ca eva saṃrabdhaḥ tām devīm bhaya vihvalām tava aham vasudhe bhartā brahmaṇā prakṛtaḥ śubhe mā anyam patim tvam icchethāḥ rakṣikṣye a aham tatas hi te babaddha nāgapāśaiḥ tām duṣṭām iva yathā aṅganām ārtām rurodha duṣṭaḥ ca kandarām iva vīryavān kiṃkarān nāma daitya indrān sahasrāṇi caturdaśa kṛṣī bale iva kṣetram su niṣpannam samīkṣya ca saṃyujya sva sutam jyeṣṭham dāraiḥ sādhuḥ iva ātmavān yajadhvam dānavāḥ sarve viprān pūjayata iti ca devam ca śūlinam sarve namasyata punar punar na tasyāḥ dhārmikaḥ kaścid daityaḥ vā dānavaḥ rājye abhavat durācāraḥ tasmin rājyam praśāsati oṣadhyaḥ svayam udbhūtāḥ tasmin rājani śāsati vinā kṛṣṭim sambhavanti sarva lokasya sādhikāḥ saḥ eva tāḥ samādāya kṣaram nayati daitya rāj saḥ eva daṇḍikaḥ abhūt ca daṇḍaḥ ca eva saḥ eva hi hiṃsakāḥ na ca tasya āsan na ca api adhārmikāḥ kvacid palvalāni taḍāgāni sarit prasravaṇāni ca na santi tasya rakṣāṃsi na piśācāḥ ca hiṃsriṇaḥ na adhīyate yajante vai eka varṇam abhūt tadā bhṛgavaḥ ye abhavan viprāḥ dānavānām mudā āvahāḥ hṛṣṭa puṣṭam abhūt sarvam vyādhi duḥkha vivarjitam iti skandapurāṇe hiraṇyākṣarājyavarṇanaḥ nāma ṣaṇnavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca dharaṇyām ca eva baddhāyām sukhitāsu prajāsu ca sthānebhyaḥ cyāvitāḥ devāḥ hi apratiṣṭhāḥ mahā balāḥ kim akurvata duḥkha ārttāḥ etat me śaṃsa sarvaśas śṛṇuṣva dharma devānām avasthā yā babhūva ha daitya dānava bhāgānām vaktāraḥ śubha sādhakāḥ yajñe gate ca daitya indrāt devāḥ sarve mṛtāḥ iva abhavan naṣṭa saṃjñāḥ ca manda vīrya parākramāḥ niḥśrīkāḥ ca nirudyogāḥ nirākrandāḥ samutsukāḥ mantra dagdhāḥ yathā sarpāḥ vajra piṣṭāḥ yathā acalāḥ garutmatā abhisandaṣṭāḥ pannagāḥ iva nirviṣāḥ vihīna adbhiḥ yathā vṛkṣāḥ bāndhavaiḥ vā api yoṣitaḥ tathā te daivatāḥ vyāsa hṛta rājyāḥ hṛta śriyaḥ atha devaḥ svayambhūḥ tān jñātvā devān tathāvidhān vimānena arka varṇena provāca idam pitāmahaḥ bho devāḥ naṣṭa saṃjñāḥ stha kimartham duḥkhitāḥ bhṛśam yūyam lokasya kartāraḥ hartāraḥ ca eva sarvaśas svīyam yogam madīyam ca tyaktvā duḥkham mahā balāḥ na tamaḥ bhāskarāt yuktam na somāt uṣṇa tā yathā na agneḥ yathā tuṣāraḥ na amṛtam bhujagāt iva na asādhoḥ sādhu bhāvaḥ ca na kulīnāt aśobhanam tathā na yuktam yuṣmākam idam devāḥ mahātmanām āpatsu na viṣīdanti ye kecid tejasā sthitāḥ te yūyam āpadam prāpya na śokam kartum arhatha mahā yoga bala upetaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ a adya devatāḥ kṣīṇe tapasi daitya indram yuddhe viṣṇuḥ vadhiṣyati te evam brahmaṇā proktāḥ labdha yogāḥ sura īśvarāḥ praṇamya sarva bhūtānām sraṣṭāram idam abruvan hṛtāni naḥ mahā yoga sthānāni diti nandanaiḥ kva tiṣṭhāma vayam brūhi diśa naḥ sthānam avyayam hṛtāni sarva sthānāni yuṣmākam viditam ca me śṛṇudhvam yatra vastavyam yuṣmābhiḥ yoga māyayā yūyam sarve śarīreṣu yogāt viśata sattamāḥ prajānām sarvatas devāḥ tatas vṛttim avāpsyatha teṣām aśita pītaiḥ ca saṃskāraiḥ ca pṛthagvidhaiḥ pṛthivī nāga baddhā api yuṣmān āpyāyayiṣyati te evam uktāḥ devena devāḥ sarve sa vāsavāḥ atha yogāt hiraṇyākṣaḥ prajāsu samavasthitān aham prajāḥ sadā udyuktaḥ rakṣāmi satatam bhayāt kṛtaghnāḥ svāmi ghātinyaḥ duṣpūrāḥ duṣṭa cetasaḥ mama śatrūn imāḥ duṣṭān anna pāna ādibhiḥ sadā āpyāyayanti durvṛttāḥ daṇḍa arhāḥ me tatas tu tāḥ palvalāni taḍāgāni nadīḥ prasravaṇāni ca sarvāṇi eva tadā yogāt aśoṣayata dānavaḥ oṣadhyaḥ a kṛṣṭapacyāḥ ca yāḥ hi āsan tasya suvrata vyanāśayat sa tāḥ ca api vṛkṣa vallīḥ apothayat tat naṣṭa vṛkṣa kṣupa valli pallavam tṛṇa oṣadhī prasravaṇa udaka āśayam sarit taḍāga avaṭa śuṣka pallavam jagat babhau kacchapa pṛṣṭha sannibham praṇaṣṭa varṇa āśrama dharma saṃyamam vinaṣṭa ghoṣa vraja pakṣi mānuṣam dvipa aśva patti ādi gaṇaiḥ vināditam yugānta kālāgnim udagra vat jagat iti skandapurāṇe brahmaṇaḥ vākyam nāma ṣaṇnavatitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ tathābhūtam jagat dṛṣṭvā devāḥ te duḥkha pīḍitāḥ vairājam lokam āsādya bhūyas apaśyan pitāmaham bhagavan hṛta rājyāḥ ca durbalāḥ ca tathā vibho na ca sthānam prapaśyāmaḥ tatra tiṣṭhāma vijvarāḥ teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā bhītānām tridivaukasām kālaḥ tasya abhisamprāptaḥ jīvitānta karaḥ surāḥ tasmāt sarve mayā sārdham yāta viṣṇum prayācata viṣṇuḥ śaktaḥ sa tam daityam jīvitāt cyāvayiṣyati pūrvam hi jāte tasmin tu vāc uvāca aśarīriṇī na ākāśe na api lokeṣu mahātmā ayam bhaviṣyati saḥ eṣa devāḥ daitya īśaḥ mahātmā dhārmikaḥ tadā avadhyaḥ sarva bhūtānām vadhyaḥ duḥkhāt bhaviṣyati vārāham rūpam āsthāya na daivam na api mānuṣam pātāle ca praviśya eva na asau bhūḥ nā api kham hi tat tatas te hṛṣitāḥ sarve praṇamya ca pitāmaham viṣṇum sahiṣṇum jiṣṇum ca dānava ayuta mardanam astuvan vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ praṇamya bahu mānataḥ namaḥ aajitāya devāya vaikuṇṭhāya mahātmane namaḥ ca aditi putrāya nara nārāyaṇāya ca namaḥ vāmana rūpāya kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāya ca namaḥ rāmāya rāmāya datātreyāya vai namaḥ namaḥ sādhyāya vedāya cakriṇe vai namaḥ namaḥ salile tapyamānāya nāga śayyā priyāya ca namaḥ kapila rūpāya mahate puruṣāya ca namaḥ jīmūta rūpāya mahādeva priyāya ca namaḥ rudra ardha rūpāya tathā umā rūpiṇe namaḥ śipiviṣṭāya ca sadā namaḥ śrīvatsa dhāriṇe dhundhumārāya śūrāya madhu kaiṭabha ghātine caturbhujāya kṛṣṇāya ratna kaustubha dhāriṇe namaḥ puruṣa ghātāya gadā khaḍga ugra dhāriṇe vṛṣa rūpāya satatam ādityānām varāya ca cekitānāya dāntāya śauriṇe vṛṣṇi bandhave mura aśvagrīva nāśāya tathā eva a surasūdine namaḥ te śārṅgadhanuṣe saubha śālva vighātnie puruṣāya vareṇyāya namaḥ te śatabāhave tava prasādāt kṛcchram vai tarāmaḥ puruṣottama hṛta rājyāḥ vayam sarve na tvam vetsi mahā bhuja hiraṇyākṣeṇa vaikuṇṭham tam nāśaya mahā bhuja yaḥ idam vaiṣṇavam stotram bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ mṛtaḥ ca sarva lokeṣu varṣa koṭi caturdaśa pūjitaḥ sarva devaiḥ ca modate na atra saṃśayaḥ uvāca sura śārdūlān idam sampūjayan sadā kriyatām martya rūpam me vārāham mām vidhāryatām sarva deva mayam rūpam vārāham nandi vardhanam tena rūpeṇa sarveṣām asmākam deva sattamāḥ udgātā tatra varuṇaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ tatas paśuḥ śamitā aham sura śreṣṭhāḥ yaśaḥ tasya mahā balaḥ harṣa utphulla īkṣaṇāḥ sarve nirīkṣantaḥ parasparam teṣām tat utphulla kuśeśaya prabham vakra īkṣaṇam cārutara avabhāsakam hataḥ sa daityaḥ narasiṃha rūpiṇā yathā purā tasya guruḥ mahā balaḥ iti skandapurāṇe hiraṇyākṣavadhopāyaḥ nāma aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha te sura śārdūlāḥ tasya rūpam pracakrire sapta loka mayam tasya śarīram cakruḥ īśvarāḥ asthīni parvatāḥ sarve nadyaḥ nāḍyaḥ ca tasya tu rudhiram ca abdhayaḥ sapta kapha pitta anilāḥ guṇāḥ purīṣam ca api oṣadhayaḥ dharmaḥ retaḥ kṛtaḥ tu mūtram tasya abhavat meghāḥ vāyavaḥ sapta koṣṭha gāḥ śiraḥ tasya abhavan sādhyāḥ rudraḥ mūrdhānam āsthitaḥ lalāṭe tasya dharmaḥ abhūt nāsikā vāyuḥ ātmavān bhruvoḥ tasya abhavan prāṇāḥ ahorātram ca pakṣa maṇī āsyam tasya agniḥ abhavat vaḍavā mukha saṃsthitā oṣṭhe aabhūt antarikṣam ca dantāḥ ca bhujagāḥ abhavan catvāri astrāṇi daṃṣṭrāḥ ca kṛtāni su mahānti vai astram pāśupatam pūrvam dvitīyam cakram eva ca brahmadaṇḍam tṛtīyam ca caturtham brahmaṇaḥ śiraḥ pravṛttiḥ ca nakhāḥ ca astrāṇi sarvaśas yamadaṇḍaḥ kāladaṇḍaḥ mṛtyudaṇḍaḥ tathā eva ca rudra daṇḍaḥ ca catvāraḥ bāhu pādāḥ kṛtāḥ prabhoḥ udaram tasya bhūtāni mahānti ṛṣi sattama vasavaḥ tasya pārśveṣu tathā dharmaḥ ca pṛṣṭhatas mṛtyuḥ kālaḥ yamaḥ ca eva hasta pāda tala āśritāḥ aśvinau tasya lāṅgūlam pitaraḥ sandhiṣu sthitāḥ niyatiḥ kāla pāśaḥ ca kṛtānta kalahau api vyādhayaḥ ca api ye kecid dṛṣṭim tasya samāśritāḥ yakṣāḥ ca rākṣasāḥ ca eva gandharvāḥ pannagaiḥ saha sarva tvacam samāśritya saṃhatāḥ samavasthitāḥ tathā sarvāṇi chandāṃsi vedāḥ iṣṭayaḥ eva ca romakūpeṣu sarvāṇi tāni tasthuḥ pṛthak pṛthak dānāni niyamāḥ ca eva yamāḥ sarvāḥ ca mātaraḥ sthāna abhimāninaḥ devāḥ paśavaḥ pakṣaṇaḥ ca ha sarve romāṇi tasya āsan varāhasya mahātmanaḥ aṅgulyaḥ tasya pādābhyām veśvedevāḥ abhavan tathā bhṛgavaḥ devāḥ tasya abhavan tadā roma antareṣu ṛṣayaḥ sarveṣu aṅgeṣu saṃsthitāḥ sas bhāti tena rūpeṇa dyām bhuvam ca api saṃspṛśan sa reje tena rūpeṇa dīptimān madhusūdanaḥ niśāyām sampradīptaḥ hi himavān iva parvataḥ tatas tam ṛṣayaḥ sarve tapasā mahatā tadā sa viṣṇuḥ tejasā teṣām ṛṣīṇām parama ojasām samprajajvāla kāla ante nādam kṛtvā ca su mahat cālayānaḥ mahī talam uvāca tān ṛṣīn sarvān hanmi daityam suradviṣam hatvā tam daitya rājam vai siṃham śarabha rāj iva mocayiṣye mahīm vignām praviśya adya rasātalam sva sthāne sthāpayitvā ca dattvā rājyam divaukasām japadhvam vijayāya adya śivāya ca rapodhanāḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ na tasya sadṛśaḥ daityaḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ purā tatas devaḥ tadā vyāsa bhagavān go vṛṣa dhvajaḥ uktaḥ praṇamya deveśaḥ viṣṇum āpyāya prabho bhagavān uvāca tasmin kāle sura īśānāḥ sarve tejaḥ mayam harim tatas brahmā svayam tasya rakṣām cakre mahātmanaḥ rakṣantu tvām vidhātā ca dhātā ca ṛṣi sattama rudraḥ sraṣṭā ca sarveṣām karmāṇi tava yudhyataḥ rasasya adhipatiḥ ca eva sūkṣma rūpaḥ ca rakṣatu sparśa vettā ca yaḥ sūkṣmaḥ nādavān ca mahāmanāḥ rakṣatu tvām mahā yogī bīja adhipatiḥ eva ca bīja adhiṣṭhāna mālaḥ ca cetanāpatiḥ eva ca pravṛtteḥ ca nivṛtteḥ ca kāla vettā ca yaḥ prabhuḥ dharma adharma gatiḥ ca eva kartR̥ṇām phala daḥ prabhuḥ guṇānām vṛtti daḥ yaḥ ca anapekṣaḥ ca karmasu vinā ca karaṇaiḥ yaḥ ca karaṇa artham pravartate sarvajñaḥ sarvagaḥ yaḥ ca adhiṣṭhātā ca yaḥ svayam yena na adhiṣṭhitam kiṃcid kathaṃcid na api vidyate sarvatas pāṇi pāda antaḥ sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukhaḥ aiśvaryam akṣayam yasya sahasra ākṛtayaḥ tathā yaḥ sraṣṭā sarva bhūtānām tattvanām ca mahā yaśāḥ yam sāṃkhyāḥ na abhijānanti yoginaḥ vidita āgamāḥ tuṣṭayaḥ jñātayaḥ nityam māyayā mohayan prajāḥ puruṣa ādīni sarvāṇi yaḥ vyāptaḥ ca na kenacid yena aham sarva lokānām kṛtaḥ pūrvam prajāpatiḥ tvam yajñaḥ ca eva viṣṇuḥ ca yena sṛṣṭāḥ purātana akāma labdhām sarvatra smṛtim ca astre mahāmanāḥ kṛta rakṣaḥ mayā samyak gaccha daityam vināśaya astuvan vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ devāḥ ca bahu mānataḥ sarvāṇi ca jaya iti ūcuḥ bhūtāni vividhāni ca anāhatāḥ tatas vyomni deva dundubhayaḥ śubhāḥ surabhīṇām ca puṣpāṇām varāha upari sarvatas vṛṣṭayaḥ petuḥ atyartham devānām harṣa vardhanāḥ japan jaya āvaham rudram sa yayau varuṇālayam varuṇālayagamanam nāma aṣṭanavatitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ekonaśatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ apaśyat sāgaram ca eva samprāpya atibalaḥ tadā nardamānam yathā megham līyamānam mṛgendra vat maṇḍalaiḥ bahubhiḥ citraiḥ carantam vasudhām tathā pūjayāmāsa devān ca ṛṣayaḥ ye ca saṃgatāḥ vigāhamānaḥ sa krīḍam arṇavam vibabhau vibhuḥ saraḥ su mahat āsādya yathā mattaḥ mahā gajaḥ sampraviśya su dūram ca saḥ aadṛśyaḥ samapadyata bhūmi lekhā āvṛtaḥ sūryaḥ yathā sampūrṇa maṇḍalaḥ tatas ā antar jalam āviśya kṣobhayāṇaḥ mahā arṇavam makarān ca eva śaṅkhān ca tathā eva aśvamukhān api tathā vai pakṣi saṃkāśān mānuṣān api ca aparān ratha cakra prakārān ca siṃha vyāghra mukhān api śarabha ṛkṣa viḍāla āsyān matsyān bahuvidhān tathā bhrāmayan su mahā tejāḥ jagāma su mahā balaḥ kutūhalāt tam āviśya kecid āghrāya ca eva hi daśanti matsyāḥ dīpta āsyāḥ śataśas a atha sahasraśas sa pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya divyam haya śiraḥ śubham kṣaṇāt maināka madhyena gatvā bhogavatīm api varuṇasya purīm gatvā payonāthasya dhīmataḥ parjanyam diggajam prāpya kṛtvā ca api pradakṣiṇam surabhīpuram āsādya gāḥ dṛṣṭvā ca eva su prabhāḥ yāḥ kṣaranti sadā vyāsa sudhām amṛtam eva ca kṣīrodam tat saraḥ divyam phenapāḥ yatra te dvijāḥ pūjitaḥ phenapaiḥ samyak tām rātrim tatra saḥ avasat vāsukeḥ ca puram prāpya takṣakasya ca dhīmataḥ ramyām manojñām divyām ca svargāt api ca tām varām śrutvā ānataḥ ca tam rājā argheṇa samapūjayat tam pūjayānam madhu hā prītyā paramayā yutaḥ bhūyas vayam tvayā sārdham kariṣyāma yadi icchasi tatas visṛjya tam nāgam rasātalam upāgamat apaśyat tam tadā āyāntam hiraṇyākṣa puram prati gātreṣu devān sūkṣmān ca varāhasya anvavaikṣata tejasā ca api viṣṭabdhaḥ durātmā tasya saḥ a asuraḥ āvedayiṣyan tasmai hi hiraṇyākṣāya sa tvaram sa yātu kāmaḥ ditija adhirājam varāha rūpam tam anantam antakam jagāma daityāya sa jīvitāntam yathā anilaḥ pradyuta dāna mālyavān sāgarapraveśaḥ nāma ekonaśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ hiraṇyākṣa pure ghorāḥ tpātāḥ hi abhavan tadā aṭṭālakāḥ viśīryante devatāḥ ca ahasan iva śivāḥ nadanti daityānām gṛheṣu ca sabhāsu ca akasmāt ca abhavat tatra paurāṇām bhairavaḥ ravaḥ pādapāḥ ca vinā vātam patanti unmūlitāḥ bhuvi bhāskaraḥ ca kabandha ābhaḥ yuddham ca api atra dṛśyate saṃlakṣya rājā daityānām asurān idam abravīt hṛta rājyāḥ ca deveśāḥ na te sthāsyanti niṣkriyāḥ nūnam te kiṃcid āśritya kurvanti samaram prati prahlādaḥ uvāca adya rātrau mayā svapne dṛṣṭaḥ a asau nara rūpavān varāha rūpam saṃgatya bhavantam nigṛhītavān hiraṇyākṣaḥ uvāca dṛṣṭavān tat yathātattvam evam etat na saṃśayaḥ tatas sa mām idam prāha bhagavān go vṛṣa dhvajaḥ yaccha imām tvam priyām putra saha yakṣāya su prabhām kṣipram etām prayaccha adya mukuṭam hāram eva ca keyūra aṅgadakam ca eva khaḍgam rucakam eva ca kaṭake śāsanam ca eva dukūlam ca tatas māma bhagavān āha mad samīpe tvayā sadā yat etat hi mayā dṛṣṭam na tat mithyā bhaviṣyati yaḥ aavadhyaḥ sarva bhūtānām balavān ajitaḥ ca ha tvayi prāṇāḥ sthitāḥ sarve daityānām dānavaiḥ saha teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā hirāṇyākṣaḥ mahā asuraḥ prahasya tān idam samyak uvāca vadatām varaḥ sraṣṭā yaḥ sarva bhūtānām dātā hartā tathā eva ca yadi mṛtyuḥ avaśyam me vihitaḥ tena dānavāḥ ayudhyamānam āsīnam etya asau mā vadhiṣyati vīkṣadhvam tat mama sthānam sarve eva asura uttamāḥ yudhyamānam yathā pūrvam na eva mām sa nayiṣyati bāle mṛtyum samāveśya tatas ca ātma antara īkṣaṇam raṇe ripūṇām kadanam kṛtvā ekaḥ ca api anekaśas pṛṣṭham dadyāt punar teṣām mādṛśaḥ dānava īśvarāḥ devāḥ hi anekaśas sarve jitāḥ naṣṭāḥ ca sarvaśas punar ca āyānti na yathā tathā sarve yatāmahe hiraṇyākṣaḥ uvāca amaram devatā jñātvā svam ātmānam su durlabham jīvantaḥ sucireṇa api bhūyaḥ lapsyāmahe vayam rājyam evam vijānantaḥ vipalāyanti nityaśas naṣṭānām api atas a asmākam jīvita āśā na vidyate tasyām asatyām paśyāma yat prāptam tat hi naḥ varam mā kṛthāḥ nāśane buddhim yuddhe buddhiḥ sthitā mama su yuddhena raṇe prāṇāḥ yāntu mā klība vat hi naḥ teṣām evam tu vadatām sabhāyām sura vidviṣām vega svāsa abhisaṃrabdhaḥ dānavaḥ pratyadṛśyata tadā sa baddha muṣṭiḥ ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ vilokayan vegena niḥśvasan gatvā dvāri dvāḥstham abhāṣata dānavaḥ uvāca āvedaya sabhāpāla rājñe prāptaḥ svayam sāgara ārakṣikaḥ kṣipram akālam śīghram ucyate tatas prahasya tam dvāḥsthaḥ sabhāpālaḥ tam na iha siṃhaḥ coraḥ vā na anyaḥ śvāpadaḥ iti api na gāvaḥ paśavaḥ a anye vā bhayam tyaja samāśvasa kruddhaḥ śabdam tadā cakre mahāntam nādayan diśaḥ te tadā vyāsa rājānam dānava īśvaram ūcuḥ eṣa kim api adya dṛṣṭam kathayate a asuraḥ sa rājan samyak āśvāsya daityam enam mahā yaśaḥ dānavānām hita arthāya pṛcchasva diti nandana teṣām sa rājā vipra indra dānavānām mahā balaḥ śrutvā tam dānavam vyāsaḥ idam vacanam abravīt brūhi sarvam yathādṛṣṭam samāśvasya tathātatham tatas sa dānavaḥ vyāsa rājānam vigata jvaraḥ nityam jayatu naḥ rājā dānavānām sukha āvahaḥ naśyantu vidviṣaḥ sarve ye a asmākam ahita āvahāḥ aham tava ājñayā sarvam vicarāmi dine dine sāgara antam mahā rāja puruṣaiḥ saha saṃgataḥ meru śṛṅga pratīkāśam jvalantam iva pāvakam tasya gāteṣu dṛśyante sūkṣma rūpa dharāḥ sthitāḥ sarve surāḥ mahā rāja ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ mahā balaḥ tvam rāja indra devānām bhaya daḥ sadā na dṛṣṭaḥ na śrutaḥ vā api vapuṣā daitya puṃgava aham tena āhataḥ dṛṣṭyā nyapatam bhū tale bhṛśam srasta hāra ambaraḥ bhītaḥ kuliśena iva tāḍitaḥ ye mama anucarāḥ ca āsan dānavāḥ bhīma vikramāḥ cālayan vasudhām sarvām kṣobhayan sāgarān tathā prahlādaḥ uvāca yādṛśam tat varāhasya tasya rūpam mayā śrutam sarva deva mayam rājan varāhaḥ a aprākṛtaḥ mataḥ su vyaktam brahmaṇā tasya cakra lāṅgala dhāriṇaḥ sarva deva mayam rūpam vārāham idam īhitam bhavān avadhyaḥ sarveṣām devānām dānava īśvara aśaktaiḥ taiḥ iyam māyā sṛṣṭā vai na tat anyathā tasya tat vacanam śrutvā hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān hiraṇyākṣaḥ uvāca yadi eṣa bhrātṛ hantā me iha āyāti durātmavān pūrṇaḥ syāt adya su cirāt yaḥ me hṛdi manorathaḥ adya aham tam durātmānam bhrātṛ hantāram āhave chittvā chittvā kariṣyāmi balim paśupateḥ śubham adya tasya vicitra akṣam śiraḥ kāyāt sa kuṇḍalam utkṛtya daityāḥ dāsyāmi rudrāya paramātmane mayā na āsāditaḥ pūrvam tasmin yuddhe sa keśavaḥ adya aham tam samāsādya neṣyāmi yama sādanam mama eva akārya tām gatvā devāḥ yāsyanti dāsa tām tatas sa dānavān śūrān daityān ca su mahā balān uvāca nāmnā vikhyātān kiṃkarān nāma dānavān daśa tāni sahasrāṇi gacchadhvam tam mahā balāḥ jānīta kaḥ a ayam iti evam tatas yāsyāmi aham svayam te tathā uktāḥ mahāmāyāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ sarve vinirgatāḥ baddha godhā aṅguli trāṇāḥ saṃnaddhāḥ tu padātayaḥ te hema citra ambara hāra sūtrāḥ mahā balāḥ dānava daitya putrāḥ vinādayantaḥ bahudhā ati kopitāḥ yathā eva nāgāḥ sa viṣāḥ viniryayuḥ iti skandapurāṇe kiṃkarādeśanam nāma śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ te vegena daṃśitāḥ daitya dānavāḥ varāham prati saṃjagmuḥ mṛgāḥ siṃham iva āturāḥ te varāha dṛśā tena nīyamāna asura īśvarāḥ ābhānti vyāsa saṃnaddhāḥ prokṣitāḥ paśavaḥ yathā tān nihatya kṛtāntena mṛtyunā ca avapāśitān nināya sa tadā daityān paśūn iva yathā naraḥ gatvā te yojanāni aṣṭau uttīrṇam sāgara ambhasaḥ varāham dadṛśuḥ sarve siṃham kṣudra mṛgāḥ iva visphārayantaḥ cāpāni saṃkruddhāḥ daitya dānavāḥ tān āpatataḥ eva atha nirīkṣya sa samantataḥ varāha indraḥ tadā daityān prāha idam su mahā balaḥ varāhsaḥ uvāca kim mā yūyam diteḥ putrāḥ abhidravatha sarvaśas dūṣayāmi na vaḥ kiṃcid asuhṛd na ca vaḥ hi aham athā evam vādinam daityāḥ varāham tam su vismitāḥ kaḥ tvam varāha rūpī iha tīrtvā sāgaram ūrjitam teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā varāhaḥ mahāmanāḥ uvāca dānavān sarvān tadā jalada nisvanaḥ varāhaḥ a aham yathā daityāḥ tādṛś rūpam ca paśyata pracāra artham imam deśam āgataḥ na saṃśayaḥ hṛta bhāryaḥ a aham anyena vimanāḥ daitya puṃgavāḥ dānavāḥ ūcuḥ na ayam pracāraḥ yuṣmākam daityānām ayam ālayaḥ an ādṛtya katham daityān imam deśam upāgataḥ vayam tvā adya vadhiṣyāmaḥ sarve mṛga kula adhama hatvā ca tvām hi neṣyāmaḥ sarve daitya īśvaram prati tatas te dānavāḥ sarve tam āyudha varaiḥ bhṛśam nijaghnuḥ parvatam yadvat meghāḥ vṛṣṭyā samuddhatāḥ balavān saḥ a api deva ātmā varāhaḥ su mahā balaḥ aparādham cakāra aham na kariṣye karomi vā atha māṃsena kṛtyam vaḥ tatas mām ghnata dānavāḥ yathā prāṇam śitaiḥ śastraiḥ yuṣmattaḥ na ca me bhayam yadā bhavantaḥ sthāsyanti tadā hantāsmi vaḥ sakṛt mattāḥ yūyam surān jitvā tam madam nāśayāmi vaḥ prasārya tasthau udyañcau bhagavān iva śaṃkaraḥ te te a api tad vacanam śrutvā dānavāḥ krodha mūrchitāḥ nijaghnuḥ bhṛśam āyastāḥ nānā śastra astra pāṇayaḥ mṛgaiḥ iva yathā vyāghraḥ śaśaiḥ iva yathā hariḥ sa yadā taiḥ śaraiḥ ca eva gadā muśala paṭṭiśaiḥ bhindipālaiḥ bhuśuṇḍībhiḥ karavālaiḥ ayomukhaiḥ etaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ vadhyamānaḥ mṛgeśvaraḥ adṛśyaḥ vibabhau sarve tadā te harṣitāḥ bhṛśam teṣām ninadatām vyāsa varāhaḥ nandivardhanaḥ śastrakūṭāt viniṣkramya śirāṃsi samapothayat karābhyām caraṇābhyām ca daṃṣṭrābhiḥ ca vyadārayat saṃkṣīṇāḥ bahubhiḥ iva upabhujyamānāḥ dravyāṇām iva nicayāḥ sadā mahāntaḥ atha tān nihatān sarvān varāheṇa abhivīkṣya tu ekaḥ kṛcchrāt vinirmuktaḥ hi aśamakam puram āviśat dvāḥsthaḥ nyavedayat rājñe preritaḥ saḥ udyata āyudhaḥ ye te gatāḥ mṛgendram tam draṣṭum hi asura sattamāḥ mā gāḥ pramādam daitya indra mā avamaṃsthāḥ mṛgeśvaram mā ca kālam pratīkṣadhvam mṛgam tam mā vijānata mahā asau na saṃdehaḥ jetum śakyaḥ na dānavaiḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahā asuraḥ bhṛkuṭī dūṣita mukhaḥ sa dhūmaḥ praṇamya ūcuḥ tadā daityam idam ślakṣṇa pada akṣaram tvam rājā sarva daityānām bhūtānām ca jaya āvahaḥ vayam tam saha devaiḥ ca ye ca tasya abhirakṣiṇaḥ hatvā māṃsam mahā rāja chittvā tasya ānayāmahe ādityānām sa rudrāṇām vasūnām aśvinoḥ api bhṛgūṇām pitṛbhiḥ sārdham tathā eva aṅgirasām api viśvedevāḥ ca ye kecid sādhyāḥ devāḥ tathā eva ca yakṣāṇām rākṣasānām ca piśācānām saha uragaiḥ gandharva pakṣiṇām ca eva manuṣyāṇām ca dānava udyuktānām sa mṛtyūnām lokapālaiḥ saha eva ca śaktāḥ nivāraṇe daityāḥ vadhe ca eva durātmanām nigrahe ca yathākālam svayam mā tvam itas gamaḥ ājñāpayati naḥ yatra rājā svāmī prajā īśvaraḥ tat vayam śirasā sarve kariṣyāma na saṃśayaḥ yat aśaktāḥ vayam kāryam sarve kartum tasya bhavān kartā mā naḥ paśya parān iva mṛga arthe danu daityānām svayam rājā mahā balaḥ tatas sa rājā daityānām sarvān eva samādiśat kāle jaladharān indraḥ yathā bhinnāñjana tviṣaḥ ājñām tasya gṛhītvā eva te daityāḥ mudā anvitāḥ saṃnahyanta mahā kāyāḥ vāhanāni ca bhejire prahlādaḥ ca anuhlādaḥ ca śiniḥ bāṣkalaḥ eva ca baliḥ bāṇaḥ ca vātaḥ ca śambhuḥ kaśyapaḥ eva ca śamabaraḥ ca mahākāyaḥ kālaśambaraḥ eva ca pradīptaḥ ca asilomā ca śilitāḥ ca eva dānavāḥ sarabhaḥ śalabhaḥ ca eva dhundhuḥ mūkaḥ ca dānavaḥ tāraḥ ca tārakaḥ ca eva mayaḥ kālaḥ ca viśrutaḥ ajakaḥ namuciḥ ca eva vyaṃsaḥ kārtasvanaḥ śubhaḥ śakuniḥ vṛṣaparvā ca śataketuḥ mahā ravaḥ marakaḥ ca eva rāhuḥ ca svarbhānuḥ kālaḥ eva ca śālvaḥ drumaḥ ca dvau etau mayūragrīvaḥ eva ca kālanemī meghanādaḥ mahā vīryaḥ sa ca andhakaḥ mahiṣānanda śamakā vāṭiḥ ca bakaḥ eva ca tatas dānava śārdūlāḥ mahā māyāḥ mahā balāḥ jagmuḥ varāham tam vyāsa hantum devāḥ iva asuram hatvā tān kiṃkarān sarvān aśmakam puram āgamat garjamānaḥ yathā meghaḥ yuga ante vṛṣṭi sarjanaḥ sa gatvā tat tadā vyāsa puram loka mayaḥ prabhuḥ apasavyam purā āvṛtya dakṣiṇam dvāram āgamat yaḥ hi bhittvā śataghnīḥ ca kavāṭam kūṭamudgarān kālacakrāṇi yantrāṇi saḥ aavacūrṇayat avyayaḥ atha ājagmuḥ bhṛśa āviṣṭāḥ te dānava mahā rathāḥ śastra varṣeṇa ca ugreṇa chādayantaḥ mṛgeśvaram atha taiḥ tomaraiḥ cakraiḥ bhindī pāpālaiḥ ca tāḍitaḥ dvāram tyaktvā vinirgamya samām bhūmim upāśritaḥ pṛṣṭhatas a anuyayuḥ vyāsa takṣayantaḥ vara āyudhaiḥ sa takṣyamāṇaḥ śara vṛṣṭi tomaraiḥ mahā gadābhiḥ muśalaiḥ ayomukhaiḥ tadā abhiniḥsṛtya diteḥ sutān asau ayodhayat deva gaṇaiḥ adhiṣṭhitaḥ iti skandapurāṇe asurasaṃdeśanam nāma dvyuttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha vyāsa samām bhūmim samprāptān dānava ṛṣabhān uvāca sarvān gambhīram mṛgān siṃhaḥ iva ajane bhavantaḥ dānavāḥ sarve daityāḥ ca su mahā balāḥ mayā mṛgeṇa samare yudhyatām tu punar bhṛśam na lajjā samare a abhyetya yuṣmākam dānava īśvarāḥ atha vā na balam vaḥ mithyā devāḥ hi vaḥ jitāḥ bahavaḥ balavantaḥ ca mṛgaḥ ca aham vanecaraḥ te yūyam yadi manyadhvam śastrāṇi tyajata adhunā mayā ca ekaikaśas sarve yudhyadhvam nyāyam āsthitāḥ evam etat yathā āha ayam mṛgaḥ a asura mahā rathāḥ saṃtyajāma adya śastrāṇi yodhām ekaikaśas tathā prahlādaḥ uvāca abuddhiḥ eṣā daitya indrāḥ yathā āha ayam mṛga adhamaḥ samānānām samaiḥ sārdham etat yuddham praśasyate na mṛgāṇām ca śastrāṇi na bāhu balam iti uta vadhyante ca sadā śastraiḥ eṣa dharmaḥ stām mataḥ te vayam katham utsṛjya svadharmam dānava īśvarāḥ mṛga dharmam samāsthāya yudhyema paśavaḥ yathā mṛga adhamaḥ a ayam durvṛttaḥ a avadhyaḥ na asma ādibhiḥ mā vicāraḥ vaḥ mṛge bhavatu sarvaśas māyām āsthāya duṣṭa ātmā kaḥ sura pāṃsanaḥ asmān vañcayitum daityāḥ kāṅkṣate su durātmavān kva ca śrutam vā dṛṣṭam vā mṛgāṇām asura īśvarāḥ manuṣya vat bāhu yuddham puruṣaiḥ saha saṃyuge eṣa viṣṇuḥ durācāraḥ durātmā daitya kaṇṭakaḥ aśaktaḥ svena vīryeṇa māyām āsthāya saṃsthitaḥ avākiran śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śataśas a atha sahasraśas śuśubhe bhāskara karaiḥ saṃviddhaḥ himavān iva sa vegam balavat kṛtvā vidhunvānaḥ śarān śitān daṃṣṭrābhiḥ ca karābhyām ca nāma śeṣam cakāra ha tam eva deśam āyātaḥ pūrvam yatra abhavat sthitaḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa ākāraiḥ bibhiduḥ indravardhanam bhidyamānaḥ ca bahudhā maṇḍalāni cacāra ha śārdūla vat kadācid ca bhumau ātmānam āhave vitatya sa mahā vīryaḥ tiṣṭhate sāyakān sahan pādena tatas utthāya avakīrya vṛṣaḥ yathā pakṣi vat sa tad ākāśe maṇḍalāni mṛgeśvaraḥ evam bahuvidhān mārgān vicaritvā mahā balaḥ bhrāmayitvā muhūrtam tau saha aśvaiḥ saha sārathī bhūmau utkṣipya cikṣepa babhañja ca punar padā tābhyām sa balavān kruddhaḥ hastābhyām rakta locanaḥ gade jagrāha yat tābhyām balāt eva mṛgeśvaraḥ tatas aacarat maṇḍalāni vividhāni janārdanaḥ gadā viśāradaḥ samyak vicitrāṇi bahūni api ākṣiptam atha vikṣiptam avākṣiptam ca maṇḍalam utkṣiptam atha vikṣiptam visṛṣṭam dhāvitam tathā parāvṛttam nivṛttam ca ardhacandram atha api ca gadā viśāradaḥ samyak bhramitvā maṇḍalāni saḥ vañcayitvā raṇe bhūyas varāham prati dānavau ādhāvitau yathā deśam utpātau vegitau eva muṣṭinā andhakam āhatya vipracittim padā avadhīt nādayānau yathā kāle kṛṣṇau iva balāhakau sa gṛhītaḥ tadā tābhyām mahātmā sura sattamaḥ utpapāta viyat vegāt pakṣirāj iva kāśyapaḥ garutmān iva pakṣi īśaḥ bhakṣa artham gaja kaccahapau abhiyātau mahīm ghorau aśanī khāt cyutau iva rathān vai sarva daityānām cūrṇayāmāsa vīryavān gṛhītvā kūbare kaṃcid saḥ uccikṣepa mahā arṇave kaṃcid padā samāhatya pāṃsu sāyujyam ānayat kaṃcid ratham rathena eva padātim ca padātinā te a api vidrāvitāḥ sarva lajjām paramikām gatāḥ daitya dānava śārdūlāḥ vinivṛttāḥ yathā abalāḥ ekena sarve vijita asura indrāḥ parasparam vīkṣya mukhāni śūrāḥ vrīḍā anvitāḥ te punar eva devam varāha atha te tam mṛgam vyāsa dānavāḥ bhīma garjanāḥ āyudhaiḥ samabhikruddhāḥ saṃtatakṣuḥ tadā bhṛśam te mṛgāḥ iva śārdūlam siṃha potam gajāḥ iva ājaghnuḥ dānavāḥ kruddhāḥ varāham śastra vṛṣṭibhiḥ sa ca api mṛga śārdūlaḥ upaviśya mahā udadhim grasitvā tāni sarvāṇi śastrāṇi sa mahā balaḥ dānavān prati saṃcakre vegam sindhuḥ iva aparaḥ gajān prati yathā siṃhaḥ siṃhān śarabha rāj iva garutmān bhujagān yadvat śārdūlaḥ ca mṛgān iva megha vṛndam yathā vāyuḥ kapotān iva pakṣirāj tathā sa bhagavān vyāsa dānavān prati lokapaḥ āsādya ca sa tān daityān mahā jalada niḥsvanaḥ sarvān vidrāvayāmāsa rudraḥ paśu gaṇān iva kāṃścid padbhyām su saṃkruddhaḥ hastābhyām aparān iti daṃṣṭrābhiḥ ca aparān tatra sa praiṣīt yama sādanam tuṇḍena śambaram bhūmau kālaśambaram eva ca narakam pāda ghātena hayagrīvam ca muṣṭinā urasā namucim ca api mahā māyam ca sa tvaraḥ āhatya āhatya saṃkruddhaḥ pātayāmāsa devapaḥ tān tathā drāvayānam ca garjamānam ca siṃha vat vipracittiḥ varāham tam muṣṭinā urasi atāḍayat vipracittim jaghāna ugram pārśva deśe sa muṣṭinā saḥ āhataḥ varāheṇa varāham krodha mūrchitaḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ tam ghātam varāhaḥ su mahā balaḥ muṣṭinā mūrdhni tam daityam vajra ābhena vyatāḍayat jagrāha padbhyām deveśaḥ drāvamāṇam diteḥ sutam bhrāmayitvā tatas ca enam narditvā ca asakṛt balī srasta hāra ambara dharaḥ cyuta mālya vibhūṣaṇaḥ cūrṇayānaḥ aapatat vyāsa parvata indram iva aśaniḥ mahatā tasya śabdena hiraṇyākṣaḥ svayam tadā vegena āgatya dadṛśe dānava indram diteḥ sutaḥ saḥ a api dānava śārdūlaḥ varāheṇa avapīḍitaḥ tam samāśvāsayat rājā tadā śītena vāriṇā tālavṛntaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ maṇibhiḥ ca diteḥ sutaḥ samāśvasya utthitam ca eva upaviṣṭam varāsane rājā papraccha tam daityam param vismayam āgataḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ uvāca kena adya himavān daitya pṛthivī vā sa sāgarā mahābalena sahasā tulitāḥ viśvakarmaṇā kena adya mandaraḥ srastaḥ mṛtyuḥ kena parājitaḥ kena tvam dānava īśāna kṣiptaḥ kaḥ balavān bhuvi pṛthivyāḥ tulanam yādṛś mandarasya ca cālanam mṛtyoḥ ca maraṇam tādṛś tava idam kṣepaṇam mahat khāpitam triṣu lokeṣu dānava īśvara kathyatām tasya tat vacanam śrutvā dānavaḥ sa mahā balaḥ tam āha dīrgham niḥśvasya nirīkṣya ca punar punar amānuṣam idam rājan atidevam tathā api ca atidaityam ca daitya indra na dṛṣṭam na śrutam kvacid varāhasya balam yādṛś na ca tādṛś kvacid kvacid na hi tulyam prapaśyāmi tasya rājan mahātmanaḥ astraiḥ śastraiḥ ca bahubhiḥ takṣyamāṇasya saṃyuge na ārtiḥ na duḥkham daitya indra na ca saṃjñā prahīyate bhavet tasya abhidaṣṭasya maśakena api anirvṛtiḥ yathā kṣudra mṛgān siṃhaḥ maṇḍūkān iva vā uragaḥ tathā sa kalayāmāsa sarvān daitya indra dānavān na tam mṛgam aham manye na devam na api ca asuram tena asmi muṣṭinā mūrdhni tāḍitaḥ bhū talam gataḥ gṛhītvā sahasā utkṣiptaḥ patitaḥ tvad gṛhu pari dānavānām sa daityānām itareṣām ca dānava na jāne samavasthānam manye te sarvaśas hatāḥ śrutvā etat diti putrāṇām hitam yat tat samācara balavān saḥ daityāḥ vayam martyāḥ sa ca amaraḥ hitvā aśmakam puram sarve samudra stambham āśritāḥ tiṣṭhāma rājan mā yuddham tena sākam punar kṛthāḥ mā avaṃsthāḥ mṛgam daitya mṛgaḥ a asau iti sarvaśas narasiṃhaḥ pūrvam mṛgaḥ tad vinibṛṃhitaḥ yāvat tvam dhriyase daitya dānavānām sukha āvahaḥ tāvat sarve a asurāḥ jīvāḥ bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ mā ruśantu diteḥ putrāḥ danoḥ ca eva su bāliśāḥ apayāma purāt asmāt asura īśvara sarvaśas tasya tat vacanam śrutvā hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān uvāca dānava īśānam bhītam tasmāt mahātmanaḥ asaṃśayam mahātmā asau mṛgaḥ dānava sattama catvāri bhuñjataḥ rājyam gatāni su mahānti me tu samprāptan tāvat devāḥ ca nāśitāḥ bhītaḥ praviśya salilam katham sthāsye bhujaṃga vat mṛga rūpī sa viṣṇuḥ ca vārāham rūpam āsthitaḥ yadi syāt tat ca kṛtyam me dānava īśvara mā bhayam yaḥ me bhayāt parityajya svam rūpam mṛga tām gataḥ tvaratā mṛtyu lokam tu gatvā dānava puṃgava yat aham mrātṛ hantāram dānavānām bhayaṃkaram sūtam tatas samāviśya ratham sajjam acīkarat samāśvāsayitum patnīḥ sa viveśa punar gṛhān sa tatra tābhiḥ kṛta maṅgalaḥ tadā diteḥ sutān tān ca nirīkṣya sarvaśas gṛhāṇa sarvam raṇa yogyam ujjvalam mahā balaḥ śatru nivāraṇa kṣamam sa dhanvī kavacī bhūtvā baddha godhā aṅgulitravān baddha pṛṣṭha iṣudhī ca eva śarī khaḍgī mahā balaḥ hari śmaśruḥ catur daṃṣṭraḥ śaṅku karṇaḥ mahā hanuḥ ājānu bāhuḥ dīrgha akṣaḥ nyagrodha parimaṇḍalaḥ dadhānaḥ jāla hastaḥ ca jāla pādaḥ bāla āditya nibha akṣaḥ ca añjana acala saṃnibhaḥ sa niryayau tadā vyāsa bhṛkuṭī bhūṣita ānanaḥ khaṭvāṅgena ca saṃyuktam dhvajena āditya varcasā divākaraḥ rahtam yadvat bhagavān tejasām patiḥ vibabhau sa tad ārūḍhaḥ ratham tam diti nandanaḥ kirīṭaḥ tu ābabhau tasya śira sthaḥ su mahā dyutiḥ yathā añjana gireḥ śṛṅge dāva agniḥ samavasthitaḥ śaṅkha bherī mṛdaṅgaiḥ ca murajaiḥ veṇubhiḥ tathā vādyamānaiḥ yayau rājā hiraṇyākṣaḥ aaśmakāt purāt agratas pṛṣṭhatas ca eva pārśvayoḥ ubhayoḥ api jagmuḥ sarve a asurāḥ vyāsa bhāskarasya yathā grahāḥ nirgacchamānaḥ ca purāt śakuntān bhaya śaṃsinaḥ āchinat tasya panthānam bhujaṃgaḥ kṛṣṇa dehavān vāmam ca aṅgam sphurati asya śarīrasya muhur muhur visphārayat mahā cāpam rathena abhyapatat balī suvarṇākṣam prati ruṣā vegena eva abhyadhāvata tasya apatata eva āśu dānavaḥ su mahā balaḥ sarva sandhiṣu tīkṣṇa agrān nicakhāna bahūn śarān na cacāla mṛgendraḥ a asau viṣṭabdhaḥ samatiṣṭhata tam stambhitam tadā vyāsa dṛṣṭvā devāḥ mahā balam sa viśalyaḥ tadā devaiḥ kṛtaḥ mṛgapatiḥ mahān grahītum nādayan vyāsa bahudhā viśva rūpa dhṛk yantā ca maṇḍalam kṛtvā bhrāmayāmāsa tam ratham prasārita karam daityaḥ mṛgam tam su mahā balam vijaghnuḥ bhṛśam āyastāḥ bahudhā krodha mūrchitāḥ muktaḥ ca sa tadā utpatya drāvayāṇaḥ diteḥ sutān hiraṇyākṣa ratham tūrṇam abhyadhāvat mahā yaśāḥ tam dhāvantam punar daityaḥ śareṇa ānata parvaṇā vivyādha hṛdaye vyāsa nardamānaḥ yathā ambudaḥ tatas hā hā kṛtam sarvaiḥ sametaiḥ deva puṃgavaiḥ ṛṣayaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca enam bhāskaraḥ ca aprabhaḥ abhavat pratilabhya tadā saṃjñām idam vacanam abravīt āpyāyayadhvam mām kṣipram mūḍhaḥ a aham sarvaśas surāḥ na alpa vīryeṇa śakyaḥ a ayam daityaḥ yodhayitum raṇe tatas te daivatāḥ sarve ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ tasya tu āpyāyamānasya ṛṣibhiḥ daivataiḥ ca ha sa dīpamānaḥ vibabhau mahātmā devaiḥ ca sarvaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ stutaḥ ca iti skandapurāṇe varāha āpyāyane pañcottaraśataḥ adhyāyaḥ sa tathā āpyāyitaḥ vyāsa balavān bhāskara dyutiḥ citram bahu ca śīghram ca maṇḍalāni paribhramat pṛṣṭhatas ca agratas ca api punar gaja vat ācarat punar vyātta ānanaḥ bhūtvā śatrāṇi grasate ripoḥ punar vṛkṣaiḥ śilābhiḥ ca dānavān sa nyasūdayat punar ākāśa gaḥ bhūtvā pakṣirāj iva saḥ aabhramat punar ca sūkṣmam ātmānam kṛtvā tasthau atha agratas evam tam valgamānam ca nardamānam ca dānavaḥ uvāca bhṛkuṭī vaktraḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ hatvā tvā aham pradāsyāmi rudrāya balim ojasā tvayā hataḥ chadmanā me bhrātā jyeṣṭhaḥ durātmanā tasya adya karmaṇaḥ prāptam phalam duṣṭa ātmanaḥ tava tasya tat vacanam śrutvā hiraṇyākṣasya saṃyuge uvāca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ krodhayānaḥ diteḥ sutam yadi tvam gacchase kham vā pātālam vā api atas param hiraṇyākṣaḥ uvāca tvam mayā śara viṣṭabdhaḥ devaiḥ mantraiḥ vimokṣitaḥ baddham ca astreṇa bhūyas tvām pakṣirājaḥ vyamocayat bhūyas tvā aham vadhiṣyāmi siṃhaḥ mṛgam iva ajane mām spraṣṭum api hastena narasya iva hutāśanam tvam loka mayam āsthāya śarīram taiḥ adhiṣṭhitam sarvaiḥ āpyāyitaḥ ca eva saṃyuge mām upāgataḥ na ca mām tvam tathā api adya śaktaḥ siṃham yathā mṛgaḥ yaḥ syāt kulīnaḥ vidvān vā satām mārge ca saṃsthitaḥ saḥ ā anena eva jitam matvā ātmānam saṃyugam tyajet ete siddhāḥ prapaśyantu cāraṇāḥ ca sahasraśas āvayoḥ antaram saṃkhye bahudhā yudhyamānayoḥ evam uktvā hiraṇyākṣaḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ saḥ aatha tena ardyamānaḥ a api varāhaḥ su mahā balaḥ gṛhītvā kūbare ca api ākṣipya utkṣipya vegavat sa aśvam sa sārathim devaḥ cikṣepa ca rarāsa ca tasya tu ākṣepa vikṣepaiḥ chinna yoktrāḥ ca te hayāḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ ratham tyaktvā padātiḥ dhanuṣā tadā mṛgendram mohana astreṇa balavān abhyatāḍayat devaiḥ mantra prabhāveṇa naṣṭa mohaḥ kṛtaḥ punar vṛkṣam utpāṭya vegena daityam mūrdhni vyatāḍayat dhanuḥ papāta vegena hasta āvāpaḥ ca pañcakaḥ tatas hā hā kṛtam daityaiḥ dānavaiḥ ca su duḥkhitaiḥ śastraiḥ ca bahubhiḥ kruddhāḥ varāham samatāḍayan mukham sarvāṇi śastrāṇi jagrāsa ca rarāsa ca tat tathā vikṛtam dṛṣṭvā hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān śūlam jagrāha saṃkruddhaḥ kṛtvā rudrāya vai namaḥ tam āpatantam bahudhā nadantam jvālāḥ sphuliṅgāḥ ca samudgirantam dṛṣṭvā surāḥ siddha gaṇāḥ ca sarve hā hā iti cakruḥ bhaya mūḍha cittāḥ iti skandapurāṇe triśūla ākṣepaṇe ṣaḍuttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ tam āpatantam vegena na śūlam dṛṣṭavān mṛgaḥ alakṣitena tena asau śūlena aditinandanaḥ tatas hā hā kṛtam bhūtaiḥ adṛśyaiḥ muni sattama udvelāḥ sāgarāḥ ca āsan bhāskaraḥ ca aprabhaḥ abhavat ulkāḥ petuḥ ca sarvatra mlāna mālyāḥ surāḥ abhavan grahāṇām abhavat yuddham vimānāni ca petire mahādevam namaskṛtya brahmā saṃsmāra tam tadā mahādevam namaskṛtya varāhaḥ ca udatiṣṭhata tejaḥ māheśvaram divyam viveśa madhusūdanam saḥ upyāyita tanuḥ tena śūlam niṣkṛṣya mādhavaḥ sahasā anala saṃkāśaḥ babhūva sa mahā balaḥ jaghāna hṛdaye kruddhaḥ krauñcam śaktyā yathā guhaḥ madhye bhinnam sa tat śūlam niṣkṛṣya ca visṛjya ca khaḍgam niṣkṛṣya vegena varāham mūrdhni atāḍayat apahasta prahāreṇa khaḍgam hastāt apātayat akurvātām tatas yuddham niyuddha kuśalau ubhau śarabhau iva ca āyastau śārdūlau iva nirghṛṇau aṅkuśaiḥ hasta yoktraiḥ ca kṣepaṇaiḥ apasarpaṇaiḥ maṇlaiḥ ca punar citraiḥ karṣaṇaiḥ apakarṣaṇaiḥ ahāni daśa ca aṣṭau ca tathā anyāni caturdaśa anyat sahasram eva āsīt varṣāṇām tat ca mānuṣam tam hīyamānam ālakṣya daitya adhipatim ūrjitam ākāśe vāc uvāca idam aśarīrā ati su svanā śṛṇu deva varāha idam śrutvā ca eva samācara aśakyaḥ a ayam tvayā hi evam hantum daityaḥ mahā balaḥ abalaḥ kṛtaḥ krūraḥ dhruvam māheśvareṇa hi māheśvareṇa vaikuṇṭha tatas mṛtyum avāpsyati mumoca daitya rājānam pādena āhatya vakṣasi bhukta muktaḥ yathā sūryaḥ saiṃhikeyena rāhuṇā bhagavān api dīpyantam śriyā daityam samīkṣya tam tatas sarvāḥ diśaḥ vyāsa vahni kuṇḍā nibhāḥ babhuḥ śabdaḥ ca mu mahān āsīt yuga anta ambuda saṃnibhaḥ siddhāḥ petuḥ ca medinyām devān ca bhayam āviśat sāgarāḥ vyaśuṣyanta vineśuḥ nāga pakṣiṇaḥ daityāḥ ca dānavāḥ ca eva sarve te viviśuḥ bilam karam āgāt varāhasya śātāśani sama svanam tadā āpatantam saṃvīkṣya sarva bhūtāni sarvatas tad yuga anta anala prakhyam kṣura antam sphoṭayan nabhaḥ jagāma dānavam kṣipram diśaḥ sarvāḥ dahan iva tat sa dānava śārdūlaḥ upayāntam mahā ravam atha māyām samasṛjat taijasīm pārthivīm api vāyavīm vāruṇīm ca eva tāmasīm indriya ātmikām tathā evā utpātakīm māyām mohanīm stambhanīm api nivartanīm jambhanīm ca cakāra anyāḥ ca saṃyuge tāḥ sarvāḥ tat tadā cakram nāśayat bhīma nādavat gatvā tasya śiraḥ kāyāt unmamātha yathā acalam daṃṣṭrālam ati udbhuta bhīma nādam papāta meroḥ iva śṛṅgam uccam rathāṅgu niṣpīta vapuḥ virāgam na bhāti tad vaktram atīva dīnam niśā prahāṇe vinivṛtta raśmi bimbam yathā candramasaḥ viśobham tad danta paṅkti chadam ādaśānam muhur ca dantān api saṃdaśānam papāta daityasya śiraḥ nikṛttam yathā gireḥ śṛṅgam atipravṛddham ṛṣayaḥ ca tapaḥ yuktāḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭyaḥ ca petire deva dundubhayaḥ neduḥ adṛśyāḥ su mahā svanāḥ bhūtānām ca abhavat śarma prakṛti stham jagat babhau jagāma adṛśyatām cakram tatas svastāḥ abhavan surāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca eva lokāḥ ca daityam tam dadṛśuḥ hatam asurāḥ api te sarve pura dvārāṇi sarvaśas pidhāya yatnāt saṃnaddhāḥ prākareṣu avatasthire te bhītāḥ mukta keśāḥ ca rajaḥ dhvastāḥ bhaya arditāḥ jīvitam samparīpsantaḥ sthitāḥ prākāra gāḥ tadā bhagavān api dīpta arciḥ haviṣā iddhaḥ iva analaḥ bhīṣayānaḥ a asurān sarvān pṛthivīm anvacinvata sa bahis sarvatas a anviṣya utpāṭya ca mahīruhān praṇaṣṭām iva gām gopaḥ samantāt anvacinvata parvatān sa tadā utpāṭya daitya udyānāni acūrṇayat ārāmān sa taḍāgāni babhañja ca rarāsa ca tatas dakṣiṇatas gatvā muhūrtam deva sattamaḥ śaṅkham parvatam āsādya nanarda jaladaḥ yathā asurāḥ hi api te bhītāḥ prākāra antara saṃsthitāḥ avaikṣanta mṛgendram tam dhāvantam sarvatodiśaḥ apaśyat pṛthivīm baddhām rakṣyamāṇām ca dānavaiḥ sāgara ambhasi vikṣipya śaṅkham tam parvata uttamam avadhīt dānavān sarvān medinyāḥ ye a abhirakṣiṇaḥ tatas vidrāvya nāga indrān pragṛhya pṛthivīm balāt jagāma daityān saṃdhṛṣya ratnāni ādāya sarvaśas sa tām daṃṣṭra aṅkure lagnām vahan bhāti mṛgeśvaraḥ viṣāṇa lagnām lambavantīm mṛṇālīm gaja rāj iva sa tām sāgara madhyena vahan bhāti mṛgeśvaraḥ varāha rūpī kāla ante brahmā iva vasudhām purā sva sthāne sthāpayāmāsa mahīm tām punar eva hi tatas śakrāya lokān trīn adāt sa madhusūdanaḥ uvāca rājā tvam naḥ aadya mitram ca aham tava anagha teṣām api vadham ghoram kariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ tatas tam ṛṣayaḥ sarve devatāḥ ca sa vāsavāḥ ūcuḥ svām mūrtim āsthāya yathā pūrvam tathā bhava varāhaḥ uvāca iyam mūrtiḥ mayā devāḥ prāptā parama varcasā na ca anayā ratiḥ kācid prāptā me sadṛśī bhuvi saḥ a aham kaṃcid vihṛtya iha kālam mūrtyā anayā sukham tasya tat vacanam śrutvā sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ pradakṣiṇam upāvṛtya jagmuḥ sthānāni sarvaśas tasya tatra upatiṣṭhanta mṛgyaḥ bhūtvā sahasraśas vaidikyaḥ a apsarasaḥ śubhrāḥ tābhiḥ saha rarāma saḥ reme mattaḥ mahā nāgaḥ yathā araṇye kareṇubhiḥ sa siṃhaḥ iva siṃhībhiḥ sārdūlaḥ iva ca unnadanan rarāma sāgara anūpe airāvataḥ iva aparaḥ ramamāṇasya siddhāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ puṣpāṇām rucirāḥ vṛṣṭīḥ pātayanti viyat sthitāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca apare nityam cakruḥ ca enam pradakṣiṇam ramayantaḥ varāham tam devāḥ ca indra purogamāḥ yakṣāḥ puṇya jananāḥ ye ca tathā deva janāḥ ca ye yātudhānāḥ ca ye kecid brahmadhānāḥ ca sarvaśas manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ ca eva ṛṣayaḥ ca eva sarvaśas rājanyaḥ kṣatriyāḥ sarve nikāyāḥ ca eva sarvaśas bahu āścarya samākīrṇam bahu ālakṣyam sadā eva ca evam tasya abhavat vyāsa varāhasya mahātmanaḥ tasya utsaḥ ūvaḥ a asau ṛṣi saṃgha juṣṭaḥ sadā suraiḥ siddha janaiḥ ca juṣṭaḥ iti skandapurāṇe varāhotsave aṣṭottaraśataḥ adhyāyaḥ bhāryāyām citralekhāyām vṛkaḥ nāma abhavat sutaḥ sa vṛkaḥ balavān nityam vicaran pṛthivīm imām nardamānaḥ aavadhīt loke bhūtāni śataśas mahān athā āsasāda śaila indram himavantam mahā girim gaurīkūṭa samīpe ca kārttikeya ālayam śubham nādayānaḥ drumān śubhrān ratna hema vibhūṣitān śilāmaṇi mayāḥ śubhrāḥ śātakumbha mayāḥ tathā haritāl samayāḥ ca anyāḥ tathā mānaḥśilā upālān utpāṭya utpāṭya vegena babhañja rūṣitaḥ yathā babhañja tat vanam śubhram kārttikeyasya dhīmataḥ skandasya gaṇapaḥ śūraḥ nirjagāma sa mandirāt sa tam dṛṣṭvā mahā kāyam taruṇam priya darśanam uvāca vacanam hṛṣṭaḥ koka vaktraḥ hasan iva na jānīṣe kim etat tvam skandasya su mahātmanaḥ kṛtam dayitam atyartham gaṇaiḥ ca api su pūjitam kumāraḥ mandaram yātaḥ sarvaiḥ saha gaṇeśvaraiḥ rakṣā artham mām iha sthāpya vārayāmi tatas hi te tuṣṭaḥ tava rūpeṇa balena vapuṣā tathā vakṣye devam ca tam samyak tvad artham śūkara īśvara tasya tat vacanam śrutvā vṛkaḥ saṃrakta locanaḥ nāma avaśeṣam etat vaḥ kartāham vanam antatas tatas sa vṛkṣam utpāṭya haimam vaidūrya pallavam koka vaktrāya cikṣepa nanāda ca yathā vṛṣaḥ vṛkam tam tena saṃkruddhaḥ śirasi abhijaghāna ha sa tena su prahāreṇa bhramitvā maṇḍalam mṛgaḥ papāta bhūmau niḥsaṃjñaḥ yathā śakra dhvajaḥ mahān tatas tam patitam dṛṣṭvā koka āsyaḥ prahasan tadā tam baddham patitam dṛṣṭvā sahāyāḥ tasya te mṛgāḥ pradrutā sahasā sarve bhaya ārtāḥ jīvita eṣiṇaḥ atha agāt tena kālena gaṇapaiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtaḥ kārttikeyaḥ mayūreṇa kūjamānena sa anugaḥ vṛkam ca darśayāmāsa pāśaiḥ baddham mahā balam bhagavan varāha rūpasya sutaḥ śrīmān vṛkaḥ kila hiraṇyākṣaḥ hataḥ yena dānavaḥ deva kaṇṭakaḥ babhañja ayam su duṣṭa ātmā sahitaḥ ā aanyaiḥ vanam tava na ayam śakyaḥ mayā adya iha moktum mṛga kula adhamaḥ devaḥ mām vakṣyate vyaktam skandaḥ bhītaḥ na saṃśayaḥ uktaḥ gataḥ ca aham adya sthāṇunā paramātmanā mā kṣamethāḥ varāhasya tanum tvā asau hvayet yadi iyam ca mama tena adya śaktiḥ dattā ati bhāsvarā saṃvarttikā iti vikhyātā sarva astra bala nāśanī saḥ aayam durātmā durvṛttaḥ sarva loka prabādhakaḥ gṛhyatām vadhyatām ca eva kṣipram āviṣkṛtam balāt tatas enam bahis sarve skandasya gaṇanāyakāḥ baddhvā bahuvidhaiḥ pāśaiḥ yātayanta sahasraśas sa yātyamānaḥ duḥkha ārtaḥ vilalāpa yathā naraḥ niraya sthaḥ durācāraḥ karmabhiḥ svaiḥ su pāśitaḥ tam yātyamānam saṃdṛśya nāradaḥ su mahā tapāḥ eṣa putraḥ vṛkaḥ tubhyam baddhaḥ pāśaiḥ anekaśas yātyate kārttikeyasya kiṃkaraiḥ duṣkṛtī yathā karoti saṃnatim skandaḥ bāla bhāvāt ca roṣataḥ nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā varāhaḥ nandivardhanaḥ jīmūtaḥ iva kāla ante nanāda rūṣita ānanaḥ utthāya ca āsanāt devaḥ sahasā eva unnirīkṣaṇaḥ sa kampayan mahīm sarvām stūyamānaḥ mahātmabhiḥ utpātān utthitān paśyan jagāma a vinivāritaḥ daṃṣṭrā ca vṛkṣam āpatya papāta dharaṇī tale vāyavaḥ pratilomāḥ ca urasā ca apatat bhuvi snehaḥ ca asya priyām smṛtvā tadā atyartham ajāyata etān ca anyān su bahuśas utpātān bhaya sūcakān an ādṛtya mṛgendraḥ jagāma eva mahā balaḥ rakṣaḥ gaṇaiḥ cāraṇa kiṃnaraiḥ ca jagāma gaurīśikharam mahātmā rarāma gaṇapaiḥ sārdham krīḍanaiḥ bahuṣu śubhaiḥ ānayāmāsa tam ca api varāhasya sutam prabhuḥ utsṛṣṭam dhāvamānam ca punar jagrāha vegitam śilām gṛhītvā mahatīm saṃkruddhaḥ aantaka saṃnibhaḥ tām āpatantīm bahudhā nadantīm vihāyasā mṛtyu samāna rūpām jagrāha vegena mahā ati vegām kokāmukhaḥ prajvalitām iva ulkām vināyakasya avyagrāya gaṇāya vyasṛjat prabhuḥ tad antaka pratīkāśam cakram sarva surāri ham tat tadā anarcitam tena cakram dānavaghātinā vṛkṣam utpāṭya vegena kumāram abhijaghnivān a gaṇya tam prahāram tu bhagavān anala ātmajaḥ śaktim saṃvarttikām krodhāt cikṣepa ca nanāda ca sā dahantī iva tejāṃsi nadantī bahudhā tadā hantum varāham prayayau śaktiḥ divyaḥ iva āśugaḥ tām āpamantīm vegena bhagavān nandivardhanaḥ tāni sā bhasmasāt kṛtvā śaktiḥ saṃvarttikā śubhā viveśa hṛdayam tasya kāminī iva dṛḍham priyā saḥ a anyat deham samāsthāya paurāṇam sura sattamaḥ tatra apaśyat mahādevam jaṭā mukuṭa dhāriṇam bhadrapīṭhe samāsīnam kāñcane maṇi mūṣaṇe bhrājamānam śriyā atyartham pārvatyā pārśva sṃsthayā gaṇaiḥ ca vividha ākāraiḥ bahubhiḥ kāmarūpibhiḥ tam dṛṣṭvā śaṃkaram viṣṇuḥ prasannena antarātmanā vārāham rūpam āsthāya tvad tejaḥ bṛṃhitena me raṇe vikramya bhagavan hiraṇyākṣaḥ niṣūditaḥ tvam deva kāraṇam nityam sambhūteḥ pralayasya ca tvayi kruddhe vināśaḥ naḥ bhavitā na atra saṃśayaḥ stuvantam evam bhagavān viṣṇum candra ardha śekharaḥ sahasra sūrya tejaskaḥ prītaḥ provāca śaṃkaraḥ viṣṇuḥ uvāca yat tat pāpa haram divyam vratam ādeṣṭum arhasi yat āśritya vayam sarve sa śakrāḥ sārvakāmikam yuddhe jeṣyāma daiteyān duḥkha śoka vivarjitāḥ vratam pāśupatam divyam yena kāmān avāpsyatha iti uktvā devadeveśaḥ devānām hita kāmyayā atha himagiri tulya cāru mūrti vṛṣabha varam bhagavān tadā adhirūḍhaḥ sura gaṇa sahitaḥ prabhuḥ sumerum vratam upadeṣṭu manāḥ jagāma śarvaḥ iti skandapurāṇe hiraṇyākṣa vadhe daśottaraśataḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca gate divam mahādeve devīm giri vara ātmajām sāvitrī deva mātā ca gāyatrī durgayā saha śrīḥ kīrtiḥ ca eva lakṣmīḥ ca dhṛtiḥ prajñā tathā eva ca khyātiḥ ditiḥ danuḥ ca eva aditiḥ siṃhikā khaśā rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī tathā eva anumatiḥ śubhā gaṅgā sarasvatī ca eva tathā anyāḥ saritaḥ śubhāḥ ṛṣīṇām ca eva yāḥ patnyaḥ devānām yakṣa rakṣasām uragāṇām khagānām ca gandharvāṇām tathā eva ca etāḥ sarvāḥ tathā āgamya namaskṛtya ca pārvatīm papracchuḥ sarva dharma jñāḥ dharmam dharma artha saṃśritāḥ kena dharmeṇa deveśe tapasā vā śubha ānane mumahat prāpyate puṇyam kim ca akṣayyam prakīrtitam tu hita arthāya lokānām ca eva suvratāḥ kathayiṣyāmi aham dharmam yathāvat anupūrvaśas anna dānāt param dānam na eva kiṃcid hi vidyate sa sarva kāmān āpnoti pūjyate ca triviṣṭape yadi mānuṣyam āyāti kadācid sa nara uttamaḥ dhana dhānya samākīrṇaḥ kulīnaḥ syāt ca rūpavān kadācid api yaḥ dadyāt annam saṃskṛtam annam pradadyāt yaḥ devyaḥ yādṛśam tādṛśam śubhāḥ tasya api narake ghore yātyamānasya rākṣasaiḥ upatiṣṭheta bahudhā tṛptiḥ yena asya jāyate yadi mānuṣyam āyāti kadācid sa naraḥ punar anna īm evam viśiṣṭam hi tasmāt na paramam bhuvi saṃvatasaraḥ ca yajñaḥ a asau yajñe sarvam pratiṣṭhitam tasmāt bhavanti bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca tasmāt annam viśiṣṭham tu sarvebhyaḥ iti vai śrutiḥ anna dānāt param dānam na eva kiṃcid hi vidyate sugandhāḥ śītalāḥ ca apaḥ rasaiḥ divyaiḥ samanvitāḥ vimānam sūrya saṃkāśam apsaraḥ gaṇa nāditam tatra asau ayutāni aṣṭau uṣitvā deva vat sukhī kule mahati asaṃkīrṇaḥ jāyate dhana dhānyavān āpām tu pūrṇam yaḥ bhāṇḍam brāhmaṇāya prayacchati rasāḥ tasya upatiṣṭhanti pūjyate ca divam gataḥ bhājanāni ca yaḥ dadyāt su pūrṇāni śubha ānanāḥ bhājanam syāt sa bhogānām tārayet ca pitR̥n bhayāt taḍāgam yaḥ tu kurvīta apām devyaḥ samṛddhimat prapitāmahān ca lokeṣu kamikeṣu vihaṃgamaḥ carate deva vat devyaḥ varṣa ayuta śātāni ṣaḍ bhogī bhavati bhogānām rājamātraḥ ca jāyate dātā yajyā ca balavān su prabhaḥ priya darśanaḥ avaṭam yaḥ naraḥ kuryāt apām pūrṇam śuci smitāḥ aṣṭābhiḥ ca vicitrābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam hiraṇyam hema bhūmim vā tilān ratnāni vā api yaḥ pradadyāt sarva bhūtebhyaḥ tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu tatas cyutaḥ ca dharma ātmā sarva kāma samṛddhimān yaḥ tu vṛkṣam prakurute chāyā puṣpa phala upagam sa yat phalam avāpnoti tat śṛṇudhvam mahā prabhāḥ yāvat vṛkṣasya puṣpāṇi upayuñjanti dehinaḥ tāvat varṣa sahasrāṇi tārayitvā pitR̥n api soma lokam samāsādya saḥ a amṛtam phalam āpnuyāt phalāni yaḥ prayaccheta brāhmaṇebhyaḥ samāhitaḥ phalānām sa tu bhāgī syāt bahūnām subhagaḥ ca ha saḥ a apsaraḥ śata saṃkīrṇe vimāne divi modate rājatam yaḥ prayaccheta viprebhyaḥ bhājanam śubhāḥ tāmram yaḥ bhājanam dadyāt brāhmaṇebhyaḥ viśeṣataḥ sarva koṭīḥ sa tatra uṣya catasraḥ tena karmaṇā gṛhamedhī yadā dātā bhogavān ca eva jāyate oṣadhīḥ yaḥ prayaccheta dhānyāni vividhāni ca sa sarva kāma saṃmṛṣṭam soma lokam samaśnute sa tu kṣetrapatiḥ bhūtvā prājāpatyam samaśnute bahūni abda sahasrāṇi carate kāma rūpavān yat hi mānuṣyam āyāti sa naraḥ kāla paryayāt yaḥ tu vastram prayaccheta brāhmaṇāya mahā yaśāḥ sa lokam prāpya vairājam varṣa koṭim sukham vaset āsanam yaḥ prayaccheta saṃvītam brāhmaṇāya vai yaḥ tu śayyām prayaccheta su āstīrṇām nara sattamaḥ sa tu bhāryāḥ priyāḥ devyaḥ bahvīḥ bhaktāḥ samaśnute yaḥ tu kanyām prayaccheta brāhmaṇāya su alaṃkṛtām sa gatvā pitṛ lokam vai varṣa ayuta śatam vaset bharyāḥ prāpnoti bhaktāḥ ca prajāvān ca upajāyate ratham aśvam gajam dāsīm kanyām gṛham atha api ca bhūmim ca yaḥ prayaccheta sa rājā bhuvi jāyate prāpām śubhām taḍāgam vā kūpam vā api su puṣkalam kṛtvā kumbhān su saṃpūrṇān gandha mālyaiḥ alaṃkṛtān bhakṣya bhojyaiḥ supta tṛptān tān tila pātrāṇi dāpayet dakṣiṇām puṣkalām dadyāt tebhyaḥ tām sparśayet tatas āpaḥ śivāḥ ca saumyāḥ ca tarpayantu pitR̥n mama kāma gāḥ kāma dātāraḥ bhavantu pitaraḥ sadā evam dattvā tu tām dhenum punar krītvā ca vai tadā tila pātrāṇi dattvā ca tathā vastra yugam navam suvarṇasya ca sāṃnidhyam phalāni vividhāni ca ghṛtam gāvaḥ prasūyante ghṛtam bhūmyām pratiṣṭhitam ghṛtam agniḥ ca devāḥ ca ghṛtam me saṃpradīyatām yaḥ naraḥ gām prayaccheta sa vatsām kāṃsya dohanīm hema śṛṅgīm rūpya khurām dukūla kṣauma vāsitām śayyā āstaraṇa saṃpannām bahu puṣpa phalaiḥ yutām brāhmaṇān tarpayitvā tu gandha mālyaiḥ alaṃkṛtām dāna kāle tatas tasyāḥ surāḥ gātrāṇi saṃśritāḥ brahmā tasyāḥ sthitaḥ mūrdhni śakraḥ a apānam samāśritaḥ candra ādityau ca netra sthau ghrāṇe vāyuḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ mukham tasyāḥ śritaḥ vahniḥ jihvām somaḥ svayam prabhuḥ karṇayoḥ tu diśaḥ sarvāḥ sirāḥ rudrāḥ samāśritāḥ pādayoḥ lokapālāḥ ca sarve aasthīni ca parvatāḥ samudrāḥ sapta jaṭhare grīvāyām tapanāḥ śritāḥ sāsnām gaṅgā sarit śreṣṭhā pārśvayoḥ vasavaḥ śubhāḥ prajāpatiḥ upasthaḥ ca mūtram tīrthāni sarvaśas purīṣam śrīḥ abhūt tasyāḥ nāgāḥ ca astrāṇi sarvaśas sādhyāḥ viśve a atha lokāḥ ca puccham āśritya saṃsthitāḥ mantrāḥ yajñāḥ ca dānāni yamāḥ ca ṛṣibhiḥ saha nakṣatrāṇi grahāḥ ca eva tārā rūpāṇi yāni ca gāyatrī ca eva triṣṭubh ca jagatī paṅktiḥ eva ca anuṣṭubh ṛc yajuḥ ca eva sāmāni ātharvaṇam tathā dharmaḥ tārāyaṇaḥ ca eva bhūtāni saritaḥ tathā romakūpāni saṃśritya tasyāḥ devāḥ vyavasthitāḥ yakṣāḥ ca rākṣasāḥ ca eva piśācāḥ pakṣibhiḥ saha yajñāḥ ca dakṣiṇāḥ ca eva tathā ca apsarasaḥ śubhāḥ gandharvāḥ ca mahātmānaḥ ye ca anye tasyāḥ viṣāṇayoḥ vyāsa
