nāmataḥ ca yaḥ ambarīvān ca vikhyātaḥ ketumān api ca aparaḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ ṛṣayaḥ devatāḥ tathā vimānāni ca sarvāṇi gandharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ jambhakāḥ ṛtavaḥ ca eva nikāyāḥ ca eva sarvaśas teṣām gagana saṃsthānām devānām prekṣatām tadā umāsahāyaḥ deveśaḥ sahasā eva anvadṛśyata taḍit jvalana piṅgena jaṭā bhāreṇa rājatā bhagīratha kva sā gaṅgā pitR̥ṇām tava tāraṇī samāhvaya mahā bāho dhārayiṣye na saṃśayaḥ tatas sa rāja śārdūlaḥ smṛtvā tat brahmaṇaḥ vacaḥ sasmāra saritam vyāsa śirasā prāñjaliḥ nataḥ sā tena manasā āhūtā svar loka nilayā nadī kṣaṇena abhyāyayau devī bhuvar lokam śubha āvahā tam lokam sā samāsādya manaḥ nila javā nadī alaṃcakre mahāvegā sarvam śubha śata araṇiḥ tatas sā tiryak āgamyaḥ ākāśa sthā mahā nadī ākāśagaṅgā saṃjajñe nāmnā oghavatī iti vai ākāśagaṅgā sā bhūyas mahāvegā mahā nadī śivam astu mama iti evam pāpāt ardha pathāt tu sā śivagaṅgā tatas proktā nāmnā śivatarā hi sā kurvatī vipulam śabdam nadī vajra aśani svanam yatas devaiḥ samam dṛṣṭā devagaṅgā tatas smṛtā tām dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ sarve deva lokāḥ ca sarvaśas jepuḥ te sahasā śāntim samprahṛṣṭa tanūruhā teṣām sā japatām vyāsa nadī loka sukha āvahā tām patantīm mahādevaḥ tribhiḥ vegaiḥ mahā javām jaṭā bhāreṇa jagrāha devānām eva saṃnidhau tam jaṭā bhāram āsādya sā tri srotāḥ nirulbaṇā na tasya antam samāsede niruddhā yoga māyayā yasmāt sā bhīta bhītā tu stuvantī patitā tadā sā tu tasmin nipatitā dhṛtā devena māyayā jaṭā randhram vicinvānā uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ pūrṇam sahasram varṣāṇām saṃsthitām tām jaṭāgṛhe devāḥ tām dadṛśuḥ sarve koṭara antargām iva tatas te sahasā devāḥ praṇipatya vṛṣadhvajam ūcuḥ vimanasaḥ vyāsa saritam mā vināśaya teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā dṛṣṭvā rājānam eva ca vidudhāva jaṭā bhāram devadevaḥ dayā mayaḥ te muktāphala saṃkāśāḥ pūrṇa candra aṃśu nirmalāḥ tasmāt śrotāṃsi sapta eva niḥsṛtāni mahānti ca nalinī hrādinī ca eva plāvanī ca eva pūrva gā sītā cakṣuḥ ca sindhuḥ ca tisraḥ tāḥ vai pratīci gāḥ bhāgīrathī iti sā gaṅgā procyate brahma vādibhiḥ niruddhāḥ himavat pāde ratna śṛṅge śiloccaye tām niruddhām tatas vīkṣya viṣaṇṇa vadanaḥ tadā rājā bhagīrathaḥ vyāsa brahmāṇam manasā asmarat tatas sa bhagavān brahmā supratīkam mahāgajam uvāca danta vajrābhyām dāraya enām śiloccayam gaṅgādvāram tu tat proktam su puṇyam ca eva tat smṛtam gajaḥ ca abhimukhaḥ yāvat na atiṣṭhata mahā yaśāḥ srotasā tāvat adhvānam ūḍhaḥ dvādaśa yojanam etat puṇyatamam vyāsa gaṅgā avataraṇam smṛtam sthānam bhastrāpadam nāma mayā yat parikīrtitam yaḥ idam śṛṇuyāt martyaḥ sadā parvasu parvasu idam mahat pāpa vimocanam śubham vimāna yāna apsarasām vilambhanam śṛṇoti yaḥ nityam adīna mānasaḥ sa yāti lokān viditān divaukasām iti skandapurāṇe gaṅgāvataraṇe aṣṭāviṃśa uttara śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi hālāhalam aśeṣatas saṃgrāmam diti putrāṇām devānām ca bhaya āvaham hālāhalaḥ iti khyātaḥ gaṇaḥ vikrānta pauruṣaḥ asurāṇām babhau vyāsa dāruṇaḥ brahma kaṇṭakaḥ gateṣu danu putreṣu sa gaṇaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ balam kṛtvā mukham sarvān devān yuddhe samāhvayat teṣām teṣām ca saṃgrāmaḥ su dhoraḥ samavartata hṛta rājyāḥ abhyagacchanta brahmāṇam loka kāraṇam te tam ūcuḥ ca saṃhatya hṛta rājyāḥ sma sāmpratam teṣām śrutvā vacaḥ tat vai devaḥ salilasambhavaḥ uvāca devān deveśam prasādayata mā ciram sa vaḥ dātā mahā vīryaḥ balam devaḥ trilocanaḥ te evam uktāḥ deveśam tapasā ārādhya śaṃkaram ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ devāḥ balam naḥ dehi yajña han teṣām tu japatām evam tapasā toṣitaḥ haraḥ tam te samprāpya viprarṣe kṛta rakṣāḥ divaukasaḥ amūḍhāḥ mūḍha vat sarve asureṣu acaran tatas asurāḥ tu tadā mūḍhān dṛṣṭvā sarvān divaukasaḥ amanyanta durācārāḥ mūḍhāḥ iti yathātatham hṛta rajyāḥ ime devāḥ sarve mūḍhena cetasā ākrośantaḥ tān tu abhijaghnuḥ ca dāruṇam babandhuḥ ca yathākāmam mumucuḥ ca tathā apare evam teṣām tadā vyāsa vartanām śubha karmaṇām su mahān abhavat dharmaḥ a asurāṇām vyanīnaśat teṣām tena apacāreṇa asurāṇām durātmanām dharma nāśāt balam kṣīṇam bubudhuḥ devatā gaṇāḥ tatas te brahmaṇā abhyuktāḥ sarve divya astra dhāriṇaḥ āhūya asura śārdūlān yuddhe sarvān nyasūdayan balaḥ yatra hataḥ saṃkhye vajreṇa śataparvaṇā deva indreṇa abhivikramya bala hā sa yatas smṛtaḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi śatāni ca punar daśa āsīt danu sutaḥ śrīmān devatāntakaḥ iti uta sa māyām samparīpsan vai rudram ārādhayat purā brahmā dadau varam vyāsa danoḥ putrāya dhīmate sa vavre tāmasīm māyām sarva bhūta prabādhanīm abhedyām anivāryām ca yām tu vetti na kaścana tasmai prādāt sa tām māyām idam ca uvāca tam tadā kariṣyasi na ced śabdam yathākāmam danoḥ suta bahubhiḥ dānavaiḥ sārdham sarvān lokān abādhata devāḥ api bhayāt tasya na avatiṣṭhan tad agratas āhūtāḥ krūra śabdena dānavaiḥ bala darpitaiḥ tathā api na avatiṣṭhanta teṣām agre divaukasaḥ ṛṣayaḥ tān idam prāpya ūcuḥ sarve pramanyavaḥ rakṣām kuruta lokānām mā avalīnāḥ avatiṣṭhata vayam ca tapasā devāḥ dhāryiṣyāma saṃyatāḥ te evam uktāḥ taiḥ vyāsa ṛṣibhiḥ loka kāraṇāt yadā na eva avatiṣṭhante tathā api uktāḥ divaukasaḥ upāyam aparam prāhuḥ tadā te muni sattamāḥ āhūya apsarasaḥ sarvāḥ visṛjyantām sura uttamāḥ kāmena āviṣṭa manasām asurāṇām upāntikam tān tāsu āsakta hṛdayān pītamaireya vihvalān tatas tāḥ prahitāḥ devaiḥ vañcana artham suradviṣām kvaṇat nupūra nirhrāda kūjita utkarṇa sārasāḥ pīna uttuṅga stana ābhoga hāra vikṣipta yaṣṭayaḥ vitrasta bāla hariṇī sadṛśa āyata locanāḥ calat kuṇḍala saṃghṛṣṭa pāṇḍarā gaṇḍa maṇḍalāḥ śikhikaṇṭa chavi hara ślakṣṇa vāsaḥ dharāḥ parāḥ vastra anta kusuma āpīḍa saṃsakta karapallavāḥ na eka ratna prabhā ākīrṇa keyūra ābaddha bāhavaḥ mayūra barha saṃkāśa cāru kuñcita mūrdhajāḥ kalpadruma samudbhūta kusuma sraj vibhūṣaṇāḥ śuka aṅga harita ākāra kañcuka uttaṃsita stanāḥ matta mātaṅga vikrānta līlā vibhrama recakāḥ matta kokila dātyūha kala nisvana bhāṣitāḥ mahatām api upāttānām tapasām vighna hetavaḥ darśayāmāsuḥ ātmānam vidviṣām vadha hetavaḥ atha te a apsarasaḥ dṛṣṭvā daiteyāḥ kāma mohitāḥ tāsām arthe vara aṅgīnām abhijaghnuḥ parasparam gadā parigha cakra asi śūla mudgara śaktibhiḥ dhanuḥ kuliśa tīkṣṇa agra bhindipāla paraśvadhaiḥ mama iyam cāru sarva aṅgī na tava iyam sumadhyamā athavā yuddha śulkā astu muñca enām praharasva mām iti uktvā vividhāḥ vācaḥ daiteyāḥ kāla coditāḥ hata śiṣṭāḥ tu ye tatra dānavāḥ śānta pauruṣāḥ yaḥ idam paṭhate viśuddha buddhiḥ nidhanam saṃsadi dānava īśvarāṇām iti skandapurāṇe andhakāra yuddhe ūnatriṃśa uttara śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca sa kadācid bala udvṛttaḥ paryaṭan pṛthivīm imām cintayitvā tu tām prāha dānava an anuyāyinaḥ ānyadhvam imām śīghram mad samīpam naga ātmaja mām prahlādaḥ vadatām śreṣṭhaḥ idam vacanam abravīt dānava indra hitam vākyam yat āyatyām viśudhyate avaśyam tat mayā vācyam bandhu snehāt viśeṣataḥ eṣā himavataḥ putrī patnī śarvasya dhīmataḥ na asyām dauṣṭyam tvayā cintyam mā naḥ dhakṣyati tejasā jagataḥ mātaram devīm pūjyām duṣprekṣya tejasam umām dānava śārdūla na adhikṣeptum iha arhasi kim kaṇṭhe mahatīm baddhvā śilām mūḍhena cetasā gambhīra āvartinīm bhīmām nadīm tvam tartum icchasi bhūtvā pataṅgaḥ kim mohāt śikhām dīptām vibhāvasoḥ dānavānām adhipate nāśāya spraṣṭum icchasi mā vināśam nayeḥ sarvān sa mūlān dānava īśvara tvam vipaścit kulīnaḥ ca kulīnānām ca gotra jaḥ prakṛtyā eva surūpa aṅgyaḥ devyāḥ cetaḥ nivartyatām yaḥ ā asmākam tapasā tuṣṭaḥ yacchate kāṅkṣitān varān tasya tvam devadevasya devyāḥ pāpam cikīrṣasi yena dakṣaḥ kratuḥ kālaḥ kāmaḥ ca gamitaḥ kṣayam icchan kuryāt hi rūpāṇām sa shasrāṇi śatāni ca pramathānām sahasrāṇi yoginām bhīma karmaṇām yaḥ haret bhāskarāt dīptim candrāt kāntim kṣiteḥ kṣamām vāsukeḥ yaḥ haret daṃṣṭrām sa haret tasya pārvatīm tasya uttamāṅgam sakalam śatadhā śakalībhavet yaḥ śarva bhāryām tām āryām avamanyeta bāliśaḥ yā eṣā śrīḥ te ditisuta mayā dattā su durlabhā kaṭukāni api pathyāni bandhūnām vacanāni ye na śṛṇvanti anayā upetāḥ te yānti nidhanam narāḥ sameṣyāma vayam devam priya arthe tava śaṃkaram iti uktaḥ sa tadā tena bandhunā śobhanam vacaḥ manasā eva hi bhūtānām vidadhānaḥ śubha aśubham tathā vā api anyathā vā api kālaḥ eva kariṣyati pratyākhyāya tatas rāgāt prahlādam dānava īśvaraḥ devīm spraṣṭum dadhe cetaḥ pataṅgaḥ aagni śikhām iva atha buddhvā bhagavatī duṣṭa bhāvam durātmanaḥ gaṇān ājñāpayāmāsa yuddhāya su mahā balān atha te jñāpitāḥ devyā vividha āyudha pāṇayaḥ dānava abhimukhībhūtāḥ somanandi puraḥsarāḥ te kṛtvā su mahat yuddham dānava anucaraiḥ saha vikṣiptāḥ dānava indreṇa vāyunā jaladāḥ iva etasmin antare devī dṛṣṭvā udīrṇam tam andhakam svayam eva abhidudrāva gṛhītvā sa śaram dhanuḥ andhakam pañcaviṃśatyā sā jaghāna stanāntare śarāṇām niśita agrāṇām sa mumoha papāta ca sa muhūrtāt tadā saṃjñām labdhvā mānāt ca dānavaḥ tatas saḥ utthāya punar devīm prati mahā asuraḥ mumoca śara varṣāṇi varṣāṇi iva balāhakaḥ tatas triśūlam udyamya devīm dīpta agni tejasam dānava indraḥ mama eva ayam śāsyaḥ mā tvam śramam kṛthāḥ aham eva asya śūlena bhetsyāmi hṛdayam raṇe evam uktā tu sā devī devadevena pārvatī virarāma tatas yuddhāt adṛśyā sambabhūva ca tatas devaḥ svayam prāha nandinam gaṇanāyakam yudhyadhvam dānavaiḥ sārdham gaṇān āhūya sarvaśas āhūya nandī tān sarvān gaṇān śarva ājñayā tadā uvāca bhūyas deveśam śṛṇu ye a abhyāgatāḥ gaṇāḥ viśiṣṭa iṣṭāḥ tvayā sṛṣṭāḥ svayam sṛṣṭau sanātanāḥ prajā bhāvena nānātvam yeṣām tattvam su durvacam vṛṣa dhvajāḥ vṛṣa rathāḥ candra avayava bhūṣaṇāḥ koṭī śata sahasrāṇām śatam eṣām mahātmanām tāvanti ca sahasrāṇi śatāni ca tathā vibho ṣaṣṭiḥ ca eva sahasrāṇi yeṣām tulyaḥ na vidyate devānām nīlakaṇṭhānām nīlakaṇṭha mahātmanām ete śurāḥ baleṣu ugrāḥ ugra udagra parākramāḥ yudhyamānāḥ kariṣyanti tava pramuditam manaḥ eteṣām eva rudrāṇām anurūpāḥ prabhāvataḥ tad mātrāḥ dvārapālāḥ vai vikrāntāḥ krānta manyavaḥ iti ime kapi siṃha āsyāḥ kapi siṃha balāḥ raṇe dānavaiḥ saha yotsyanti vāraṇāḥ iva vāraṇaiḥ rudrāḥ ca rudraputrāḥ ca rudrāṇām ye ca pārṣadāḥ rudra adhipa na kiṃcid hi yeṣām sādhyam na vidyate pañca pañca mahā vīryāḥ kākapakṣa dharāḥ ca te eṣām ṣaṣṭiḥ smṛtāḥ koṭyaḥ sahasrāṇi ca ṣoḍaśa gaṇapānām gaṇa adhyakṣa tvad priyāṇām iha āgatāḥ evam deva priya artham te dakṣa yajñaḥ samṛddhimān koṭī śata sahasra ākhyāḥ te samupasthitāḥ mahā analāḥ yathā vṛkṣān pradīptān vāyunā saha guhā vāsa guhyasya api krīḍamānasya ye suraiḥ priya artham gaṇapāḥ dattāḥ nānā mṛga śata ānanāḥ jvalana acala vat teṣām triṃśat koṭyaḥ maheśvara gaṇapānām anuprāptāḥ priyam kartum tava anagha oṣṭha jāt rudhirāt jātāḥ raktāḥ nāma gaṇeśvarāḥ aṅgārakasya anucarāḥ mahā bala parākramāḥ ṣaṣṭi koṭi sahasrāṇi te ime samupasthitāḥ mantavyam na balam ca api etad mātram tvayā anagha ete hi aṣṭaguṇa aiśvaryam tava deva prasāda jam sambibhrāṇāḥ maheśāna kariṣyanti bahūn api lokān ete samudyuktān sa deva asura mānuṣān saṃyuge yuga mūla antam daheyuḥ sura dānavān ye ete kunda saṃkāśāḥ svarṇa utpala vibhūṣitāḥ daṃśitāḥ sarve yuddha kutūhalāḥ brahmaṇyāḥ te ime śūrāḥ candra avayava bhūṣaṇāḥ rudrāḥ rudra pate prāptāḥ paśya imān yuddha lālasān bāla arka sama varṇa ābhāḥ sa śastrāḥ ca catur bhujāḥ dvārapālāḥ hi amī deva kapīndra sadṛśa ānanāḥ rakta ambarāḥ rakta mālyāḥ raktacandana rūṣitāḥ brahmaṇyāḥ vara dāḥ śūrāḥ kaumāra brahmacāriṇaḥ matta barhi samārūḍhāḥ sarve vai śakti pāṇayaḥ ete vikrāntavikrāntāḥ skandāḥ nāma kumārakāḥ uccaiḥśravaḥ pratisamāna śvān ye hema mālinaḥ virejuḥ āsthitāḥ deva pīta kauśeya vāsasaḥ bāla arka sama varṇa ābhāḥ bāla utpala dala īkṣaṇāḥ viśākhāḥ nāma te putrāḥ rudrāṇām śaktipāṇayaḥ yān etān īkṣase deva sita vastrān sita ānanān vidyotamānān vapuṣā bahūn candrān iva uditān kākapakṣa dharān muṇḍān tāmracūḍa īśu avasthitān ete vikhyāta vīryāḥ te śākhāḥ nāma kumārakāḥ ye ime chāga meṣa sthāḥ kiṃśuka aśoka varcasaḥ śūrāḥ ca audāryavantaḥ ca śiśu tāmarasa ānanāḥ naigameṣāḥ iti khyātāḥ hi ete deva kumārakāḥ ye ime kāla megha ābhāḥ kāla megha nibha svanāḥ keśa jāḥ tava te deva pramathāḥ samupasthitāḥ ime ca raktāḥ bahavaḥ gaṇāḥ para bala ardanāḥ nānā praharaṇāḥ sarve sarve yuddha viśāradāḥ kṛtinaḥ yuddha śauṇḍāḥ ca sarve eva ca daṃśitāḥ sita asitānām meghānām girīṇām ca sama tviṣaḥ siṃha vyāghra varāha āsyāḥ parigha aśani pāṇayaḥ ete vai pārṣadāḥ śūrāḥ skandasya paramātmanaḥ tridaśaiḥ krīḍanam dattāḥ sarvaśas tvām upasthitāḥ dṛpta pramuditam sphītam pramatha anīkam īśvara pravihāya anya kāryāṇi parama ādaram āsthitam deva arīṇām anarthāya vidhvaṃsayat anantaram gaṇapati śata yūtha saṃvṛttaḥ visṛja vibho a avanatān gaṇeśvarān athā apaśyat tadā āyātān bhagavān gaṇa nāyakān svaiḥ anīkaiḥ su bahuśas saṃnaddhān yuddha lālasān diṇḍim ca bhārabhūtim ca somaśarmāṇam eva ca āditya mālam vikrāntam su keśam ca mahā balam tālaketum jvaram ca eva daṇḍapāṇim ūrjitam etān ca anyān ca vikhyātān guhyān ca gaṇanāyakān yūyam eva gaṇa adhyakṣāḥ paryāptāḥ tān prabādhane tasmāt yūyam mahāsattvāḥ sa gaṇāḥ sa padānugāḥ gacchadhvam saṃvināśāya pūjitaḥ aasmi mahā balāḥ niśāmya dānava ārāvam śrotra āyāsa karam bhṛśam tau anyonya bala uddhūtau abhūtām sainya sāgarau ākāśa sthāḥ ca ye hi ete nadanti ambumucaḥ yathā ākāśa gān eva ripūn ete bādhantu dānavān bṛhaspatiḥ juhāva agnim nandī ca api rarakṣa tam ārohamāṇam tat tūrṇam cālayat tam iva acalam tatas halahalā śabdaḥ pramathānām ajāyata daityān vāryatām yuddhe taru pāṣāṇa sāyakaiḥ dānavāḥ vāryamāṇāḥ tu pramathiḥ jita kāśibhiḥ vidārya pramatha anīkam śīghram āruruhuḥ tadā gṛhṇīṣva muñca tiṣṭha iti sthitaḥ tvam kim kariṣyasi anyonyam cūrṇayanti sma nirghṛṇāḥ pramatha asurāḥ tatas dākṣāyaṇī putraiḥ dakṣa adhvara vināśanāḥ parāṅmukhāḥ na śakitāḥ kartum bhakti a parāṅmukhāḥ a rohaṇe a acala agrasya aśaktān nirjitān ripūn krīḍā artham mama yudhyadhvam ebhiḥ saha gaṇādhipāḥ bhujaga pati śiromaṇi pradīpa pratihata cāru śilāgṛha andhakāram kvacid abhipatita aṃśu candrakānta pravisṛta śaila nadī vikīrṇa toyam pramudita gaṇa bhairava aṭṭahāsa prasṛta mahā rava pūrita antarālam bahu kaṭaka vicāri matta nāgam bahu mṛga śāva nipīta nirjhara ambum bahu viṣama taṭa prapāta kuñjam bahuvidha gulma latā avatāna vṛkṣam marakata maṇi padmarāga śṛṅga dyuti śabalīkṛta pāda pādapa agryam yasmin sadā pramuditāḥ jita mṛtyu śokāḥ gorocanā añjana śilā āla nidhāna siddhāḥ siddhāḥ sadā pramuditāḥ vanitā sahāyāḥ tiṣṭhanti candra kiraṇa upama cāru hārāḥ vidyādharāḥ priyatamā vinibaddha rāgāḥ pīneṣu tuṅga taṭavatsu payodhareṣu sevanti nirjhara jala praṇaya ati śītam abhyāgatam pavanam apasarasaḥ nūpura rāvi bodhita haṃsam haṃsa tanūruha ghaṭṭita padmam padma rajaḥ ruṇita amala toyam toya pariṣkṛta kāñcana śṛṅgam śṛṅga samutthita candana vṛkṣam vṛkṣa samāsthita kokila vṛndam ṛkṣa tarakṣu nilīna nikuñjam kuñja guhā mukha nirgata siṃham ratna mayūkha vibhāsita pṛṣṭham pṛṣṭha samāsthita śaṃkara pādam pāda samutthita pādapa ṣaṇḍam ṣaṇḍa latā kusuma utkara mārgam mārga mārga maṇi toraṇa citram citra citra maṇi toraṇa paṭṭam paṭṭa paṭṭa viniveśita puṣpam puṣpa puṣpa paricumbita bhṛṅgam nānā dhātu vicitra nitambam nānā puṣpa latā gṛha ramyam nānā matta vihaṃgama ghuṣṭam nānā śṛṅga samāsthita siddham daityāḥ tadā bhagavatā anumata praveśāḥ sarve samāruruhuḥ ātma jaya eṣiṇaḥ te tatas visṛṣṭāḥ pramathaiḥ ārohanta diteḥ sutāḥ manvānāḥ pramathāḥ bhītāḥ nivṛttāḥ iti satvaram mandarasya tatas pṛṣṭhe nānā druma samākule baddha skandhāḥ sthitāḥ daityāḥ āditya sadṛśa prabhāḥ sa mandaraḥ bhīma śilā upala drumaḥ vivṛddha śārdūla tarakṣu vāraṇaḥ kṣipanti śubhra abhra nibhāḥ śilāḥ kvacid tarūn samutpāṭya nadanti megha vat nivāryamāṇāḥ pramathān samārdayan vaneṣu siṃhāḥ mṛga yūthapān iva virājate ditisuta bāhu pālitam vanam yathā mṛgapati bāhu pālitam ekatriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ prāñjaliḥ śukram āha idam śakra arka sadṛśa adyutim prāptāḥ sma bhagavan śailam mandaram cāru kandaram pramathaiḥ bhīma saṃkāśaiḥ saṃniruddha śilā talam khecarāḥ māyinaḥ ca eva yoginaḥ ca mahā balāḥ prasabham dānavaiḥ jetum na śakyāḥ gaṇanāyakāḥ tad upāyam samāsthāya viśeṣeṇa samāhitāḥ pramathān saṃprabādhāma yathā vā rucitam tava ke ca ime sūrya koṭīnām prabhā varṇa vapuḥ dharāḥ pramatha anīka madhyeṣu sthitāḥ paśyanti mām muhur śukraḥ uvāca yaḥ eṣa madhu piṅga akṣaḥ tryambakaḥ candra bhūṣaṇaḥ taruṇa arka samaḥ bhāti nandī eṣa gaṇanāyakaḥ brāhmaṇa adhipatiḥ hi eṣa bṛhat buddhiḥ bṛhaspatiḥ yaḥ eṣa na ati dūra sthaḥ vṛṣaketoḥ triśūladhṛk eṣaḥ mahākāyaḥ mahāgaṇapatiḥ varaḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ āsthāya kūjantam bhāti citra kalāpinam mayūram bāla sūrya ābhaḥ śaktipāṇiḥ mahā balaḥ skandaḥ eṣa hi devānām agraṇīḥ dānavāḥ raṇe yaḥ eṣa tāmracūḍa sthaḥ tāmracūḍa śilā prabhaḥ kākapakṣa dharaḥ hi eṣa pūrṇa candra nibha ānanaḥ viśākhaḥ nāma kaumāraḥ kaumāra brahmacaryavān taruṇaḥ taruṇa prajñaḥ taruḥ śākhā yutaḥ yathā svāhāyāḥ tanayaḥ hi eṣa śākhaḥ nāma mahā dyutiḥ etasya yaḥ hi asau pārśvam savyam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati darśayānaḥ pradeśinyāḥ mām ca tvām ca punar punar meṣam āsthāya balavān bālaḥ eva vyavasthitaḥ caturbhiḥ eṣa putraiḥ tu dṛśyate a asura hā vṛtaḥ devam īśam mahā iṣvāsam nandisūnu puraḥsaram aham utthāpayiṣyāmi śasyāni jaladaḥ yathā tam bhārgavaḥ iti procya dānavān dānava adhipam mūle sa andhakam sa aśva sārathim pādātaiḥ bahu sāhasraiḥ pādān tasya cakāra ha teṣu pāda sahasreṣu giri vyūhasya dānavaiḥ vṛkṣa śaila śilā saṃghān kārayamāsa bhārgavaḥ koṭibhiḥ daśabhiḥ tasya dānavānām mahātmanām nitambān tāmra nayanān pracakāra graheśvaraḥ dhātu nisyanda citreṣu nitambeṣu api dānavān tṛṇa vat kṣupa vat ca api sthāpayāmāsa bhārgavaḥ triṃśatā koṭibhiḥ ca api tridaśādhipa vidviṣām giri vyūhasya śṛṅgāni cakāra arka sama prabhaḥ teṣu śṛṅgeṣu tuṅgeṣu dānavān sa āyudhān atha amī prapātāḥ iti evam ācakhyau bhṛgunandanaḥ śastra toyāni muditāḥ kṣarantaḥ iva saṃsthitāḥ bala sthāḥ ye java upetāḥ daityāḥ daivata kaṇṭhakāḥ nivāta kavacān sarvān vividha āyudha dhāriṇaḥ prahlādam atha saṃhrādam anuhrādam śinim tathā virocanam balim bāṇam vātam kārtasvanam kuśam śambhum ca bhāvayatyam ca ilvakam bilvakam tathā vitam vṛttam tuhuṇḍam ca huṇḍam daṇḍam ca dānavam añjanam ruṣaṇam rāhum svarbhānum ajakam gajam etān ca anyān ca balinaḥ daityān daivata kaṇṭakān vyūham rakṣata yudhyadhvam iti uvāca asura adhipaḥ sa giri vyūhaḥ ābhāti śastra kaṇṭakita drumaḥ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā giri vyūham pramathāḥ vismayam yayuḥ neduḥ te a asura śārdūlāḥ meghāḥ loka atyaye yathā ūcuḥ ca na hi śakyaḥ a ayam bhettum devaiḥ sa vāsavaiḥ pramathāḥ kim kariṣyanti su alpa vīrya parākramāḥ jīvayiṣyati naḥ śukraḥ mṛtān api na saṃśayaḥ yudhyadhvam dānava śreṣṭhāḥ niśśaṅkaiḥ antarātmabhiḥ giri vyūham tatas dṛṣṭvā bhārgava uttama nirmitam devaḥ kapardī prāha idam bṛhat buddhim bṛhaspatim vācaspate giri vyūham paśya śukreṇa nirmitam śṛṅgavantam darīvantam himavantam yathā girim lokān sa jala pātālān sa viṣṇūn sa pitāmahān na enam devāḥ na gandharvāḥ na nāgāḥ na nagāḥ tathā sa tvam brahma vidām śreṣṭha giri vyūha vidāraṇam vajra vyūham kuruṣva adya pramatha ayuta saṃvṛtam bāhujān bahu sahasrān bhaktān ca eva gaṇa adhipān skandasya pārṣadaiḥ śūraiḥ sura asura nighātibhiḥ koṭim koṭi pravīrāṇām pramathānām prahāriṇām vajra dhārāsu sarvāsu sthāpayāmāsa sa dvijaḥ kumāram ca viśākham ca śākham chāgamukham tathā kuḍmala agre catur bāhuḥ kapi indra vadanaḥ a ari hā kuṇḍodaram nandiṣeṇam ghaṇṭākarṇam mahodaram sa arka candra ayuta prakhyaḥ sthitaḥ vai paṭṭiśa āyudhaḥ rudrāṇām dvārapālāḥ ca rudrāḥ rudra sutāḥ ca ye itas ca itas ca vinyastāḥ vajra vyūha abhirakṣiṇaḥ tasthau īśaḥ bhavaḥ śarvaḥ kapardī nīlalohitaḥ mandaraḥ candra bimbena juṣṭa śṛṅgaḥ iva acalaḥ śata dhāraḥ na eka parvā cāru śobhita kuḍmalaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā nirmitam vyūham deva gandharva guhyakāḥ atha gaṇapa baleṣu siṃhanādāḥ paṇava mṛdaṅgama śaṅkhanāda miśrāḥ dvātriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ tau dṛṣṭvā nirmitau vyūhau pramatha asurayoḥ surāḥ vimāna koṭibhiḥ śīghram rurudhuḥ sarvatas nabhaḥ meru kūṭa vanam ramyam dahyamānam iva agninā deva dundubhi śabda āḍhyam divya strī śata saṃkulam tat deva maṇḍalam bhāti yathā eva āditya maṇḍalam divya puṣpa samākīrṇam divya gandha adhivāsitam prekṣakaiḥ śataśas pūrṇam kha talam divyam ābabhau vāditrāṇi abhyahanyanta jaguḥ ca sura gāyanāḥ rambhā ādyāḥ nanṛtuḥ ca api śubha apāṅgāḥ sura aṅganāḥ samīyatuḥ mahā nādaiḥ vāta uddhūtau yathā arṇavau mā tvaradhvam iti proktāḥ śukreṇa su mahātmanā yodhāḥ nivāryamāṇā api cakruḥ yuddham asaṃhatam tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca paṇavāḥ goviṣāṇakāḥ āḍambarāḥ ḍiṇḍimāḥ ca maṇḍūkāḥ paṇavāḥ hi api bheryaḥ dundubhayaḥ ca api mṛdaṅgāḥ kiṃkhara ānakāḥ ubhayatra bale gāḍham prāvādyanta sahasraśas tatas sura gaṇaiḥ nādāḥ saha gandharva cāraṇaiḥ kṛtāḥ tūrya ravam śrutvā pramatha asura sainyayoḥ mandare ruruvuḥ ghoram siṃha śārdūla kuñjarāḥ abhindantaḥ svakam vyūham yuyudhuḥ pramatha asurāḥ prathame saṃnipāte tu teṣām yuddhe kṛtātmanām tat śūla vajra upala vṛkṣa bāṇa dṛḍha prahāra atiśaya ati harṣam vivardhate pāriṣada asurāṇām yuddham yugam tiṣyam iva ati ghoram śrūyante kārmuka ravāḥ siṃhanādāḥ ca dāruṇāḥ vyāviddha aṅgulayaḥ devāḥ cāraṇa uraga guhyakāḥ śūra ārasita śabdena tena udīrita vikramāḥ cakruḥ karmāṇi asahyāni darpitāḥ pramatha asurāḥ asibhiḥ vyāyataiḥ chinnāḥ paṭṭiśiḥ bhinna vakṣasaḥ śara saṃkṛtta marmāṇaḥ patanti pramatha asurāḥ śirasām patyamānānām bāhūnām ca ūrubhiḥ saha rāśayaḥ tatra dṛśyante pramatha asura saṃyuge bhagna cakrāḥ vidhvajāḥ ca vivarūthāḥ vikūbarāḥ dṛśyante śataśas vyaśvāḥ hata sārathayaḥ a arathāḥ sa patākāḥ sa keyūrāḥ sa varma āyudha ketavaḥ niṣkṛṣṭa danta muśalāḥ patanti gaja puṃgavāḥ śara prahāra rugṇa aṅgāḥ cāmara āpīḍaka ujjvalāḥ sa sādinaḥ nipātyante hayāḥ sūrya haya upamāḥ vāsobhiḥ ātapatraiḥ ca mukuṭaiḥ maṇi kuṇḍalaiḥ hāra ardha hāraiḥ keyūraiḥ aṅgulīyaiḥ sraj uttamaiḥ kara ānanaiḥ prakṛttaiḥ ca caraṇaiḥ ca nipātitaiḥ rudhira āsrāva vasanāḥ nānā ābharaṇa bhūṣaṇāḥ atha vāji gaja oghānām śoṇita udaka vāhinī nadī pravavṛte ghorā yama sādana vāhinī mṛga hasti khara aśva uṣṭra mahā grāha samākulā māṃsa medaḥ yakṛt paṅkā dhanuḥ dhvaja śatadrumā chinna śīrṣa upala śatā hasta pañca ānana uragā keśa śaivāla saṃchannā dhanuḥ jyā śata tantukā pāṇḍara ambara harṣā vai mukuṭa ati kula ākulā bherī kacchapa saṃkīrṇā vara ābharaṇa dardurā śara mīna samākīrṇā khaḍga nakra durāsadā viśīrṇa hāra sikatā kapha saṃjāta pheninī rakta utpalānām mālā iva kauṅkumī sraj iva ujjhitā jihvā iva uraga rājasya yamasya ājñā iva adbhutā bhaya dā bhiru yodhānām śūrāṇām harṣa vardhinī vivardhamāne saṃgrāme tasmin pāriṣada asure giri vyūha prapāta sthāḥ kruddhāḥ dānava sattamāḥ te krodhāt śūla śakti ṛṣti gadā varṣam atandritāḥ vavarṣuḥ pramatha anīke varṣam jaladharāḥ iva śastra varṣeṇa patanāt tāḍyamānāḥ hi anekaśas meghāḥ sasyāni hi yathā dviradāḥ pādapān iva pṛṣatān iva śārdūlāḥ śarabhāḥ iva vāraṇān vajrāḥ iva yathā śailān kāla dūtāḥ narān iva vighnān iva ca śānti arthāḥ naya anavinayāḥ iva bhāvān iva yathā bhāvāḥ doṣāḥ doṣān yathā api ca tathā nivāta kavacān śūla śakti ṛṣti vṛṣṭibhiḥ nijaghnuḥ pramathāḥ śūrāḥ śataśas aatha sahasraśas śūla nirdārita uraskāḥ muśalaiḥ bhinna mastakāḥ vajra avaghāta mlāna aṅgāḥ dānavāḥ patitāḥ bhuvi teṣām ninādāḥ śrūyante nadatām ati dāruṇāḥ saṃvartakānām meghānām nadatām iva sarvatas ceṣṭante hi asurāḥ bhūmau bhagna pṛṣṭhāḥ iva uragāḥ tatas vīkṣya śūraḥ tatra mahā asurāḥ nivṛttāḥ śataśas tatra krodha saṃrakta locanāḥ taiḥ bhṛśam pramathāḥ te viddhāḥ vyāsa trapā anvitāḥ saṃmīlita akṣāḥ vṛṣabhāḥ varṣam nipatitam yathā te ca api yuddham tumulam kṛtvā ante pīḍitāḥ tadā bhagnāḥ parāṅmukhāḥ jātāḥ chinna bhinna aṅgāḥ asandhayaḥ daśa cakruḥ mahā vegam daśa nāga śata upamāḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ ca balavān ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ ca vīryavān mahākālaḥ ca kāla ābhaḥ nandiṣeṇaḥ ca viśrutaḥ piṅgalaḥ lohitākṣaḥ ca somanandī ca vīryavān vināyakaḥ ca nandī ca chāgaḥ kuṇḍodaraḥ skandaḥ mayūra varam āsthitaḥ viviśuḥ ca asuram sainyam samudram makarāḥ iva śaṅku karṇa hatāḥ daityāḥ ghaṇṭā karṇa vidāritāḥ nandiṣeṇa śara abhyastāḥ mahā kāla prakālitāḥ kuṇḍa udara gadā veśaiḥ cūrṇita astra vibhūṣaṇāḥ piṅgala āloḍitāḥ neśuḥ skanda śakti vidāritāḥ muṣṭi prahāra bhinna āsyaiḥ tala tāḍita mastakaiḥ apāhasta prahāraiḥ ca kṣipyamāṇaiḥ itastatas indra vajra āhataḥ pūrvam yathā vindhyaḥ mahā giriḥ bhinna vyūhān tatas daityān pramathāḥ jita kāśinaḥ dudruvuḥ śataśas vṛkṣān pakvān śakunayaḥ yathā pramathānām ca śūrāṇām asurāṇām ca dāruṇam saṃnipāte punar teṣām gajānām iva dāruṇe neduḥ devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ siddhāḥ ca divi harṣitāḥ nānāvidhāḥ tūrya ravāḥ tatas dānava pārṣadaiḥ aśrūyanta kṛtāḥ ghorāḥ meghānām nadatām iva gajaiḥ ca nīla acala saṃnikāśaiḥ rathaiḥ ca gandharva vimāna kalpaiḥ hayaiḥ ca vāyu pratimāna vegaiḥ caranti daityāḥ samare hi abhītāḥ te śūla śakti ṛṣti bhuśuṇḍi bāṇaiḥ śaila upalaiḥ cakra sa śūla vajraiḥ anyonyam utsādayitum pravṛttāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ dānava puṃgavāḥ ca iti skandapurāṇe gaṇa yuddhe pañcatriṃśottaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ viveśa pramatha anīkam megha anīkam iva aṃśumān mandara agra pratīkāśam īṣā dantam kṣarat madam udaya agram samāsthāya sahasrāṃśuḥ jvalan iva tomaraiḥ sa śaraiḥ ca api divākara kara prabhaiḥ pramathān apatastāra śataśas aatha sahasraśas vainateyaḥ yathā nāgān siṃhaḥ go vṛṣabhān yathā drāvayāmāsa pramathān tathā śūraḥ virocanaḥ yāntam āyāntam aprāptam prāptam dūra stham eva ca pramatham paśyate yam yam tam tam dārayate aasuraḥ mṛgāḥ siṃham yathā dṛṣṭvā garuḍam ca yathā uragāḥ virocanam tathā dṛṣṭvā pramathāḥ dudruvuḥ bhayāt gaṇeśvara balam dṛṣṭvā gaṇeśvara varaḥ drutam prasārayan karam ghoram pūrvam airāvataḥ yathā virocanam saḥ aabhyadhāvat śārdūlaḥ hariṇam yathā tam āpatantam saṃvīkṣya tīkṣṇa dantam gajānanam kumbha antare tomareṇa dārayāmāsa dānavaḥ tam tomaram kara agreṇa niṣkṛṣya sa vināyakaḥ ghūrṇamānam tadā ālakṣya dānava indram virocanam dantābhyām candra śubhrābhyām nirbibheda vināyakaḥ vaināyakam tat tu samīkṣya karma devāḥ sa śakrāḥ mumucuḥ praṇādān tasya uttamāṅga upari puṣpa mālā papāta devasya yathā tri mārgā tayā tu nānāvidha puṣpavatyā vibhāti devaḥ sa tadā srajā raṇe nakṣatra mālā vali cāru śobhaḥ samunnataḥ meruḥ iva aparaḥ sthitaḥ udbhinna raktam tu vidāryamāṇam virocanam vīkṣya vināyakena jambhaḥ a ambuda ābhaḥ a turam ārasitvā dudrāva mā bhaiḥ iti bhāṣamāṇaḥ jambhe a avasanne a ari bale prasanne ṣaṭ dānavāḥ ṣaṇmukha pūrvajam tam kuṭhāra śūla asi paraśvadhaiḥ tu mlecchāḥ yathā kruddha mukhāḥ tatakṣuḥ vināyaka ābhān sa vināyakaḥ tu ṣaṭ dānavān ṣaṇmukha sannikāśaḥ kari indra vaktraḥ karam ucchrayitvā karī surāṇām iva jāta darpaḥ prākālayat dānava puṃgavān tān yathā gajān darpita siṃha potaḥ siṃha īkṣitānām iva gopatīnām kāla īkṣitānām iva mānavānām vināyakena īkṣita kālitānām bhayam tadā āsīt miṣatām balānām dṛṣṭvā balam tat balinā abhibhūtam baleḥ sutaḥ a asau balinām variṣṭhaḥ vināyakam hantu manāḥ sasāra mattam raṇe mattaḥ iva dvipa indraḥ tam āpatantam tapatām iva īśam kruddham raṇe kālam iva ātta cāpam sasāra roddhum samare ca yoddhum kuṇḍodaraḥ siṃhaḥ iva anya siṃham śatāni pañca eva sa kārmukāṇām vikṛṣya vajra aśani nisvanānām kuṇḍodarāya iṣu varān sasarga garjan sa bāṇaḥ tu yathā payodaḥ tān āgatān tīkṣṇa mukhān tadānīm bāṇasya bāṇān kupita ahi kalpān kuṇḍodaraḥ śailaruheṇa sarvān manorathān vighne iva ājaghāna tān niṣphalān prekṣya śarān surāriḥ suretara ari prahatān kṣitisthān śaktyā sa kuṇḍodaram ājaghāna śaktyā guhaḥ krauñcam iva acala indram vakṣaḥ pradeśāt tu gaṇeśvarasya bāṇasya śaktiḥ kṣatajam papau sā śakra upanītam ruciram sugandhi yathā amṛtam vajradharasya bhāryā śakti prahāra abhihataḥ tu yakṣaḥ kuṇḍodaraḥ dardara mandara ābhaḥ papāta saṃjñām vipulām prahāya dāva agninā dagdhaḥ iva ucca vṛkṣaḥ kuṇḍodaram tam nihatam samīkṣya vināyakaḥ cyuta padma mālaḥ dudrāva bāṇam prati hantu kāmaḥ karī iva bhṛṅgāra kara ucchrayeṇa tam ānane vajra nibha ānanaiḥ śaraiḥ vināyakam hi ātatam eva bāṇaḥ tṛṇa agra pātān iva sa iṣu pātān a cintayitvā eva gaja indra vaktraḥ īṣa iṣa netram sa varūtha cakram babhañja bāṇasya ratham sa sūtam bāṇasya vāhān tu tam ārujantam vināyakam bhūmi gatam yathā ibham siṃhī sutaḥ siṃhaḥ iva abhipatya sa bāhu pāśena babandha rāhuḥ sa rāhuṇā bāhu yuga avabaddhaḥ vināyakaḥ sarpa sahasra mālaḥ tam rāhu bāhu pratibaddha ceṣṭam vināyakam vīkṣya tadā divi sthāḥ devāḥ sa śakrāḥ saha yakṣa siddhaiḥ hā hā iti hā hā iti asakṛt vineduḥ kuṭhāram ādāya jaghāna rāhum jatru antare saṃhata muṣṭinā ca kuṭhāra ghātāt sa tu muṣṭinā ca dṛḍha āhataḥ yakṣa vareṇa rāhuḥ vināyakam bhīma balaḥ mumoca śubhetaram karma yathā kulīnaḥ tam vai parāvṛtya karī iva mattaḥ gajānanaḥ kānana ṣaṇḍa vāsī padbhiḥ ca dantaiḥ ca jaghāna rāhum prakīrṇa hastena ca bhīma hastaḥ rāhau tu kuṇḍodara muṣṭi ghātaiḥ vināyakena eva ca pīḍyamāne kujambha saṃhrāda mayāḥ sa tārāḥ huṇḍaḥ tuhuṇḍaḥ ca tadā tam īyuḥ mayaḥ tu kuṇḍa udaram ājaghāna śūlena tāraḥ meśalena kukṣau balaḥ tu lamba ambuda sannikāśam tam muṣṭinā vajra nibhena ca api hiraṇyanetra avaraja ātmajaḥ ca vināyakam bhīma balam talena tasya ātmajaḥ ca api jaghāna roṣāt sa ca api gatvā balavān tuhuṇḍaḥ vināyakaḥ tam tu tadā gṛhītvā kareṇa vikramya tuhuṇḍam ājau ākṣipya ca utkṣipya ca bhīma vegaḥ cikṣepa dūram yama dūta kalpam prahrādam āhatya tatas sa devaḥ mayam ca matta añjana tulya vakṣāḥ utpāṭya tam ghora ravam nanāda śubhra ambu pūrṇaḥ nabhasi iva meghaḥ kuṇḍodaraḥ ca api balam sa tāram kujambham āhatya ca yakṣa varyaḥ ubhau raṇa sthau gaja yūtha pālau vyādhūta mālau bhṛśa jāta kopau sasarjatuḥ tau śara vṛṣṭim ugrām yathā ambu vṛṣṭim jaladau sa nādau balāni tāni āsura pārṣadānām saṃsakta bhāvam paramam gatāni ṣaṭtriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ tatas vyatikaraḥ bhūyas pārṣada asura sainyayoḥ sambabhūva udadhi kṣobhāt makarāṇām iva adbhutaḥ paṭṭiśa asi dhanuṣmantaḥ vidyutvantaḥ iva ambudāḥ teṣām eva pravadatām aśrūyanta giraḥ muhur śūlaiḥ triśūlaiḥ cakraiḥ ca huṇḍaiḥ laguḍa kampanaiḥ ṭaṅkaiḥ kaṭaṅkaiḥ prāsaiḥ pāśaiḥ paraśu paṭṭiśaiḥ druma upala śilā ghātaiḥ girīṇām śikharaiḥ api tvam kaḥ kuṇḍodaraḥ aham vai vṛtraḥ aham kuṇḍakodara viśākhaḥ baliḥ aham aham bāṇaḥ guhaḥ hi aham iti evam dānavānām ca pramathānām ca bhairavāḥ darpa udrekāt adhikṣepāḥ śrūyante yudhyatām raṇe gajānām iva mattānām meghānām iva ca āgame bhidyatām iva śailānām samudrāṇām kṣayeṣu iva pralaya anteṣu mahatām vāyūnām javatām iva teṣām āsīt mahān śabdaḥ paraspara nijaghnuṣām brahmadaṇḍa pratīkāśaiḥ yama daṇḍa nibhaiḥ api vajrāṇām iva śaileṣu vaṃśānām iva dahyatām abhūt caṭacaṭā śabdaḥ śastrāṇām pātyatām tadā gaṇeśvara vimuktābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ su dṛḍha āhatāḥ druma prahāra bhagna aṅgāḥ gadā cūrṇita sandhayaḥ dānavāḥ nipatanti urvyām vājinaḥ cyuta jīvitāḥ chinna dhvaja patākā īṣāḥ bhagna akṣa yuga kabūrāḥ vidhvastāḥ tatra dṛśyante vimāna pratimāḥ rathāḥ mātaṅgaiḥ ca turaṅgaiḥ ca syandanaiḥ ca avacūrṇitaiḥ tatra devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ sa yakṣa uraga kiṃnarāḥ utkruṣṭa vara śabda āḍhyam cakruḥ su bahuśas divyānām su vicitrāṇām amṛta upama gandhinām varṣam papāta puṣpāṇām yudhyante yatra te raṇe tathā tu te gaja ghana nāda garjanāḥ śara asi śakti ṛṣṭi gadā visarjanāḥ parasparam yuyudhuḥ atīva saṃhatāḥ diteḥ sutāḥ pramatha gaṇāḥ ca darpitāḥ aṣṭatriṃśat uttara śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ tāmyamāneṣu daityeṣu daitya yūthapa yūthapāḥ cakruḥ vegam mahā vegāḥ yuga anteṣu iva sāgarāḥ prahrādaḥ ca anuhrādaḥ ca saṃhrādaḥ śini bāṣkalau prahlādasya ca ye putrāḥ catvāraḥ bhīma vikramāḥ baliḥ bāṇaḥ ca vātaḥ ca śambhuḥ kārtasvanaḥ kubhaḥ añjanaḥ rūṣaṇaḥ vyaṃsaḥ gaviṣṭhaḥ pṛthivīṃjayaḥ vṛṣaparvā śatāvartaḥ gavākṣaḥ gomukhaḥ tathā saraḥ nisundaḥ sundaḥ ca mahā bala parākramāḥ pākaḥ vipākaḥ santāpaḥ hastī duryodhanaḥ tathā hayaśīrṣaḥ ca indraśirāḥ triśirāḥ śaṅkuḥ eva ca tathā gaganamūrdhā ca aviromā mahāmanaḥ asi lomā tuhuṇḍaḥ ca huṇḍaḥ vṛtraḥ ca dānavaḥ daśagrīvaḥ ca bāliḥ ca meghanīlaḥ prabhākaraḥ yaḥ ca āditya rathāt cakram jahāra bala darpitaḥ ete ca anye ca ditijāḥ samadāḥ te gajāḥ iva āmiṣa arthe yathā siṃhāḥ vāsita arthe yathā gajāḥ dānavāḥ viviśuḥ tadvat pramathān saṃjighāṃsavaḥ teṣām āpatatām vegaḥ bhīmaḥ aabhūt deva vidviṣām te vai śastra upala śilā pāda pāśani pāṇayaḥ gaṇeśvara adhipaḥ nandī mahākāyaḥ ca vīryavān ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ kuṇḍodara mahodarau nandiṣeṇaḥ somanandī karikaḥ ca gaṇeśvaraḥ pañcākṣaḥ vīrabhadraḥ ca viṭpatiḥ pāvaka ardanaḥ āditya āpyāyanaḥ ca eva soma āpyāyanaḥ eva ca samudrāpyāyanaḥ ca anyaḥ pāvakāpyāyanaḥ tathā varabarhidhvajaḥ ca eva viśākhaḥ śākhaḥ eva ca naigameṣaḥ ca balavān rudra vīrya parākramāḥ bāhuleya udbhavāḥ ye ca pramathāḥ bhīma rūpiṇaḥ te aabhyayus dānavān yuddhe vṛṣabhāḥ vṛṣabhān iva teṣām teṣām ca saṃgrāmaḥ tumulaḥ samapadyata ajane gandhahastīnām śarabhaiḥ iva dāruṇaḥ sāgarāḥ sāgaraiḥ yadvat pāvakaiḥ iva pāvakāḥ tathā surāḥ jāta darpāḥ krodha vaiśvānara āvṛtāḥ dhṛtāḥ pāriṣadaiḥ śūraiḥ vighnāḥ dharma paraiḥ iva ṭaṅkaiḥ vidāryamāṇāni giri agrāṇi samantataḥ gṛdhra cakrāyamāṇāni patanti urvyām sahasraśas cakrāṇi cakraiḥ chidyante śūlaiḥ śūlāḥ vidāritāḥ iṣubhiḥ ca iṣavaḥ viddhāḥ patanti bhujagāḥ iva āstṛtā medinī bhāti vyāghra carma ambaraiḥ iva medaḥ majja asthi paṅka aṅkam keśa kaśmala saṃkulam babhūva āyodhanam ghoram śmaśāna vana sannibham hayāḥ gajāḥ rathāḥ ca api dānavānām gaṇa īśvaraiḥ saṃcūrṇitāḥ pradṛśyante tatra tatra mahī tale parīkṣaṇīyaḥ samitau tvam adya suretarāṇām sura rāja śatro baddhvā tri śākhām bhṛkuṭīm lalāṭe sa nandinam prāha tadā kujambhaḥ vānara ānana kim vāgbhiḥ mām bhīṣayitum icchasi hiraṇyakaśipoḥ pautraḥ na aham prākṛta dānavaḥ yam ātma daṇḍāt varuṇāt sa pāśāt indrāt sa vajrāt sa gadāt haneśāt na aham raṇa sthaḥ bhayam āharāmi bhayam na daityeṣu palāyitam vā mad bāṇa lūnam patatām avanyām tālāt yathā tāla phalam su pakvam iti evam uktvā śara jāla vṛṣṭyā nandīśvaram dānava rāja meghaḥ tarum yathā pakva phalam śakuntāḥ valmīkam uccam bhujagāḥ iva ugrāḥ tathā śarāḥ dānava rāja muktāḥ nandīśvaram dīpta mukhāḥ viśanti vajreṇa vajrī sa tu tān śara oghān śailaḥ payodhān iva san nivārya jaghāna vajram śatadhā kujambhaḥ saṃvartaka agnim samaye meghaḥ viṣṭambhitam vajra varam niśāmya niśāmya nādam ca kujambha muktam balāt sa saṃgṛhya ratham kareṇa īṣā vara agre pramatha īśa pālaḥ ākṣipya cikṣepa sa sūta vāham kṣiptvā ca bhūyas sa rarāsa ghoram sambhrānta cakraḥ sa visandhita aśvaḥ prabhraṣṭa sūta asi śira ugra nemiḥ tām sarpa jihvām iva lelihānām mṛtyum kṣudhā ārtām iva bhoktu kāmām śikhām mahā agneḥ iva dīpyamānām sa nandine sampramumoca jambhaḥ sā śaktiḥ indra ari bhuja pramuktā ugrā ati dīptā āṅgirasī iva kṛtyā sa vajra ghātāt avacūrṇita asthiḥ saṃśīrṇa danta īkṣaṇa bhagna jānuḥ tasmin hate deva gaṇāḥ vineduḥ sarve surāṇām arayaḥ ca daityān bhūta adhipam bhūtapatiḥ ca devam prapūjayāmāsa śaśāṅka cihnam aṣṭatriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ūnacatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kujambham nihatam dṛṣṭvā nandinā deva nandinā ninādam cakrire devāḥ cāraṇāḥ ca mahā uragāḥ jambhaḥ dānava śārdūlaḥ krodham āhārayat mahat tasya kruddhasya gātrebhyaḥ niṣpetuḥ pāvaka arciṣaḥ sa ulkā ambuda nibha ābhāsaḥ jambhaḥ krodha samāvṛtaḥ dudrāva nandinam hantum kuñjaram siṃha rāj iva tiṣṭha idānīm durācāra mayā dṛṣṭaḥ kva yāsyasi eṣa tvām vajra saṃkāśaḥ parighaḥ cūrṇayiṣyati parigham tasya cikṣepa daṇḍam yamaḥ iva aparaḥ parighaḥ nandinam yāti hantum kāla anala upamaḥ tam vāsuki bhujaṅga ābham brahmadaṇḍa nibham mahat śakra agniḥ iva durdṛśyaḥ pradhāvan nandinam prati kṛtaḥ ninādaḥ su mahat pramathaiḥ ca sahasraśas śrutvā ninādam devānām parigham vīkṣya ca āgatam śaṅkukarṇena parigham gṛhītam vīkṣya tad balāt vineduḥ muditāḥ devāḥ śaṅkukarṇam ca tuṣṭuvuḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ a api parigham gṛhītvā balavān punar tatas dānava śārdūlaḥ sasāra raṇa lālasaḥ tatas gaṇeśvara bale dānavānām bale tathā jajñe vāditra ninadaḥ siṃhanāda vimiśritaḥ danu tanaya gaṇa adhipa īśa yuddham tat upaniśamya divaukasām tadānīm pramatha gaṇa varāḥ sa nāga rudrāḥ hi asura varāḥ ca saha andhakāḥ raṇa sthāḥ vyuparata kalahāḥ tadā avatasthuḥ gaṇapati dānava yuddham īkṣamāṇāḥ ūnacatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ catvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śaṅkukarṇam tu dhāvantam jambham prati mahā balaḥ utsṛjya śaṅkukarṇaḥ jambham gaṇapa puṅgavaḥ vṛtram eva abhidudrāva vighātaḥ vai damam yathā parigheṇa ahanat ca enam śaṅkukarṇaḥ gaṇeśvaraḥ mahā girim yathā śakraḥ vajreṇa śata parvaṇā svarṇa dhātu rasa udgārī nīla acalaḥ iva ābabhau tatas cirāt samāśvasya vṛtraḥ dānava puṃgavaḥ gireḥ śṛṅgam samutpāṭya śaṅkukarṇam adhāvata gaṇeśvarāya acala agram cikṣepa ca rarāsa ca niṣṭanantau iva ādityau dīpyamānau iva analau garjamānau iva ghanau bṛṃhantau iva kuñjarau mattau iva ca śārdūlau niḥśvasantau iva uragau nardamānau yathā siṃhau valgamānau vṛṣau iva calantau iva śaila indrau ghūrṇamānau iva arṇavau iti evam śaṅkukarṇaḥ ca vṛtraḥ ca asura puṃgavaḥ muṣṭibhiḥ vajra kalpaiḥ ca talaiḥ ca aśani sannibhaiḥ pāda prahāraiḥ ghoraiḥ ca ūrdhvam utkṣepaṇaiḥ tathā ākṣepaiḥ atha vikṣepaiḥ karṣaṇaiḥ apakarṣaṇaiḥ pauruṣa ākhyāpanaiḥ ugraiḥ nāma saṃśravaṇaiḥ api siṃhanādaiḥ sa vāditraiḥ vṛkṣa śaila śilā upalaiḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ gaṇādhyakṣaḥ sa ca vṛtraḥ danoḥ sutaḥ śaṅku karṇena vṛtraḥ tu dṛḍha mūlaḥ iva drumaḥ hasta avabandhana utkṣiptaḥ sahasā pātitaḥ kṣitau tatas gaṇeśvara bale dānavānām tathā bale muṣṭinā tam atha āhatya vṛtram bhuvi nipātya ca śaṅku karṇaḥ hi apakrāntaḥ vṛtraḥ tu su mahā vīryaḥ muṣṭi tāḍana vihvalaḥ tam āpatantam vṛkṣeṇa śaṅkukarṇaḥ gaṇeśvaraḥ śālena tāḍayāmāsa itas ehi iti ca abravīt kruddhena śaṅkukarṇena vṛtraḥ vai śāla tāḍitaḥ upetya pāde jagrāha śaṅku karṇam balī balāt śaṅkukarṇsam gṛhītvā tu vṛtraḥ nāgaḥ iva aṇḍajam bhrāmayāmāsa vivaśam lokam mohaḥ iva udyataḥ śaṅkukarṇasya vṛtreṇa bhrāmyamāṇasya sarvaśas śarīrāt samadīryanta bhūṣaṇāni sahasraśas tam bhrāmyamāṇam prasamīkṣya devāḥ vṛtreṇa sarve ca tadā gaṇeśaḥ hā hā iti kṛtvā dhṛta śastra bāṇāḥ pradudruvuḥ tasya vimokṣaṇa artham āgacchataḥ tān prasamīkṣya vṛtraḥ sarvān gaṇeśān śiti śastra hastān mumoca tam saṃsadi śaṅku karṇam nāgam garutmān iva pakṣirājaḥ vṛtra muktaḥ tu gaṇapaḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ mahā balaḥ yoddhu kāmaḥ punar vṛtram nivṛttaḥ hasti rāj iva catvāriṃśottaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ekacatvāriṃśat uttara śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śaṅku karṇam bhrāmayitvā vṛtraḥ tyaktvā ca bhū tale mamarda pramatha anīkam vanam mattaḥ yathā gajaḥ tam śūlena mahā kāyaḥ nandī vajreṇa dānavam somanandī kuṭhāreṇa nandiṣeṇaḥ talena ca bāṇānām ca sahasreṇa viṭpatiḥ vṛtram āhave saḥ a arditaḥ gaṇa yūtha īśaiḥ dānavaḥ parvata upamaḥ atha maya bala mūka tāra jambhāḥ namuci gaṇa ilvala bāṇa bāṇa putrāḥ rucira kanaka cāru hāra śobhāḥ cala valāya ābharaṇāḥ mahā indra kalpāḥ diti vara tanaya ati hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ pramatha baleṣu caranti kāla rūpāḥ muśa lahala śarāva dārita āsyāḥ giri śikhara aśani vajra cūrṇita aṅgāḥ vraṇaja pṛṣata vipruṣa ukṣita āścyuta sita hāra vibhūṣaṇa srajaḥ visasṛjuḥ uru vega dāruṇāḥ dititanayāḥ śara vṛṣṭim ardanīm vimala śita visṛṣṭa bāṇa jālāḥ pramatha gaṇān praharanti daitya mukhyāḥ atha parigha śara asi paṭṭiśaiḥ kara vara yantra śata praniḥsṛtaiḥ giri śikhara nibhāḥ ca danti varyāḥ druta gamanāḥ bahavaḥ ca vāji mukhyāḥ iṣu vadana dṛḍha avatakṣitāḥ vraṇa ja samukṣita sūkṣma vāsasaḥ prasṛta nayana sattva jīvitāḥ danu tanayāḥ śataśas yama varuṇa dhaneśa vāsavāḥ bhaga vasu sūrya śaśāṅka mārutāḥ aśani śara śatahradā āvilam na tu virarāma raṇa anta durdinam ekacatvāriṃśa uttara śatatamaḥ dvicatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ dhanuṣām śrūyate śabdaḥ prāvṛṣ ambudhara upamaḥ garjatām ca gaja indrāṇām hreṣatām ca eva vājinām yuddha gāndharva raktānām nādāḥ ca amara rakṣasām śrotra āyāsa karāḥ ghorāḥ vajra aśani ravāḥ iva sa rathī kārmukī bāṇī kavacī kuṇḍalī tathā pramatha anīkam adahat śuṣkam tṛṇam iva analaḥ kārtasvana dhanuḥ muktāḥ kārtasvana mahā śarāḥ pramathān dārya niḥsaṅgān dārayanti raṇa avanim śalabhāḥ iva kedāra ānanayāḥ iva mānavān khagāḥ iva tarūn pakvān garuḍaḥ pannagān iva tathā te pṛthavaḥ bāṇāḥ kārtasvana dhanuḥ cyutāḥ pramathān vyākulīcakruḥ vāsa vṛkṣān iva aṇḍajāḥ śara vrātāḥ gaṇa anīke nipatanti girau iva praśānta vādya ninadam śara ghāta ativejitam gaṇeśvara balam jajñe bandhujīva vanam yathā pṛṣatān iva śārdūlaḥ tam aughān iva bhāskaraḥ tathā kārtasvanaḥ kruddhaḥ śara vajraiḥ su dāruṇaiḥ nirdadāha gaṇādhyakṣān lokān saṃvartakaḥ yathā gaṇeśvara balam dṛṣṭvā dagdham jagdham rujā āturam viṭpatiḥ kupitaḥ devaḥ kārtasvanam atha abravīt kārtasvana balam vīryam pratāpaḥ ca tava uttamaḥ kim etān abalām haṃsi dānava indra gaṇa īśvarān mayā kuruṣva saṃmardam mā nardaḥ paśya me balam kuṇḍala alaṃkṛtam te a adya daṃṣṭra aṅkura vibhūṣaṇam pātayāmi śiraḥ daitya tālāt vātaḥ phalam yathā yadi api tvā adya rakṣanti dānavāḥ sa andhakāḥ raṇe tathā api te hariṣyāmi prāṇān asura pāṃsana jvalamānaḥ sa tu śaraḥ ghṛta siktaḥ iva analaḥ gharma arka sadṛśaḥ bhāsā prādhāvat viṭpatim prati saḥ bhāsā yutaḥ bāṇaḥ saṃvartakaḥ iva analaḥ viṭpateḥ kaṅkaṇe magnaḥ niraye duṣkṛtī yathā tatas tam eva niṣkṛṣya dānava prahitam śaram sa viṭpati vinirmuktaḥ śaraḥ dānava nāśa kṛt dānavasya śiraḥ yantuḥ jahāra iṣu pathān daśa hate yantari tasya aśvāḥ capalāḥ śabalāḥ raṇe udbhrāntāḥ ratham ādāya śyenāḥ iva yathā āmiṣam kārtasvana ratham yāta kim āsata nigṛhṇata iti evam dānava indrāṇām babhūva ninadaḥ mahān kārtasvanaḥ dhanuṣpāṇiḥ abhidudrāva viṭpatim viṭpatiḥ pūryamāṇaḥ vyathām nā eva tadā agamat ā karṇāt kārmukam saḥ a atha vikṛṣya balavān balāt tān iṣūn śātayitvā tu patribhiḥ prāṇabhojanaiḥ pṛṣṭhatas dṛśyamāna āsyaiḥ śaraiḥ taiḥ dānavaḥ babhau atha asya kārmukam khaḍgam śarāvāpam ca pañcakam śara rāj sa rudra vara samprahitaḥ samara aṅgaṇe visṛta dhūma lavaḥ asura ānanam yudhi jahāra balāt kamalam yathā muniḥ udāra matiḥ tat areḥ mukham hṛtam udīkṣya tadā vaḍavāmukha agni damanena raṇe dvicatvāriṃśa uttara śatatamaḥ tricatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kārtasvanam arim hatvā kārtasvara mahā iṣuṇā dadāha viṭpatiḥ daityān analaḥ śalabhān iva sa vyāyata dhanuḥ devaḥ cāru kāñcana kuṇḍalaḥ jagarja iṣūn dānaveṣu sṛjan sūryaḥ karān iva te kāñcana mayaiḥ puṅkhaiḥ garuḍa aṅgaruha chadaiḥ daiva sṛṣṭāḥ iva anarthāḥ dānaveṣu apatan śarāḥ chinna ānanāḥ chinna karāḥ chinna pāda udara ūravaḥ dānavāḥ śataśas petuḥ kṣitau kṣitidharāḥ yathā pṛṣṭheṣu abhihatāḥ kecid kecid pārśveṣu dāritāḥ mṛgān iva ca śārdūlaḥ garuḍaḥ panagān iva kṛtaghnaḥ sukṛtāni iva tamāṃsi iva divākaraḥ tathā tān asurān devaḥ viṭpatiḥ pāvaka ardanaḥ anāśayata tīkṣṇa agraiḥ śaraiḥ vajra anala ānanaiḥ virathāḥ pātita gajāḥ śara ātura turaṅgamāḥ dhāvante dānavāḥ trastāḥ viṭpateḥ śara vejitāḥ atha dṛṣṭvā asura balam mukta śastra yaśaḥ umbaram ye ye bala utkaṭāḥ tatra prakhyātāḥ ca suretarāḥ abhidrutāḥ viṭpatinā siṃhena iva aitare mṛgāḥ prahrādaḥ ca anuhrādaḥ ca saṃhrādaḥ śini bāṣkalau vipracittiḥ tuhuṇḍuḥ ca huṇḍaḥ vakraḥ ca dānavaḥ ariṣṭaḥ ca eva riṣṭaḥ ca añjanaḥ rūśabhaḥ kubhaḥ kālaḥ ca kālanemiḥ ca kālakāvadanaḥ tathā hastiḥ vipākaḥ pākaḥ ca vikarṇaḥ śambhuḥ eva ca viṭpatim dudruvuḥ kruddhāḥ siṃhāḥ iva vineduṣaḥ te tam śūla upalaiḥ huṇḍaiḥ sāyakaiḥ ca aśani svanaiḥ toya vṛṣṭim yathā meghāḥ visṛjanti anala īritāḥ sasṛjuḥ dānavāḥ deve śara vṛṣṭim tathā eva te tām śastra vṛṣṭim āmitrīm amitra gaṇa mardanaḥ acchinat viṭpatiḥ tūrṇam samprītim kalahaḥ yathā nardamānāḥ iva ambhodāḥ giri varṣam sṛjanti uta mumucuḥ sāla saralān devadārūn ca viṭpatau viṭpatim vimukham dṛṣṭvā dānavaiḥ parvataiḥ citam na marṣeyuḥ bhīma balāḥ prakhyātāḥ ye gaṇeśvarāḥ somanandī ca nandī ca nandiṣeṇaḥ ca pārṣadaḥ prabhā mayaḥ vīrabhadraḥ sūrya āpyāyanaḥ eva ca pañcākṣaḥ kopapālaḥ ca trinetraḥ piṅgalekṣaṇaḥ rākṣasaḥ piṅgalaḥ ca eva śmaśānanilayaḥ ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ sa ca kuṇḍodaraḥ balī airāvata mukhaḥ ca eva annapālaḥ kapāladhṛk ete ca anye ca gaṇapāḥ śataśas śabditāḥ gaṇaiḥ viviśuḥ dānavān dagdhum drumān śuṣkān iva analāḥ triśūla cakra iṣu bhuśuṇḍi hastāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ yuddha dhiyaḥ pratīyuḥ teṣām ca teṣām ca tatas babhūva saṃsakta yuddham samara uddhatānām mada uddhatānām sahavāsitānām mahā gajānām iva kānaneṣu tam dānavānām sa gaṇa īśvarāṇām mukhya āhavam vīkṣya divaukasāḥ te ceruḥ nabhaḥ divya vimāna yānaiḥ sa hiṃsā nādāḥ sa tala abhighātāḥ tricatvāriṃśottaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ catuścatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ te a ati saṃrambha saṃyuktāḥ darpitāḥ pramatha asurāḥ śakti ullālita hastena kumāreṇa avaniṃjayaḥ kālanemiḥ kāla kalpaḥ viśākham samayodhayat yaḥ ca āditya rathāt cakram jahāra bala darpitaḥ naigameṣaḥ hayagrīvam sugrīvam dānava adhipam huṇḍaḥ vināyakam śūram ayodhayata dāvanaḥ piṅgalābhyām gaṇeśābhyām ilvakaḥ pilvakaḥ sa ca śaṅkukarṇena hrādaḥ tu hi anuhrādena viṭpatiḥ āditya āpyāyanaḥ rudraḥ saṃhrādena samāgataḥ kuṇḍodaraḥ ca yakṣa indraḥ ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ ca pārṣadaḥ bala ilvakābhyām saṃsaktau siṃhābhyām iva kuñjarau pañcākṣeṇa baliḥ sārdham rudreṇa āditya varcasā mayūraḥ vajra romāṇam kukkuṭaḥ muram āgamat śeṣāḥ hi api gaṇādhyakṣāḥ śeṣaiḥ daityaiḥ samāgatāḥ paraspareṇa saṃsaktāḥ gajāḥ siṃhaiḥ iva āhave dahyatām iva veṇūnām vijane kṛṣṇavartmanā abhūt taṭataṭā śabdaḥ śastrāṇām mā dravīḥ drava tiṣṭha iti paśya paśya iti vādinaḥ anyonyam abhijaghnuḥ te saṃsaktāḥ gaṇa dānavāḥ vapā medaḥ abhidigdha aṅgāḥ chinna ānana karoravaḥ dānavāḥ pramathāḥ ca eva hi adhāvan śastram akṣitāḥ ānanaiḥ urubhiḥ pādaiḥ kara danta īkṣaṇaiḥ api hāraiḥ vikīrṇaiḥ keyūraiḥ sraj ambara vibhūṣaṇaiḥ vināyakasya sa śaram tuhuṇḍuḥ sūrya tejasam tasya api hasataḥ vaktram bṛhat kuṇḍala maṇḍitam asinā tīkṣṇa dhāreṇa ciccheda sa vināyakaḥ tuhuṇḍam nihatam dṛṣṭvā huṇḍaḥ bhrātṛ vadha āturaḥ śaktim cikṣepa nāga āsye śakraḥ a aśanim iva acale vināyakasya sā śaktiḥ maṇau maṇi śata ācitā indranīlam maṇim prāpya rekhā cāmīkarī yathā sa huṇḍa śaktim kara puṣkareṇa nikṛṣya devaḥ ravi raśmi kalpām tayā eva huṇḍam sahasā jaghāna tasya anujaḥ krauñcam iva avanīdhram pramāpitau vīkṣya tuhuṇḍa huṇḍau vināyakena ari vināyakena balam samastam gaṇa nāyakānām unmatta gaṅgā pratimam babhūva catuścatvāriṃśa uttara śatatamaḥ pañcacatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vināyakena huṇḍe ca tuhuṇḍe ca pramāpite gaṇeśvara asurāṇām tat yuddham saṃkulam ābabhau asṛj sravaiḥ su rakta aṅgāḥ saṃdaṣṭa daśanacchadāḥ anyonyam abhisaṃjaghnuḥ śūla śakti ṛṣṭi paṭṭiśaiḥ śaktīnām kṣipyamāṇānām asīnām ca śrāvya tām nāmadheyānām dhanuṣām kūjatām api śrotra āyāsa karān śabdān niśāmya balinām varaḥ jambhaḥ bhrātṛ vadha amarṣī praviṣṭaḥ prāmatham balam vyāghra pūrvam triśūlena jambhaḥ bhittvā gaṇeśvaram śiraḥ a abhihatya śaktyā tu śeṣān daityān pradudruve tatas khyātāḥ khyāta vīrya yaśaḥ śrutāḥ pratīyuḥ asurān yuddhe śarabhāḥ kuñjarān iva tatas a asura gaṇa īśānām saṃnipātaḥ aabhavat mahān saṃghaṭṭaḥ iva vajrāṇām saha kāñcana parvataiḥ virocanaḥ ca andhakaḥ ca vavarṣatuḥ amarṣaṇau śara vṛṣṭīḥ su saṃrabdhau jala vṛṣṭīḥ iva ambudau saṃśoṣayat dīpta marīci maṇḍalaḥ yathā vivasvān jagataḥ kṣaye śukram prati prāpāya sārathe mām sa naḥ sadā suḥkha haraḥ guruḥ ca pañcacatvāriṃśa uttara śatatamaḥ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śukra antikam upāgamya idam āha nata ānanaḥ bhagavan tvām samāśritya vayam devān saha anugān gaṇayāmaḥ tṛṇaiḥ tulyān sadā satyam bravīmi aham kuñjarāḥ iva siṃhānām garuḍānām iva ahayaḥ asmākam bibhyati sadā devāḥ yuṣmad prasādataḥ durgam deva gaṇa vyūham bhavatā pratipālitāḥ viviśuḥ nirbhayāḥ daityāḥ hradam uṣṇa arditāḥ iva vayam tvad śaraṇāḥ bhūtvā pāṣāṇāḥ iva niścalāḥ sthitvā vadhāma niḥśaṅkāḥ brāhmaṇa indra indram āhave sa dārāḥ sa sutāḥ ca eva śuśrūṣāmaḥ divāniśam bhayeṣu satatam devān nārāyaṇaḥ iva aparaḥ paśya huṇḍam tuhuṇḍam ca kujambham jambham eva ca pākam kārtasvanam ca eva vipākam ca mahā asuram tam ca indra damanam śūram śūra amara nipātanam sūditān patitān etān hariṇaiḥ iva candanān yā pītvā kaṇadhūmam vai sahasram śaradām purā vidyā harāt varā prāptā tasyāḥ kālaḥ āgataḥ atha vidyā phalam tat te jīvayānasya dānavān paśyantu pramathāḥ sarve lokāḥ ca utphulla locanāḥ tvayā saṃjīvitān dṛṣṭvā dānavāḥ dānavān yudhi vidyā kila tvayā sā vai dānavānām hita arthinā ārādhya devam samprāptā tām darśaya namaḥ tava īṣat smitam tadā kṛtvā dānava adhipam abravīt vidyā upārjanam etat hi dānavānām mayā kṛtam pītvā varṣa sahasram vai kaṇadhūmam su duḥsaham eṣā prāptā mayā vidyā bāndhavānām sukha āvahā utthāpayiṣye sasyāni mlānāni ambudharaḥ yathā asmin muhūrte draṣṭāsi dānavān dānava adhipa utthitān dānavān dṛṣṭvā hatān yuddhe gaṇeśvaraiḥ vismayāt ca bhayāt ca eva draviṣyanti gaṇeśvarāḥ āvartamānayā tatra vudyayā brāhmaṇena ha uttasthuḥ dānavāḥ suptāḥ śayanāt iva nidrayā veda arthāḥ iva ca abhyastāḥ samayena iva ca ambudāḥ kālena pralayam prāptau yathā vā dhūmaketavaḥ tathā śukreṇa te daityāḥ pramathaiḥ saṃniṣūditāḥ utthāpyamānāḥ vibabhuḥ yathā svasthāḥ purātanāḥ śukreṇa ujjīvitān dṛṣṭvā dānavān tān gaṇeśvarāḥ ujjīvitān tu tān dṛṣṭvā tuhuṇḍa ādyān mahā asurān vineduḥ pūrvadevāḥ te jala mattāḥ iva ambudāḥ tān utthitān vīkṣya sahasraśas aanye kuṭhāra vajra aśani śūla hastāḥ pradudruvuḥ śaṃkara kiṃkarāṇām balam samuddhūta mahā arṇava ābham samāgamaḥ tatra punar babhūva gaṇa asurāṇām ati bhīma nādaḥ yuga atyate māruta vejitānām yathā samudyogaḥ iva arṇavānām ṣaṭcatvāriṃśottaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ saptacatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ utthāpiteṣu daityeṣu bhārgaveṇa ugra karmaṇā neduḥ devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ dānavāḥ ca saha andhakāḥ tatas śaṅkha rava unmiśrāḥ māḍu kānaka nisvanāḥ babhūvuḥ siṃhanādāḥ ca ratha hasti ravaiḥ saha huṇḍa tuhuṇḍau jambhaḥ ca kujambhaḥ ca mahā asuraḥ śaila śūla śilā ghātaiḥ yuyudhuḥ devatā arayaḥ mamarduḥ pramatha anīkam vairam praticikīrṣayā teṣām vegam saṃnivārya pramathāḥ api darpitāḥ śilā taru karāḥ sarve dānavān abhidudruvuḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ surāṇām tu tasmin yuddhe a ati bhairave śrūyante dhanuṣām śabdāḥ ratha śabdāḥ ca bhairavāḥ pramathānām jaye saktāḥ dānavānām tathā apare cakruḥ kolāhalam ghoram pakṣa vādān tathā ambare garjatām dhāvatām ca eva balānām samabhūt svanaḥ garjatām dhāvatām ca eva samudrāṇām iva atyaye yuddha atiśaya mattāḥ ca siddha gandharva cāraṇāḥ neduḥ ca eva utsasarjuḥ ca nānā kusuma saṃcayān nānāvidhāni puṣpāṇi patamānāni rejire siddha cāraṇa muktāni nakṣatrāṇi yathā atyaye yuddha saṃsakta bhāvānām viremuḥ ca punar punar tam āpatantam dṛṣṭvā tu dānavam jambham āhave utkṣipya dānavam yuddhe tatāḍa sa vināyakaḥ śṛṅgayoḥ acala indrasya taḍitvān iva ca āmnudaḥ sa śara āroṣita manāḥ vidhūya sa śiraḥkaram vināyakam śaraiḥ ugraiḥ avatastāra roṣitaḥ śalabhāḥ iva kedāram bhramarāḥ iva pādapam rudhiram kṣaramāṇāḥ te trivittraiḥ dārita ānanāḥ śarāḥ vināyake rejuḥ sarpāḥ merum iva āśritāḥ dhunvan kara agram ca śiraḥ ca devaḥ dudrāva jambham tṛṣitaḥ yathā ambhaḥ sa tam kara agreṇa dṛḍham dṛḍhena muhur samāhatya muhur vinadya ratham gṛhītvā balavān tadā ājau cikṣepa sa aśva dhvaja śastra cakram sa uddhūta bhagna ati patāka ketuḥ cyuta asi śakti ṛṣṭi sahasra bāṇaḥ patīṣyamāṇam tu ratham vihāya prahrādiḥ indra ambudhara prabhāvaḥ sa tām sa ghaṇṭām kanaka avadātām kṛśānu lekhām iva dīpyamānām vināyakāya asura rāja putraḥ cikṣepa śaktim samudīrṇa śaktiḥ sā khāt patantī bhujaga aṅganā iva śastra aṅganā prajvalamāna vaktrā śara āhatā viṭpatinā papāta śaktiḥ yathā agryā puruṣe hata āśe āścarya bhūte pramatha asurāṇām tasmin tathā vartati yuddha yajñe amarṣitaḥ bhārgava karma dṛṣṭvā śilāda putraḥ aabhyagamat maheśam gaṇeśvarāṇām raṇa karma deva devaiḥ saha indraiḥ api duṣkaram yat tat bhārgaveṇa adya kṛtam vṛthā naḥ saṃjīvayānena hi dānava indrān ete hi te dānava yūtha pālāḥ yama ālayāt adya punar nivṛttāḥ vidrāvayantaḥ pramathān caranti nāgān iva ājau śarabhāḥ sa darpāḥ jayaḥ kutas vai bhavitā maheśa gaṇeśvarāṇām kutas eva śāntiḥ vakra sthitaḥ ca eṣa na ca eṣa vadhyaḥ a yudhyamānaḥ vṛṣa vāha śukraḥ na eva abhināśaḥ tava prasādāt hatam ca tam tvam kuruṣe prasādam iti evam uktaḥ pramatheśvareṇa nandīśvareṇa īśvaradevadevaḥ uvāca devaḥ prahasan tadānīm sa nandinam sarva gaṇeśa nāyakam madhyāt samutpāṭya tam ānayasva yathopahāram dhanavān namuṣyaḥ saḥ evam uktaḥ vṛṣabhadhvajena vṛṣadhvajaḥ vai vṛṣa siṃha nādaḥ jagāma tūrṇam pravigāhya senām yatra abhavat bhārgava vaṃśa dīpaḥ tam rakṣamāṇam diti nandanaiḥ taiḥ pāśa asi vṛkṣa upala śūla hastaiḥ vikṣobhya daityān vṛṣarāj jahāra śukram sa nandī śarabhaḥ yathā ibham srasta ambaram tam cyuta bhūṣaṇam ca vimukta keśam ripuṇā gṛhītam vimokṣayiṣyantaḥ iva abhyadhāvan surārayaḥ siṃha ravān sṛjantaḥ te vajra śūla iṣu paraśvadhānām sa cakra daṇḍa upala kampanānām nandīśvarasya upari dānava indrāḥ varṣam vavarṣuḥ jaladāḥ iva ugrāḥ sa bhārgavam prāpya gaṇādhipa agryaḥ vaktra agninā śastra śatāni dagdhvā āyāt sa śukram tu kare gṛhītvā nandīśvaraḥ dānava yūtha pālam teṣām ca teṣām ca tatas babhūva pramukta śastra astra su bhīma pātaḥ jahi iti gṛhṇa iti ca vādinām vai mahā āhavaḥ deva manaḥ pratoṣaḥ tena antareṇa etya bhavasya pārśvam nandīśvaraḥ krodha vivarṇa netraḥ ayam sa śukraḥ bhagavan iti īśe nivedayāmāsa bhavāya śīghram saptacatvāriṃśa uttara śatatamaḥ aṣṭacatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śukre aatha śukra patinā gīrṇe aannā iva bhujaṅginā babhūvuḥ dānavāḥ sarve daridrāḥ iva niṣkriyāḥ viśarīrāḥ yathā jīvāḥ garuḍāḥ virayāḥ iva vihastāḥ iva mātaṅgāḥ viśṛṅgāḥ iva go vṛṣāḥ nirviṣāḥ iva nāga indrāḥ nirvidyāḥ iva ca dvijāḥ sāgarāḥ iva nistoyāḥ vivegāḥ iva mārutāḥ payodāḥ iva niḥśabdāḥ viśikhāḥ iva ca agnayaḥ gata utsavāḥ vaḥ divasāḥ vipuṣpāḥ iva pādapāḥ hariṇāḥ iva saṃtrastāḥ vipakṣāḥ iva pakṣiṇaḥ grahāḥ iva praśānta ābhāḥ grāhāḥ iva jala uddhṛtāḥ nandinā apahṛte śukre gīrṇe ca api kapardinā dānavāḥ jajñire śūrāḥ dīna māna parākramāḥ vaimanasyam param prāptaḥ dānavānām raṇe uvāca megha ninadaḥ saṃyuga sthaḥ sa dānavaḥ vikramya nandinā śukram nayatā nayinām varam hṛtāni naḥ sarveṣām jīvitāni na saṃśayaḥ bhārgavam tam ṛte śukram kaḥ a anyaḥ naḥ dhārayiṣyati dhairyam ca vikramaḥ tejaḥ sattvam vīryam balam dhṛtiḥ śatrubhiḥ naḥ hṛtam sarvam deve śukre a apavāhite na tu aham saṃyugam jahyām pramathaiḥ samabhidrutaḥ sūdayiṣyāmi aham sarvān pramathān saha nandinā adya etān vivaśān kṛtvā hatvā ca tridaśān api bhārgavam mokṣayiṣyāmi pañjara stham yathā harim śarīrāt niṣkramet tasya asmākam śeṣa pālinaḥ iti andhaka vacaḥ śrutvā dānavāḥ megha nardanāḥ pramathān nardayāmāsuḥ martavya kṛta niścayāḥ tatra ṣāṇāśi vajra oghaiḥ kaṭaṅkaṭa śilā upalaiḥ kārmukāṇām vikṛṣṭānām visṛṣṭānām ca patriṇām nipātyatām asīnām ca śabdaḥ aabhūt bhṛśa dāruṇaḥ bhagna dhvaja patākāni kṣīṇa praharaṇāni ca rudhira āsrāva citrāṇi vraṇa ākusumitāni ca pipāsitāni śrāntāni hata vāji gajāni ca sa tūṇīra patākena aṅkuśa āroṣitena ca jambhaḥ dānava śārdūlaḥ abhidudrāva nandinam kṛṣṇā parvata śṛṅga sthaḥ sa balākaḥ iva ambudaḥ stabdha lāṅgūla dṛś karṇaḥ prasārita mahā karaḥ turaṅgāḥ ye ca mātaṅgāḥ pramathāḥ ye ca dānavāḥ tasya mārgāt apakrāntāḥ mṛtyoḥ iva yathā narāḥ tam matta nāgam dhāvantam nadantam iva nīradam vārayāmāsa balavān vikramya sa vināyakaḥ athā āśvasya ca viśramya saṃvartya ātma karam karī vināyakam uraḥ deśe tāḍayāmāsa nardayan sa vindhya kūṭa kalpena tena nāgena tāḍitaḥ nāsayā sa gṛhītvā tam nāsāyām dānava dvipam ākṣipya pātayāmāsa giri varṣmā vināyakaḥ tam nāgam pātayānam tu nāga vaktram asṛj sravam bibheda tomareṇa āśu kareṇa arkaḥ iva ambudam mocayantam tu caraṇau grīvāyām dānava uttamam tena eva tomareṇa atha ājaghāna vināyakaḥ punar ca asya vadha ākāṅkṣī asim jagrāha vīryavān tam ca api su vikṛṣṭena śareṇa asṛj bhujā tadā sa dṛḍha abhihataḥ tena ghūrṇitaḥ sāla vṛkṣa vat airāvataḥ iva ābhāti bala udvṛttaḥ vināyakaḥ vyaṃsaḥ tam dhāvamānam tu kujambha vadha kāṅkṣiṇam vavāra sa gataḥ pātayāmāsa tam kṣitau vyaṃsam aṃsena hatvā tu nāgavaktraḥ mahā balaḥ tribhiḥ prahāraiḥ sa babhau śoṇita aktaḥ vināyakaḥ dharāyām nāsayā ādāya kujambham tu vināyakaḥ pracikṣepa mahā vīryaḥ yathā bhūta balim naraḥ saḥ a arditaḥ dānava śataiḥ nānā āyudha vitakṣitaḥ cacāra devaḥ daityeṣu pṛṣateṣu yathā hariḥ sa dantaiḥ caraṇaiḥ ca api śuṇḍayā ātatayā api ca mamarda dānavān kruddhaḥ kuñjaraḥ naḍvalān iva tatas gaṇeśāḥ hi api vīkṣya dānavaiḥ vināyakam śastra śataiḥ parikṣatam gṛhīta śastrāḥ gaja siṃha vikramāḥ vimukta rāvāḥ śataśas tatas punar śastra sahasra vejitam śara asi śakti ṛṣṭi nipāta duḥsaham gaṇa asurāṇām asu nāśanam mahat babhūva yuddham hata vāji kuñjaram aṣṭacatvāriṃśa uttara śatatamaḥ ūnapañcāśat uttara śatatamaḥ nigīrṇaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ saḥ candra avayava dhāriṇā katham ca tapasām śreṣṭhaḥ yogī yogena sa dvijaḥ na niḥsṛtaḥ yoga balāt deva dehāt mahā tapāḥ andhakaḥ ca asura śreṣṭhaḥ sa tadā bhārgavam vinā cakāra katham āvāpam gaṇeśaiḥ samabhidrutaḥ kathayasva na me tṛptiḥ śṛṇvānasya īśa ceṣṭitam sūtaḥ uvāca nigīrṇe bhārgave tena bhūtomādeva bandhunā dṛṣṭvā sva sainyam pramathaiḥ bhajyamānam punar punar dudrāva ratham āsthāya svayam eva andhakaḥ gaṇān pramathāḥ petira vanyām nistoyāḥ iva toyadāḥ kroḍeṣu ūru kapoleṣu pṛṣṭha bāhu udareṣu ca ruruvuḥ bāṇa nirbhinnāḥ pramathāḥ kuñjarāḥ yathā yāntam āyāntam aprāptam prāptam dūra stham eva ca apaśyat yam yatas tam tam nirbibheda śaraiḥ bhṛśam sahasram ca sahasreṇa koṭim koṭyā tathā eva ca dhvajāḥ patākāḥ chitrāṇi vaijayantyaḥ a aṅkuśāḥ kuthāḥ cāmarāṇi kirīṭāni kuṇḍalāni ambarāṇi ca tat sarvam cicchide tūrṇam śaraiḥ andhaka dānavaḥ visphuliṅgān yathā eva agniḥ dhārā sārān yathā ambudaḥ sindhurājaḥ yathā udgārān karān iva divākaraḥ nādān siṃhāḥ iva araṇye sīkarān iva kuñjarāḥ mumoca bāṇān tīkṣṇa agrān para sainya vimardanān nivāta kavacāḥ ye te anyonya sadṛśāḥ bhṛśam kāleyāḥ ṣaṣṭi sāhasrāḥ kāla kalpāḥ mahā asurāḥ bāhujaiḥ ṣaṣṭi sāhasraiḥ pramathaiḥ yuyudhuḥ saha prahrādaḥ ca anuhrādaḥ ca saṃhrādaḥ śini bāṣkalau virocanaḥ baliḥ bāṇaḥ kujambhaḥ a atha avaniṃjayaḥ ekādaśā ete prakhyātāḥ ekādaśa ravi prabhāḥ ekādaśa eva pramathān ardayan kalaha eṣiṇaḥ prabhā mayam vīrabhadram viṭpatim piṅgalam tathā vegapam pavanādam ca soma arka āpyāyanau api saṃvarttaka analam ca eva pāvaka āpyāyanau api yakṣaḥ aanna daḥ ca balavān vidyutkeśaḥ ca rākṣasaḥ vihasta śastra kavaca āvṛtāḥ śastra śata ācitāḥ dvārapālāḥ ca rudrāṇām rudrāṇām ye ca sūnavaḥ skanda pāriṣadāḥ ye ca ye ca śakti gaṇa īśvarāḥ te danoḥ tanayaiḥ sārdham danoḥ putra anvayāḥ ca ye cakruḥ kṛtānta sadṛśāḥ kalaham kalaha praiyāḥ tasmin tathā vartati samprahāre viśīrṇa hāra ābharaṇa sraj astraiḥ vyāviddha vastrāḥ vikasat sunetrāḥ neduḥ surāḥ siddha gaṇāḥ ca kha sthāḥ ūnapañcāśat uttara śatatamaḥ pañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca māyā vīryam ca vīryam ca andhakasya amara dviṣaḥ sṛṣṭam bhagavatā samyak deva rūpa nimitta jam nigīrṇaḥ yasya devena śarīre bhārgavaḥ muniḥ katham tu kṛtavān tatra devadeva śarīra gaḥ katham ca tapasaḥ vīryāt yoga vīryāt ca sa dvijaḥ śveta abhrāt iva vai candraḥ niḥsṛtaḥ bhṛgu nandanaḥ kathaya īśāna caritam bhārgavasya ca dhīmataḥ sūtaḥ uvāca sa lokān agni varṇa ābhān rudra koṭi śataiḥ vṛtān kunda indu śaṅkha varṇānām daṃṣṭriṇām nakhinām api dīrgha lāṅgūla juṣṭānām sa darpāṇām kṣamāvatām jvalana prabha keśānām nandyāvartaka dhāriṇām kiṃśuka prabha jihvānām kailāsa giri varṣmaṇām agni bandhana baddhānām siṃhānām bhīma rūpiṇām surān ca sa indrān sa ādityān sa apsaraḥ gaṇa mānavān gaṇeśa asura yuddham ca saḥ aapaśyat hara deha gaḥ varṣāṇām tu śatam kakṣau bhramamāṇaḥ bhavasya saḥ na tasya dadṛśe chidram śuceḥ iva yathā kaliḥ atha śabdaḥ mahān āsīt pramatha asura sainyayoḥ tam śrutvā śabdam āvignaḥ bhārgavaḥ pratibodhitaḥ tuṣṭāva iṣṭaiḥ stavaiḥ devam sa umam soma vibhūṣaṇam āpad bhāvam prapannasya tasya devena śūlinā liṅgena niṣkamasva iti prasāda abhyudayaḥ kṛtaḥ sūkṣma rūpaḥ tatas bhūtvā sa śukraḥ muni sattamaḥ śukra vat niḥsṛtaḥ liṅgāt devadevasya dhīmataḥ śakra vat niḥsṛtaḥ yasmāt śiśnāt bhārgava nandanaḥ tasmāt śukraḥ iti khyātim gataḥ gatimatām varaḥ viveśa dānava anīkam megha anīkam śaśī yathā tam dṛṣṭvā candra saṃkāśam candra udaya nibha udayam candra udaye yathā nR̥ṇām prītiḥ āsīt suradviṣām te dṛṣṭvā danu daiteyāḥ śukram candra sama prabham sarve siṃha ravān cakruḥ samprahṛṣṭāḥ yuyutsavaḥ nihatāḥ dānavāḥ ye tu pramathaiḥ jita kāśibhiḥ tān āgatān mṛtyu mukhāt menire bhārgava āgamāt vavanduḥ tam nananduḥ ca praseduḥ ca mahā asurāḥ śukra udaya mudam lebhe sa dānava mahā arṇavaḥ atha śākhaḥ viśākhaḥ ca chāgavaktraḥ caturmukhaḥ nandī ca somanandī ca nandiṣeṇaḥ ca vīryavān ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ kuṇḍodara mahodarau saṃvartaka anala ūrvau ca yaśodīptaḥ vibhākaraḥ vegapaḥ ca śikhaṇḍī ca tāmracūḍaḥ ca kukkuṭaḥ annadaḥ piṅgalaḥ yakṣaḥ piṅgalaḥ ca vaṭuḥ paṭuḥ vidyutkeśaḥ sukeśaḥ ca rākṣasau ca aparājitau ete ca anye ca gaṇapāḥ lokapāla sama tviṣaḥ viviśuḥ dānava anīkam śukra udaya samuddhatam atha vāditra śabdāḥ tu suṃhanāda ravaiḥ saha babhūvuḥ senayoḥ ugrāḥ sarva bhūta prakampanāḥ nandīśvaram puraskṛtya kārttikeyam ca ṣaṇmukham mṛdranti pramathāḥ daityān sarpān tārkṣyaḥ iva āhave asi pāta avalūna agrāḥ muśala āhata mastakāḥ dānavāḥ śerate bhūmau vajra bhinnāḥ iva acalāḥ rirṅguḥ samare daityāḥ sarpāḥ tārkṣya arditāḥ iva bhagna trika ūru jaghanāḥ ghana bāṇa avapīḍitāḥ daityāḥ viniṣṭananti ārttāḥ iva ambudāḥ tasmin gaṇapa daityānām mathane bhṛśa dāruṇe babhūva pūrṇā daityānām dharā dyauḥ iva nīradaiḥ kirīṭaiḥ mukuṭaiḥ hāraiḥ valaya ābharaṇa aṅgadaiḥ pārihāryaiḥ sa keyūraiḥ śroṇī sūtraiḥ sa kuṇḍalaiḥ rakta kuṅkuma citra aṅgī nānā ābharaṇa bhūṣaṇā dhana āḍhyā strīḥ iva ābhāti tatra tatra raṇa avaniḥ siṃhānām iva dṛptānām hastinām api vā yathā utsāhaḥ abhūt gaṇeśānām dānavān sampramardatām te hanyamāna aśaraṇāḥ bhaya ārttāḥ śaraṇa arthinaḥ pramathaiḥ anubaddhāḥ ca dānavāḥ sāgaram śritāḥ dṛṣṭvā tat recitam sainyam dānavaiḥ pramatha arditaiḥ praviṣṭeṣu ca daityeṣu sāgaram makara ālayam bhārgavaḥ su mahā tejāḥ yathā agniḥ iva mūrchitaḥ sa samudra ālayān daityān śaśāpa kupitaḥ bhṛśam yasmāt sahāyān utsṛjya mām ca api pitṛ vat hitam prāṇa trāṇa artham abalāḥ praviṣṭāḥ stha payonidhim tasmāt tatra eva nirhrīkāḥ mama śāpa parikṣatāḥ mīna bhāvam anuprāptāḥ jāta ajātāḥ bhaviṣyatha yāvat lokāḥ bhaviṣyanti parvatāḥ ca sa sāgarāḥ tāvat yūyam jale matsyāḥ bhaviṣyatha jalecarāḥ nara māṃsa aśanāḥ pāpāḥ nara bhakṣyāḥ bhaviṣyatha kṣapayiṣyatha mad śāpam varṣa koṭī śatāni uta iti śāpa hatān śeṣān kṛtvā arṇava jalaukasaḥ virarāma mahā tejāḥ śukraḥ candra sama dyutiḥ tatas te vā ardhi toyeṣu guru śāpa hata asurāḥ sa āyudhāḥ sa tanutrāḥ ca dṛśyante daṃśitāḥ ca ha uvāca pāṇinā spṛśya jīvayan iva tam girā mā bhaiḥ tvam dānava śreṣṭha pratiyudhyasva śatruṣu aham tvām dhārayiṣyāmi āhāre iva jīvitam iti evam uktaḥ śukreṇa saḥ a andhakaḥ dānava īśvaraḥ tatas praviṣṭeṣu asureṣu sāgaram nihanyamāneṣu ca śaṅkara anugaiḥ dadhāra sarvān pramathān tadā andhakaḥ nadīnadān bhūri jalaḥ yathā arṇavaḥ viśākaśākhau daśabhiḥ śatena ca sa naigameṣam pratutoda dānavaḥ sa vīrabhadram ca tathā ca viṭpatim prabhā mayam yakṣa varam ca piṅgalam bibheda bāṇaiḥ tapanīya bhūṣaṇaiḥ yathā aṅkuśa agraiḥ iva hastipaḥ gajam śarān na yaḥ dhārayate pradīpta kāla anala sūrya sannibhān vivṛścitāḥ candana vat gaṇeśvarāḥ bhuja udare vakṣasi mūrdhni ca asakṛt tatas aasuraiḥ siṃha ravāḥ tadā kṛtāḥ sa śaṅkha bherī śata dundubha utkaṭāḥ punar ca yuddham prababhau bhayānakam gaṇa īśvarāṇām saha dānava īśvaraiḥ pañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ ekapañcāśat uttara śatatamaḥ tridaśa adhipatim śakram iti uvāca pitāmahaḥ asau vikṛṣṭa cāpaḥ ca sa indrāyudha ghana upamaḥ sṛjati iṣu mayam varṣam andhakaḥ kṣapayan ripūn kṣamamāṇāḥ hi atiṣṭhadhvam kasmāt etat parājayam jitvā hi eṣa gaṇān sarvān andhakaḥ dānava īśvaraḥ asmākam api mūlāni nirmūlāni kariṣyati tat yāvat eṣa naḥ bāṇaiḥ pramathān nayati kṣayam tāvat eva vayam pārṣṇim gṛhṇāma kṛttivāsasaḥ svayambhu vacanam śrutvā bala vṛta nibarhaṇaḥ gṛhīta varma śastra astrāḥ śīghram śighra parākramāḥ sāhāyyam karavāma adya gaṇānām yudhyatām raṇe pūṣā aryamā bhagaḥ mitraḥ yamaḥ ca ravinandanaḥ aṃśaḥ tvaṣṭā jayaḥ ca eva jayantaḥ ca eva śakra jaḥ marutaḥ vasavaḥ sādhyāḥ tathā aśvi garut oragāḥ tuṣitāḥ ca eva lekhāḥ ca viśvedevāḥ ca guhyakāḥ gandharvāḥ ca eva yakṣāḥ ca ye ca anye deva pakṣiṇaḥ atha dundubhi śabdāḥ ca siṃhanādāḥ ca bhairavāḥ babhūvuḥ deva sainyeṣu pramathānām priyaṃkarāḥ devaiḥ patadbhiḥ tat sainyam dānavānām viloḍitam prabhūta mīnam kṣīṇa ambu rājahaṃsaiḥ yathā saraḥ tatas halahalā śabdaḥ saṃjajñe devatā adhyuṣite sainye dānavānām samākule janyate dānava anīkam ajā vṛka śataiḥ iva okāraḥ iva vedānām teṣām āsīt puraḥsaraḥ duritāni tu sarvāṇi prāyaścitta analaḥ yathā krodha rāga andhaḥ dānavān dānava adhipaḥ utpādya vairam rudreṇa sarva loka abhirakṣaṇā na śakyam pramathān jetum anirviṇṇaiḥ saha amarān maraṇāt ca na bhetavyam yudhyadhvam daitya dānavāḥ bhārgavaḥ tiṣṭhati hi eṣa yaḥ naḥ saṃjīvayiṣyati tat vai yūyam deva gaṇa īśvarān yathābalam yathotsāham vārayadhvam a śaṅkitāḥ māyābhiḥ etān bahvībhiḥ gūḍābhiḥ gūḍha rūpiṇaḥ cakruḥ ghorāṇi kalpa ante nīradāḥ iva dhanuḥ śabdān prakurvāṇāḥ siṃhanāda ravān tathā vikṛṣya tu mahā cāpam sāgara ambuda nardanaḥ tam durvāram dhāvamāna vārayāmāsa śaila adriḥ dharma cittam iva aśubham gāḍham vidāritaḥ tena dānavena gaṇeśvaraḥ saṃjughūrṇa tadā nandī vāyu nunnaḥ yathā drumaḥ ghūrṇamānaḥ babhau nandī mṛṣṭa kuṇḍala bhūṣaṇaḥ calat pallava puṣpa āḍhyaḥ yathā aśoka taruḥ tathā tatas cirāt samāśvasya suyaśāḥ suyaśā patiḥ hasataḥ tasya netrābhyām su bhrūbhyām aśru bindavaḥ nyasravanta yathā arkasya kiraṇāḥ dīpta maṇḍalāt tam dhāvamānam ākāśe taru māruta vījitāḥ tam api asya andhakaḥ bāṇaiḥ cāru kāñcana bhūṣaṇaiḥ cakarta dhartā lokānām diti garbham yathā ahi hā vṛkṣe kṛtte tatas nandī sa mṛga vyāla pannagam mandara agram samutpāṭya dudrāva andhakam āhave girikūṭam tu tam nandī girikūṭa vana ālayaḥ sa rathaḥ tena śṛṅgeṇa nandinā dṛḍham āhataḥ sa cakra kūbara hayaḥ pāṃsu sāyujyam āgamat tatas aandhaka ratham dṛṣṭvā sa cakra akṣam vicūrṇitam neduḥ devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ pramathāḥ ca sa guhyakāḥ nandinam tāḍayāmāsa gaja indraḥ iva pādapam triśūli dayitaḥ tena triśūlena abhitāḍitaḥ nandīśvare ghūrṇamāne prahāreṇa bhṛśa ardite asurāṇām bale jajñe simha nāda ravaḥ muhur siṃhanādena śatrūṇām tena nandī prabodhitaḥ paraśvadha hataḥ raktam cakṣara andhaka dānavaḥ andhakam viratham dṛṣṭvā rarakṣuḥ amara dviṣaḥ āśāsu avasthitāḥ lokam imam tathā atha bāṇaḥ baleḥ putraḥ bāṇa puṣpa sama prabhaḥ sa tam ratham dānava indraḥ āruroha tadā andhakaḥ yathā udayam tu bhagavān dinakṛt pūrṇa maṇḍalaḥ dvipañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ viṣṇum ardayamānam tu dānavān dānava ardanam jambhaḥ iva ārāvam kṛtvā dudrāva dānavaḥ na sa saṃvivije devaḥ siṃhaḥ dṛṣṭvā iva kuñjaram kujambhaḥ ca eva jambhaḥ ca yavīyān dānava acalaḥ anantam antam śatrūṇām āvavāra rarāsa ca vṛtraḥ saṃvarttaka nikāśa dṛś jighṛkṣuḥ abhyagāt idram nadamānaḥ payoda vat tam dhāvantam nadantam ca dānavam śata locanaḥ kuhare girī saṃkāśam ājaghāna purandaraḥ bhāvayatyaḥ gadā yodhī śata āyum vāyum āhave tuhuṇḍa huṇḍau aśvibhyām ayudhyetām mahā asurau prahlādena bhagaḥ sārdham aṃśena ca virocanaḥ aryamāṇam yamam ca eva ayudhyetām bilva kelvalau vipracitti mukhāḥ ye ca baliṣu agrāḥ mahā asurāḥ gaṇeśvarān te devān ca ayudhyanta sahasraśas tatakṣe vatsa radanaiḥ śaraiḥ kārmuka niḥsṛtaiḥ saḥ aandhakena dṛḍham viddhaḥ śaraiḥ marma vidāraṇaiḥ rarāsa nandī saṃrabdhaḥ payodaḥ iva saṃkṣaye vajreṇa śatadhāreṇa saḥ a andhakasya gaṇeśvaraḥ cūrṇayāmāsa turagān niyantāram ratham tathā tatas a andhakam karṇa mūle kuṇḍala alaka śobhite ājaghāna ghana ārāvaḥ vara daḥ cāru kuṇḍalaḥ pātitaḥ nandinaḥ kroḍe kuñjareṇa iva saṃyuge apāsarpat padāni aṣṭau tāni eva āpatitaḥ punar sa tena su prahāreṇa dānavam prati roṣitaḥ vajreṇa śatadhāreṇa khaṇḍaśas pracakāra ha bāhu pāśena ca eva enam baddhvā bhūtapatiḥ svayam iyeṣa bhūmau niṣpeṣṭum andhakaḥ ca avamocayat sa mocayitvā hi ātmānam māyām āsthāya mohanīm abhidudrāva śailādim tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca ūcivān tam āpatantam vegena gaṇeśvara mahattarāḥ ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ vīrabhadraḥ sa ca devaḥ prabhā mayaḥ bhartāram abhirakṣantaḥ teṣām pāriṣada agragāḥ andhakam yodhayanti sma siṃhāḥ śakra gajam yathā tam nandiṣeṇaḥ śūlena somanandī ca muṣṭinā śareṇa vīrabhadraḥ ca ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ aasinā api ca śaṅku karṇaḥ cala agreṇa pādapena prabhā mayaḥ nandīśvaraḥ tu gaṇapaḥ gaṇapaiḥ vimukhīkṛtam ājaghāna uttamāṅge tu andhakam dānava adhipam dṛṣṭvā surapatim devaiḥ gaṇapaiḥ samabhidrutam asurāṇām bale jajñe dhāva gṛhṇa iti nisvanaḥ tān yuddhāya āgatān ekaḥ viṣṇuḥ sarvān adīdharat cakra hastam tu dṛṣṭvā evam vikrāntam raṇa mūrdhani vyāyacchamānam niśceṣṭam pradhāvantam pragarjitam yam yatas paśyate a asau vai tam tam vivyādha sāyakaiḥ pṛthavaḥ pīta niśitāḥ garuḍa aṅgaruhandharāḥ andhakasya śarāḥ ghorāḥ cyavante dhanuṣaḥ a akṣayāḥ mukheṣu dantaveṣṭeṣu udareṣu kareṣu ca devam nārāyaṇam ca anye nandinam ca apare gaṇāḥ anye śākham viśākham ca kumāram api ca apare vyapāśritya sthitāḥ devāḥ śakuntāḥ iva pādapān yathā aśani bhayāt martyāḥ yathā siṃha bhayāt mṛgāḥ yathā ca garuḍāt nityam bhujagāḥ bhujaga āśinaḥ vitresuḥ sura jāla ārttāḥ mūḍhāḥ iva ca babhramuḥ tathā vraṇa ja sikta aṅgam tat babhau pārṣadam balam kampante pādapāḥ yadvat kānaneṣu anila īritāḥ tathā andhaka bhayāt devāḥ santrastāḥ raṇa mūrdhani tatas nārāyaṇaḥ aanantaḥ ūrjitaḥ śakraḥ eva ca aśvinau vasavaḥ ca aṣṭau ādityāḥ dvādaśa eva ca nandī viśākhaḥ śākhaḥ ca vīrabhadraḥ prabhā mayaḥ viṭpatiḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ ca somanandī vināyakaḥ dudruvuḥ sa āyudhāḥ devāḥ tam dānava gaṇa adhipam cakrāyudham sa cakreṇa śakram vajreṇa dānavaḥ muṣṭinā nandinam ca eva paṭṭiśena prabhā mayam bhallena ca eva pūṣāṇam gadayā yamam eva ca āhatya vairiṇaḥ tūrṇam sarvān eva raṇe sa kūṭa yodhī kūṭāni girīṇām giri sannibhaḥ a virāmam a viśrāmam nirucchvāsam bhaya ākulam chinna nāsā akṣi danta oṣṭhāḥ bhagna pāda kaṭī karāḥ uttrasta udbhrānta cakitāḥ dṛśyante pramatha amarāḥ saudha agra śṛṅga upala śastra varṣī muhur sṛjan bhāti asuraḥ a ambara sthaḥ tāḥ me abjam mahat dhūma latā āvṛtam ca khadyota tulyam ca mahā agni cūrṇam tripañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas suparṇa puṅkhinām suparṇa patra patriṇām suparṇa tulya pātinām suparṇa tuṅga tuṇḍinām śatam śarīra bhedinām śarīra sāra bhojinām dhanuḥ prapūrita īritāḥ raṇa pracāritaiḥ vṛtāḥ sva mārga yāna deśikāḥ jave manaḥ nila upamāḥ yathā divākara īritāḥ karāḥ mahā acaleṣu iva śara āhatāḥ ca kuñjarāḥ śara āhatāḥ ca vājinaḥ śara āhatāḥ ca devatāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ ca sarvatas vinirgata antra śoṇitāḥ vikīrṇa hāra bhūṣaṇāḥ vimukta keśa bandhanāḥ patanti gāḍha vedanāḥ hayam gajam suram yathā prapaśyate hi yam yatas yathā mada andha kuñjara praṇaṣṭa pādapam vanam mukheṣu kecid āhatāḥ nirīkṣaṇeṣu ca apare urā udareṣu ca apare tathā hatāḥ ca pṛṣṭhatas śataghnayaḥ yathā ācitāḥ śaraiḥ tathā marut gaṇāḥ gaṇāḥ ca bhīma vikramāḥ na bhūmim āpuḥ āhatāḥ sura asuraiḥ pravartitā tatas vraṇa ambu vāhinī gaja indra nakra saṃkulā rathāṅga cāru kacchapā kirīṭa kūṭa dardurā vikīrṇa hāra śarkarā sita ambara ati pheninī sura asuraiḥ pravartitā tatas aañjanā muda tviṣaḥ taḍit prahāsa hāsinaḥ piśāca yakṣa rākṣasāḥ pipāsayā atikarṣitāḥ surāḥ yathā vara amṛtam papuḥ tathā eva śoṇitam tadā andhake śara āhate mahā iṣuṇā atha nandine yuddhabhūmivarṇana tripañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ catuṣpañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ cukrudhuḥ dānavāḥ ghorāḥ caturviṃśati darpitāḥ prahlādaḥ ca anuhlādaḥ ca saṃhlādaḥ śiti vāṣkulau tathā tuhuṇḍaḥ huṇḍaḥ ca śambhuḥ kārtasvanaḥ kubhaḥ mayaḥ tāraḥ tārak akṣaḥ vidyunmālī pramohanaḥ ete aamarṣa vaśam prāptāḥ caturviṃśati dānavāḥ te aañjana acala saṃkāśāḥ kāñcana acala sannibham nandinam tāḍayāmāsuḥ śūla śakti ṛṣṭi paṭṭiśaiḥ nā akṣubhyata tadā nandī nā ārttim āpan ca vyathām tatas vikṛṣya bhagavān ātatam kārmukam mahat te bāṇa mārga nisrāvaiḥ dānavāḥ śoṇita kṣarāḥ kṣarantaḥ iva śaila indrāḥ tapanīya rasān babhuḥ tatas toṣa uddhataḥ nandī śukreṇa ujjīvitam punar jīvita sraṃsanam prāpya sa dānava mahā acalaḥ śīrṇa upalaḥ papāta āśu vajra āhataḥ iva acalaḥ baliḥ utpāṭya śaila agram cikṣepa uddiśya nandinam tat sa dhātu mṛga vyālam sa ṛkṣa vṛkṣam gireḥ taṭam nirbhrānta upala vṛkṣa ālam abhyadhāvat gaṇeśvaram śṛṅgasya bali muktasya tasya vyāla ādayaḥ javāt apakrāntā anayā ārttasya puruṣasya iva bāndhavāḥ tadā apatat tad giri agram nandī bāṇena vīryavān tat vidārya gireḥ śṛṅgam giri śṛṅga niketanaḥ saḥ gaṇeśena prāhlādi tanayaḥ vaśaḥ papāta sahasā bhūmau vāta āhataḥ iva drumaḥ jahuḥ sa samara mārāt tam dānavāḥ śara pīḍitāḥ prasṛta ambuda saṃkāśān tatas a ambuda nibha ākṛtiḥ andhakaḥ khāt kṣitin prāpya dānavān idam abravīt adya dākṣāyaṇī putrāḥ nibodhadhvam vacaḥ mama kuleṣu jātāḥ vīrāḥ ca sarva astra kṛta niścayāḥ dravadhve vai kim uddiśya paṭu nārāca vejitāḥ ekena nandinā bhagnāḥ śataśas a atha sahasraśas hrīḥ katham vai na bhavati jalpatām vaḥ gṛha ajire prāśnikāḥ pārśvatas sthitvā nirvairāḥ vīta matsarāḥ iti andhaka vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te dānavāḥ raṇe punar nivṛttāḥ yuddhāya pragṛhīta vara āyudhāḥ andhakaḥ saḥ abhyayāt nandim sārdham dānava puṅgavaiḥ śita agra rukma vikṛtāḥ pṛthavaḥ priya darśanāḥ andhakasya dhanuḥ sṛṣṭāḥ niṣpatanti mahā iṣavaḥ śalabhaiḥ iva kedārāḥ bhramaraiḥ iva pādapāḥ andhakena kṛtāḥ devāḥ śataghnayaḥ iva uttamāḥ yathā ca apratighāḥ sūktāḥ niyatam brāhmaṇa āśiṣaḥ tathā te niśitāḥ hi ugrāḥ brahmadaṇḍāḥ iva udyatāḥ anivāryāḥ hi amoghāḥ ca te mahā iṣavaḥ saḥ a api nitya āyata dhanuḥ pariveṣī iva bhāskaraḥ asṛjat bāṇa nikarān kiraṇān bhāskaraḥ yathā tasya bāṇa rujaḥ prāpya nadī tīre iva drumāḥ sīdanti gaṇapāḥ sarve devāḥ ca saha vāsavāḥ sa viṣṇum ekena śareṇa viddhvā dvābhyām anantam tribhiḥ eva śakram yamam ca somam ca jalādhipam ca vasūn ca nirdārya rarāsa ghoram aśvi dvayam ca api śara dvayena viddhvā bhaga aṃśāḥ ryama candra pūṣṇaḥ tatas nandīśvaram ugra karmā gaṇeśvarān ca api śaraiḥ tatakṣa tathā dahati andhakaḥ ātatāyī yathā pataṅgān bhagavān hutāśaḥ nivāritāḥ te śara dāritāḥ ca tadā andhakena amara yodha mukhyāḥ na spanditum śekuḥ udīkṣitum vā raṇe a andhakam khe manujāḥ iva arkam yaśāṃsi dīptāni tatas prahāya devāḥ sa nārāyaṇa devapālāḥ viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ ca eva anantaḥ śatakratuḥ ādityāḥ vasavaḥ sādhyāḥ aśvinau ca sura uttamau tuṣitāḥ ca eva viśvāḥ ca devāḥ ca eva svadhābhujaḥ andhakena śaraiḥ bhagnāḥ mārutena yathā drumāḥ candramāḥ bhagavān vahniḥ vitta pālaḥ ca rākṣasaḥ andhakena raṇe bhagnāḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ gandharvāḥ guhyakāḥ sarpāḥ garuḍāḥ ca mahā uragāḥ viṭpatiḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ ca somanandī prabhāmayaḥ piṅgalaḥ nandiṣeṇaḥ ca ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ mahodaraḥ vidyutkeśaḥ sukeśaḥ ca sa ca devaḥ vināyakaḥ anye ca pramathāḥ śūrāḥ vīrabhadra purogamāḥ andhakena raṇe bhagnāḥ śataśas a atha sahasraśas catuṣpañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ pañcapañcāśat uttara śatatamaḥ brahmaṇā sahitāḥ jagmuḥ śaraṇyam śūlapāṇinam te praṇamya mahādevam idam ūcuḥ bhaya arditāḥ mayā datta varaḥ yasmāt tasmāt yūyam vinirjitāḥ krīḍā artham eva ca mayā saṃgare saḥ upekṣitaḥ tatas devaḥ smitam kṛtvā pārśva stham śūlam aikṣata deva abhiprāya tattva jñaḥ śūlaḥ jajvāla tad kṣaṇāt tatas aandhakam tadā bhittvā sa śūlaḥ tam mahā balam dānava indram mahā kāyam āninye śaṅkara antikam patitāḥ puruṣāḥ bhūtvā te aapi ayudhyanta duḥsahāḥ nānā śastra praharaṇāḥ te a api ayudhyan gaṇeśvaraiḥ jaghnuḥ kecid gaṇān eva dravataḥ te mahā balāḥ na teṣām yudhyamānānām kaścid tasthau gaṇeśvaraḥ saṃgrāme dānava indrāṇām bhayāt sarve pradudruvuḥ tān dṛṣṭvā vidrutān sarvān gaṇān saha sura īśvaraiḥ vā devadevaḥ tadā prāha sarvāsḥ praharaṇa udyatāḥ asṛj bindu samudbhūtān bhakṣayadhvam mahā asurān evam uktāḥ tu tāḥ sarvāḥ yoga īśvaryaḥ mahā balāḥ hatvā hatvā asurān yuddhe cakhāduḥ ca ma devaḥ jvalitam śūlam abravīt andhaka anta kṛt andhakam paca sūrya agnau sahasram śaradām śatam pūrṇe sahasre varṣāṇām sāttvikam bhāvam abhyagāt lokānām kāraṇam devam bubudhe go vṛṣa dhvajam snāyu asthi śeṣaḥ tuṣṭāva devam candra ardha maulinam saṃhāra hetuḥ api yaḥ punar anta kāle tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi dhyāyanti niścita dhiyā amita divya bhāvam tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi yaḥ candra khaṇḍam amalam vikasat mayūkham baddhvā asayam priya tayā śirasā bibharti yaḥ ca ardha deham adadat girirāja putryai tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi yaḥ siddha cāraṇa niṣevita cāru toyām gaṅgām mahā ūrmi rabhasām gaganāt patantīm mūrdhnā dadhe srajam iva a pratilola puṣyām tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi kailāsa śṛṅga śikharam pravikampyamānam kailāsa śṛṅga sadṛśena daśānanena yaḥ pāda padma paripīḍanayā dadhāra tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi yena asakṛt diti sutāḥ ca danoḥ sutāḥ ca vidyādhara uraga gaṇāḥ ca varaiḥ samagrāḥ saṃyojitāḥ muni varāḥ phala mūla bhakṣāḥ tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi dakṣa adhvaram ca nayanam ca tathā bhagasya pūṣṇaḥ tadā daśana paṅktim aśātayat ca vyaṣṭambhayat kuliśa yukta mahā indra bāhum tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi trividha bandha vimokṣa bhāvāḥ jñāna anvaya śruta gaṇaiḥ api na eva yuktāḥ tam saṃśritāḥ sukha bhujaḥ puruṣāḥ bhavanti tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi yaḥ kālakūṭam apibat samudīrṇa vegam tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi brahma indra viṣṇu marutām ca sa ṣaṇmukhānām yaḥ aadāt varān su bahuśas bhagavān maheśaḥ nandim ca mṛtyu vadanāt prabhuḥ ujjahāra tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi kāmaḥ ca kārmuka dharaḥ bhuvi pañcabāṇaḥ hāsyāt kṛtaḥ bhagavatā sa tadā videhaḥ eka iṣuṇā tripuram eva purā jaghāna tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi saṃjīvanīm adita yaḥ parama artha gamyaḥ tasmai namaḥ śivakarāy śivāya nityam yaḥ a abhyarcyate a amara gaṇaiḥ saha lokapālaiḥ tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi krīḍā artham eva bhagavān bhuvanāni sapta nānā nadī vihaga pādapa maṇḍitāni sa brahmakāni sasṛje sukṛte hitāni tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi yaḥ kāraṇam su mahatām api kāraṇānām tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi mām kṣitidhara indra suta anuyāta vibhūṣaṇa aṅgam tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi baddhvā tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi paricintyamānam tam śaṃkaram śaraṇa dam śaraṇam vrajāmi mūḍhāḥ jānanti na asya jagantaḥ bhava bandha rūpāḥ prasādāt hi tasya evam stuvataḥ devaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ pūrṇe varṣa sahasre tu prītaḥ provāca śaṃkaraḥ divyam dadāmi te cakṣuḥ paśya mām dānava īśvara yat kiṃcid kāṅkṣitam phalam uttamam brāhmam vaiṣṇavam aindram vā padam vibudha durlabham athavā sarva lokānām bhava rājā yathā purā brāhmam vaiṣṇavam aindram ca padam āvṛtti lakṣaṇam yadi tuṣṭaḥ deveśa gāṇapatyam vidhatsva me aviśeṣyam viśuddham ca tat akṣayyam ca sarvadā kāmarūpī mahā yogī mahā sattvaḥ mahā balaḥ aṇima ādi guṇaiḥ yuktaḥ priyaḥ puruṣa sattamaḥ mahādevaḥ bhūtvā tatra eva antaradhīyata ro śūlam paramam vikramaiḥ stambhayitvā vāc manobhiḥ te vā stuvanti mūḍhāḥ mṛgāḥ iva vane mṛgatṛṣṇikābhiḥ pyaṭena pūṣā karoti vimalam kiraṇa ogha jālaiḥ naktam tu śūla hasitaiḥ rajamī mukhāni sampūrṇa maṇḍala vapuḥ dhavalīkaroti bhṛgu ādayaḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ tava deva siddhāḥ siddhim gatāḥ caraṇa padma vara prasādāt sā asi pūrvam a dṛṣṭa pūrvā sā sā spṛhām prakuruṣe mahatīm janasya tasmāt jaṭā induḥ iva jā ardha śarīra yogāt gaṅgām ca deva bhajase tvam apūrvavat tām na samyak vara īśvara ruṣā sadasā ugra kaṇṭha sametya śaktāḥ tejaḥ sṛjā āśu gamita liṅgasya yaḥ hara hariḥ pra hi adhastāt ūrdhvantu aham bruvāṇaḥ mātā pitā asi jagataḥ prabhuḥ avyayaḥ aasi śāntaḥ śivaḥ aasi paramaḥ aasi śivam karosi iti skandapurāṇe pañcapañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ṣaṭpañcāśat uttara śatatamaḥ evam stutaḥ sa bhagavān brahmaṇā ayugmalocanaḥ uvāca devān tān sarvān brahmaṇā sahitān tadā prītaḥ vibudhāḥ yāta nāśitaḥ deva kaṇṭakaḥ kim anyat karavāṇi adya priyam vaḥ varata anaghāḥ stuvantaḥ prahva mūrdhānaḥ deveśam hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ tvam eva deva sarveṣām asmākam śaraṇam param tvam pitā sarva lokānām tvayā ayam nāśitaḥ a andhakaḥ brahmaṇā sahitāḥ jagmuḥ yathāsthānam mudā yutāḥ tatas gaṇān api īśānaḥ yuddha kṛta śramān evam tam andhakam jitvā kṛtvā ca gaṇanāyakam brāhmaṇaḥ labhate yaḥ rakṣām na saṃśayaḥ śarīra nm yogam rūpam dharmam ca vindati iti skandapurāṇe ṣaṭpañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ saptapañcāśat uttara śatatamaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca anugṛhya andhakam devaḥ visṛjya sa gaṇān surān divam deveṣu yāteṣu gaṇape ca andhake kṛte praviśya rañjayāmāsa meru gṛhān iva sakhīnām dṛśyate madhye tārāṇām iva rohiṇī dṛṣṭvā devī api deveśam upāyātam vṛṣadhvajam uttasthau āsanāt tūrṇam sakhībhiḥ sahitā tadā andhakam ca jitam yuddhe devyāḥ priya cikīrṣayā śaṅkaraḥ kathayāmāsa punar ca pravarīkṛtam āsuram tyājitaḥ bhāvam tvām avajñātavān hi naḥ praṇataḥ prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā vyajñāpayata pārvatīm tava preṣya tvam āyātaḥ paśya mām saumya cakṣuṣā devena anugṛhītaḥ a aham tava hāsaḥ ca kiṃkaraḥ kṣāntam dāntam ca bhaktam ca tvad āśraya parāyaṇam iti evam uktvā girijām giri kūṭa nibhaḥ a andhakaḥ vāgbhiḥ āhavanīyābhiḥ astuvat prāñjaliḥ nataḥ dhṛtiḥ matiḥ tathā kīrtiḥ dīptiḥ prāptiḥ pramohinī medhā sudhā tathā sādhvī svadhā svāhā mahā dyutiḥ puṣṭiḥ iṣṭiḥ tathā tuṣṭiḥ gṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭiḥ truṭiḥ taḍit smṛtiḥ prītiḥ spṛhā hāniḥ vāṇī glāniḥ dayā kriyā lakṣmīḥ śrīḥ sannatiḥ śraddhā māyā māyādhara arcitā aditiḥ ditiḥ tathā kadrūḥ siṃhikā surasā danuḥ rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī carṣaṇī sukha dāyinī dīkṣā dakṣā avarā rakṣā śikṣā kakṣa niketanā dharaṇī dhāraṇī dhanyā vīraṇī vai guhāraṇī lā golā tathā ca eva maṅgalāvidhā tathā raḥ vṛtā sa tā ca sakṣatra nandinī nakṣatra citrā dyauḥ pṛthvi kriyā smṛtiḥ a lolupā śuddhā śuddhiḥ sudhīḥ kīrtiḥ kṛttivāsaḥ aadharapriyā dhanuḥ jyā jayinī pūjyā vrajyā jaya pradā bhūtiḥ bhūta adhijananī sukṛtiḥ sumanāḥ ratiḥ bhāratī bhāsam āyuktā yukta rakta vacodharī ājñā prajñā tathā saṃjñā ulkā nāsāsamudbhavā vedamātā atha gāyatrī durgā sāvitrī atha api ca dharmiṇī dharma jananī tejanī tejasām varā rajanī rañjanī dhīrā yoniḥ vanaja locanā śradarthinī danunadī śrutārthā śrutavattarā balayā alātaka dharā mekhalā mekhalā dharā prīyatām me jagat hartrī śyāmā śyāma ambarā hi umā andhakasya tutoṣāti tuṣṭā ca idam uvāca tam prītā asmi putra yat prāptam gāṇapatyam tvayā śubham bhavānīm vara dām dṛṣṭvā saḥ a andhakaḥ gaṇapa uttamaḥ praṇataḥ prāñjaliḥ prāha himavat tanayām umām yam ca tvam me varam devi dadāsi īśāna vallabhe uvāca andhakam āsādya prīyamāṇā punar tadā jñānena anena tuṣṭā
