asmi tava putra śubhena vai mad chandāt eva ca api etat gāṇapatyam tava anagha pāpa vyayaḥ mahān āsīt tena asi pravarīkṛtaḥ mama devasya ca api iṣṭaḥ kiṃkaraḥ mama ca api atha bhava tvam anaghaḥ śrīmān gaṇeśvara gaṇa īśvaraḥ ye ca tvām kīrtayiṣyanti divā rātrau atha api vā teṣām kīrtiḥ yaśaḥ svargaḥ dharmaḥ ca eva bhaviṣyati anujñātaḥ ca pārvatyā mumude hara pārśva gaḥ iti evam andhakam devaḥ tamaḥ ūri kṛta mūṣaṇaḥ saptapañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ aṣṭapañcāśat uttara śatatamaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca anndhakam gaṇapam kṛtvā devyā saha maheśvaraḥ kim cakre a atas param brūhi nuda kautūhalam mama jitvā andhakam tatas vyāsa kṛtvā ca gaṇanāyakam girīndra sutayā sārdham vijahāra sura ārtti hā atha bhūteśa jananī ṣaḍānana tanūkarī apṛcchat putra sambaddham praśnam praśna vidām varā varam bhūmiruhāḥ pañca na ca koṣṭharuhāḥ daśa ṣoḍaśa iha aṅgam aṅgāni bhittvā putraḥ a abhijāyate tasmāt putrāt katham śreṣṭhaḥ koṣṭha jāt bhuvijaḥ sutaḥ iti evam pṛcchatīm pṛcchām śikṣām dīṣām kriyām matim sūkṣma arthaḥ eṣa rambhā ūru yam pṛcchasi varānane koṣṭha jāt tanayāt yasmāt bhūmijaḥ tanayaḥ varaḥ śālmalau vaitaraṇyām ca asipattravaneṣu evamādyeṣu ca anyeṣu kukṛtaiḥ anuveṣṭitān śāsyataḥ mṛtyu vacanāt rākṣasaiḥ krūra karmabhiḥ pitR̥n tathā aśubhaiḥ ghoraiḥ veṣṭitān rākṣasa arditān tatra ye duṣṭa cāritrāḥ putra saṃkhyām na te gatāḥ śaṭhaḥ yadvat balīvardaḥ ṣaṇḍhaḥ vā api narādhipaḥ tatra api codyate duḥkham duḥkham ca narakam viduḥ yat pitR̥n trāyate tasmāt sutaḥ putraḥ tatas smṛtaḥ indriyāṇām tu prābalyāt tat putreṣu api pārvati ime hi taravaḥ devi dakṣa śāpāt hata indriyāḥ pāpakāni na kurvanti saṃvṛtaiḥ karaṇaiḥ ca ha etasmāt kāraṇāt devi koṣṭha jānām śatāt api ekaḥ bhūmiruhaḥ putraḥ śasyate na tu koṣṭha jaḥ chedam bhedam tathā trāsam pāṭanāt ca niśācaraiḥ kurvadbhiḥ taravaḥ putrāḥ pitR̥ṇām chedam bhedam trāsanam ca rākṣasaiḥ niraya upagaiḥ katham pitR̥ṇām taravaḥ vārayanti yama kṣaye śṛṇuṣva chedam bhedam ca pitR̥ṇām yama sādane yajñe a arthitāḥ te devānām taravaḥ dakṣa śāpena devaḥ salilasambhavaḥ yajña vṛkṣa artham āha idam vṛkṣān vṛkṣapatiḥ vacaḥ sthāvarāḥ svāgatam vaḥ a astu tuṣyāmi śaraṇa eṣiṇām nāśayāmi eṣa vaḥ vatsāḥ dakṣa śāpa kṛtam tamaḥ śālāḥ bilvāḥ palāśāḥ ca varuṇāḥ kiṃśukāḥ tathā rohītakāḥ ca ye ca anye yajña aṅga prabhavāḥ drumāḥ te su upayuktāḥ yajñeṣu tvak patra phala śākhinaḥ mūrtīḥ su bhāsvarāḥ prāpya mama loke nivatsyatha eṣām yajñiya vṛkṣāṇām yūyam api anugāminaḥ yajña upayuktāḥ gacchadhvam teṣām eva salokatām sthāṇu liṅga upayuktāḥ ca janaiḥ bhakti puraḥsaraiḥ dharmeṇa śuddha dehāḥ ca gatim iṣṭām avāpsyatha tam bhayāt trāyatām ca eva dharmaḥ vaḥ bhavitā mahān taravaḥ ūcuḥ katham vayam putra kṛtāḥ tān pitR̥n niraya upagān ye ca prāṇi vadhe yuktāḥ pṛṣṭha māṃsa āśinaḥ ca ye rājñām ākrośakāḥ ye ca ye ca piṇḍa apahārakāḥ aho bhṛśam yātanābhiḥ aśivābhiḥ abhidrutāḥ śāsyante mṛtyu vacanāt rākṣasaiḥ bhīma vikramaiḥ tān evam tudyamānān ca kuṭyamānān ca rākṣasaiḥ tān tathā tudyamānān ca kuṭyamānān ca rākṣasaiḥ tat me sumanasaḥ bhūtvā niśāmayata pādapāḥ tasya tasya smṛtāḥ śīghram tam deśam yāsyatha anaghāḥ garbhādhāna ādibhiḥ kṛtvā putra tve kalpayet naraḥ ye ca api pūrva jātān yaḥ vidhinā niṣparigrahān putra prakṛtakān kuryuḥ tān ca nistārayiṣyatha sarva kāmān ca dāsyadhvam sukham ca eva tathā uttamam karma kṣayam ca sarveṣām lokān ca eva tathā akṣayān tām pṛcchatīm mahādevaḥ idam vacanam abravīt śṛṇuṣva yena vidhinā gṛhyate sutaḥ śvas bhūte a aham bhuviruham grahīṣyāmi iti pārvati sa upavāsā bhavet nārī śuci śīlā tatas śata sahasra aṃśau asta śṛṅgam gate ravau viprān āmantrayet rātrau pāvanān veda vādinaḥ śrutīnām ākarāḥ hi ete ratnānām iva sāgarāḥ viprāḥ vipra adhipa mukhi pūjanīyāḥ sahasraśas variṣṭham etat dānānām yat brāhmaṇa mukhe hatam mahāsattve aṇadhātuḥ tu bhakṣaṇe jāyante ye punar jātāḥ hi upanītāḥ mahātmabhiḥ viyat iti ucyate vyoma prakāraḥ prāpaṇe smṛtaḥ divam samprāpayanti ete devi viprāḥ tatas smṛtāḥ satya sāra mayāḥ hi ete viprāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayambhuvā siddhiḥ na teṣu atuṣṭeṣu śakyāḥ prāptum suraiḥ api aham nārāyaṇaḥ a anantaḥ brahmā śakraḥ a anilaḥ śikhī tat dānam na abhinandāmaḥ viprāḥ yatra na pūjitāḥ yeṣām prasādāt sulabhā āyuḥ dharmaḥ balam sukham śrīḥ yaśaḥ svarga vāsaḥ ca tān viprān arcayet budhaḥ viprān āmantrayitvā atha śuci vastrā śuci smitā śayīta sa namaskārā sa darbhā bhūmim āśritā tatas tam sa patākam ca sa ātapatram sa bhūṣaṇam tarukam pramadā kṛtvā taru chāyā anugāminī puṇyāham kārayitvā atha ṛtvijā hi athavā ātmanā tṛptānām brāhmaṇānām ca tattvena ākūtam ātmanaḥ grahīṣye tad anujñām vai kartum arhatha me tatas taiḥ abhyanujñātam tam tarum taruṇam priye bhūmideva samakṣam vai gṛhṇīyāt tanayam priye pitR̥ṇām niraya sthānām madhu saḥ aamuñca varṣati gṛhītaḥ vidhinā anena subhru bhūmiruha ātmajaḥ sat putrāṇām śatāt ca api devi candra nibha ānane ekaḥ bhūmiruhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ putra tve kalpitaḥ sutaḥ iti etat te mayā śiṣṭam yathā bhūmiruhaḥ putraḥ viśiṣṭaḥ koṣṭha jāt sutāt aśoka tarukaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ komalaḥ su manoramaḥ asīt ca me tadā bhāvaḥ eṣa me taru potakaḥ ābhyām ca me mahādeva kucābhyām dvija pāvana kṣīram āgāt sudhā sāram putra snehāt sukha pradam tam aham deva gṛhṇīyām putra prakṛtakam tarum yadi me kuruṣe tava aham vaśa vartinī tuṣṭi pradaḥ hi aputrāyāḥ putrakaḥ bhavitā anagha iti evam bhāṣamāṇām tu bhavānīm bhagavān bhavaḥ sadbhāvāt niḥsṛtam vākyam avadat para tāpanaḥ devi phulla aravinda akṣi katham nāma na te sutaḥ aham ca te pradāsyāmi putrān parama śobhanān anujñātā mayā devi kuru aśoka tarum sutam anukūlam patim jñātvā tam tāmarasa locanā praṇipatya avyayā tuṣṭā idam āha maheśvaram deva jānāmi aham dharmam yathā strīṇām na vidyate yā tu bhartāram āmantrya nārī dharmam samācaret avamanya tu yā nārī bhartāram daivatam gurum atītam api yā nārī bhartāram paripṛcchati anujñātā hi sā tena prīyamāṇena cetasā pati śuśrūṣaṇasya ete kalām ṣoḍaśīm śuśrūṣām kurute bhartuḥ sā satyā iva vibhāvyate tena agryā saha vicacāra cāru rūpā bhānoḥ bhās iva saha bhānunā bhavānī aṣṭapañcāśaduttaraśatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ūnaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ pārvatyāḥ niścayam jñātvā bhagavān tryambakaḥ tadā sumālim piṅgalam yakṣam prāha vākya vidām varaḥ pārśva stham nandinam tatra bhagavān śaṃkaraḥ svayam parvata indra sutā aśokam tarum putram grahīṣyati tvayi āyattam ca tat sarvam tasmāt kuru mama ājñayā iti uktaḥ parameśena piṅgalaḥ piṅgala īkṣaṇaḥ uvāca somayā sārdham tridaśānām patim patim gaṇādhipa yathā ājñaptam tat kariṣyāmi yajñahan tasya aśoka taroḥ pārśve vidadhau annam uttamam nandinam tejasām rāśiḥ diṇḍicaṇḍeśvaraḥ abravīt brahmaṇyān brahmaṇān nandin devī yajñena yakṣyati audakāyām virūpāsya brāhmaṇāḥ brahma sambhavāḥ upāsate ye varuṇam pātāla tala saṃśrayāḥ saṃyamanyām tathā ca eva ye yamam paryupāsate brāhmaṇāḥ brahmaṇā tulyāḥ tān nimantraya bhūtapa tathā udayagireḥ śṛṅge satyaḥ nāma mahā hradaḥ vasanti yatra te satyāḥ satya nāma tapodhanāḥ satyena yeṣām ādityaḥ dinam nayati nityaśas teṣām niṣkalmaṣaḥ tasmin hrade snātaḥ divākaraḥ pratyaham kurute devaḥ prayāṇam śubha karma kṛt teṣām praṇamya śirasā hi ātmānam san nivedya ca atharva aṅgirasaḥ tān ca nimantraya gaṇa dvijān ye ca cakracarāḥ siddhāḥ ye kapota uñcha vṛttayaḥ upāsate ye ca śakram tān āmantraya vai dvijān brahmāṇam ca sa patnīkam brāhmaṇān ca nimantraya kṣīroda velā nilayāḥ tapovana nivāsinaḥ ye mām sa dārāḥ sa sutāḥ sa agnihotra paricchadāḥ bhaktāḥ yeṣām aham nityam prasāda su mukhaḥ tān bālakhilyān vāgīśa vyālān iva durāsadān āmantraya yatas bhūtvā suyaśāḥ suyaśā pate saṃcaran ca tribhuvanam vāyuḥ avyāhataḥ yathā te ca sarve samāyāntu viprāṇām pariveśakāḥ sāgaram saḥ aambara ākāram sa ambaraḥ aamba gocaraḥ āsasāda pravalgantam raṅga stham iva vāraṇam sa tam timi śata ākīrṇam arṇavam pramatha agraṇīḥ apaśyat kṣaratīm kṣīram divyam tat amṛta ākaram surabhīm abhivādya eva śaṃkara anucaraḥ a ari hā viveśa nandī varuṇaḥ yatra āste sa gaṇaḥ varuṇam dvārapālena pūrvam eva niveditaḥ sa ca api apāt tadā rājā dūrāt eva prahṛṣṭa vat tasya argham gām ca pādyam ca nivedya varuṇaḥ svayam āsīnam tam apām goptā papraccha vadatām varaḥ bhagavan kim cirasya adya tvayā vayam apekṣitāḥ vada sarvān abhiprāyān kartā te a aham na saṃśayaḥ tatas sa varuṇam prāha dānavaiḥ aparājitam aśoka tarukam putram giri putrī grahīṣyati krīḍā artham umayā sārdham nimantrayati te haraḥ tad deva putra abhivṛtaḥ sa dāraḥ saha phenapaiḥ śvas yāhi mandara girim prītim vardhaya śūlinaḥ iti uktvā saḥ varuṇena gaṇeśvaraḥ niṣkrāntaḥ varuṇa āvāsāt śveta abhrāt iva bhāskaraḥ sa pūjyamānaḥ siddhaiḥ ca cāraṇaiḥ ca suraiḥ api prāpa udayagirim nandī hara iṣuḥ tripuram yathā saḥ a atha tasya gireḥ rañjite tāpanaiḥ karaiḥ nililye garuḍaḥ pakṣī prabhañjana pathe yathā hradam tatra arṇava ākāram kāñcana ambuja śobhitam śīrṇa utpala taraṅga āḍhyam apaśyat saḥ a apsaraḥ vṛtam hradasya tasya rodhaḥsu sa aśokeṣu sahasraśas apaśyata ṛṣīn satyān āditya ayuta sannibhān sa tān tapodhanān dṛṣṭvā tapanābhān tapodhanān nandī prahva añjali puṭaḥ hi āsādya avandata dvijān nandinam samayujyanta vāsa drumam iva aṇḍajāḥ taiḥ sūryakiraṇa āpītaiḥ pīta cīra ambaraiḥ api saṃvṛtaḥ sa babhau nandī jambudvīpaḥ iva acalaiḥ atīva prababhau vyāsa tīrtheṣu iva maheśvaraḥ te nandinam sukha āsīnam satyam satyāḥ tapodhanāḥ ūcuḥ harṣa ākulaiḥ vākyaiḥ vismita ānana locanāḥ samākrāntaḥ tvayā tāta dharmeṇa nirayaḥ yathā vihartum āgataḥ devaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ a asmābhiḥ tatas bhavān satyam su caritam śuddham tapaḥ a asmābhiḥ gaṇeśvara saha umam yat tvayā sārdham drakṣyāmaḥ iha śaṃkaram aham tu kāryavān āgām yuṣmākam imam āśramam aśoka tarukam putram giri putrī grahīṣyati tatra śarvam amara adhipa prabhum tāraka adhipa vibhūṣaṇam śivam brāhmaṇa āmantraṇe ūnaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ ṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ āmantrya tān ṛṣīn sarvān satya vīrya yaśaḥ śrutān hara ājñayā ravim devam upāsarpata bhūtapaḥ sūrya raśmi sahasreṣu tāpasān sa marīcipān apaśyat sa sukha āsīnān chāyāsu iva vihaṅgamān tatas sūrya ratham śīghram upetya arūṇasārathim saḥ a aṃśumālinam atrim ca atharva aṅgirasau api devān ṛṣīn bhujaṅgān ca aśvān ca amantrayat śubhaḥ āditya aśva ādibhiḥ nandī rudra piprīṣubhiḥ tadā devān ṛṣīn bhujaṅgān ca tatas āmantrya bhūtapaḥ sa vāyuḥ iva śīghraḥ tu garuḍaḥ vā yathā aṇḍajaḥ dhaneśa bhavanam nandī kailāsam samupāgataḥ parvatam dhanada āvāsam paśyamānaḥ sa bhūta īśaḥ dhaneśasya girīśa vacanaṃkaraḥ asasāda nagasya agre bhavanam kāñcanam śubham kailāsa agre sanniviṣṭam kailāsa agra sama tviṣam pātākābhiḥ dhvajaiḥ ca api kiṅkiṇī jāla mālibhiḥ hāsaiḥ ca pura ghoṣāṇām sat nāditam aharniśam bheryā parama ghorāṇām vāditra śata nāditam bhābhiḥ juṣṭām sabhām tasya tatas rudra sabhāsadaḥ tam ṛddhyā parayā yuktam sevyamānam śriyā tathā śuktikarṇam śuktikarṇaiḥ yakṣa indraiḥ abhisaṃvṛtam upagīyamānam gandharvaiḥ eka piṅga āyata īkṣaṇam mādyantam svarṇayā naddha mālayā amala lolayā dhanadaḥ ca api tam dṛṣṭvā śaṃkara anucaram varam pūjayan śaṃkaram somam utpapāta āsanāt drutam sa aśokāt iva puṣpa āḍhyāt udagrāt parvatāt raviḥ grahāḥ yathā dīpyamānāḥ dina hānau grahādhipam sa putra dāraḥ sa amātyaḥ praṇeme manasā haram tatas kathāḥ bahuvidhāḥ kṛtvā uddiśya maheśvaram aśoka tarukam putram giri putrī grahīṣyati nimantrayati tatra tvām draviṇa īśa maheśvaraḥ śvas sa putraḥ sa dāraḥ ca sa anugaḥ sa apsaraḥ gaṇaḥ mandaram yāhi vitteśa deveśaḥ prīyate tvayā sa yamam dharma vaktāram hartāram prāṇinām prabhum sa agnim sa dharmam sa vyādhim apaśyat gaṇanāyakaḥ āyāntam nandinam dṛṣṭvā yamaḥ bhūta śata āvṛtaḥ pādābhyām nandinaḥ saḥ a atha nipapāta tutoṣa ca aśoka tarukam putram giri putrī grahīṣyati tatra tvām sa anugam devaḥ nimantrayati śaṃkaraḥ tān ca āmantrayate devaḥ sammānya bahu mānataḥ kalyam sa bhagavān kalyaḥ kālaḥ kālapriyam girim sūrya ātmaja gṛhāt nandī śakra lokam tatas gataḥ sukṛtīnām tam āvāsam vāsavam lokam adbhutam viveśa tvaritam nandī ditigarbham yathā ahi hā gāndharvam upaśṛṇvāṇam nandī śakram apaśyata sa pūjām rudra sadṛśīm avāpya tridaśeśvaram upāviśat ameya ātmā śakra abhyāse varāsane tam āsīnam upāsīnaḥ śatakratuḥ arindamaḥ paryapṛcchata harṣeṇa kim cirāt āgataḥ bhavān mandāra vāsitaḥ a avyagraḥ provāca kuliśa adharaḥ aśoka tarukam putram giri putrī grahīṣyati tatra tvām sa amaram devaḥ nimantrayati bhūtapaḥ dvija pūrvam dvijāḥ ye ca tava ālaya nivāsinaḥ sa putra dārān tān ca api nimantrayati śaṃkaraḥ śvas sa putraḥ sa dāraḥ tvam devadevasya śāsanāt prītim yāsyati deveśaḥ parām sura nara ārtti hā śita śūla dharam pinākinam giri rāja indra sutāpatim prabhum ṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ ekaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śakreṇa tu kṛta anujñaḥ nandī pramatha nāyakaḥ sa muhūrtāt mahā vegaḥ mahā vegaḥ iva anilaḥ vairājam bhavanam prāptaḥ caturvaktrasya pārṣadaḥ hata klamām sa tu sabhām sabhām meru gireḥ iva tām kathām iva citra arthām citra arthaiḥ bahubhiḥ yutām dadarśa sa sabhām nandī bahu āścarya samākulām tasyām sabhāyām ālīnam yatibhiḥ saha saḥ apaśyat abjajam nandī devaiḥ pañcabhiḥ āvṛtam veda artham bhāṣamāṇam tam yatīnām paripṛcchatām tān ca bhāṣya vidaḥ sarvān śrutvā sādhu iti vādinaḥ nandī pitāmaham samyak pūjayāmāsa satvaram tatas pitāmahaḥ prāha nandinam gaṇanāyakam kim cirāt āgataḥ sa ca tam pratyabhāṣata aśoka tarukam putram giri putrī grahīṣyati imān ca tapasā agni ābhān sa vedān veda vādinaḥ vraja mānada devānām ekam ājñāpayati ajaḥ iti evam vacasām kartā vacaḥ śrutvā sa nandinaḥ japya priyam uvāca idam hṛṣṭa rūpaḥ pitāmahaḥ aham api āgamiṣyāmi ebhiḥ saha śiva antikam mokṣyate ca api aśokaḥ dakṣa śāpa kṛtam tamaḥ iti uktaḥ pratimānya īśam īśasya dayitaḥ brahmaṇaḥ bhavanāt tūrṇam kṣīrodam udadhim yayau sa velā nilayān viprān bālakhilyān tapodhanān nānā niyama saṃyuktān apaśyat gaṇanāyakaḥ vandamānam tam ālokya gaṇeśam suyaśā patim āśīrbhiḥ anukūlābhiḥ nananduḥ te tapodhanāḥ tapodhanānām hṛṣṭānām nandī madhya gataḥ babhau grahāṇām saumya rūpāṇām yathā madhya gata uḍupaḥ kaccit drakṣyāma deveśam sa ambam ambāpatim bhavam tatas nandī dvijaśreṣṭhān śreṣṭhaḥ vai pramathādhipaḥ sa alāṅkāram idam vākyam abravīt dvija saṃsadi iha ca āgamanam yat me tat śṛṇudhvam tapodhanāḥ aśoka tarukam putram giri putrī grahīṣyati śvas sarve dāra sahitāḥ sa śiṣya tanaya agnayaḥ mandaram yāta vipra agryāḥ mām ambām ca anugṛhṇata iti evam nandinā proktaḥ bālakhilyāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ bho nandin āgamiṣyāmaḥ śvas prabhāte vayam prabho dhanada vara dam etya bhūtanātham gaṇapati nāthaḥ idam tadā avabhāṣe ekaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ dviṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ āmantriteṣu vipreṣu nārāyaṇa pada traye bhagavān kratu kāma ghnaḥ pūṣṇaḥ danta nipātanaḥ mālī maulī balī kālaḥ kāle vacanam abravīt ambike jagataḥ sarve brāhmaṇāḥ brāhmaṇaḥ samāḥ yāmaḥ a aśoka taroḥ pārśvam tathā kuru girīndraje sa ākāśa jāla pātālam jagat janani tatra hi piṇḍīkṛtam tvad hita arthe bhaviṣyati gireḥ sute krāntam trivikrama ākrāntam nārāyaṇa pada trayam atha devī divaḥ nātham ḍiṇḍimuṇḍeśvaram haram avadat vara dam kāntam kāntam candra ardha bhūṣaṇam ayam nandīśvaraḥ devaḥ āvayoḥ paramaḥ hitaḥ vara koṭī sahasrāṇi tvattaḥ a arhati na saṃśayaḥ vara daḥ hi asi lokānām lokānām api ca īśvaraḥ yadi tuṣṭaḥ śailādeḥ diśasva pravaram varam uvāca pramatha īśānam vriyatām īpsitaḥ varaḥ tatas kapīndra vadanaḥ sureśa sadṛśa dyutiḥ praṇamya śirasā prāha nandī śaṃkara vallabhaḥ prabhāvāt tava deveśa vara dā asmi ajara amaraḥ śiṣṭānām mad viśiṣṭānām gaṇānām gaṇapa adhipaḥ iti evam nandinam devaḥ bhāṣamāṇam tadā natam prītyā apaśyat virūpākṣaḥ śaśāṅka kṛta śekharaḥ pramṛjya prāha harṣeṇa harṣayan nandinam bhṛśam bhaktimān asi me nandin sa dāram sa gaṇa āśrayam tām ca bhaktim puraskṛtya pārśva sthaḥ mayā kṛtaḥ yaḥ ca tvām dveṣṭi vidviṣṭaḥ sa me dharma rataḥ hi sandhyā kālam tu kāla jñaḥ kālaḥ kāla nihā haraḥ upoḍham vīkṣya nṛttasya devaḥ kālam amanyata upaspṛśya tatas saḥ a adbhiḥ apām sraṣṭā trilokapaḥ anvāsta bhagavān sandhyām loka saṃsthām nu pālayan bhartāram vīkṣya nṛtyantam viṣakta karapallavam sahadharmacarī devī bhartāram sā anvanṛtyata dampatī vīkṣya nṛtyantau sa aṭṭahāsam gaṇāgraṇīḥ prānṛtyata tatas nandī devayoḥ prītim āvahan pramathāḥ nīla megha ābhāḥ pranṛttāḥ tūrya nisvanaiḥ tatas bheryaḥ jharjharāḥ ca kikhira ānaka maṇḍukāḥ āḍambarāḥ ḍiṇḍimāḥ ca śaṅkhāḥ ca eva prasasvanuḥ nandī visṛjate hāsam pramathāḥ neduḥ ulbaṇāḥ tat tūrya vara śabda āḍhyam śiva aśaniḥ iva ākulam jaguḥ ca anye gandharvāḥ iva pārṣadāḥ mṛgāṅke hi udite candre candra avayava bhūṣaṇaḥ samāpya niyamam devaḥ sāmba nandīśa pārṣadaḥ virarāma utsavāt tasmāt pārvatīm ca idam abravīt uṣitvā śarvarīm etām śarvari amita vikrame aśoka tarukam putram tatas śvas tvam grahīṣyati dhāreyī sā sa darbhāyām dhārāyām dhāraṇīdharā suṣvāpa deva vacanāt ekām rātrim yata vratā tatas śata sahasra aṃśau udite aarke aarka bhāvanaḥ umām āha prayāma iti yatra aśokaḥ sutaḥ sa te bhavam āha prayāma iti siñjamāna vibhūṣaṇā pāda cāreṇa bhagavān pādapam pādapa ālayaḥ tam aśoka tarum prāpa sa nandī sa ambikaḥ haraḥ sādhayānam dadarśa annam anna dam pramathaiḥ saha saḥ aapaśyat parvata prakhyān rāśīn rāśi vidām varaḥ sa sādhitam tatas dṛṣṭvā yakṣeṇa annam pinākadhṛk tatra agāt muditaḥ bhūtvā yatra sāmbaḥ te praṇamya mahādevam devāḥ tena abhipūjitāḥ parivārya tadā aśokam idam ūcuḥ hara agratas adya prabhṛti vṛkṣaḥ sarvatas sukha saṃyutaḥ sarva ābharaṇa puṣpa āḍhyaḥ sarva gandha rasa anvitaḥ bhaviṣyati na saṃdehaḥ devyāḥ ca su dṛḍham priyaḥ tatas girīndra tanayām girīśaḥ praṇata ārti hā paśya anna parvatān etān iti provāca kāma daḥ dṛḍham tutoṣa deva īśā piṅgalasya guhā araṇiḥ sumālinam yakṣa varam piṅgalam parvata ātmajā yat te manīṣitam kāryam tat kuruṣva kim āsyate tatas sā ati pramuditā divya ambara nivāsinī manojavam anujñāpya śaṃkaram bhuvaneśvaram daitya śoka pradā devī tam aśokam vibhāvarī alaṃcakāra sa snehā alaṃkāraiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ ātapatram ca tasya agre muktā dāma avabhāsitam ucchrāyamāsa girijā mayūra aṅgaruhaiḥ saha mūlāt akarot devī vara paṅka aṅkitām tanum jāmbūnada mayaiḥ ca api paṭṭaiḥ maṇi virājitaiḥ sarvatas bhūṣayāmāsa aśoka tarukam priyam tasya śākhā praśākhāsu muktā dāmāni pārvatī atha vāsaḥ yugaiḥ śvetaiḥ tam aśokam guhā araṇiḥ vāsayāmāsa lokānām jananī putra lālasā śrīveṣṭakam namerum ca guggulam ghṛtam eva ca tatas śaṅkha ninādena deva tūrya raveṇa ca balim balavataḥ bhāryā cakāra caratī tapaḥ tathā arcayantyāḥ tam vṛkṣam candra hāra amṛta prabham stanābhyām asravat kṣīram putra sneha abhisaṃgamāt umayā saḥ a arcitaḥ vṛkṣaḥ aśokaḥ vana dīpakaḥ nandinātha samānītān brāhmaṇān brahmaṇaḥ samān vācayāmāsa puṇyāham dattvā teṣām yathā īpsitam tatas puṇya aha ghoṣa ante āśīrvādasya ca ubhayoḥ anumānya patim devī ṛṣīn tān abravīt tu sā iti evam bruvatīm devīm pārvatīm putra lālasām samam ūcuḥ dvijāḥ sarve iṣṭatas gṛhyatām iti tatas śaṅkha ravaḥ divyaḥ sarva tūrya rava anvitaḥ vedān uccārayan viprāḥ nṛtyanti apsarasām gaṇaḥ ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ ca saṃhṛṣṭāḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ kusuma saṃcayaiḥ tat pravādita gāndharvam pranṛtta apsarasām gaṇam paśyanti hṛṣitāḥ devāḥ aśoka taruka utsavam vādayan kacchapīm vīṇām vīṇa vādayatām varaḥ nāradaḥ nṛtyate harṣāt vāta nunnaḥ iva analaḥ samāpya niyamam sā atha gṛhītvā aśoka putrakam girīndra tanayā bhāti dharā iva jala ukṣitā atha nandīśvara ādiṣṭāḥ pramathāḥ te sahasraśas adadan sva āsanāni āśu viprāṇām vipra vatsalāḥ svarṇānām rajatānām ca sphaṭikānām pramathaiḥ kīryamāṇānām āsanānām abhūt svanaḥ meroḥ śikhara varṣāṇām mahatī kuśajaiḥ iva tathā āsanāni udvahatām pramathānām babhau ravaḥ varṣa anna mṛṣṭa akāmānām meghānām stanatām iva āsanaiḥ pramathāḥ rejuḥ sa arka agnayaḥ iva acalāḥ pramathāḥ te hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ hi āsanāni mahā āsanāḥ asaṃsakta āsanā paṅktiḥ nirmitā viśvakarmaṇā mandarasya śubhe pṛṣṭhe vipra paṅktyaḥ viniḥsṛtāḥ snāte pathaḥ iva dṛṣṭvā rejatuḥ āsana bhūṣaṇāḥ dvijātīn anuliptān tu yakṣa jambāla miśrakān sa śekharān sa sragdāmān anuhūya sama udyatān anilaiḥ sa aṅga nādāḥ ca rejuḥ devāḥ iva dvijāḥ su ślakṣṇaiḥ ca sugandhaiḥ ca gandha cūrṇaiḥ sa piñjaraiḥ avakīrṇāḥ tatas devaiḥ bhūmidevāḥ samantataḥ divya candana paṅka aṅkāḥ divya cūrṇa avacūrṇitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ rejuḥ ekasthāḥ ekasthāḥ iva pāvakāḥ divyam dhūpam cārayitvā mām ājñā sarvaśas ca ha tatas sphaṭika saṃkāśam padma reṇuḥ iva arjitāḥ hasta śaucam muhūrtena dattam śaṃkara kiṃkaraiḥ baddha kakṣāḥ tatas śūrāḥ baddha kakṣāḥ iva dvipāḥ pariveṣṭum upakrāntāḥ pramathāḥ brāhmaṇa ṛṣabhān bhājanāni atha svarṇāni rājata sphāṭikāni ca muhūrtena dvijātīnām daduḥ devāḥ vinīta vat hṛtvā hṛtvā babhuu rekham daṇḍe vāri sa maṇḍalam brāhmaṇānām viduḥ ca eva daduḥ ca pramathādhipāḥ bhṛṅgāraiḥ kāñcanaiḥ kecid pānīyam guṇa vardhanam āvījuḥ brāhmaṇān hṛṣṭāḥ pramathāḥ tapasā anilaḥ ekaikam brāhmaṇān tatra sevante vāsavam yathā apsaraḥ vāra saṅghāḥ ca sarva alaṃkāra bhūṣitāḥ nanṛtuḥ deva cetāṃsi muṣṇantyaḥ sarvatodiśam viśvāvasuḥ nāradaḥ ca tumburuḥ parvataḥ tathā nameruḥ guggulūn miśraḥ ghṛta dhārā avasecitaḥ dhūpaḥ saṃcāryate tatra pratīhārībhiḥ uttamaḥ pūjyamānaḥ suraiḥ sa indraiḥ ślokaḥ dhūpa traya aṅkanaḥ tṛptim na devāḥ gacchanti priyāṇām iva darśanāt trayāṇām eva dhūpānām jahuḥ na pavanāḥ gatim tam dṛṣṭvā candramauliḥ tu taruka utsavam īśvaraḥ pārvatī harṣa daḥ harṣam pupoṣa anuttamam muhur carācaram paśupatau trailokyam harṣaṇāyate pranṛtta apsarasaḥ vāram divya dhūpa adhivāsitam ṛtubhiḥ kusumaiḥ kīrṇam tat sadaḥ gaganāyate tatas śālyodanam tūrṇam bhakṣya bhojya anna pānena tatṛpuḥ loka pūjitāḥ tatas śrutimukhaḥ puṇyaḥ rākṣasa asura vejanaḥ puṇyāha śabdaḥ prakṛtaḥ vipraiḥ trailokya pūraṇaḥ tatas sa ambam aśokam tam sa haram saha nandinā kusuma akṣata saṃyuktam āśīrbhiḥ abhinandya ca mahāntaḥ su svanāḥ sarve brahmasūtra jaṭā dharāḥ praṇamantaḥ virūpākṣam yayuḥ viprāḥ yathāgatam surāḥ ca pūjitāḥ dānaiḥ vāc pradānaiḥ ca śūlinā yathāgatam gatāḥ sarve parivārya śatakratum gaṇāḥ ca gaṇapālena pūjitāḥ sa gaṇa adhipāḥ yathāvāsam yayuḥ sarve harṣāt uddhūta vāsasaḥ yā nā evam dayitā bhartuḥ yathā īśasya gireḥ sutā katham sā subhagā nāma strī tvam ca api bibharti kim aho strīṇām balam sūkṣmam devaiḥ api su durjayam yena rudra samāḥ īśāḥ strīṇām vaśya tvam āgatāḥ anye tān abruvan tatra mahātmānaḥ gaṇa adhipāḥ devaḥ eva eṣa rūpeṇa bhāryā bhūtvā avatiṣṭhate mā avamanyata devīm tām yogāt kim nā avabudhyatha iti evam jalpamānāḥ te anyonyena gaṇa uttamāḥ jagmuḥ sva bhavanāni eva dīpyamānāḥ yathā agnayaḥ devaḥ a api nandinā sārdham saḥ aambayā ca abhirūpayā aśoka tarukasya adhas upaviṣṭaḥ tatas praṇamya vara dam somā soma vibhūṣaṇam uvāca vacasām yoniḥ bhūta saṃgha patim patim su nirvṛttā asmi saṃvṛttā tripura andhaka sūdana yat mayā aśoka tarukaḥ putraḥ prakṛtakaḥ kṛtaḥ nūnam me su kṛtam deva tapaḥ parama bhāsvaram devaiḥ yat ca api muṣitam iṣṭa putra phalam purā bhavam bhavānī prītyā evam uktvā muktā āvalī dharā papāta padbhyām devasya netra asra āpūrita īkṣaṇā tām utthāpya girīśaḥ tu pariṣvajya ca pīḍitam brahmaṇyā ca śaraṇyā ca tvam me nityam priyā priye kim punar yat yaśaḥ unmiśram īdṛśam dharma saṃyutam tarpitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ devi devāḥ ca sa gaṇāḥ tvayā gṛhītaḥ putrakaḥ ca ayam tvayā aśoka taruḥ priye ehi devi gṛhān yāma sampūrṇaḥ te manorathaḥ bhūyas sutam tam drakṣyāmaḥ stabakaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam iti uktā patinā sādhvī harṣa pūrṇa mukha īkṣaṇā prāha idam vacanam tatra haritam hariṇa īkṣaṇā gopāyasva hare yatnāt gaja aśvāt ca aṇḍaja aṇḍapāt yadi vā api bhavet eṣa stabakaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ aśoka putrakaḥ mahyam tadā mām draṣṭum arhasi iti saṃdiśya haritam udbhrānta hariṇa īkṣaṇā sa apāṅga cakṣuḥ vikṣepam kṛtvā umā patinā saha viveśa sadanam devī prabhā iva āditya maṇḍalam dvisaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ triṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca śārvam tejaḥ samādāya vahniḥ kim kṛtavān tadā senāpatye katham ca asau abhiṣiktaḥ sura uttamaiḥ iti vijñāpitaḥ dhīmān vyāsena akliṣṭa karmaṇā provāca vadatām śreṣṭhaḥ pitāmaha sutaḥ tadā dāha ātmakaḥ bhūtānām dahyamānaḥ sa tejasā gaṅgām abhyarthayāmāsa dhāraṇe tasya tejasaḥ sā tena abhyarthitā devī hutāśena triloka gā tadā saṃkrāmayāṃcakre gaṅgāyām yoga māyayā jñātvā api durdharam tat sā pratipede varānanā arthi praṇaya nirbhaṅga doṣa bhītā sarit varā bhinnāñjana rucā tanvyā romarājyā rarāja sā ghana rājyāḥ ghana apāye lekhā iva an uṣṇa dīdhiteḥ jagāma ca tadā glānim kiṃcid āvipluta īkṣaṇā na upalebhe tadā devī ratim śayyā āsaneṣu ca amṛta syandibhiḥ śītaiḥ spṛṣṭā api śaśinaḥ karaiḥ mamlau sā tejasā tena dahyamānā tadā anaghā śara madhyāt samabhavat bālaḥ bāla parākramaḥ ṣaḍvaktraḥ dvādaśa bhujaḥ sūrya koṭi sama dyutiḥ samidhya vidhinā tatra pāvakam pāvaka tviṣaḥ kṛttikāḥ tam tadā dṛṣṭvā prasnuta uru payodharāḥ upatasthuḥ ca tam vedāḥ sa upavedāḥ sa saṃgrahāḥ kalāḥ vidyāḥ ca nikhilāḥ lakṣmīḥ medhā sarasvatī kāntiḥ dharmaḥ dayā kṣāntiḥ dhṛtiḥ dhairyam parākramaḥ yogaḥ tejaḥ balam prajñā sthiti gāmbhīrya satkriyāḥ sandhāya līlayā bāṇam sa mumoca girau tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam sattvānām tad nivāsinām atha prekṣya bhayam tasmāt ātmanaḥ balasūdanaḥ mātR̥ḥ sampreṣayāmāsa vināśāya amita dyuteḥ āgatya mātaraḥ tatra dṛṣṭvā tam tejasām nidhim airāvata gaja skandham ārūḍhaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ āgacchataḥ surān dṛṣṭvā nanāda uccais mahā dyutiḥ babhūvuḥ tena nādena muhur mūḍhāḥ divaukasaḥ abhūt airāvaṇasya api mada dhvaṃsaḥ kapolayoḥ arcīṃṣi ca pradīptāni visasarja sahasraśas trilocana sutaḥ teṣām surāṇām sura darpa hā roṣāt ātāmra netra antaḥ visasarja śatakratuḥ atha darpam vihāya āśu praṇeme pākaśāsanaḥ gṛhāṇa rājyam api etat prārthanīyam manasvinām tvam eva yuktaḥ lokānām pālane pāvaka ātmaja agnau eva haviḥ puṇyam hūyate prāha prabhavatām śreṣṭhaḥ vihasya vibudha adhipam śādhi śakra tvam eva idam rājyam ciram abhīpsitam niśāmya tad vacaḥ śrīmān skandasya akliṣṭa cetasaḥ arthavat vacanam ślakṣṇam punar āha śacīpatiḥ darśaya naḥ vicitrāṇi kārya jātāni anekadhā saṃgatāni vibhinnāni na vicālayitum cetaḥ śakra śaktāḥ haṭhāt mama rājyam rājīva patra akṣa na jātu manasā api aham doṣāṇām nityam āvāsam kāmaye pākaśāsana vapuḥ saṃmānayāmi iha na aham ājñāpaye vibho atha tat vacanam śrutvā puruhūtam mahā bhujaḥ dvādaśākṣaḥ sahasrākṣam idam āha uru vikramaḥ mama prabhavati śrīmān lokānām prabhuḥ avyayaḥ ananya bhūḥ ameya ātmā vṛṣaketuḥ purandara tam ārādhya prabhum bhaktyā gṛhāṇa ājñām śatakrato tasya abhiprāyam ājñāya devadevaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ ājagāma sa patnīkaḥ didṛkṣuḥ tanayam tadā svāhayā sahitaḥ vahniḥ gaṅgā ca saritām varā kṛttikāḥ ca su saṃhṛṣṭāḥ śvetam śikhariṇām varam cintayāmāsuḥ āyāntaḥ kam nu skandaḥ atha teṣām abhiprāyam jñātvā matimatām varaḥ ṣoḍhā samabhavat skandaḥ yogi īśaḥ bala vat tadā naigameṣaḥ yayau gaṅgām vahnim śākhaḥ mahā dyutiḥ svāhām jagāma saṃhṛṣṭaḥ kākapakṣa dharaḥ guhaḥ kṛttikāḥ ṣaṇmukhaḥ śrīmān vegāt abhisasāra ca manorathān sa sarveṣām devadeva ātmajaḥ prabhuḥ yugapad yoginām īśaḥ pūrayāmāsa mūrtibhiḥ sudhā kaṇa parisrāvi cūḍāratnam ca pārvatī sva manaḥ nirmalām gaṅgā viśuddhām amṛta udbhavām dviṣat prāṇa harām gurvīm amoghām havyavāhanaḥ arciṣmatīm dadau ca asmai śaktim śaktāya sūnave patākām mahatīm raktām jvalat pāvaka saprabhām kiṅkiṇī nāditām divyām prādāt svāhā mahātmane su puṇya gandhām utphullām sva rajaḥ paripiñjarām kṛttikāḥ ca daduḥ tasmai mālām añcita kesarām atha ājagmuḥ surāḥ sarve pitāmaha puraḥsarāḥ śvetādreḥ śikharam ramyam vṛṣaketum didṛkṣavaḥ tān āgatān samam sarvān tadā tatra divaukasaḥ dṛṣṭyā sambhāvayāmāsa mahādevaḥ prasannayā praṇamya devadeveśam labdhvā anujñām divaukasaḥ śilāsu śaśi gaurīṣu niṣeduḥ amita ojasaḥ prottuṅga śikharaḥ śvetaḥ dyutimān api bhūdharaḥ vyajñāpayat mahādevam praṇamya vadatām varaḥ tāraka ākhyena naḥ lakṣmīḥ āmṛṣṭā prasabham prabho vajram vakṣaḥ sthale tasya kaṭhine kuṇṭha tām yayau āsādya mṛdu tām bheje kaṇṭham tasya amara dviṣaḥ daṇḍaḥ vaivasvatasya api pradīpta anala bhāsvaraḥ samare ripu survāraḥ mahā pāśaḥ pracetasaḥ tasya kaṇṭhe samabhavat mantreṇa iva vaśīkṛtaḥ utpāṭya prasabham tena nandane kalpapādapāḥ niveśitāḥ yathākāmam sva gṛha udyāna bhūmiṣu samīpe tasya sa āśaṅkaḥ tālavṛntāyate miṣatām sarva devānām devadeva diteḥ sutaḥ abhiṣicya surāḥ skandam senāpatye mahā dyutim evam vijñāpitaḥ tatra vajriṇā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ dadau anujñām skandāya senāpatya abhiṣecane iti skandapurāṇe skanda abhiṣeka anujñāne trisaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ atha te skandam ādāya surāḥ brahma puraḥsarāḥ vistīrṇe śvabhra pāṣāṇa kaṇṭaka ūṣara varjite skandasya paritas sarve tadā saṃhṛṣṭa cetasaḥ niṣeduḥ te sura śreṣṭhāḥ jvalita anala varcasaḥ tat puṇyam amaraiḥ pṛktam sthānam puṇyataram punar abhūt gāṅgaiḥ iva ambhobhiḥ sametam yāmunam payaḥ ājagāma atha tam deśam kṣitiḥ mūrtimatī tadā skanda abhiṣeke saṃjāte harṣa samphulla locanā atha asau kṣipram abhavat deśaḥ kanakabālukaḥ adhyāsata mahātmānaḥ yam deśam apamatsarāḥ nirasta duritaḥ saḥ tatra teṣām vibhūtibhiḥ atha siṃhāsanam divyam śātakumbham susaṃskṛtam gṛhītvā giribhiḥ sārdham ājagāma himālayaḥ ratnaiḥ oṣadhibhiḥ gandhaiḥ pūrṇān puṇyaiḥ ca vāribhiḥ ādāya kalaśān haimān phulla amburuha mālinaḥ udanvantaḥ su sambhrāntāḥ pracalat maṇi kuṇḍalāḥ gaṅgā ratna mayān cārūn kalaśān sphurita tviṣaḥ haima ambuja kṛtta uttsaṃsān pūrṇān parama vāriṇā gṛhītvā saha sarvābhiḥ saridbhiḥ saritām varā ājagāma tadā harṣāt praskhalantī sameṣu api abhiṣecanikān kumbhān grāhayitvā su saṃskṛtān devībhiḥ saha bahvībhiḥ ājagāma divaukasām ākrāmantī iva tejāṃsi tejasā svena pārvatī adbhiḥ parama puṇyābhiḥ pūrṇān ratna aṃśu mālinaḥ kalaśān sphāṭikān śubhrān grāhayitvā susaṃskṛtān nānā ratna vicitra aṃśu samūha sphurita udaram hāram ca nirmalam śuddham śaśāṅka kiraṇa tviṣam kāntam muktā vitānam ca cetaḥ hāri su nirmalam abhyāgamat tadā tatra prahṛṣṭaḥ yādasām patiḥ dānava adhipa mātaṅga viṣāṇa ullikhita aṅgadaḥ ratna aṅgadāni cārūṇi dyutimanti dhaneśvaraḥ samādāya abhyagāt sāram sarvāsām iva sampadām niśākara aṃśu gaurāṇi dīrghāṇi rucimanti ca ādāya ratna daṇḍāni cāmarāṇi mahā dyutiḥ ṛtavaḥ tam tadā deśam ājagmuḥ tuṣṭa cetasaḥ arundhatī śacī svāhā sinīvālī girīndrajā aditiḥ deva mātā ca niśā sā anumatiḥ kuhūḥ hrīḥ śrīḥ puṣṭiḥ diśaḥ dyauḥ ca sutāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpateḥ rākā ca dhiṣaṇā ca eva surabhiḥ devayoṣitaḥ oṣadhyaḥ mūrtimatyaḥ ca kauśikī vana devatā ahar kāṣṭhāḥ muhurtāḥ ca māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ kalāḥ airāvaṇaḥ supratīkaḥ vāmanaḥ kumudaḥ aañjanaḥ puṣpadantaḥ mahāpadmaḥ sārvabhaumaḥ ca diggajāḥ ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tvaritāḥ abhiyayuḥ guham niyamita ūrjita nitya tapaḥ kriyāḥ upayayuḥ garuḍāḥ ca vimatsarāḥ bhujaga rāja surūḍha bala udayāḥ nanṛtuḥ āyata lola vilocanāḥ vividha bhāva vilāsa rasa anvitāḥ parama yauvana rūpa guṇa anvitāḥ pramuditāḥ paritas a apsarasaḥ a alasāḥ virajasaḥ mṛdu vṛttayaḥ vibudha citta sukhāḥ ca samīraṇāḥ ābhiṣecanikam kṛtvā vidhim tasya bṛhaspatiḥ āśīrbhiḥ āśiṣām dhāma samāśliṣya śivātmajam maṅgalāni jaguḥ tasya gandharvāḥ nāradaḥ ca yaḥ pratisārya tadā vīṇām tāram raktam an ākulam atha tam dakṣiṇe pāṇau gṛhītvā kṛta maṅgalam guruḥ siṃhāsane tasmin prāc mukham saṃnyaveśayat bhṛśam dundubhayaḥ citrāḥ samyak cetaḥ upahāriṇaḥ matta dvirepha saṃgītāḥ sva kiñjalka aruṇa tviṣaḥ puṇya gandhāḥ vicitrāḥ ca nipetuḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭayaḥ ādade kalaśam pūrvam pūrṇam puṇyena vāriṇā samādhāya ambaram pītam tatas viṣṇuḥ samādade kalaśam kaustubha maṇeḥ parāmṛṣṭam gabhastibhiḥ tatas keyūra ratna aṃśu khacitam pākaśāsanaḥ uttarīyam niyamya āśu jagrāha kalaśam tadā nibadhya śaśi lekhā aṅkāḥ jaṭāḥ jvalana piṅgalāḥ jagṛhuḥ kalaśān rudrāḥ bhujaṅga kṛta kaṅkaṇāḥ bibhrataḥ parām dīptim sukha saṃsparśa mūrtayaḥ ādityāḥ jagṛhuḥ pūrṇān kalaśān puṇya vāribhiḥ ādaduḥ kalaśān tatra pūrṇān puṇyena vāriṇā aśvinau api puṇyābhiḥ pūrṇāvadbhiḥ su saṃskṛtau ādadāte tadā kumbhau haimau ratna aṃśu mālinau haima amburuha saṃchannān citrān ratna gabhastibhiḥ nāga gandharva rājānaḥ lokapālāḥ marut gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ bālakhilyāḥ ca pitaraḥ pataga īśvarāḥ dharmaḥ dhātā vidhātā ca kālaḥ mṛtyuḥ vasundharā sandhyā kāntiḥ dhṛtiḥ medhā kīrtiḥ lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī samudrāḥ saritaḥ vedāḥ tīrthāni girayaḥ grahāḥ kumbhān ādadire tatra pūrṇān parama vāriṇā atha te hṛṣṭa manasaḥ prahṛṣṭam pāvakātmajam jayinaḥ śarvaputrasya ṛṣayaḥ ca samāgatāḥ jagrāha maghavā tasya śvetam ātapa vāraṇam dudhuvuḥ cāmaraiḥ dīrghaiḥ śarad candra aṃśu nirmalaiḥ paritas ratna daṇḍaiḥ ca lokapālāḥ mahā dyutim amṛtāt utthitam divyam upanītam pracetasā hema avadāte vistīrṇe śaśāṅka kiraṇa dyutim tasya vakṣaḥ sthale hāram babandha saritām varā hāreṇa alaṃkṛtam vakṣaḥ kim tu hāraḥ guhā urasā ābabandha mahā bāhoḥ aṅgadāni su alaṃkṛtā bhujeṣu pāraṇa ālāna stambha pīneṣu arundhatī dīptimān pāvaka sutaḥ tadā abhūt dīptimattaraḥ mahā pāriṣadān śūrān balinaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ ghaṇṭākarṇam su rakta akṣam nandiṣeṇam ca durjayam caturtham balinām śreṣṭham khyātam kumudamālinam dadau sthāṇuḥ mahā vīryam mahāpāriṣadam kratum sampravṛtte tadā ghore saṃgrāme tārakā maye kruddhaḥ jaghāna daityānām yaḥ yutāni caturdaśa vibudhāḥ ca daduḥ tasmai senām nairṛta saṃkulām daitya yakṣa kṣaya karīm ajeyām viśva rūpiṇīm unmātham ca pramātham ca mahā vīrya parākramau kārttikeyāya saṃhṛṣṭaḥ raṇe parama durjayau jvālājihvam tathā jyotim ātmajāya vibhāvasuḥ parigham paṭaham bhīmam daha atidahanau tathā aṃśaḥ pañca dadau skandāya dhīmate dadau jvalana putrāya viṣṇuḥ prītaḥ mahā yaśāḥ skandāya dadatuḥ prītau aśvinau ca mahā balau ḍambara āḍambarau ca ubhau dadau dhātā agni sūnave dadau tvaṣṭā mahā māyau skandāya anucarau ubhau suprabham ca mahā māyam śubhakarmāṇam eva ca prādāt vidhātā skandāya śatru pakṣa niṣūdanau pālintakam mahā vīryam kālakam ca mahā balam dadau pāriṣadau pūṣā skandāya amita tejase balam ca atibalam ca eva mahā kāyau mahā balau pradadau kārttikeyāya vāyuḥ prītaḥ mahātmane dadau jvalana putrāya varuṇaḥ pāśa dhāriṇau suvarcasam mahā vīryam tathā ca api ativarcasam kāñcanam ca mahā māyam tathā jīmūta mālinam ucchṛṅgam ca viśṛṅgam ca śilā pāṣāṇa yodhinau pradadau kārttikeyāya mahā pāriṣadau tadā unmādam puṣpadantam ca śaṅkukarṇam ca durjayam mahā vīryān mahāsattvān prādāt putrāya pārvatī jayam mahājayam ca eva daduḥ nāgāḥ mahātmane dadau ca parama prītaḥ skandāya vṛṣavāhanaḥ bahūn pāriṣadān śūrān samare durjayān paraiḥ sanandam dvādaśabhujam tathā kṛṣṇa upakṛṣṇakau kṛta grīvam kapi skandham kāñcana akṣam jalandhamam akṣisantardanam kuṇṭham pārśvagrīvam mahodaram eka akṣam dvādaśa bhujam eka pādam mahā jaṭam sahasra bāhum vikacam vyāghra āsyam kṣiti kampanam pṛṣṭhavaktram sunāmānam pārśvānana mahānanau jvālā jihvam karālam ca śita keśam tata udaram aṣṭa jihvam catur daṃṣṭram megha nādam pṛthu udaram vidyut akṣam dhanuḥ vaktram jaraṭham mārutāśanam udarākṣam jhaṣākṣam ca vajranābham ca suprabham dhūmram śvetam kaliṅgam ca siddhārtham varadam tathā kṣepavāham sujātam ca siddhayātram mahā varam govrajam kanakāpīḍam mahāpārśvam mahodaram gāyanam hasanam ca eva bāṇa khaḍga dharam prabhum vaitālim ca atitālim ca tathā śaṭhika vātikau raṇa utkaṭam prabhāsam ca śveta mūrdhānam acyutam kālakaṇṭha śarīram ca kuṣmāṇḍam śatru tāpanam gomāyu vaktram śyena āsyam bhū tala unmāthanam tathā yajñavāham pravāham ca kāka āsyam kāka locanam mañjulam vakra nāsam ca mahā nāsam gajodaram madhuram su prasādam ca kirīṭam makuṭa utkaṭam vasanam madhu varṇam ca kalaśam kalaśa udaram śveta vaktram su vaktram ca cāru vaktram ca pāṇḍaram kaṇṭhabāhum subāhum ca bakam kokilakam tathā acalam kanakākṣam ca balānām agra nāyakam saṃcāram ca kokamukham gṛdhrāsyam jambukam tathā lomaśam ca jarā āsyam ca uṣṭra grīvam kamaṇḍalum daṇḍakam dīrgha vaktram ca haṃsa vaktram mahā balam ṭuṇḍukam śatapādam ca śatākṣam cāpapṛṣṭhakam śikṣakam ca apavaktram ca śākhavaktram ca kuṇḍakam mahā yogān mahāsattvān satatam brahmacāriṇaḥ apradhṛṣyān mahā vīryān samare ripu sūdanān nānā śastra praharaṇān nānā rūpān mahā ojasaḥ nānā vaktraiḥ parivṛtān gaṇaiḥ ca gaṇanāyakān gaja indra carma vasanān vyāghra kṛṣṇa ajina ambarān rakta keśān hari śmaśrūn muṇḍān digvāsasaḥ ā aparān jaṭinaḥ piṅga netrān ca bhujaṅga kṛta mekhalān pannaga aṅgadinaḥ śūrān śavasat bhogi indrakuṇḍān pāvanaiḥ paridigdha aṅgān bhasmabhiḥ candra pāṇḍuraiḥ nṛtyataḥ valgamānān ca hāsa utphulla vilocanān gaṇaiḥ parivṛtān anyaiḥ bahubhiḥ gaṇanāyakān kūrma kukkuṭa vaktraiḥ ca śaśa godhāvṛka ānanaiḥ khara uṣṭra aśva mukhaiḥ bhīmaiḥ varāha mahiṣa ānanaiḥ manuṣya meḍhra vaktraiḥ ca śva śṛgāla mṛga ānanaiḥ bhīmaiḥ makara vaktraiḥ ca śiśumāra jhaṣa ānanaiḥ ākhu babhru viḍālānām tulya āsyaiḥ ripu durjayaiḥ chāga meṣa mukhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ śuka kāraṇḍava ānanaiḥ ṛkṣa śārdūla vaktraiḥ ca dvipi siṃha ānanaiḥ tathā garuḍa kroṣṭuka āsyaiḥ ca kāka kokila vaktrakaiḥ go vānara mukhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ śyena gṛdhra mukhaiḥ tathā mahā jaṭhara pāda aṅgaiḥ tāraka akṣaiḥ mahā balaiḥ pārāvata mukhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ kṛkavāku mukhaiḥ tathā pīta kauśeya vāsobhiḥ cīra valkala dhāribhiḥ phaṇi indra ānaddha gātraiḥ ca citragonasa kaṅkaṇaiḥ sthūla udaraiḥ kṛśa aṅgaiḥ ca sthūla aṅgaiḥ ca kṛśa udaraiḥ hrasva grīvaiḥ mahā karṇaiḥ nānā vyāla vibhūṣaṇaiḥ nānā kṛli bhujaiḥ vīraiḥ nānā bhujaga bhīṣaṇaiḥ nānā veṣaiḥ mahā yogaiḥ nānā sthāna nivāsibhiḥ nānā vastra dharaiḥ ca anyaiḥ nānā mālya anulepanaiḥ nānā carma abaraiḥ anyaiḥ nānā ābharaṇa dhāribhiḥ uṣṇīṣibhiḥ mukuṭibhiḥ kambu grīvaiḥ su saṃsthitaiḥ kirīṭibhiḥ pañcaśikhaiḥ jaṭā mukuṭa dhāribhiḥ śikhaṇḍibhiḥ dīrghajaṭaiḥ muṇḍaiḥ kapila mūrdhajaiḥ kṛṣṇa nirmāṃsa vaktraiḥ ca dīrgha pṛṣṭhaiḥ kṛśa udaraiḥ sthūla pṛṣṭhaiḥ mahā grīvaiḥ lamba udara mahā udaraiḥ mahā bhujaiḥ mahā vaktraiḥ hrasva grīvaiḥ kṛśa ānanaiḥ kubjaiḥ ca dīrgha jaṅghaiḥ ca hasti karṇa śirodharaiḥ dīrgha uṣṭhaiḥ dīrgha jihvaiḥ ca dīrgha akṣaiḥ dīrgha nāsikaiḥ mahā daṃṣṭraiḥ sudaṃṣṭraiḥ ca citra daṃṣṭraiḥ mahā balaiḥ su vibhakta śarīraiḥ ca dīptimadbhiḥ su alaṃkṛtaiḥ piṅgala akṣaiḥ mahā karṇaiḥ śaṅku karṇaiḥ akarṇakaiḥ dīrgha daṃṣṭraiḥ pṛthu uraskaiḥ sthūla uṣṭhaiḥ hari mūrdhajaiḥ nānā pāda uṣṭha daṃṣṭraiḥ ca nānā hasta śirodharaiḥ nānā carmabhiḥ ācchannaiḥ nānā vāsobhiḥ āvṛtaiḥ hṛṣṭaiḥ paripatadbhiḥ ca nṛtyadbhiḥ ca mahā ravaiḥ śveta aṅgaiḥ lohita grīvaiḥ piṅga akṣaiḥ bhīma darśanaiḥ kalmāṣa pāṇi pādaiḥ ca jātī hiṅgulaka prabhaiḥ cāmīkara āpīḍa nibhaiḥ śvetaiḥ lohita rājibhiḥ rājāvartta savarṇaiḥ ca mayūra sadṛśa prabhaiḥ pāśa udyata karaiḥ kaiścid vyātta vaktraiḥ mahā ravaiḥ piṅga akṣaiḥ nīlakaṇṭhaiḥ ca mahā parigha bāhubhiḥ śataghnī śakti hastaiḥ ca gadā muśala pāṇibhiḥ śūla asi pāṇibhiḥ kaiścid mahā kāyaiḥ mahā balaiḥ bhuśuṇḍī prāsa hastaiḥ ca vīraiḥ paraśu pāṇibhiḥ pāśa mudgara hastaiḥ ca cakra tomara pāṇibhiḥ citra āyudha dharaiḥ vīraiḥ āvṛṇvadbhiḥ diśaḥ diśam ghaṇṭā jāla vinaddha aṅgaiḥ kiṃkiṇī jāla dhāribhiḥ vṛtāḥ gaṇaiḥ gaṇa adhyakṣāḥ mahāsattvaiḥ mahā balaiḥ mahā balāḥ mahāsattvāḥ samareṣu aparājitāḥ prabhāvatīm viśāla akṣīm palitām vṛṣa nāsikām śrīmatīm bahulām siṃhīm vijayām bahu putrikām gopālīm suprabhām ṣaṣṭhīm bṛhat ambālikām kṛśām jayāvatīm mālatikām dhruvaratnām prabhākarīm suprabhām vasudām ca eva viśokām nandinīm tathā vajracūḍām mahā cūḍām vajranemim mahā prabhām añjanīm ca bharatsenām kamalākṣīm śaśiprabhām śatruñjayām mahā nāsām krodhanām śalabhīm khaṣīm mādhavīm śuka vaktrām ca kīrtinemim aninditām gītapriyām mahāmāyām vāyasīm amṛtām satīm sarasvatīm bhogavatīm subhrūm ca kanakāvatīm sutām lakṣmīm vīryavatīm vidyujjihvām mahā balām padmāvatīm su nakṣatrām kandarām bahu yojanām santānikām śivām ca eva kamalām maladām api sudāmām bahudāmām ca suprabhām ca yaśasvinīm nṛtta priyām varārohām sita ulūkhala mekhalām śata ghaṇṭām śata ānandām śata netrām yaśasvinīm vapuṣmatīm ca śīlām ca bhadrakālīm ca bhairavām saṃhārikām niṣkuṭikām bhūtām catvara vāsinīm su maṅgalām svastimatīm vṛddhi kāmām jana priyām dhana dām su pradām ca eva bhava dām sukha dām api ailīm bhelīm samelīm ca vetālīm jananīm niśām kaṇḍūm piṅgalikām ca eva devamitrām yaśasvinīm lambuṣīm sanakām ca eva citrasenām atha acalām kukūnikām śaṅkhinikām tathā jharjharikām api kuṇḍālikām lokavilām kaṇḍarām ca śatodarīm utkvāthinīm jurelām ca mahāvelām ca kaṅkaṇām manojavām kaṇṭakinīm vighasām pūtanām tathā vaiśayām carcikām vāmām krodhanām mukhamaṇḍikām maṇḍodarīm ca ṭuṇḍām ca koṭarām meghavāsinīm subhagām lambinīm lambām vāma dhūlīm vikatthanām ūrdhva veṇī dharām ca eva lalāṭa nayanām tathā pṛthu barhām mahā kāyām madhu kumbhām taḍit prabhām manthānikām unmanikām jarāyum jarjara ānanām khyātām dahadahām ca eva tathā dhamadhamām api khaṭaṃkhaṭām mahā vīryām vṛṣaṇām maṇituṇḍikām baddha veṇīm dharā dhārām piṅga akṣīm lamba karṇikām āmodām ca pramodām ca tathā lamba payodharām śaśa ulūka mukhīm kṛṣṇām khara jaṅghām mahā ravām śiśumāra mukhīm śvetām lohita akṣīm vibhīṣaṇām jaṭālikām kāmacarīm dīrghajihvām ca lolupām kanelikām vāsanikām mukuṭām ca mahābalām lohita akṣīm mahā kāyām haripiṇḍīm ca durjayām paśudām vittadām vīrām aṅgadām ca mahā balām payaḥ dām go pradām śaṅkhām su niṣaṇṇām tarasvinīm pratiṣṭhām supratiṣṭhām ca rocamānām su rocanām gokarṇīm aśvakarṇīm ca aśirām kharikām tathā kacakracām megha ravām megha mālām virocanām etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca bahulāḥ mātaraḥ mārutasya dāḥ ekākṣarām sugandhām ca kṛṣṇakarṇīm ca dāruṇām kṣura karṇīm catuṣkarṇīm karṇa prāvaraṇām tathā catuṣpatha niketām ca gokarṇīm mahiṣa ānanām kharakarṇīm mahākarṇīm bherī svana mahā svane śaṅkha kumbha śravām ca eva saṃgrāmeṣu aparājitām gaṇām ca sugaṇām ca eva tathā vātīm ca kāmagām catuṣpatha ravām ca eva bhūtinīm vanya gocarām kārttikeya anuyāyinyaḥ nānā rūpāḥ sahasraśas dīrgha dantyaḥ dīrgha vaktra ati bhīṣaṇāḥ caturāḥ madhurāḥ ca eva yauvana sthāḥ su alaṃkṛtāḥ māhātmyena ca saṃyuktāḥ kāmarūpāḥ mahā balāḥ nirmāṃsa gātryaḥ śvetāḥ ca jāmbūnada sama prabhāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ jīmūta varṇāḥ ca dhūmra keśyaḥ mahā bhayāḥ asurāṇām mahā daṃṣṭrāḥ dīrgha daṃṣṭrāḥ sita ambarāḥ ūrdhva karṇī dharāḥ ca eva piṅga akṣyaḥ lamba mekhalāḥ tāmra akṣyaḥ tāmra vaktrāḥ ca hari akṣyaḥ hari mūrdhajāḥ vṛkṣa catvara vāsinyaḥ catuṣpatha niketanāḥ guhā śmaśāna vāsinyaḥ śaila prasravaṇa ālayāḥ nānā ābharaṇa dhāriṇyaḥ nānā sraj anulepanāḥ nānā vastrāṇi bibhratyaḥ nānā āyudha dharāḥ tathā etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca saṃhṛṣṭāḥ dadau skandāya kauśikī vaijayantīm dadau tasmai mālām añcita kesarām viṣṇuḥ vividha gaṇḍa āḍhyām utphullām cāru darśanām samprītā prīta manase dadau skandāya pārvatī kamaṇḍalum sudhā vāri sampūrṇam amṛta udbhavam dadau prītā kumārāya gaṅgā gambhīra cetase garutmān dayitam putram citrabarham śikhaṇḍinam dadau skandāya samprītaḥ balinam kāmarūpiṇam tāmracūḍam adāt vīram aruṇaḥ caraṇa āyudham mahā bhāra saham chāgam kāmagam kāmarūpiṇam brahmaṇyāya dadau brahmā medhyam kṛṣṇa ajina ambaram tejasām nidhaye tasmai dadau daṇḍam bṛhaspatiḥ skandāya parama prītaḥ cāru cāmīkara srajam senāpatim tam abhiṣicya hutāśa putram samyak prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ vibudhāḥ sametāḥ daitya īśvarasya nidhanāya mahā prabhāvāḥ yātrām surāri jayinī sahitāḥ pracakruḥ iti skandapurāṇe senāpatya abhiṣeke catuḥṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ pañcaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ skandam purodhāya surāḥ samastāḥ sannāhayāmāsuḥ anīkam āśu āhatya bherīḥ śataśas mahadbhiḥ daṇḍaiḥ dṛḍham hāṭaka ratna citraiḥ digvāraṇān bhūdhara kūṭa kalpān mandākinī vāribhiḥ āpluta aṅgān teṣām su yatnāt gaja vāji mukhyān haimāni yantrāṇi tathā āyudhānām citrāḥ samucchiśriyire patākāḥ dhvajāḥ ca cāmīkara cāru daṇḍāḥ kṣurapra mālāḥ vividhāḥ babandhuḥ pakṣeṣu ghaṇṭāḥ ca samāsasarjuḥ ratham ca kārtasvara cāru cakram sāṃgrāmikam ratna marīci citram saṃyojayāmāsuḥ udāra veṣaiḥ prahṛṣṭa cittaiḥ khagamaiḥ turaṅgaiḥ babandhuḥ uccais viniyamya piṅgāḥ jaṭāḥ bhujaṅgaiḥ bṛhatīḥ śvasadbhiḥ citrāṇi hṛṣṭāḥ kavacāni rudrāḥ vakṣaḥsu daitya dvipa vikṣateṣu citram dadhānaḥ kavacam mahā dyutiḥ nibaddha nistriṃśa tala aṅgulitravān bibhrat dhanuḥ sajjam api iddha pauruṣaḥ jahau śaśāṅkaḥ sahajām na saumya tām yatnāt babandhuḥ kavacāni sūryāḥ kiṃcid pradīptāni tadā sva dīptyā lauhāni abhedyāni śaraiḥ parāstaiḥ cārūṇi cāmīkara citritāni nibaddha bhāsvat kavacaḥ sudhanvā su pīna nistriṃśa nibaddha pārśvaḥ rucā parītaḥ parayā atimātram sphuran muhur pronnata pūrva kāyaḥ parābhavam vidviṣatām samāje pracetasaḥ khyāpayati iva pāśaḥ dṛṣṭim dhaneśaḥ hutāśa piṅgām dadhat gadāyām parigha ūru bāhuḥ īśa prasādena nijena vā iti suradviṣām āhanane vināśam sainye aatha deva dviṣatām nipetuḥ ulkāḥ sphurat vahni kaṇāḥ bṛhatyaḥ vinā ghanaiḥ vyoma rarāsa bhīmam sa vṛkṣa śailā vicacāla ca urvī rajaḥ nabhastaḥ paritas papāta vāta īritam rāsabha pṛṣṭha dhūsram dhvajāḥ nipetuḥ dṛḍha hema daṇḍāḥ rakta ambu vṛṣṭim sasṛjuḥ payodāḥ kapola bhittīḥ prajahau gajānām madaḥ ca pārāvata kaṇṭha nīlaḥ sthāneṣu dīpteṣu vineduḥ uccais dīpta svarāḥ pakṣi mṛga aśva saṃghāḥ senā prahṛṣṭā mahatī surāṇām abhyāyayau daitya patim rarāṇā sainyāni tāni tridaśa asurāṇām anyonyam āseduḥ udāyudhāni kṣubdhāni atīva pralaye mahā abdheḥ pūrva aparāṇi iva tadā jalāni niśāmya daityāḥ raṇa tūrya nisvanam prarūḍha garvāḥ balinaḥ jaya utsukāḥ ati praharṣāt asamāpta maṅgalāḥ gṛhīta śastrāḥ samarāya niryayuḥ ratha aśva pādāta samuddhatam rajaḥ raṇa ajire vānara kaṇṭha dhūsaram svanaḥ ca teṣām ati dāruṇaḥ mahān nabhaḥ tadā vyāpa diśaḥ ca sarvatas śastrāṇi gātreṣu tantutravatsu nipātyamānāni parasparasya dṛṣṭvā asurān sattva bala upapannān surāḥ sahāyān an apekṣya kecid sannehire matta gajān iva ibhāḥ mada ambubhiḥ śyāma kapola deśāḥ balāni vegāt abhisṛtya dūram agresarāṇi tridaśa asurāṇām sva jīvita āśām apahāya jaghnuḥ anyonyam āviṣkṛta pauruṣāṇi nikāma vaira āśaya mānasānām jighāṃsatām tatra paraspareṇa sa samprahāraḥ tumulaḥ tadā āsīt sura asurāṇām anavaḥ mahā jau seduḥ gajāḥ tomara śakti bhinnāḥ turaṅgamāḥ bāṇa hatāḥ nipetuḥ sa phenam āsyaiḥ rudhiram vamantaḥ dṛḍha prahārān mumuhuḥ ca yodhāḥ chināni petuḥ niśitaiḥ kṣurapraiḥ sa kuṇḍalāni ānana paṅkajāni muṣṭi prahāraiḥ tala pārṣṇi ghātaiḥ vikarṣaṇa āveṣṭana pīḍanaiḥ ca mātaṅga mukhyān dviradaiḥ prabhinnaiḥ turaṅgamān vājibhiḥ uttamān ca rathān rathaiḥ patti gaṇān padātaiḥ gaṇāḥ nijaghnuḥ yudhi dānavānām utpatya vegāt iṣubhiḥ gaṇa indrāḥ gaja adhirūḍhān ditija indra yodhān muṣṭi prahāraiḥ kuliśa ugra pātaiḥ vibhinna mastiṣka vinirgata akṣān paraśvadhaiḥ cicchiduḥ ātta roṣāḥ khaḍgaiḥ cakartuḥ bibhiduḥ ca śūlaiḥ mahā dvipālān anitānta pīnaiḥ prapothayāṃcakruḥ arīn bhujaiḥ ca utpatya vāji pravara adhirūḍhān ratha sthitān vāraṇa dhūrgatān ca pracukṣubhe tat balam āsuram tadā gaṇa indra niṣpiṣṭa bala agra nāyakam garutmataḥ pakṣa samīraṇa āhatam mahā hradam yadvat agādham ambudheḥ atha abhivīkṣya prasabham gaṇādhipaiḥ nihanyamānāni balāni tārakaḥ ruṣā tadā tāmratara āyata īkṣaṇaḥ samabhyagāt mauli bala abhipālitaḥ saṃchādayan bāṇa talaiḥ nabhastalam marma atigaiḥ kaṅka mayūra patribhiḥ tasya āgamam daitya pateḥ viditvā tadā nanāda analasūnuḥ uccais sva pāṇi saṃsthām abhivīkṣya śaktim vicitra cāmīkara cāru ghaṇṭām nabhaḥ vigāhya pradiśaḥ diśaḥ ca sa kārttikeyasya tadā ninādaḥ manāṃsi deva dviṣatām prasahya vimohayāmāsa mahā samāje atha apatantam samabhīkṣya tārakam balena guptam mahatā mahā āhave mumoca śaktim jvalita anala prabhām vināśanāya amara vidviṣām guhaḥ sā tena muktā jvalanātmajena jvālābhiḥ āvṛtya nabhaḥ diśaḥ ca papāta vakṣaḥsu ca saṃhateṣu suradviṣām citra tanutra bhṛtsu samam samastaiḥ tu anivārya vegā vidārya corāṃsi viveśa tūrṇam deva dviṣaḥ te a abhihatāḥ samastāḥ paryasta pṛthu āyata rakta netrāḥ saṃdaṣṭa jihvā adhara vihvala aṅgāḥ prāṇān jahuḥ śoṇitam udvamantaḥ bibheda tadvat dviṣatām balāni raṇa ajire śaktibhiḥ agni sūnuḥ dititanaya samūhaiḥ sārdham āvi pratāpaiḥ tridaśa samiti mukhyaiḥ stūyamānaḥ prahṛṣṭaiḥ pratigamat amita ojāḥ śūlapāṇeḥ samīpam pañcasaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ ṣaṭṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tatas param sa deveśaḥ tripurāriḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ kva jagāma ca deveśaḥ kim uvāca acala ātmajā kāni ca enam umā prāha śaṃsa etat pṛcchataḥ mama sūtaḥ uvāca vyāsena evam tadā pṛṣṭaḥ ākhyātum upacakrame sarva āgama para artha jñaḥ brahma sūnuḥ mahā tapāḥ nānā ratna samākīrṇe hema śṛṅge iva ucchrite tasya pārśve sthitā devī rarāja himavat sutā vyabhre viyati pūrṇa indoḥ rohiṇī iva samīpa gā sā uvāca parameśānam praṇamya girijā tadā pūrva praṇaya labdhā ca tena pṛcchāmi aśaṅkitā pāvanāni pavitrāṇi nāmāni tava kāma da sārthāni śrotum icchāmi kathitāni tvayā vibho evam pṛṣṭaḥ tadā gauryā prāha sarvam surādhipaḥ mṛtyu hartā yatas ca api haraḥ tena prakīrtitaḥ puram śarīram ākhyātam sarveṣām prāṇinām iha sarva prāṇi gatam yasmāt tat puram śayanam mama pālayāmi paśūn yasmāt sṛjāmi ca yadṛcchayā teṣām ca patiḥ eva aham tasmāt paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ īśe eva aham anyeṣām na ca mām īśate pare nayāmi ca īśatām bhaktān īśānaḥ tena kīrtitaḥ diśaḥ hi mama vāsāṃsi sarva dikṣu vasāmi aham vāsaḥ ca aham diśām yasmāt digvāsāḥ tena saṃsmṛtaḥ bhūtānām śaṃkaraḥ yasmāt tena aham śaṃkaraḥ smṛtaḥ lokānām śiva kṛt yasmāt śivaḥ tasmāt aham smṛtaḥ nīlam yena mama aṅgasya saṃraktam lohita tviṣam śūlī śūlena samproktaḥ lakulena ca lākulī īśāna iti mahā aiśvaryam mahādeva iti ca akṣayam digvāsā iti param mokṣam śaṃkara iti sukham mahat śivā iti śivam atyartham śūlī iti paramam balam lākulī iti parā lokān kīrtaya labhata naraḥ śūlinā devadevena devyāḥ priya hita icchayā vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇu vatsa yathā dattam punarjanma pinākinā yamena hriyamāṇāya śvetāya vigata āyuṣe sarva vidyā vinīta ātmā yasya putraḥ kuśadhvajaḥ babhūva su mahā tejāḥ viśvāmitraḥ iva aparaḥ chāyā iva anapagā bhaktiḥ babhūva vṛṣabhadhvaje sarva bhāvena deveśam dhyāyan tasthau mahā muniḥ na ca tasmai sutām prādāt tām asau sura vidviṣe jāmātā kāṅkṣitaḥ ca āsīt tena cakra gadā dharaḥ viṣṇuḥ parama dharma ātmā duhitrā ca asya suvrata tasya tam duhitā jñātvā hatam pitaram ātmanaḥ śvetaḥ tat tatas jñātvā vairāgyam param āsthitaḥ rudram eva arpita avasthaḥ tad niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ athā agāt su mahān kālaḥ tapyataḥ tasya dhīmataḥ kṣīṇa āyuṣam atho jñātvā śvetam mṛtyu viceṣṭitam sutaḥ vivasvataḥ hṛṣṭaḥ kāla mṛtyu purogamān kiṃkarān preṣayāmāsa tam ānetum dvijottamam tam athā abhyetya te dūtāḥ sthitāḥ śveta jighaṃsayā tān dṛṣṭvā sa tadā śvetaḥ yamadūtān avasthitān hā hā iti maraṇāt bhītaḥ trāsāt duḥkha pariplutaḥ anvacintayat avyagraḥ paritrāṇāya śaṃkaram tam tathā duḥkhitam jñātvā bhaktam mṛtyu vaśam gatam śaṃkaraḥ prahasan devīm idam āha sureśvaraḥ kṣīṇa āyuḥ abhavat mūḍhaḥ mṛtyu pāśa vimohitaḥ vyavasthā eṣā purā sṛṣṭā brahmaṇā loka kartṛṇā prāṇinām āyuṣaḥ hāniḥ kāla saṃsthāna saṃkṣaye brahmā api hi sṛja lokān mūḍhaḥ bhavati śailaje mṛtyu duḥkha anvitān lokān yasmāt sṛjati mohitaḥ anujñātā mayā api eṣā sṛṣṭiḥ mṛtu samanvitā eka bhakti tayā tasya dṛḍham prītaḥ asmi pārvati trātā tasya bhaviṣyāmi jīvayiṣyāmi tam munim evam uktaḥ sa pārvatyā devadevaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ nandīśvara purogān tān gaṇeśān gaṇapa adhipaḥ śaṅkukarṇam ca gaṇapam tathā anyān ca sahasraśas muneḥ śvetasya rakṣā artham preṣayāmāsa śūladhṛk mahā balāḥ te gaṇanāyaka indrāḥ ājñām gṛhītvā parameśa vaktrāt tūrṇam yayuḥ śvetamuneḥ upāntam dūtān didhakṣantaḥ iva antakasya mṛgam ekam iva araṇye vyādhaiḥ bahubhiḥ āvṛtam grīvāyām kālapāśena hasta pāde ca yantritam mṛtyunā svayam ākṛṣṭam sravat rudhira cakṣuṣā vikṛta āsyaiḥ mahā daṃṣṭraiḥ saṃrakta śmaśru mūrdhajaiḥ vidyut sadṛśa netraiḥ ca loha daṇḍa ugra pāṇibhiḥ yama dūtaiḥ mahā ghoraiḥ kṣipyamāṇam samantataḥ dṛṣṭvā tathā tam munim ārttam uccais krośantam īśa iti asakṛt gaṇa indraḥ mumoca pāśāt munim āśu tasmāt pāśāt paśūnām iva bandham īśaḥ gacchadhvam yama kiṃkarāḥ munim itas tyaktvā śarīraiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ bhaktaḥ hi eṣa sura asura īśvaram ajam śambhum jagat kāraṇam yaḥ sraṣṭā pavana agni śakra marutām brahma ādibhiḥ vanditaḥ trātā saḥ vṛṣā indra ketuḥ ajitaḥ na enam yamaḥ drakṣyati te dṛṣṭvā gaṇapān dūtāḥ kāla mṛtyu puraḥsarāḥ bhayāt muktvā munim śvetam abruvan dūratas sthitāḥ pūrṇaḥ kālaḥ muneḥ asya kṣīṇam āyuḥ gaṇa īśvarāḥ akṣatāḥ gacchata kṣipram kṛpaṇāḥ yama kiṃkarāḥ yāvat ca ete na kupyanti pramatha indrāḥ su roṣaṇāḥ mā vaḥ siṃhāḥ iva araṇye vāraṇān mada mohitān sakṛt eva samāhatya kariṣyanti gata āyuṣaḥ athā evam uktā gaṇanāyakena nandīśvareṇa amita vikrameṇa bhītāḥ yayuḥ te pitṛrāja dūtāḥ gatvā ca cakruḥ yamasya teṣām upaśrutya tadā vacāṃsi tīvrāṇi nandīśvara bhāṣitāni ādityasūnuḥ pracukopa mohāt svayam prayātum ca matim cakāra dṛṣṭvā munim śvetam apeta moham vṛtam gaṇa indraiḥ hara tulya rūpaiḥ muñcadhvam enam tarasā iti avocat nandīśvara ādyān graha rāja sūnuḥ saṃrakṣyamāṇam svayam eva mūḍham gaccha akṛtātman iti nandī uvāca gaṇa indrāḥ gata jīvaḥ a ayam vipraḥ tiṣṭhati mūḍha vat kālena paripūrṇena kṣīṇa āyuḥ iha kaścana saṃtyajya tat imam deham prāpnotu gaṇapa adhipāḥ mama āyattam idam sarvam bhūta grāma parīkṣaṇam puṇya pāpīyasoḥ nityam karmaṇoḥ pravicāraṇam tena arpayata me kṣipram śvetam enam gata āyuṣam athavā enam gṛhītvā iha sarve eva gaṇeśvarāḥ prayāma śūlinaḥ a abhyāsam niyatam sa vimokṣyati pitṛrāja vacaḥ śrutvā nandīśvara purogamāḥ nyavedayat yathāvṛttam nandī sarva gaṇa adhipaḥ śrutvā tu bhagavān vākyam nandinā samprabhāṣitam prāha vaivasvatam sākṣāt snigdha gambhīrayā girā atas kṣīṇa āyuṣaḥ aapi asya mṛtyuḥ na prabhaviṣyati mad prasādāt jitaḥ mṛtyuḥ śvetena anena tāpana mama ādeśāt tvayā api asya na eva kāryaḥ parābhavaḥ asya bhakti viśeṣeṇa pareṇa paritoṣitaḥ iti deva vacaḥ śrutvā praṇamya tapanātmajaḥ parama artham a vijñāya provāca idam pinākinam tvayā eva bhagavan eṣā sthitiḥ sṛṣṭā purātanī adhikāra nivṛttau hi śakrasya api vṛṣadhvaja tvayā eva pavanaḥ sṛṣṭaḥ hi aham ca eva sureśvara na kenacid ayam panthāḥ kāla mṛtyu kṣaya ātmakaḥ vyabhicīrṇaḥ mahādeva kāla atikrama dhāraṇāt evam etām parām sṛṣṭim vicintya vibudha īśvara moktum arhasi vipra agryam kāle pūrṇe gata āyuṣam evam sthitiḥ abhinnā syāt aham ca na vimānitaḥ mṛtyuḥ ca antar śarīra sthaḥ śvetaḥ tad varam āpsyati iti uktam pretarājena śrutvā vākyam vṛṣadhvajaḥ dīpta aṅgāraḥ iva ekasmāt saṃhāraḥ iva pāvakaḥ nandīśasya tatas skandham upāśritya pinākadhṛk idam prāha vacaḥ vyāsa tam dṛṣṭvā yamam āsthitam aho dinakṛtaḥ sūnoḥ asya śāṭhya prabhāṣitam paritrātaḥ mayā śvetaḥ yama gaccha iti bhāṣitaḥ kim nu ayam mūḍhaḥ eva syāt uta pauruṣa garvitaḥ tiryak dṛṣṭim samādhāya sa roṣam yamam aikṣata mahā vṛkṣaḥ iva araṇye mahā vāyu samīritaḥ bhasmasāt tvam yayau tūrṇam prajahāsa tatas bhavaḥ śvetam tatas tam praṇatam munim tu sa gadgadam mṛtyu bhayāt viṣaṇṇam prādāt varam śūla dharaḥ ca tasmai mṛtyuḥ na te vipra bhaviṣyati iti dadau ca nityam gaṇapa tvam eva provāca ca enam parituṣṭaḥ īśaḥ tyakṣyanti ye deham apeta mohāḥ teṣām gatiḥ śveta samā smṛtā me tava eva nāmnā ca nadī su puṇyā śvetasya gaṅgā iti bhaviṣyati iyam santarpaṇa anna ekavidham pitR̥ṇām svar loka dam sthānam atīva yasyām nandīśa caṇḍeśa samāna dharmāḥ praṇamya devam puratas sthitaḥ dṛṣṭvā atha sūnum vigata asum arkaḥ śoka abhitaptaḥ tvaritaḥ javena brahma ādibhiḥ śakra puraḥsaraiḥ taiḥ sārdham jagat kāraṇam ājagāma vijñāpayāmāsuḥ atha amarāḥ te ādityasūnu pratijīva hetoḥ mūḍhaḥ yatas jagat īśvareṇa kṛcchram tatas tīvram idam prayātaḥ prasīda deveśa kuru prasādam jīvatu ayam preta gaṇa adhirājaḥ yathā purā ca eṣa bhavatu idānīm ārttim hi naḥ chindhi sura asura īśa vijñaptim evam tridiva ālayānām brahma ādi śakra arka puraḥsarāṇām śrutvā yamam tam karuṇāyamānaḥ uttiṣṭha putra iti vibhuḥ babhāṣe protthāya tūrṇam bhagavantam āśu nanāma padbhyām sahasā gṛhītvā brahma ādayaḥ te ca sura indra saṃghāḥ dṛṣṭvā tatas tān praṇatān avocat brahma arka viṣṇu jvalana ādi nāthaḥ kartā surāṇām sura nāthaḥ ekaḥ sureśvaraḥ soma jaṭā ardha mauliḥ devāḥ prayāta sva niketanāni vijñaptiḥ eṣā saphalā kṛtā vaḥ mā evam kṛthāḥ tvam punar ātma moham pragṛhya saurim pitṛrājam āśu śvetaḥ tasthau maraṇāt vihīnaḥ iti kathitam idam te śveta mṛtyu praṇāśam himagiri tanayāyāḥ bhartuḥ īśasya śambhoḥ ṣaṭṣaṣti uttara śatatamaḥ saptaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca puṇyāni āyatanāni iha devadevasya śūlinaḥ yāni dṛṣṭvā na śocanti janma mṛtyū mahā mune evam kṛtārtham ātmānam mucye yat muni sattama sādhu vyāsa mahābuddhe bhaktimān asi śaṃkare sthānāni śūlinaḥ yaḥ tvam puṇyāni śrotum icchasi kṛtārthaḥ tvam mahā yoga muktaḥ saṃsāra bandhanaiḥ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te vatsa guhyam etat param hi me sthāna anuvarṇanam śambhoḥ mṛtyu janma bhaya apaham ādityabandhanam nāma kūṭam vindhya gireḥ śubham tat dṛṣṭvā manujaḥ vyāsa janma prati na śocati hemasomodbhavam nāma kūṭam himagireḥ śubham ye tad āyatanam śambhoḥ abhigacchanti mānavāḥ satyaḥ nāma hradaḥ puṇyaḥ hema padma samāvṛtaḥ yatra te munayaḥ satyāḥ satya anala ravi prabhāḥ dhārayanti mahātmānaḥ āśīrbhiḥ sa ratham ravim puṇyam āyatanam tatra sthāpitam taiḥ pinākinaḥ yaiḥ tat āyatanam dṛṣṭam bhava bhaktaiḥ viyat gamaiḥ uśīravījaḥ śaila indraḥ tatra āśrama padam mahat āgastyasya tṛṅāṅgasya deva dānava pūjitam tasmin āyatane rudram tṛṇāṅgaḥ sa mahān ṛṣiḥ dakṣiṇāmūrtim āsthāya stauti nityam kapardinam meru śṛṅge mahā utsedhe sauvarṇam sthāpitam mahat liṅgam bhagavataḥ vyāsa yatra āste śūladhṛk svayam sthāpitam su mahat liṅgam devadevasya śūlinaḥ tat dṛṣṭvā mānavaḥ vyāsa rudra lokam avāpnuyāt mokṣa vidyāsu abhijñāḥ ca sāṃkhya yoga viśāradāḥ bhavanti manujāḥ dṛṣṭvā tat liṅgam parama adbhutam tapanīya mayam śubhram devatāḥ yat upāsate tat dṛṣṭvā devatāḥ liṅgam prāpnuvanti param padam kṣīrode sāgare divyam bālakhilyaiḥ svayam kṛtam tasmin candra prabham liṅgam sphāṭikam maṇi rañjitam sauvarṇam yakṣarājena sthāpitam gandhamādane yaiḥ tat āyatanam dṛṣṭam kuberasya sura asuraiḥ ebhyaḥ puṇyatamāni iha yāni gamyāni mānuṣaiḥ śṛṇu tāni mahābuddhe sthānāni śaśimaulinaḥ sarva parvata rājasya śṛṅge himavataḥ śubhe mahālayam iti khyātam sthānam ādyam svayambhuvaḥ yatra sarva amarāḥ vyāsa caturvaktra puraḥsarāḥ saṃsiddhāḥ munayaḥ ca eva ye ca yogi īśvarāḥ bhuvi yatra sākṣāt mahādevaḥ nyastavān padam ātmanaḥ abhigamya tam īśānam mahālaya nivāsinam na tam paśyanti adharma jñāḥ ye pāpa kṛtaḥ narāḥ mahāgaṇapatiḥ tatra dvāra saṃsthaḥ mahā balaḥ sa teṣām gamanam hanti ye narāḥ pāpa kāriṇaḥ yoginaḥ yate devāḥ ca siddhāḥ ca parama ṛṣayaḥ tam praṇamya yayuḥ siddhim puṇyam paśupateḥ padam tasya saṃkalpanāt eva drakṣyāmi iti mahā ālayam mahālayam mahat kṣetram mokṣa siddhi pradam śubham kulāni ubhayatas sapta dṛṣṭvā trāyati mānavaḥ tatas puṇyatamam vyāsa kedāram nāma nāmataḥ param dhāma vṛṣāṅkasya tasya eva uttaratas śubham jaṭā bhārāt jalam puṇyam mumoca te bhavanti gaṇāḥ vyāsa kuṣmāṇāḥ rudra vallabhāḥ mahārūpāḥ mahātmānaḥ nandinaḥ kedāra vāsinam dṛṣṭvā devadevam jagatpatim brahmā śakraḥ tathā viṣṇuḥ somaḥ yakṣa gaṇa adhipaḥ kedāra salilam pītam yaiḥ naraiḥ su mahātmabhiḥ katham śocanti te vyāsa prāptam kim nu na taiḥ sukham mūrdhnaḥ soma mahā indra viṣṇu marutām sraṣṭuḥ vibhoḥ śūlinaḥ gatvā tam api deveśam gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt abhigamya tam īśānam na śocet maraṇam prati trayāṇām api lokānām pradeśe himavat gireḥ eṣa śreṣṭhatamaḥ vyāsa sarva siddhi pradaḥ śubhaḥ vipannasya pramādāt vā gāṇapatyā gatiḥ varā na atas puṇyatamam kiṃcid sarva lokeṣu vidyate yāti sāyujya tām śambhoḥ parama aiśvarya saṃyutaḥ girau iha mṛtaḥ jantuḥ kim tatas paramam padam kucakuṇḍe iti khyāte tīrthe yatra umayā kṛte tat gaurīśikharam puṇyam ye mānavāḥ aśvamedha phalam prāpya te yānti paramām gatim ṛṣabham śṛṅgam aparam vajra sphaṭika sannibham yatra nandī tapaḥ tepe varam ca avāpa śaṃkarāt ṛṣabham prāpya tat kūṭam sthānam puṇyam umāpateḥ dṛṣṭvā pāpa vinirmuktaḥ rudra lokam avāpnute anyat himagireḥ kūṭam hemakūṭa sama prabham tam namasya mahādevam kinnara uraga cāraṇāḥ mṛtyu bhītāḥ ca puruṣāḥ janma duḥkhaiḥ tathā arditāḥ tad āyatanam āsādya krāmān āpuḥ yathā īpsitān tam dṛṣṭvā manujaḥ vyāsa rājasūya phalam labhet gaṅgādvāre śubhadvāre mahā puṇye mahātmanā dakṣeṇa sthāpitam liṅgam bhakti hetoḥ kapardinaḥ vṛkṣāḥ kanakhalāḥ nāma yatra āsan kanaka ātmakāḥ mānuṣāṇām aśīla tvāt saṃvṛkṇāḥ dāravaḥ babhuḥ viśvātmā yatra viśveśaḥ śambhuḥ ambikayā saha mānavāḥ yat na paśyanti janma ca iṣa mumukṣavaḥ vājimedham daśaguṇam yam dṛṣṭvā prāpnute naraḥ dṛṣṭvā īśvaram nīla payoda kuṇḍam saṃsāra paṅke na punar patanti yatra japyam purā kṛtvā liṅgam sthāpitavān dvijaḥ japya īśvaram tam āsādya prāṇān tyakṣyanti ye narāḥ anyat āyatanam vyāsa śaśi bimba ardha maulinaḥ yatra śūla dharaḥ devaḥ svayam eva vṛṣadhvajaḥ cakāra bhairavam rūpam nandi umā gaṇa bhīṣaṇam yat dṛṣṭvā himavat putrī babhūva bhaya vihvalā krīḍā hetoḥ bhavaḥ yatra trāsayitvā girīndrajām saumya rūpaḥ aabhavat bhūyas sāntvayāmāsa śailajām maraṇam janma ca vyāsa na asau punar avāpnuyāt yat eva āśramiṇām puṇyam tathā īśa vrata cāriṇām tat phalam bhairavam dṛṣṭvā prāpnoti nara puṅgavaḥ avāpa śaṃkarāt vyāsa gaṇeśa tvam tathā uttamam yaiḥ tat āyatanam dṛṣṭam te yānti paramām gatim yatra vaikhānasāḥ viprāḥ śiva bhakti parāyaṇāḥ bhāskara anala saṃkāśāḥ nivasanti tapodhanāḥ bhikṣā hetoḥ vanam tat tu prāviśat kila śūladhṛk vimūḍhaiḥ pātitam vyāsa devadāru vana āśrame jñātvā śaṃkara jam sarvam tad apāyam su dāruṇam saṃstutya vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ śaṃkaram paryatoṣayan tatas tat abhavat liṅgam yathāpūrvam pinākinaḥ jagataḥ ca tatas puṃs tvam tad kṣaṇāt samapadyata tatra taiḥ sthāpitam liṅgam parameśasya bhaktitaḥ tat dṛṣṭvā vājimedhānām daśānām prāpnute phalam evam dāru vanam puṇyam īśasya āste mahā mune dadhīcena mahat divyam puṇyam āyatanam kṛtam sthāneśvaram iti khyātam triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam takṣakena bhujaṅgena dṛḍha bhaktena śaṃkare takṣakeśvaram iti evam sthāpitam jāhnavī taṭe tam dṛṣṭvā puruṣaḥ devam aśvamedha phalam labhet agastyena kṛtam ca anyat puṇyam āyatanam mahat dṛṣṭvā paramayā bhaktyā puruṣaḥ tam śuci vrataḥ girau kālañjare liṅgam dṛṣṭvā sthānam umāpateḥ yat tat rāvaṇa putreṇa meghanādena rakṣasā sthāpitam toṣa yānena sarva bhūta patim bhavam yatra mandodarī putraḥ sthāṇunā śaśimaulinā māyā ratha pradānena kṛtaḥ prāpta manorathaḥ puruṣāḥ svargam āyānti divya yoga samanvitāḥ tatra śrīparvataḥ nāma parvataḥ śrīniketanaḥ siddha amara śata ākīrṇam siddhikṣetram tat uttamam śūlinaḥ yatra liṅgānām puṇyānām vara dāyinām sahasram sthāpitam vyāsa śilādena mahātmanā ye paśyanti tam īśānam śrīparvata nivāsinam janma mṛtyu bhayam teṣām na asti puṃsām kadācana yoga abhyāsa parāḥ viprāḥ siddhim yānti yathā īpsitām manasā api abhigacchanti ye narāḥ śrīgirim mune na te yānti yama āvāsam mṛtyau api samāgate tatas ca uttara gokarṇam hara liṅga aṅkita āśramam taptam yatra tapaḥ tīvram rākṣasaiḥ piśita aśanaiḥ rāvaṇa ādyaiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ labdhaḥ ca varaḥ īpsitaḥ purā yatra tapaḥ kṛtvā prasādya ca pinākinam aśvamedham daśaguṇam tat dṛṣṭvā labhate naraḥ mṛtaḥ ca rudra sāyujyam gacchati atra na saṃśayaḥ tatas dakṣiṇagokarṇam sthānam puṇyam pinākinaḥ spṛkkayā jātayā yatra laṅkā malaya sānuṣu ekaḥ rākṣasa śārdūlaḥ yatra adya api vibhīṣaṇaḥ samabhyarcya amara īśānam bhuṅkte rājyam aśaṅkitaḥ mānavāḥ ye gokarṇa āyatana āśramam daśānām aśvamedhānām prāpnuvanti phalam śubham jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa yasmin āyatanam kṛtam yatra devāḥ ca siddhāḥ ca yakṣa guhyaka kinnarāḥ hariścandra gireḥ śṛṅgam ākūṭam yaiḥ nirīkṣitam kārohaṇam iti sthānam trinetra āyatanam mahat yatra kākām tapasyantīm āruroha prajāpatiḥ āruroha yatas kākām tasmin deśe prajāpatiḥ tasmāt kārohaṇaḥ nāmnā sa deśaḥ parikīrtitaḥ tasmin deśe a avatīrṇaḥ ca bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ kṣīṇe kṛta yuge vyāsa tretā yuga mukha udaye dvitīyam dvāpare tṛtīyam ca kalau yuge evam sa dharma saṃvāsāt deśaḥ puṇyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ bhārabhūtiḥ tu asau bhūtvā tasmin deśe pinākadhṛk bhārān baddhvā dvijātīnām narmadāyām vicikṣipe tretāyām diṇḍi muṇḍaḥ ca śirāṃsi dvāpare ca aṣaḍhiḥ bhūtvā nṛttena anugṛhītavān evam pratiyugam vyāsa tasmin deśe śivaḥ svayam avatīrṇaḥ ca anugṛhya brāhmaṇān śuddha mānasān teṣām āyatanāni sma sarveṣām eva suvrata yena dṛṣṭāni devasya īśāna lokam āpnuyāt vartamāne kalau ca api jñātvā duḥkha arditam jagat caturaḥ puruṣān sṛṣṭvā svasmāt mukha catuṣṭayāt yūyam yāta mahīm sarve dvijāḥ bhūtvā tapasvinaḥ mām eva eṣyatha yogi īśāḥ nītvā viprān param padam mānuṣeṣu tadā viprāḥ mokṣa dharma parāyaṇāḥ ujjayinyām guru jyeṣṭhaḥ kauśikaḥ nāma nāmataḥ dvitīyaḥ gārgyaḥ iti eva jambūmārge sa tāpanaḥ tṛtīyaḥ ca abhavat mitraḥ mathurāyām mahāmanāḥ atri vaṃśa prasūtasya nāmnā vai somaśarmaṇaḥ rūpam kṛtvā sita aṅgam tu jagāma atreḥ gṛham śubham jagāma ujjayinīm devaḥ śmaśānam ca viveśa ha sa tatra bhasmanā ātmānam avaguṇṭhya vṛṣadhvajaḥ ulmukam vāma hastena gṛhītvā samupāviśat tatra prathamam ādāya śiṣyam kauśikam īśvaraḥ jambūmārge dvitīyam ca mathurāyām tatas sva siddhāntam dadau yogam uvāca idam ca lākulī rahasyam paramam hi idam pañca arthaḥ iti saṃjñitam anayā dīkṣayā viprān prāpayadhvam param padam nadī tīreṣu medhyeṣu puṇyeṣu āyataneṣu ca śūnya āgāreṣu araṇyeṣu vāsaḥ vaḥ saṅga varjitaḥ vacaḥ bhagavataḥ śrutvā śiṣyāḥ paśupateḥ svayam dharmapāda aṅkite deśe avatīrṇaḥ yatas bhavaḥ sa deśaḥ paramaḥ tasmāt mahā puṇyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ āśramaḥ yoginām yatra pravṛttaḥ pāpa nāśanaḥ aṣṭa āyatanam iti evam sthānam atra mahātmanaḥ yat dṛṣṭvā manujāḥ vyāsa prāpnuvanti param padam kārohaṇam śiva sthānam ye a abhigacchanti mānavāḥ etat paśupateḥ kṣetram purāṇam ṛṣibhiḥ stutam sarva pāpa vinirmuktaḥ yathā iṣṭām prāpnuyāt gatim kārohaṇam sthānam atīva puṇyam śaivāni yatra āyatanāni dhīmat gatvā narāḥ tāni mahā phalāni saṃsāra geham na punar viśanti vārāṇasyāḥ muni śreṣṭha yatra sannihitaḥ haraḥ tatra bhāgīrathī puṇyā uttarām bhajate diśam siddhikṣetram bṛhat kṣetram lokeṣu triṣu viśrutam avimuktam smṛtam nāmnā na vimuktam hareṇa tu avimukteśvaram dṛṣṭvā devam tatra hi umāpatim gāṇapatyā gatiḥ proktā mṛtyu kāle mahā mune yatra āste gaṇapaḥ dvāri vidyutkeśaḥ mahā balaḥ daṇḍapāṇiḥ mahā tejāḥ samādeśāt svayambhuvaḥ tam a dṛṣṭvā na paśyanti devadeva īśvaram haram yoginaḥ mahātmānaḥ puṇyam tasya api darśanam daṇḍa pāṇim śuciḥ dṛṣṭvā hara datta varam gaṇam yatra siddhāḥ mahātmānaḥ yoga aiśvarya bala anvitāḥ channāḥ pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā praṇamanti svayambhuvam śakraḥ pitāmahaḥ viṣṇuḥ dhaneśaḥ varuṇaḥ yamaḥ tathā saptarṣayaḥ siddhāḥ gandharvāḥ pannagāḥ tathā tatas puṇyatamam na asti siddhikṣetram iti śrutiḥ gaṅgā dakṣiṇatas tasmin uttareṇa varāṇasī sthāpayet vidhinā yoṣā pumān vā vidhi pūrvakam sahasram sthāpitam tena liṅgānām bhavati prabhoḥ tryakṣaḥ sa gaṇapaḥ bhūtvā rudra sāyujya tām vrajet atas kṛtvā muni śreṣṭha brahma āditya purassaraiḥ tasmin bhagavataḥ kṣetre kāśi puryām anekaśas dṛśyante aadya api liṅgāni sthāpitāni mahātmabhiḥ siddhāḥ pāśupatāḥ ye ca bhava bandha mumukṣavaḥ prāpya vārāṇasīm puṇyām siddhikṣetram anuttamam vedeṣu gīyate vyāsa tat kṣetram śaśimaulinaḥ na avimuktāt param kṣetram na avimuktāt param padam na avimuktāt param puṇyam na avimuktāt parā gatiḥ yā gatiḥ dhyāyataḥ nityam pare brahmaṇi līyataḥ sā eva saṃtyajataḥ prāṇān avimukte smṛtā gatiḥ kṣetram puṇyam umāpateḥ sura vṛṣaiḥ juṣṭam sadā siddhaye ye sevanti tad īśa bhakti paramāḥ martyāḥ śama prāptaye tat dṛṣṭvā manujaḥ samyak iṣṭām gatim avāpnuyāt dṛṣṭvā pāpa vinirmuktaḥ svarga lokam avāpnuyāt tena dṛṣṭena vipra indra gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt rudra lokam mṛtaḥ ca asau prāpnuyāt sarvakāmikam gāyāyām anyat īśasya sthānam bhagavataḥ śubham gṛdhrakūṭa īśvaram nāmnā sarva pāpa vimocanam na tam dṛṣṭvā vimuhyanti mṛtyu kāle nara uttamāḥ dvādaśa abda vrataḥ tāpī dvijaḥ phalam avāpnuyāt ayanda āyatanam puṇyam magadhāsu pinākinaḥ nagare pāṭalīputre nāmnā prahasiteśvaram magadhāsu smṛtāni aṣṭau sthānāni śaśimaulinaḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛtaḥ yāni babhrāma nakuli īśvaraḥ yāni dṛṣṭvā bhavet sadyas pumān pāpa vivarjitaḥ yavaneṣu smṛtam sthānam puṇyam anyat umāpateḥ tripiṣṭapam avāpnoti tam dṛṣṭvā mānavaḥ prabhum aṅga deśe param puṇyam sthānam proktam pinākinaḥ hemacūḍa īśvaram nāmnā tam dṛṣṭvā na vimuhyati bhāgīrathyāḥ tatas vyāsa sāgarasya ca saṃgame brahmaṇā sthāpitam liṅgam puṇyam tatra pinākinaḥ daśānām aśvamedhānām tam dṛṣṭvā prāpnute phalam prabhāse śūlinam dṛṣṭvā dehabhede gaṇaḥ bhavet puṣkare śaṃkaram dṛṣṭvā na śocet mṛtyu janmanī mahākāleśvaram devam ujjayinyām mahā vrataḥ abhigamya āpnuyāt vidvān gaṇa tvam tripuradviṣaḥ drimacaṇḍeśvaram devam dṛṣṭvā trāyati mānavaḥ śaṅkukarṇeśvaram dṛṣṭvā na śocet maraṇam naraḥ ḍiṅgeśvaram iti khyātam rudrasya āyatanam mahat abhigamya ca dṛṣṭvā ca tam devam jagataḥ prabhum śiva bhakti paraḥ vyāsa sarva kāmān avāpnuyāt mṛtasya ca gatiḥ proktā gāṇapatyam mahātmanaḥ suvarṇākṣe param sthānam devadevasya saṃsmṛtam tat dṛṣṭvā manujaḥ vyāsa rājasūya phalam labhet saptagodāvare sthānam dṛṣṭvā puṇyam kapardinaḥ sthānam puṇyatamam ca anyat śreṣṭham jagati kīrtitam tam vīkṣya mānavaḥ vyāsa sarva yajña phalam labhet janma prabhṛti yat kiṃcid kṛtam karma aśubham mahat tad kṣanāt naśyate sarvam dṛṣṭvā bhadreśvaram haram yatra tatra mṛtaḥ ca api gāṇapatyam labhet naraḥ ekāmre ca vibhoḥ sthānam dṛṣṭvā svargam avāpnuyāt virajāyām haram dṛṣṭvā vājimedham avāpnuyāt nepāleṣu ca deveśam dṛṣṭvā paśupatim prabhum daśa aśvamedhān āpnoti rudra lokam ca gacchati bhaktānām praṇatānām ca sarva kāma pradam smṛtam kathitāni mayā vyāsa yaiḥ gatiḥ prāpyate śubhā tasya sāyujya tām devaḥ dadāti vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ maṅgalyam paramam puṇyam medhyam sarva bhaya apaham sthānānām kīrtanam śambhoḥ nityam kuryāt śuciḥ naraḥ iti skandapurāṇe śivāyatana varṇane saptaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ aṣṭaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca śrutvā kathām āyatana anubaddhām candra ardha bimba āsthita maulinaḥ tu vyāsaḥ muniḥ tam vacanam babhāṣe brahma ātmajam brahma vidam muni indram dharmyā su puṇyā bhagavan tvayā eṣā guhyā kathā me vidhivat pradiṣṭā sthānāni śambhoḥ dayitāni kaḥ aanyaḥ evam parijñātum ṛṣiḥ samarthaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ tathā evam muninā muni indraḥ praśnam yathāvat kathayāṃcakāra dagdham yathā tat tripuram tathā tvam śṛṇuṣva putra iti vacaḥ bruvāṇaḥ bhagneṣu daityeṣu sa dānaveṣu mayaḥ babhūva ādhṛti duḥkha taptaḥ ādāya daityam sa hi tārakākṣam vidyutprabham ca indra sama prabhāvam te śīta kāle hima parvata sthāḥ grīṣme ca pañca jvalana abhitaptāḥ vyabhre payaḥ plāvita bhūmi bhāge ceruḥ tapaḥ prāvṛṣi ca prayattāḥ teṣām agāt divya samā sahasram tathā su tīvre tapasi sthitānām carma asthi śeṣāḥ jvalana prabhāvāḥ tapaḥ viśeṣāt diti putra siṃhāḥ āditya tejaḥ pratimāna vīrāḥ babhūvuḥ āditya vapuḥ prakāśāḥ pitāmahaḥ tān abhigamya sarvān priyam bahu uktvā vacanam babhāṣe taptam tapaḥ vaḥ vigata pramohāḥ varam tu idānīm vṛṇuta iti hṛṣṭāḥ tam prāñjaliḥ bhūmi niviṣṭa jānuḥ mayaḥ sureśam praṇataḥ avadhya tām apratimam balam ca jñānam ca divyam paramam sukham ca dātum na śakyaḥ varaḥ eṣa tubhyam tasmāt param sa antaram eva ca anyam tvam putra yācasva tatas pradāsye cintā ca te mā danuja anyathā bhūt pūrṇe sahasre tripuram samānām sameṣyate hi ardha nimeṣa mātram tasmin kṣaṇe yaḥ triṣu saṃgateṣu pureṣu divyeṣu sura pravīra eka iṣuṇā tat tripuram daheta sa naḥ vināśī tripurasya bhūyāt śrutvā tatas tat vacanam mayasya brahmā varam tam hṛṣita antarātmā prādāt abhīṣṭam danuja adhipāya dattvā ca tūrṇam sva puram jagāma candra aṃśu saṃsṛṣṭa talaiḥ ca harmyaiḥ śīta anila āhlāda sukha praveśaiḥ muktā pravālaiḥ maṇi khaṇḍa citraiḥ ālambitaiḥ citra taḍit prakāśaiḥ prāsāda paṅkti sthita ratna khaṇḍaiḥ mahā maṇi indu dyuti sannikāśaiḥ sa toraṇa abhyucchrita harmya pṛṣṭhaiḥ alaṃkṛtam tat tripuram rarāja ramyaiḥ tathā udyāna śataiḥ upetam prabhrānta ṣaṭpāda mayūra haṃsaiḥ vāpībhiḥ ākrānta vihaṅgamābhiḥ praphulla nīlotpala saṃvṛtābhiḥ sa vrīḍam īṣat capala īkṣitābhiḥ yoṣidbhiḥ ākīrṇam atīva reje lauham puram yat tat adhas cakāra tat tārakākṣāya mayaḥ pradattvā haimam tṛtīyam svayam eva divyam jagrāha rājā mayaḥ ātmanaḥ a arthe adhiṣṭhitam tat tripuram tadā abhūt samam tribhiḥ taiḥ danu rāja siṃhaiḥ te sarvatas svaḥ prabhavān vijitya priyā sahāyāḥ saha mitra bhṛtyaiḥ matvā ca teṣām prasabham nipatya nānāvidhāḥ cakruḥ atīva pīḍāḥ vanāni vaibhrāja puraḥsarāṇi saṃchinna vīrudh kusumāni cakruḥ vāpīḥ pracakruḥ kamalaiḥ vihīnāḥ jahruḥ ca rambhā ādi puraḥsarāḥ tāḥ saṃtrasta gātrīḥ sura yoṣitaḥ taiḥ anyāḥ ca cakruḥ mahatīḥ prapīḍāḥ teṣām atītaḥ su mahān atha evam prakurvatām deva vināśanāni vṛttam yathā sarvam aśeṣatas tat nyavedayan āśu pitāmahāya tān āha devaḥ kamalāsana sthaḥ sarvān sura īśān parisāntvayitvā mahā balāḥ te tripura asura indrāḥ hantum na śakyāḥ hi balāt bhavadbhiḥ tasmāt ayam viṣṇuḥ aham ca yuṣmān pragṛhya śambhum śaraṇam prayāma gatiḥ sadā naḥ śaśibhṛt sura īśāḥ sa tān balāt haṃsyati śūlapāṇiḥ tathā iti te praṇipatya devāḥ brahma arka śakra anila pāvaka ādyāḥ kailāsam āgamya sureśvara īśam dṛṣṭvā haram tuṣṭuvuḥ ādṛta arthāḥ hari arka śakra agni pitāmahānām sraṣṭre namaḥ deva sūkṣmāya nityam parameśvarāya nityam namaḥ sarvagatāya dhātre namaḥ parāya atipare pumāṃse purāya ṣaḍviṃśaka saṃjñitāya soma anila arka jvalana ambu bhūmi vyoma ātmakāya ādi namaḥ a astu pūṣṇaḥ namaḥ danta vināśanāya kamā aṅga nāśāya namaḥ a astu nityam namaḥ pradhānāya parāya puṃse yoga adhigamyāya sadā namaḥ a astu vidyā sṛje dharma sṛje namaḥ a astu sraṣṭre namaḥ yajña sura surāṇām namaḥ tṛtīya īkṣaṇa dhāriṇe ca namaḥ namaḥ nīlaśikhaṇḍine ca namaḥ a astu nityam puruṣottamāya śmaśāna vāsāya namaḥ sadā eva namaḥ a astu daitya andhaka nāśanāya namaḥ sadā moha vināśanāya tamaḥ vināśāya namaḥ aastu nityam ajñāna nāśāya namaḥ aastu nityam namaḥ sadā mokṣa vara pradāya namaḥ sadāya amṛta saṃsthitāya yogeśvarāya amara saṃstutāya namaḥ a astu rudrāya parāya dhāmne harāya śarvāya śivāya goptre namaḥ a astu bhīmāya ca śambhave ca guṇaiḥ vihīnāya guṇa utkaṭāya guṇeṣu atītāya guṇa āsthitāya gītāya sāṃkhye puruṣāya nityam namaḥ a astu yoga upaniṣad sthitāya mahā purāṇāya parāt parāya sthūlāya sūkṣmāya namaḥ sadā eva prasādyamānaḥ kuru naḥ prasādam tuṣṭaḥ para īśāna varam prayaccha śambhuḥ tathā evam stuvatām surāṇām brahma indra viṣṇu arka puraḥsarāṇām prītaḥ tayā stotra viśeṣa bhaktyā jagāda vākyam parama adbhuta artham tuṣṭaḥ devāḥ vṛṇuta adya śīghram samīhitam vaḥ yadi kiṃcid asti aṣṭaṣaṣṭi uttara śatatamaḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ durgam tat tripuram kṛtvā bādhyamānaḥ bala darpitaiḥ hṛtāḥ apsarasaḥ sarvāḥ dhvaṃsitāni vanāni ca na teṣām nigrahe śaktaḥ brahmā api eṣa pitāmahaḥ tathā kuru suraśreṣṭha varaḥ aayam naḥ pradīyatām idam āha mahā tejāḥ surān āśvāsayan iva śatam aṃśam sura īśāḥ vai gṛhītvā mama tejasaḥ rudra tejaḥ mayāḥ bhūtvā dānavān vinihaṃsyatha tatas te punar eva īśam prāhuḥ vākyam idam surāḥ śaktāḥ sahasram api aṃśam udvoḍhum na vayam tava kā naḥ śaktiḥ sureśāna tejaḥ māheśvaram param draṣṭum dhārayitum vā api prasādam kuru naḥ prabho na kathaṃcid vayam śaktāḥ tān hantum dānavān balāt tebhyaḥ kila varaḥ dattaḥ brahmaṇā anena śūladhṛk nimeṣa ardham kṣaṇe tasmin etat vaḥ tripuram balī sakṛt ekam iṣum kṣiptvā yaḥ pradhakṣyati dānavān bhaviṣyati sa vaḥ mṛtyuḥ na anyathā maraṇam hi vaḥ tat ca kartum na śaktāḥ smaḥ prasādam tena naḥ kuru tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ praṇatān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ punar āśvāsayan prāha samudvignān divaukasaḥ yadi evam sura śārdūlāḥ tripuram durgamam mahat iṣum ekam sakṛt kṣiptvā pradhakṣye nimiṣe kṣaṇe brahma viṣṇu priya artham hi śakrasya anugrahāya ca dhakṣyāmi tripuram durgam ākrāntam dānavaiḥ tribhiḥ yādṛśaḥ ca hi mām voḍhum śaktaḥ syāt sura puṅgavāḥ tatas devāḥ praṇamya īśam prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ aabhavan tatas sa bhagavān brahmā tathā viṣṇu hutāśanau dhātāram bhāskaram śakram pavanam dhanadam yamam vasūn rudrān tathā ādityān gandharvān aśvinau api garuḍān parvatān nāgān guhyakān sa mahodadhīn ṛṣīn siddhān tathā yakṣān sitam kālam tathā ca eva vanaspatīn divasāni muhūrtāni kṣaṇān kāṣṭhā lavān tathā ayane ca ṛtūn māsān pakṣān saṃvatsarān tathā sthāvaram jaṅgamam yat ca nakṣatrāṇi tathā eva ca kāṃścid cakra dvaye cakruḥ pratāpa ca anyān yuyujuḥ sura puṃgavān kṛtvā aśvān caturaḥ devān rathe tasmin nyayojayan viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ praṇamya parameśvaram rathaḥ sajjaḥ iti prāhuḥ vināśāya suradviṣām tatas sa bhagavān śambhuḥ stūyamānaḥ suraiḥ tribhiḥ pitāmaham tatas vīkṣya provāca vacasām patiḥ dagdhavyam tripuram yena tam iṣum śīghram ānaya tatas provāca tam brahmā praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam tatas pārśva sthitau dṛṣṭvā śambhuḥ viṣṇu hutāśanau dṛṣṭipātena tau devau samāhvayat arindamaḥ tau dvau añjalim ādhāya sureśānam upasthitau oṣadhīnām patim somam puṅkhe tasya nyayojayat śalyam ca pāvakam cakre brahmāṇam sa tatas abravīt mahyam dadāsi yadi ājñām aham eva hi sārathiḥ rudrapāriṣadāḥ ye ca nandīśvara purogamāḥ śaṅkukarṇa purogāḥ ca ye ca caṇḍeśvara ādayaḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ mahā yogāḥ tri akṣāḥ paṭṭiśa pāṇayaḥ nanāśa stra praharaṇāḥ nānā yuddha viśāradāḥ nānā ābharaṇa vastrāḥ ca nānā vidyā viśāradāḥ vādayantaḥ samam vādyān bherī śaṅkha svanān bahūn ājagmuḥ gaṇa mukhyāḥ te sahasrāṇi caturdaśa nānāvidhānām puṣpāṇām upariṣṭāt sahasraśas aśaktāḥ bhāram udvoḍhum mumuhuḥ devatāḥ bhṛśam tatas tān devedeveśaḥ jñātvā mūḍhān divaukasaḥ jagāma tripuram śīghram viśvakarma didṛkṣayā atha āgatam ṛṣim dṛṣṭvā viśvakarmā mayaḥ tadā sa dattvā hi āśiṣaḥ tasmai vetrāsane upāviśat brahmāṇam sārathim kṛtvā svayam āyāti śaṃkaraḥ nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā sa tadā dānava adhipaḥ tārakākṣam samāhūya vidyunmālinam eva ca tathā anyān asurān bhrātR̥n bāṇanemi puraḥsarān nāradena yat ākhyātam sarvam aśrāvayat tadā yodhayet nirbhayaḥ yaḥ tvām cintām tvam maya mā kṛthāḥ saṃgatya daivatāḥ sarve yadi yoddhum iha āgatāḥ durbalaḥ kurute bhedam dānam sāntvam atha api vā praṇāmam jyāyasaḥ śatroḥ vayam tu balinaḥ sadā durbalasya ripoḥ daṇḍaḥ balinā vijigīṣatā tat vayam balinaḥ daityāḥ hīnāḥ ca tridivaukasaḥ hatvā daṇḍena tān sarvān sthāsyāmaḥ nirvṛtāḥ sukham tārakākṣa vacaḥ śrutvā vidyunmālī vacaḥ abravīt mama api etat atīva iṣṭam rājñaḥ vacanam śubham na śaktāḥ yoddhum asmābhiḥ devatāḥ bala varjitāḥ te ced yotsyanti saṃmūḍhāḥ prayāsyanti tatas kṣayam anyonyam tu vayam yuddhāt upāyam teṣu yuñjamahe adya hatvā surān sarvān kuru rājyam triviṣṭape hiraṇyakaśipum smṛtvā hiraṇyākṣam ca daityapa tatas śrutvā mayaḥ vyāsa vidyunmāli vibhāṣitam yaḥ tulyaḥ sva bale śatruḥ hīnaḥ vā daitya puṅgavāḥ samāḥ divaukasaḥ balena asura puṅgavāḥ taiḥ devaiḥ sārdham asmākam yuktam sāma ādi yojanam yaḥ eṣa bhagavān īśaḥ sarva bhūta īśvara īśvaraḥ asmākam devatānām ca sraṣṭā hartā ca sa prabhuḥ sa hantum svayam āyāti upāyaḥ tasya kīdṛśaḥ praṇāmaḥ saṃśrayaḥ ca eva guṇa upāyau kapardinaḥ yadi kārkaśyam āsthāya yodhayāmaḥ pinākinam brahma ādyāḥ śaraṇam śambhum arditāḥ yānti śāntaye abhidhyānāt kṣaṇena eva praṇaśyeta bhavet api kīdṛśam tena yuddham naḥ devadevena śambhunā kim na vettha śiśu prajñā loṣṭu giryoḥ yat antaram īpsadhve mohitāḥ yuddhe kāla pāśena yantritāḥ yadi yūyam api prājñāḥ mama śuśrūṣavaḥ yadi mā kṛḍhvam śambhunā yuddham gacchadhvam śaraṇam śivam tam evaṃvādinam śrutvā viśvakarmāṇam ūrjitam nāradaḥ bhagavān prāha dānava anta karam vacaḥ bhavatām tat tapaḥ kṣīṇam aiśvaryam bhuktam eva ca klība tām api kurvantaḥ yūyam naṃkṣyatha dānavāḥ vṛtaḥ sarva amaraiḥ śambhuḥ vadha artham bhavatām iha praṇatān api asau yuṣmān tad priya artham nihaṃsyati katham danu sutāḥ bhūtvā rājānaḥ bala darpitāḥ bhītāḥ mṛtyum jigīṣadhvam kṛpaṇāḥ iva dānavāḥ prāpsyatha adhikam aiśvaryam tyakṣyatha asūn raṇe yadi vinā yuddham vipannānām aśubhā vaḥ gatiḥ bhavet pramatha indrāḥ tatas yūyam bhaviṣyatha na saṃśayaḥ guṇam sandhi gatam na asti yuṣmākam devataiḥ saha śauryeṇa bhavatām prītaḥ kadācid vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ kariṣyāmi ca vaḥ rakṣām śastra āghāta niṣedhanīm uttiṣṭhata danoḥ putrāḥ vijayāya yuyutsayā nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā tārakākṣaḥ mahā balaḥ vidyunmālī ca daitya indrāḥ bāṇa ādyāḥ ca mahā asurāḥ kāla pāśa arditāḥ mūḍhāḥ kṣīṇa puṇyāḥ gata āyuṣaḥ nāradaḥ tatas hṛṣṭaḥ rakṣām baddhvā tu māyayā yuyutsūn asurān kṛtvā yayau śarva ratham prati tatas te dānavāḥ sarve yuddhāya kṛta niścayāḥ nānā praharaṇa upetāḥ babhūvuḥ yuddha lipsavaḥ avādyanta tatas śaṅkhāḥ tūryāṇi ca sahasraśas dānavānām bale ghore kātarāṇām bhaya prade sa rathaḥ a ayam iha āyāti asau anyaḥ pradṛśyate katham āhataḥ iti evam vacāṃsi ūcuḥ parasparam vigata bhaya viṣādāḥ traipurāḥ daitya saṃghāḥ te vīkṣya durgam tripuram gaṇeśāḥ nandīśa caṇḍīśa mukhāḥ su yattāḥ nādam pracakruḥ sahitāḥ pravīrāḥ yuyutsavaḥ dānava rāja siṃhaiḥ caṇḍeśvaraḥ caṇḍa vapūḥ mahātmā jvalat pradīpta ugra kuṭhāra pāṇiḥ dīptam triśūlam parigṛhya nandī tryakṣaḥ pratasthe hara tulya varṣmā pārśve sthitaḥ sa ca śaṅku karṇaḥ pragṛhya dīptam muśalam gaṇa indraḥ bhṛṅgiḥ hara ātmā sa ca vīrabhadraḥ tathā gaṇa indrāḥ śataśas pravīrāḥ vajtra triśūla asi bhuśuṇḍi hastāḥ yuyutsavaḥ tasthuḥ upeta harṣāḥ samāgatam tam ratham īkṣya daityāḥ yuddhāya nirjagmuḥ upeta mohāḥ te tārakākṣa pramukhāḥ su vīrāḥ sannahya nānā āyudha dīpta hastāḥ sārdham gaṇa indraiḥ samaram pracakruḥ danoḥ sutāḥ kopa vaśam prayātāḥ tasthau tathā eva asakṛt ātmanā ca paśyan raṇam tat gaṇa daityapānām vivyādha bhṛṅgim daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ vidyutprabhuḥ kopa virakta netraḥ bhṛṅgim samāsādya śilīmukhāḥ te na aśaknuvan tasya rujam prakartum vidyut prabham bhṛṅgiriṭiḥ tatas a asau śūlena dīptena jaghāna pṛṣṭhe sa tena śūlena hataḥ jaghūrṇa tyaktvā ca bhṛṅgim prayayau bhaya ārtaḥ vivyādha tīkṣṇaiḥ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ vināyakam saptabhiḥ aṃsa deśe punar triṣaṣṭyā daśabhiḥ ca bhūyas vidyutprabhaḥ tam gaja rāja vaktram sa puṣkara agreṇa gaja indra siṃhaḥ grīvām tadā daitya pateḥ viveṣṭya utpāṭayāmāsa śiraḥ śarīrāt padmam hradāt nāgaḥ iva pramattaḥ kruddhau upāgamya hi śaṅkukarṇam śilīmukhaiḥ vivyadhatuḥ gaṇa indram tam jaghnatuḥ na ekavidhaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ vajra abhighāta pratimaiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ dīptena hatvā muśalena vīrau sampreṣayāmāsa puram yamasya anye ca daityāḥ tripura adhivāsāḥ kruddhāḥ viniṣkramya gaṇa indra siṃhaiḥ nārāca cakra asi kuṭhāra hastāḥ ghoram mahat yuddham atīva cakruḥ daitya adhipāḥ te hara tulya kalpaiḥ gaṇeśvaraiḥ prāpta śiva prasādaiḥ prabhraṣṭa nānā āyudha vastra hārāḥ chinnaiḥ bhujaiḥ śoṇitam udvahantaḥ vajra āhatā petuḥ samudre giri śṛṅga kalpāḥ tam śaṅkukarṇaḥ ditija adhipa īśam muñcantam ugram śara varṣam āśu bhallena daityam giri sannikāśam jaghāna mūrdhni prasabham gaṇeśaḥ protthāya tūrṇam sa hi tārakākṣaḥ cikṣepa tasmai gaṇapāya cakram kruddhaḥ tatas a asau abhavat gaṇa indraḥ tam tārakākṣam sa hi saṅkukarṇaḥ nipātya muṣṭyā
