prajaghāna mūrdhni samāhataḥ saḥ a api jagāma kṛcchram mumoca roṣam virarāva tīvram mamāra paścāt asu vipramuktaḥ dṛṣṭvā vipannam ditija adhipa indram pragṛhya daityāḥ bhavanam mayasya tatas mayaḥ tān rudataḥ sureśān āśvāsayan prāha vacaḥ suresaḥ sṛṣṭam mayā vaḥ aamṛtam etat āste tena enam utthāpaya āśu daityāḥ tatas gṛhītvā amṛtam uttamam tat daitya adhipam daitya vṛṣāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ cakruḥ sa jīvam hi yathā purāṇam mayam praṇemuḥ ca muhur śirobhiḥ sa tārakākṣaḥ tatas āśu bhūyas yuyutsayā yuddha patham jagāma āyāntam ālakṣya pitāmahaḥ tam pūrvam mṛtam jīvitam āśu bhūyas provāca vākyam sa sura asura īśam nivedayan vāmakāreṇa daityam hataḥ śaṃkara tārakākṣaḥ kṛtaḥ mayena āśu sa jīvaḥ eva tasya asti deva amṛtam uttamam hi tena asurān jīvayate doṣaḥ mahān eṣa sura indra hetoḥ mṛtān mṛtān jīvayate yadā ājau tatas a amṛtam tanmaya saṃstham āśu pradhyāna mātreṇa jahāra śambhuḥ pitāmahaḥ tam punar eva hṛṣṭaḥ pinākinam prāha vacaḥ praṇamya dṛṣṭam mayā yuddham idam gaṇānām daitya adhipaiḥ sārdham ahīna sattvaiḥ divyam sahasram vigatam samānām kṣayam na ca etat tripuram jagāma kṣipasva dīptam tam iṣum sureśa prayāntu nāśam sura vidviṣaḥ te saṃkalpa mātrāt idam eti nāśam daitya adhivāsam tripuram tava īśa yadi tu aham mānayitavyaḥ īśa vimu`nca śīghram tripure śaram tam vijñaptaḥ evam caturānanena pratīpam ālīḍham anaṅgahantā kṛtvā dhanuḥ tat balavat vikṛṣya yuyoja dīptam tam iṣum pināke saṃkalpa mātreṇa tadā sa tāni purāṇi devaḥ sahitāni trīṇi cakre jagat sṛṣṭi vināśa kartā jagat ca niṣpandam abhūt tadā āśu viṣṇu ātmakam pāvaka soma puṅkham trailokya saṃhāre iva pradīptam cikṣepa devaḥ tam iṣum tadā ugram kṣiptvā ca kaṣṭam dhik iti iti ca āha nandī samāgamya tatas maheśam provāca vākyam kim iti praṇamya nandīśvaram tam bhagavān uvāca mayasya bhaktasya śubham cikīrṣuḥ nandī pragṛhya atha sureśvara ājñām tūrṇam yayau viśvakṛtaḥ puram tat dṛṣṭvā mayam tatra sa dānava īśam mūrdhnā nata aṅgam vṛṣabhadhvajasya mṛtyoḥ bhaya ārtam śaraṇa arthinam ca nandī samāśvāsayat īśa bhaktam nandīśvaram dānava rāj sa dṛṣṭvā śrutvā priyam tad śiva samprasādam atha agniḥ āgāt tripuram didhakṣan pradīpayitvā sakalam samantāt tam āgatam viśvakṛtaḥ nivāsam viṣṇu indu yuktam jvalanam sa nandī nandī hutāśam sa tatas aabhyuvāca mayaḥ aatra tiṣṭhati amara īśa bhaktaḥ tam vahniḥ āha asura rājam āśu tūrṇam vinirgaccha mayā iti vākyam haimam gṛhītvā sa maheśa liṅgam purāt viniṣkramya mayaḥ pātālam āśu praviveśa hṛṣṭaḥ kurvan namaskāram umāpriyasya nandīśvaraḥ saḥ aapi sureśa pārśvam āgamya ca ākhyāya ca saṃsthitaḥ aabhūt tatas pradīptam tripuram babhūva viśkiṣṭa yantra argala naṣṭa veśma vātāyane harmya vimāna saṃsthāḥ candra ānanāḥ pīna payodhara āḍhyāḥ paryaṅka suptāḥ mada vihvala akṣyaḥ mārgam priyāṇām muhur īhṣamāṇāḥ vilocanaiḥ tāmra nibha aṅgarāgaiḥ śyāma avadātā jaghanaiḥ viśālaiḥ daitya aṅganāḥ svam dadṛśuḥ pradīptam āliṅgyamānāḥ śara pāvakena prāsāda saṃsthāḥ prayayuḥ bhaya ārttāḥ trāsena kinnaryaḥ iva acala sthāḥ priyān atha udvīkṣya samāgatān tān moham samāliṅgya bhṛśam vijagmuḥ priyāḥ gṛhītvā ditijāḥ tatas te pranaṣṭa kāmāḥ tarasā abhijagmuḥ niṣkrānta mātrāḥ śiva śakti mūḍhāḥ petuḥ samudre bala viprayuktāḥ daityān samudre patitān tatas tān matsyāḥ mahāntaḥ giri sannikāśāḥ tīvrāḥ ca nakrāḥ makarāḥ ca ghorāḥ saṃjagrasuḥ naṣṭa balān vimūḍhān jalecara indrāḥ tu apare mahāntaḥ saṃchinna hārāḥ patitāḥ striyaḥ tāḥ hīnāḥ priyaiḥ bhakṣayitum pravṛttāḥ karāla daṃṣṭrāḥ vivṛta ānanāḥ ca tāḥ bhakṣyamāṇāḥ patitāḥ taruṇyaḥ priyān sa roṣam bahuśas nirīkṣya rujā mahatyā parikhidyamānāḥ saṃcukruśuḥ dīnataram yuvatyaḥ tāsām tadā daitya vilāsinīnām reje bhṛśam krodha nirīkṣitam tat rata avasāne parikheditānām priyaiḥ iva anyām abhigantu kāmaiḥ sarve tatas daitya vṛṣāḥ sa bhāryāḥ pradahyamānāḥ tripura analena śaraḥ ca saḥ a agni indu janārdana ātmā pradahya kṛtsnam tripuram puram tat kṣiptvā samudre sma śamam prayātam śaśāma śambhoḥ ca karam jagāma pūrvam yathā divya śarīra yuktān cakāra sṛṣṭi pralaya ādi hetuḥ daityāḥ hatāḥ tat tripuram pradagdham śāntiḥ kṛtā naḥ sma sura asura īśa namaḥ a astu sarvatra sadā sthitāya sraṣṭre surāṇām parama īśa tubhyam tān āha devaḥ sa tadā sura indrān brahma arka viṣṇu indra dhaneśvara ādyān sadā eva yūyam pratipālanīyāḥ rakṣyāḥ ca devāḥ suta vat mayā eva pūrṇa abhilāṣāḥ hata vidviṣaḥ ca prayāta hṛṣṭāḥ sva niveśanāni devāḥ tatas deva varam praṇamya jagmuḥ svakīyāni niveśanāni devaḥ siddhaiḥ abhivandyamānaḥ kailāsa śṛṅgam sahitaḥ gaṇa indraiḥ caṇḍeśa nandīśvara vīrabhadraiḥ jagāma kartā jagataḥ trinetraḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca kasmāt kruddhaḥ naga indram tam krauñcam dāritavān guhaḥ pakṣān sarva giri indrāṇām kasmāt ciccheda vāsavaḥ śṛṇu vyāsa mahābuddhe yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi kumāreṇa yathā bhinnaḥ mainākiḥ krauñcaparvataḥ apaśyat vāsavaḥ skandam saṃghātam tejasām iva śara stamba vane dṛṣṭvā kumāram anala prabham sura rājya mada āviṣṭaḥ śakraḥ papraccha ṣaṇmukham na mām pūjayase dṛṣṭvā devarājam iha āgatam tam evaṃvādinam śakram prāha śūladhara ātmajaḥ brahma ādyāḥ mām vijānanti siddhāḥ veda vidaḥ ca ye kim tvayā jānatā śakra kāryam kim pūjitena vā ehi ehi tvam mayā sārdham kuru śīghram pradakṣiṇam bāḍham iti evam uktvā atha kumāraḥ ṣaṇmukhaḥ tadā śakreṇa saha saṃgatya mayūra varam āsthitaḥ kṛtvā su nirvṛtaḥ tasthau upaviṣṭaḥ śilā tale javena atha kumāraḥ tam krauñcam kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam provāca indram tadā dṛṣṭvā jetā aham iti sa tvaraḥ asakṛt bruvataḥ evam tayoḥ śakra kumārayoḥ tatas śakraḥ uvāca idam kumāram vacanam tadā eṣaḥ eva āvayoḥ krañcaḥ jaya sākṣī mahā balaḥ na anṛtam vakṣyati hi eṣa pautraḥ himagireḥ varaḥ pṛcchyatām śakra kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha jvalanātmajaḥ tam śakram sa ādaram prāha kena tvam acala agratas kṛta pradakṣiṇaḥ brūhi pramāṇam hi tvam āvayoḥ tatas krauñcaḥ vimūḍha ātmā saṃcintya su ciram nagaḥ ayam śacīpatiḥ cakre mām iha agre pradakṣiṇam papāta śikharam tūrṇam kuliśena yathā hatam tatra āsan yāni bhūtāni sura ādyāni girīśvare tāni saṃtyajya śīghram tam prayayuḥ sarvatas diśam jahṛṣe vāsavaḥ ca api manasā pūjayan girim tatas cukrodha rudra ātmā gireḥ krauñcasya ṣaṇmukhaḥ guham draṣṭum saṃkruddham vāsavaḥ tadā kṣīṇa āyuṣaḥ yathā puṃsaḥ mṛtyu pāśa mūrtimān apatat bhūmau saṃjñā prāṇa vivarjitaḥ patim vinihatam dṛṣṭvā patnyaḥ tasya su duḥkhitāḥ vilapantyaḥ tadā dīnam petuḥ krauñca acala upari pāriyātraḥ ca sahyaḥ ca niṣadha udaya vāmanāḥ sarve parvata rājānaḥ ājagmuḥ śoka pīḍitāḥ parivārya girim krauñcam ruruduḥ duḥkhitāḥ bhṛśam bhrātṛ putram hatam jñātvā devadevī girīndrajā śarveṇa sahitā krauñcam ājagāma mahā vratā kumāreṇa hatam dṛṣṭvā krauñcam bāndhavam ātmanaḥ pīḍitā abhūt tadā devī dṛṣṭvā pitaram arditam śuśoca girijā dṛṣṭvā muhur vīkṣya sureśvaram śokena api su santaptāḥ namaḥ cakruḥ mahā balāḥ vyajñāpayata dīna ātmā duḥkha śoka pariplutaḥ śakreṇa anena bhagavan ātmānam bahu manyatā nidhanam nāyitaḥ pautraḥ mama abhāva pīḍitāḥ pitaram duḥkhitam dṛṣṭvā tathā anyān bāndhavān girīn atha tān duḥkhitān dṛṣṭvā sarvān go vṛṣa vāhanaḥ mā kārṣṭa śokam iti uktvā tanayam prāha ṣaṇmukham na aśubham kurvate kasmāt parama adbhutam śakrasya apanayāt deva krauñcaḥ eṣa hataḥ mayā asat mantritavān yasmāt vijñaptim aparām śṛṇu tvad prasādāt aham krauñcam jīvayāmi naga uttamam uttiṣṭha iti tatas krauñcam bhrātaram prāha ṣaṇmukhaḥ sa bibhrat pūrva vat deham krauñcaḥ nagapatiḥ kṣaṇāt uttasthau nīrujaḥ vyāsaḥ āścaryam tat abhūt tadā jīvitena acalena evam ṣaṇmukhaḥ vahni saprabhaḥ samakṣam sarva devānām śakrasya ca mahā balaḥ vāyu viṣṇu yamānām ca brahmaṇaḥ ca mahātmanaḥ devadevam praṇamya īśam pitaram hi umayā saha babhāṣe vacanam devaḥ kumāra vara rūpadhṛk śakreṇa anena deva indrāḥ mad samakṣam prabhāṣitam tat mayā eṣā mahā śaktiḥ nikhātā vasudhā tale utpāṭayatu sa hi etām mahām mattaḥ tatas hi saḥ evam uktvā tatas devaḥ bāla arka sadṛśa prabhaḥ tūṣṇīm babhūva hṛṣṭa ātmā tasthau ca pitṛ pārśvatas utpāṭayitum utsehe tām śaktim vasudhām gatām na ca cālayitum śaktaḥ yatnāt api surādhipaḥ tatas aanye daivata śreṣṭhāḥ yama anila puraḥsarāḥ matim cakruḥ samuddhartum yatnam śaktyāḥ ca daṃśitāḥ na ca cālayitum śekuḥ tām śaktim amara uttamāḥ tatas viṣṇuḥ ameya ātmā devān dṛṣṭvā hata ojasaḥ tena asau cālyamānā api yasmāt śaktiḥ dharā tale na cacāla mahā vīryā skanda tejaḥ bala anvitā tatas viṣṇuḥ ameya ātmā jñātvā tattva artham ādṛtaḥ kumāram pūjayan bhaktyā śakti utkṣepāt nyavartata atha sarve aamarāḥ vyāsa viṣṇuḥ ca sura sattamaḥ devānām mahādeva sutaḥ prabhuḥ nāthaḥ pālayitā sraṣṭā ārti ghnaḥ pravaraḥ mahān tvayā nāthena deveśa vayam sarve su nirvṛtāḥ tiṣṭhāmaḥ sahitāḥ sarve tvam asmān pāhi sarvatas śakra vyatikramam ca eva bāliśyāt moha kāritam praṇayāt yācitaḥ a asmābhiḥ kṣantum arhasi sarvadā evam sa bhagavān sarvaiḥ kumāraḥ saṃstutaḥ aamaraiḥ devarājaḥ tathā śakraḥ hṛṣṭāḥ guham apūjayan bhagavān api saṃtuṣṭaḥ tanayāya varān dadau yayau ca api gireḥ śṛṅgam divyam himavataḥ śubham sārdham guhena devyā ca mātR̥ṇām gaṇanāyakaḥ krauñcena sahitāḥ ca api meru vindhya ādayaḥ śakraḥ ca surarāj devaḥ svāni sadmāni bhejire evam etat yathā krauñcaḥ krauñca sārasa vāsinaḥ guhena dāritaḥ śaktyā paścāt ca eva kṛtaḥ dṛśyate ca api tat krauñce kṣatam śaktyā acala uttame yaḥ imam śṛṇuyāt martyaḥ sarva pāpaiḥ sa mucyate vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavan parameśānaḥ mātRṇām nāyakaḥ katham kāḥ etāḥ mātaraḥ ca api śaṃsa etat pṛcchataḥ mama katham mātṛ gaṇāḥ jātāḥ kiṃnimittam atha api ca kiṃvīryāḥ kimprabhāvāḥ ca sambhutāḥ te gaṇāḥ prabho kaḥ ca āsām āśrayaḥ tena vartante tad gaṇāḥ śubhāḥ kena sṛṣṭāḥ svayam vā api etat icchāmi veditum atra te vartayiṣyāmi mātR̥ṇām udbhavam śubham purā hi bhagavān brahmā sṛṣṭvā imāḥ vividhāḥ prajāḥ avekṣamāṇaḥ kāleya cacāra vibudha īśvaraḥ sa kadācid prajādhyakṣaḥ saṃdhyā kāle upāgate deśam ramyam samāsādya tīre pūrva mahā udadheḥ ramye cakāra saṃdhyām hi varṣa koṭim atandritaḥ cintayāmāsa ramyaḥ a ayam deśaḥ dṛṣṭi manoharaḥ aṭṭa aṭṭahāsakaiḥ ca eva khātakaiḥ ca samanvitam śṛṅgāṭaka catuṣkeṇa catuṣpādam iva sthitam vapra khātaka saṃyuktaiḥ gṛhaiḥ ca api mahādhanaiḥ madhye mandākinī vāpī sarit divyā manoharā nalinī vana saṃchannā prahṛṣṭa khaga nāditā tat sṛṣṭvā tu puram brahmā sauvarṇam maṇi bhūṣitam avadhyāḥ te jarā hīnāḥ tejaḥ bala samanvitāḥ bhaviṣyanti mahābhāgāḥ mad prasādāt na saṃśayaḥ asmin sadā eva kāmānām iṣṭānām sura sattamaḥ devaḥ varṣati koṭim vai tena asmin sukhinaḥ janāḥ evam sa bhagavān uktvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ adhiṣṭhitam puram tat vai sarvaiḥ brāhmaṇa kaṇṭakaiḥ yeṣām patiḥ asu krodhaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ brahma hā yajña hā vipra deva antaka sura antakaḥ siṃhanādaḥ bhīmanādaḥ madaḥ iti evamādayaḥ atha daityāḥ samāgamya haima kuṇḍa puraḥsarāḥ tasmin pura vare sthitvā pīḍām cakruḥ anekaśas yajña homa ādikāḥ chinnāḥ kriyāḥ taiḥ asura adhamaiḥ tān evaṃkāriṇaḥ jñātvā sarve eva divaukasaḥ vacaḥ divaukasām śrutvā jñātvā daitya viceṣṭitam ājagāma bhavam draṣṭum ramyam hīmagireḥ vanam yatra gaurī tapaḥ tepe bhartṛ deha ardha dhāriṇī praviṣṭāḥ tatra te devāḥ brahma ādyāḥ sarve eva hi striyaḥ eva abhavan tūrṇam pārvatyāḥ tapasaḥ balāt tatas tān devadeveśaḥ strī bhūtān hi sura uttamān kimartham āgatāḥ yūyam iti papraccha śūladhṛk nivedya śambhave paścāt kṛcchram strī bhāvam ātmanaḥ yathā evam puruṣāḥ pūrvam bhavāmaḥ iti te abruvan tān uvāca atha deveśaḥ surān strī bhāvam āgatān yāta yūyam surāḥ sarve striyaḥ bhūtvā asura antikam strīṇām eva hi te vadhyāḥ dānavāḥ bala darpitāḥ tanūḥ mūrtimatīḥ kṛtvā paratas mātaraḥ śubhāḥ ye ye eva yathā pūrvam bhaviṣyatha sura uttamāḥ atha bhūyas praṇamya īśam devatāḥ idam abruvan yayā sārdham balāt daityān haṃsyāmaḥ parameśvara tatas devaḥ asṛjat devīm rudrāṇīm mātaram śubhām vikṛtam rūpam āsthāya dvitīyām api mātaram nāmnā tu bahu māṃsām tām jagat saṃhāra rūpiṇīm mātarau asṛjat dve tu vārāhīm vaiṣṇavīm api abhūt pitāmahāt brāhmī śarvāṇī śaṃkarāt api kaumārī ṣaṇmukhāt ca api viṣṇoḥ api ca vaiṣṇavī vārāhi mādhavāt devī māhendrī ca purandarāt sarva tejaḥ mayī devī mātR̥ṇām pravarā śubhā bahu māṃsā mahā vidyā babhūva vṛṣabhadhvajāt sarvāsām devatānām ca dehebhyaḥ mātaraḥ śubhāḥ sva rūpa bala dhāriṇyaḥ nirjagmuḥ daitya nāśanāḥ vāyavyā vāruṇī yāmyā kauberī ca mahā balāḥ mahākālī tathā āgneyī anyāḥ ca eva sahasraśas tāḥ gatvā tat puram ramyam daityān bhīma parākramān daitya hīnam ca tat cakruḥ purā agryam hema bhūṣitam ājagāma pradeśam tam mātRṇām vara ditsayā tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān sarvān daityān amara vidviṣaḥ parituṣṭaḥ tadā tāsām varān prādāt vṛṣadhvajaḥ jagataḥ mātaraḥ yūyam mātṛ bhūtāḥ bhaviṣyathaḥ yuṣmākam ye bhaviṣyanti bhaktāḥ puruṣa puṅgavāḥ striyaḥ vā api mahābhāgāḥ na tān hiṃsanti hiṃsakāḥ mṛtāḥ mama gaṇāḥ ca api bhaviṣyanti ajara amarāḥ bhavatīnām idam sthānam koṭī varṣam iti śrutam aham hetuḥ hi yuṣmākam yasmāt sṛṣṭāḥ mayā eva ca hetukeśvara nāmnā aham sthāsyāmi atra vara pradaḥ yaḥ tu yuṣmān mayā sārdham vidhivat pūjayiṣyati sarva pāpa vimukta ātmā sa parām gatim āpsyati dānavāḥ nihatāḥ yasmāt śūlena bahu māṃsayā śūlakuṇḍam idam nāmnā khyātam tīrtham bhaviṣyati iha śūla udakam pītvā bahu māṃsām praṇamya ca adhṛṣyaḥ sarva hiṃsrāṇām bhaviṣyati nara uttamaḥ pratikūlā iti vikhyātā ramyā mandākinī nadī aham brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ mātṛtantrāṇi divyāni mātṛyajña vidhim param puṇyāni prakariṣyāmaḥ yajanam yaiḥ avāpsyatha brāhmam svāyambhuvam ca eva kaumāram yāmalam tathā sārasvatam sa gāndhāram aiśānam nandiyāmalam tantrāṇi etāni yuṣmākam tathā anyāni sahasraśas narāṇām yajamānānām varān yūyam pradāsyatha yāḥ ca nāryaḥ sadā yuṣmān yakṣyante sa rahasyataḥ yoga īśvaryaḥ bhaviṣyanti rāmāḥ divya parākramāḥ chagalaḥ kumbhakarṇaḥ ca madīyau gaṇa nāyakau yuṣmākam dvārapāla tve sthāsyataḥ tau mama ājñayā koṭī varṣam idam sthānam mātR̥ṇām priyam uttamam śmaśānam pravaram divyam bhaviṣyati sukha pradam varān evam hi tān labdhvā mātaraḥ loka mātaraḥ bhaktyā praṇamya deveśam mumuduḥ bhṛśam arditāḥ tatas prabhṛti tāḥ sarvāḥ sahitāḥ śaśimaulinā koṭī varṣe vasanti sma sarva loka abhaya pradāḥ evam sa bhagavān devaḥ mātR̥ṇām gaṇanāyakaḥ abhavat śaṃkaraḥ vyāsa yat mām tvam pṛṣṭavān asi utpattim etām jagatī īśvarīṇām brahma indra śakra anila vanditānām paṭhet manuṣyaḥ śṛṇuyāt ca nityam yaḥ svarga lokam sa mṛtaḥ labheta śakreṇa girayaḥ pūrvam chinna pakṣāḥ yathā kṛtāḥ tat pravakṣyāmi te vyāsa śṛṇu sarvam aśeṣatas purā siṃha vapuḥ kṛtvā viṣṇunā parama ojasā hate pitari sa śrīmān mahā daitya pati īśvaraḥ bahūni abda sahasrāṇi cakāra ugram mahā tapaḥ praṇamya uvāca vara dam idam brahmāṇam āgatam rājānam hatavān viṣṇuḥ pitaram mama māyayā saṃgrāme tam aham viṣṇum yathā hanyām tathā kuru ajayyaḥ samare viṣṇuḥ avadhyaḥ ca sura asuraiḥ prasādāt devadevasya jagatsraṣṭuḥ umāpateḥ na eṣa śakyaḥ mayā dātum varaḥ tubhyam mahā asura anyam vṛṇu yathā iṣṭam tvam varam yāvat dadāmi te tasya viṣṇoḥ tatas deva śakrasya anyasya vā ripoḥ katham hanyām aham viṣṇum śakram ca eva śatakratum sarva śaila adhipaḥ śrīmān cakramat himavān giriḥ dvābhyām utpatya pakṣābhyām ājagāma viyat caraḥ purā hi girayaḥ vyāsa āsan pakṣa samanvitāḥ tam āgatam atho dṛṣṭvā prahrādaḥ himavat girim prāha idam vacanam prītaḥ kṛtvā svāgatam āditas devatāḥ bhrātaraḥ bhūtvā asmākam devatāḥ ca hi avamanya asurān asmān rājyam kurvanti darpitāḥ vayam yūyam ca saṃgatya jitvā devān aśeṣatas devānām yajanam yeṣu hūyante yeṣu ca agnayaḥ prīyante devatāḥ yeṣu deśān tān acala īśvara ijyā hīnān tatas devān sukham haṃsyāma nirvṛtāḥ na etat yuktam iti prāha sa āśaṅkaḥ dānava adhipam eṣa tvām sahitaḥ śailaiḥ neṣyāmi nidhanam samam daitya rājam tatas kruddham dṛṣṭvā parvata sattamaḥ atha śailaiḥ tadā sārdham himavān acala uttamaḥ pitṛ deva ātmikāḥ sarvāḥ yajña homa ādikāḥ kriyāḥ śakrāya aśrāvayat sarvam parvatānām vyatikramam imam vyatikramam prāptāḥ na doṣaḥ naḥ kathaṃcana tena idam kāritam sarvam yajña deśa upamardanam tān evam bruvataḥ śakraḥ sutarām manyumān girīn pakṣa hīnān tadā cakre kṣiptvā vajram punar punar hīna pakṣāḥ tatas te tu sarve eva acala īśvarāḥ petuḥ mahī tale vyāsa chinna pakṣāḥ khagāḥ iva pakṣa chedam naga indrāṇām bhṛśam cukrodha pīḍitaḥ kim karomi iti saṃcintya ciram daitya gaṇa adhipaḥ badaryāśramam āgatya dadarśa viṣṇum āsthitam tasya āsīt su mahat yuddham viṣṇunā sārdham adbhutam na śaśāka ca tam viṣṇuḥ jetum prahlādam ojasā ātmānam veda hīnam ca viṣṇuḥ prahlāda dānavāt aśaktaḥ dānavam jetum manyumān abhavat prabhuḥ atha dhyātvā mahādevam praṇamya ca punar punar prasādam tam anusmṛtya śaivam viṣṇuḥ surottamaḥ hīyamānam atha ātmānam hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ jñātvā ca balinam viṣṇum yuddha deśāt apākramat ajitam viṣṇunā ātmānam śiva tejaḥ vimohitaḥ prahrādaḥ jitam ātmānam bubudhe dānava īśvaraḥ prahrāda asura saṃgrāmam ghoram deva bhayaṃkaram abhūt abda śatam divyam viṣṇunā sārdham adbhutam na śrutena na vīryeṇa na śauryeṇa na tejasā hiraṇyakaśipuḥ na āsīt rājā tad sadṛśaḥ mahān na andhakaḥ na hiraṇyākṣaḥ prahlāda sadṛśaḥ bale bhṛgu śāpāt kila āyātaḥ daitya tvam viṣṇuḥ eva saḥ na abhavan tasya rājye tu duḥkha śoka anvitāḥ prajāḥ evam sa dānava śreṣṭhaḥ kṛtvā yuddham tu viṣṇunā paścāttāpa upatapta aṅgaḥ viṣayebhyaḥ gata spṛhaḥ vara dānam anityam tat jñātvā ca tapasaḥ phalam niḥspṛhaḥ sarva kāryeṣu viṣaya īpsā vivarjitaḥ sarva sannyasta karmā tu dhyāna abhyāsa parāyaṇaḥ punarāvartakam janma buddhvā ca anitya tām parām kaṣṭam rājyam iti jñātvā prahrādaḥ parama artha vid abhiṣicya sutam rājye ditijānām virocanam daitya dānava rājānam kṛtvā tam asura īśvaram mokṣa siddhim parām icchan pravrajyā kṛta niścayaḥ param tattvam atha anveṣṭum guṇa atītam ajam śivam sākṣāt bhagavataḥ śiṣyam kapilasya āsurim munim śiṣya tvena upasaṃgamya mokṣa vidyām avāptavān prakṛtīnām param tattvam vikārāṇām param tathā kṣetrajñam puruṣam jñātvā bhoktāram bhoktṛ varjitam mokṣa vidyā para artha jñaḥ sāṃkhya siddhānta pāragaḥ sa yogam paramam labdhvā sāṃkhya ācāryaḥ mahā muniḥ śrīmān evam tribhuvana ripuḥ daitya rājaḥ mahātmā kṛtvā vairam vibudha guruṇā viṣṇunā dīrgha kālam siddhaḥ paścāt jagat abhaya daḥ prāpta yogaḥ ca bhūtvā muktaḥ paścāt sa padam amṛtam brahma ca ādyam hi avāpa kṣetrajña boddhā guṇa viprayuktaḥ duḥkhaiḥ vihīnaḥ bhava pāśa bandhaiḥ evam tān chinna pakṣān tu girīn sarvān purandaraḥ pracakāra muni śreṣṭha prāk pṛṣṭaḥ yat aham tvayā vyāsaḥ uvāca yātaḥ himavataḥ śṛṅgam pārvatyā sahitaḥ haraḥ kim anyat akarot devaḥ kim ca enam prāha pārvatī sūtaḥ uvāca ṛṣiḥ parama yogi īśaḥ kathayāmāsa tattvataḥ babhāṣe girijā devam praṇamya parameśvaram uñcha vṛtteḥ hiraṇyasya naimiśa araṇya vāsinaḥ svayam eva prayātā aham dvijam pūjām pratīcchitum māhātmyam tasya tat dṛṣṭvā brāhmaṇasya tapasvinaḥ gatā aham vismayam deva dvijāḥ śreṣṭhatamāḥ iti devebhyaḥ a api garīyāṃsaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ iti me matiḥ śreṣṭhāḥ tapasvinaḥ viprāḥ devebhyaḥ a api garīyasaḥ madīyāḥ yāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ prathamāḥ prabhavaḥ hi aham rudrāḥ dvijātayaḥ pūrvam mayā sṛṣṭāḥ mahā ojasaḥ madīyām sṛṣṭim ālokya brahmaṇā api sisṛkṣuṇā brāhmaṇāḥ mūrdhataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ pūrvam eva mahā prabhāḥ agra bhūtaḥ hi aham teṣām dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ tadā abhavam uttamā eṣā aparā sṛṣṭiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ dharma ādikam caturvargam sarvam teṣu pratiṣṭhitam jagat pratiṣṭhitam sarvam brāhmaṇānām hi tejasā mṛtyu janma apaham yat tat mama pāśupatam vratam na varṇāḥ sādhayanti anye muktvā brāhmaṇa sattamān lakṣaṇam sampravakṣyāmi dvijātīnām idam śṛṇu brāhmaṇaḥ tu bhavet jātyā saṃskārāt dvijaḥ ucyate vidyayā vipra tām yāti brāhmaṇyam trividham smṛtam yaḥ ca jātyā bhavet vipraḥ yaḥ ca syāt vedapāragaḥ tayoḥ trāṇe vadhe ca api puṇya pāpe same smṛte jātyā ca yaḥ bhavet vipraḥ sarva āgama viśāradaḥ tādṛśam bhojayet śrāddhe daive karmaṇi vā api yaḥ saḥ a api śreṣṭhaḥ smṛtaḥ devi pūjitaḥ tārayet kulam sarvathā jāti mātreṇa yaḥ syāt brāhmaṇaḥ kvacid na anṛtam brāhmaṇaḥ brūte na hanti prāṇinam dvijaḥ vidvas brāhmaṇa tām labdhvā kim na labdham hi dehinā mūrtayaḥ yāḥ smṛtāḥ hi aṣṭāu arka soma ādayaḥ mama prabhavanti sadā devi viprāḥ śreṣṭhatamāḥ tatas na asādhyam vidyate teṣām dvijānām parama ojasām ruṣitāḥ te prasannāḥ vā prayacchanti śubha aśubham dvijāḥ tapasvinaḥ ye tu veda vidyā viśāradāḥ aham pitāmahaḥ ca eva teṣām yoni dvayam smṛtam mattaḥ pūrvam prasūtāḥ te tatas devi pitāmahāt āvām hetū dvijātīnām prakṛti tvāt tvam eva ca prakṛtiḥ tvam samākhyātā puruṣaḥ paramaḥ hi aham brahma viṣṇū smṛtau yau tau rajaḥ sattva guṇa ātmakau āvābhyām tau prajāyete sṛṣṭi kāle prajāpatī aham hi agniḥ tamaḥ viṣṇuḥ sattvam brahmaṇi saṃsthitam sattvam nāśayate tau hi sa ca agneḥ samprajāyate vahnitejāḥ smṛtāḥ hi ete mahātmānaḥ dvijātayaḥ sarvatas prabhavanti ete na asti teṣām nivāraṇam ārjavam samatām ca eva viddhi tejaḥ dvijātiṣu tapaḥ vidyā samāyuktāt ārjavaḥ tu viśiṣyate a śāṭhyam hanti pāpāni sama tā moha bandhanam purā bhāgīrathī tīre dvijaḥ parama dharma vid nāmnā dānaruciḥ nāma uñcha vṛttiḥ babhūva ha ṣaṣṭhe kāle tatas tasya idam vratam uttamam athā evam vartamānasya bhūyān kālaḥ jagāma ha babhūva atyartham arciṣmān arka agnī iva tejasā tasya evam tapasaḥ vahniḥ prītaḥ tuṣṭim agāt parām kadācid atha kālena ṣaṣṭhe kāle samāgate na apaśyat atithim kaṃcid bubhukṣā klama kheditaḥ a prāśya eva tadā kiṃcid upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ yathā eva asyāḥ patiḥ cakre tathā sā api akarot tadā śīta kṣudh upatapta aṅgaḥ na eka dvandva samāvṛtaḥ dvitīye aatha samāyāte ṣaṣṭhe kāle sa ha dvijaḥ śīta durdina jāt doṣāt na eva atithim avaikṣata atha agniḥ tasya tat jñātvā niścayam paramam mahat śvapāka sadṛśam rūpam vikṛtam kutsitam ca hi apaśyat vṛkṣa mūla stham ghoram vikṛta rūpiṇam śvapākam śīta saṃkhinnam na eka vraṇa śata aṅkitam durdṛśam vṛddham ārtam ca prasravat kṛmi śoṇitam kṛpaṇam tam atho dṛṣṭvā śvapākam dvijasattamaḥ śīta apanayana artham ca vahnim asya anayat dvijaḥ atha tam vahni saṃsargāt samāśvastam uvāca saḥ tam uvāca tatas dīnam śvapākaḥ tapasām nidhim na aham saṃskṛtam āhartum yogyaḥ a annam iti ca abravīt tam evaṃvādinam dhyānāt jñātvā vahnim upasthitam provāca dvija śārdūlaḥ idam vacana kovidaḥ na aham jātim garhayāmi pūjayāmi na ca anagha ātmā sarva gataḥ hi eṣa sarva prāṇiṣu saṃsthitaḥ ātmānam tam aham bhaktyā pūjayāmi param śivam tiryakṣu na hi me kutsā tvadvidheṣu viśeṣataḥ kṛmi kīṭa ākhu sarpeṣu śva pāc deva dvijātiṣu yadā sarva gataḥ hi ātmā tadā kutsā katham ca naḥ bhuṅkṣva saṃskṛtam annam tu prāpaya asmān anugraham evam uktaḥ dvijendreṇa śvapākaḥ prītimān tadā vimuktaḥ saha patnyā tu prāptavān amṛtam padam evam ārjava sampannaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṛta lakṣaṇaḥ śṛṇvan nityam idam paṭhan ca vidhivat vidvān śuciḥ mānavaḥ sṛṣṭeḥ prabhavāt mama te dvijendrāḥ māhātmyam ittham paramam hi avāpuḥ dvija māhātmyam ullikhya pārvatī parameśayoḥ babhūva ittham su saṃvādaḥ puṇyaḥ pāpa vināśanaḥ pārāśarya tapodhana iti skandapurāṇe dvijamāhātmyavarṇanam nāma vyāsaḥ uvāca prāpya pāśupatam yogam brahma ādyāḥ tridivaukasaḥ kīdṛśam tat param yogam jñānam pāśupatam śubham yat jñātvā brāhmaṇāḥ siddhāḥ prāpnuyuḥ mokṣam uttamam iti pṛṣṭaḥ tu śiṣyeṇa provāca muni sattamaḥ yat mām pṛcchasi tat jñānam yogam māheśvaram param sarvāsām yoga vidyānām yat tattvam parikīrtyate sāṃkhya yoga āgama upetāḥ sarva adhyātma viśāradāḥ yat a buddhvā mahābhāga jñānam śaṃkara bhāṣitam tat yathā kathitam teṣām tryambakeṇa divaukasām tat te aham saṃpravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepāt tattva viniścayam tasya aham sthita pakṣam tu saṃsāra utpatti nāśanam namaskṛtya maheśānam puruṣam bhūtabhāvanam prakṛteḥ paramam guhyam pudgalam parameṣṭhinam yam sāṃkhyāḥ puruṣam prāhuḥ pañcaviṃśam ajam vibhum yogāḥ ca api hi ṣaḍviṃśam vyāpinam triguṇa ātmakam yaḥ aasṛjat sṛṣṭi kāle tu devau sarva jagat sṛjau prajāpatī mahātmānau dhyātvā viṣṇu pitāmahau tam praṇamya mahādevam tryakṣam vara dam īśvaram lakṣaṇam viddhi yogasya procyamānam idam mayā chidyante paśu pāśāni yasya abhyāsāt mahā mune eṣa bhogaḥ iti vyāsa kīrtitaḥ śambhunā purā bhava janma apahaḥ sūkṣmaḥ prapannānām divaukasām śarīre tiṣṭhataḥ puṃsaḥ yadā ātmani manaḥ sthitam kṛtānām pratyayaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ sukha duḥkha ādi saṃjñinām aśeṣa lopaḥ iti uktam sādhakasya tu yuñjataḥ abhisandhiḥ tadā yasmāt īśvarasya ātmanaḥ ca ha sukha ādānam atha ekena bhāvanā pra atha adhikaraṇam tatra kramaśas parikīrtyate pratyāhāram atas vidyā prāṇāyamaḥ tathā eva ca dhyānam ca dhāraṇā ca eva yoga abhyāsaḥ udāhṛtaḥ vaśyāḥ hi dhātavaḥ tasmāt bhavanti asya na saṃśayaḥ antarikṣe ca sarvāḥ tu kīrtitāḥ hi na saṃśayaḥ sthāna traya nibaddhāḥ tu catur lakṣaṇa saṃsthitāḥ kriyāḥ pramādinā na etāḥ śakyāḥ sādhayitum kvacid tisraḥ etāḥ sadā mṛtyum pravṛttāḥ moha lakṣaṇāḥ ajñānam kampate tāsu bahis antar carāsu api bhūta indriya manaḥ kāla diś nivṛttiḥ prabhāvataḥ daśa eva āśāḥ trayaḥ kālāḥ bhūtāni indriya vistaraḥ manaḥ pracāra saṃyuktaḥ viṣaya abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ tri kāla viṣayam jñānam aiśvarya udayam eva ca cale manasi na abhūtām bhavetām saṃsthite samam manaḥ sarvam idam yasmāt sādhanam yoga karmaṇaḥ prāṇa nigrahaṇe dhyānam prāṇāyāmam iti smṛtam prāṇaḥ eva hi vāyūnām sārathye vartate sadā prāṇa nigrahaṇe yogī nityam abhyāsam ācaret dvis apāne sakṛt prāṇe samāne ca ebhiḥ dhyāna gatiḥ sūkṣmā vāyu saṃrodha kāri tā sakṛt eva samāhārāt asakṛt parimokṣaṇāt kumbhakam ca etat uddiṣṭam prāṇāyāma ādi dhāraṇāt prāṇaḥ vāyuḥ asau ātmā śarīre jīva vidyāt rūpa dvayam tasya sthūlam sūkṣmam ca sarvatas avyaktam sūkṣma rūpam tu sthūlam ākāra lakṣaṇam sthūlāt ārabhya sūkṣmam tu dhyāna abhyāsāt nirūpayet sūkṣma saṃropaṇāt jyotiḥ prakāśaḥ jāyate mune dhyāyataḥ sthūlalakṣyam tu sarva dikṣu sṛtam manaḥ yadā dīptimat utpadyet tadā āśu sthāpayet punar girau vṛkṣe marut pṛṣṭhe śvabhre prāsāda paṅktiṣu samudre vasudhāyām vā manaḥ saṃyogam ācaret acaitanyam diśet mohāt vāyuḥ dṛṣṭam atas saṃhṛtya ca tatas vyāpi bhūyas dhyāna gatim caret pravṛtta jñāna yogasya viṣaya asaṃga saṃkṣaye prātibhāni hi vighnāni sattva ādi guṇa jāni tu ākāśagamanam divyam apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃgajam sattvāt etāni vighnāni prātibhāni tu lakṣayet rajaḥ vighnāni saṃvidyāt prātibhāni na saṃśayaḥ kṣaya śūla jvara unmāda kuṣṭha sarpa grahāṇi tu yātanā udgama pūrvāṇi tāmasāni vinirdiśet guṇatraya samutthāni prātibhāni sadā muniḥ yuñjan saṃlakṣayet śīghram cikitset āśu ca eva hi prāṇa ādyān abhisaṃdhāya manaḥ saṃhṛtya ca eva hi prāṇāyāmena kumbhena hanyāt vighnāni sarvatas rajaḥ sattvam tamaḥ ca eva pradhānasya guṇāḥ trayaḥ nirīhaḥ nirvṛtaḥ yogī sa cetāḥ ghaṭate yadā prātibhāni tadā yānti vighnāni hi samam kṣayam prādurbhāvaḥ tatas teṣām guṇānām moha kāraṇam tamaḥ raudram vijānīyāt sattvam brahmaṇi saṃsthitam rajaḥ tu vaiṣṇavam vidyāt teṣām hantā maheśvaraḥ mahādevam param jñātvā yoga abhyāsa rataḥ dvijaḥ guṇatraya vinirmuktaḥ śaṃkare layam āpnuyāt tatas śāstra praṇītena dharma adharma vivarjitaḥ krameṇa sa upadeśena dhyāna abhyāsam samācaret śabda ādīn viṣayān jitvā śrotra ādi indriya gocarān sa abhimānam sa niyamam tyaktvā sāṃkhya viniścayam aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ nityāḥ vikārāḥ ca eva ṣoḍaśa puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ ca sāṃkhya siddhānta gocaraḥ etat eva param guhyam sāṃkhyānām tattva viniścaye prakṛteḥ antaram jñātvā puruṣasya ca mucyate iti skandapurāṇe pāśupatasyogavarṇanam nāma dhyāna vidhau yogam sāṃkhyam ca sarvatra dvividham jñānam ucyate tatra sāṃkhya ratāḥ kecid kecid yoga patha āśritāḥ avyaktam prakṛtiḥ ca eva tathā ahaṃkāraḥ eva ca aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ hi etāḥ tanmātraiḥ pañcabhiḥ saha pañca buddhīndriyāṇi āhuḥ pañca karmendriyāṇi ca manaḥ pañca ca bhūtāni vikārāḥ ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ ca sarva ārambha vivarjitaḥ nityaḥ sarva gataḥ sūkṣmaḥ cetāvān triguṇa ujjhitaḥ saṃśuddhaḥ vimalaḥ bhoktā akartā sākṣi vat sthitaḥ viditvā na viśanti enam bhūyas saṃsāra pañjaram pañcaviṃśati tattvāni sāṃkhyaiḥ etāni yogibhiḥ sūkṣmā prakṛtiḥ avyaktā bhojyā sarva ratā calā nityā ca acetanā ca eva vijñeyā sarvakāmikī bhinna kārya pracārāṇām eteṣām guṇa saṃjñinām hetunā puruṣa arthena sādhikā vṛttiḥ ucyate avikalpyam ca mānuṣyam sarvam etat guṇa ātmakam mūḍham niścetanam bhūtam sthūlam sūkṣmam atha api vā amūrtam mūrtimat vā api triguṇam sarvam ucyate mokṣa vighna karāḥ hi ete kīrtitāḥ yoginaḥ guṇāḥ vibhāgena vikāra sthāḥ yathādharmam samāśritāḥ bhūta sargaḥ tridhā bhūtaḥ sāṃkhya jñaiḥ paripaṭhyate saṃsiddhaḥ prākṛtaḥ ca eva tathā vaikṛtaḥ ucyate tatra dharmeṇa saṃsiddhāḥ yoge māheśvare sthitāḥ na icchanti saṃbhavam vyāsa pañca ātmataḥ smṛtaḥ te punar dravya saṃbandhāt sāṃkhya dṛṣṭānta paṇḍitāḥ icchanti kāryam āśritya kāraṇa āśrayiṇaḥ na hi pradhānāt puruṣāt buddhiḥ abhūt sattva adhikā asakṛt guṇānām pariṇāmena prākṛtānām jala ādi vat vyavasāyaḥ tathā rūpam niścayaḥ ca iti bhāṣyate aham eva hi kartā iti ahaṃkāraḥ udāhṛtaḥ buddhi bhūtāt ahaṃkārāt sattva utpannāt prakāśinaḥ buddhīndriyāṇi jātāni pañca sattva udayāni tu atas karmendriyāṇi āhuḥ guṇāt jātāni rājasāt tāmasāt api ahaṃkārāt tanmātrāṇi abhavan punar śaktam sarva āśrayam sūkṣmam anivārita dikpatham liṅgam tat ca samākhyātam dehinām yat ca kāraṇam prākṛtasya vikārasya dehabhedāḥ sahasraśas tattva sargaḥ smṛtaḥ pūrvaḥ piṇḍa sargaḥ tatas pratyayānām tatas sargaḥ tṛtīyaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ bhedāḥ pratyaya sarge tu vaiṣamyāt apare smṛtāḥ pañcāśat paritas bhedāḥ ye ca teṣām guṇāḥ daśa ṣaṣṭiḥ ete padārthāḥ hi gīyante kapila ādibhiḥ sā tuṣṭiḥ navadhā bhinnā siddhiḥ ca eva aṣṭadhā punar smṛtaḥ pañcavidhaḥ ca api teṣām eva viparyayaḥ aṣṭa bhedāḥ tri bhinnā syāt daśabhiḥ kārya bandhanaiḥ ete ṣaṣṭi padārthāḥ tu saṃkhyā jñānam iti śrutiḥ nyūnām eka adhikām eke ṣaṣṭim anye tu jānate antaram tattvam anveṣṭum prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca sāṃkhya tantram mahat buddhvā jñātvā tat prakṛteḥ param pañcaviṃśam ajam tattvam bhoktāram abhimāninam saṃdeha apagamaḥ na abhūt a buddhvā parameśvaram sva yogam śambhunā vatsa grāhitaḥ gata saṃśayaḥ tadā ṣaḍviṃśakam tattvam jñātvā sarvagam īśvaram yaḥ tayoḥ paratas nityaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ tu īśvaraḥ vibhuḥ tam jñātvā paramam tattvam mucyate janma bandhanāt sāṃkhyam kṛtsnam api jñātvā guṇa antara vicāraṇāt pañcaviṃśaka saṃbodhāt nā eva muktiḥ prajāyate sa baddhaḥ bhoktṛ pāśaiḥ tu guṇaiḥ prakṛti saṃbhavaiḥ abhimāna ātmakaḥ bhoktā puruṣa tvāt amocakaḥ eṣaḥ uktaḥ samāsena sāṃkhya siddhānta vistaraḥ yoga abhyāsam para asaṃgam sūkṣma jñānam aninditam matam paśupateḥ kṛtsnam amṛta āspada lambhanam ṣaṭsaptati uttara śatatamaḥ ākāśaḥ pavanaḥ tejaḥ bhūmiḥ āpaḥ tathā eva ca eṣām ekatra saṃghātāt śarīram nāma jāyate rasāḥ soma ātmakāḥ sarve tathā āhāraḥ caturvidhaḥ dehinām tu rasa utpattiḥ āhārasya niṣevaṇāt rasāt rakta samutpattiḥ śoṇitāt piśitam smṛtam medaḥ utpadyate māṃsāt tasmāt asthīni ca abhavan majjā ca asthi bhavā jñeyā tatas śukra samudbhavaḥ rakta śukra samāyogāt garbhaḥ saṃbhavati striyāḥ ṛtu yoga samādhānāt daiva karma vaśāt api kalalam tu eka rātreṇa pañca rātreṇa ca arbudam piśitam sapta rātreṇa māsāt ca aṅkura saṃbhavaḥ śiraḥ pāṇi mukha skandha grīvā pṛṣṭha ādi saṃyutaḥ pañcānām atha māsānām akṣi karṇa ādi saṃbhavaḥ pañcabhūta ātmakam tat tu cetaḥ vat avatiṣṭhati mṛtaḥ punar aham jātaḥ jātaḥ ca eva punar mṛtaḥ idānīm jāta mātraḥ tu yogam eva abhyāsāmi aham na punar yena saṃsāram pravekṣyāmi aśubha udayam deham āviśate vāyuḥ smṛtim ākṣipya tāmasaḥ agnīṣoma ātmakam sarvam bhūta grāmam caturvidham āgama anveṣaṇe saktāḥ pāpa anuṣṭhāna varjitāḥ matvā saṃsāra jam kleśam janma mṛtyu bhaya arditam vairāgyam janmataḥ kṛtvā sarva ārambha parikṣayāt sarveṣām yoginām guhyam sarva yoga nidarśanam tatas māheśvaram yogam ākhyāsye tat param tava teja agniḥ kāma jaḥ vahniḥ krodha agniḥ vīkṣaṇa analaḥ jaṭhara agniḥ ca bhūtātmā pañca ete deha vahnayaḥ prāṇaḥ samānaḥ ca udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca pañca ete vāyavaḥ nityāḥ dehinaḥ deha saṃbhavāḥ ākāśa prabhavāḥ hi ete śarīram ca eṣu tiṣṭhati māṃsa rakta samākīrṇam snāyu medaḥ sthi saṃcayam tvacā avanaddham durgandham śakṛt mūtra samāvṛtam taḍit abhra āgama anityam mṛd pātra āpāta saṃnibham sarva anartha samāyuktam na cirāt nāśa gāmi ca eka rūpam nava dvāram tri sthūṇam pañca devatam viṣaya indriya saṃkīrṇam na eka vyādhi sama arditam prāṇa ādibhiḥ avaṣṭabdham śarīram yantra vat sthitam āma pātram iva āpātāt śīryate kāla paryayāt pañcabhūtāni bhūtāni dehāt niṣkramya sarvaśas āviśanti tathā ātmānam ātmā ca viśate drutam bhūteṣu pavanaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ jīvaḥ tad vinibandhanaḥ vāyu agnī sahitau jīvaḥ na jīvaḥ prāṇinām pṛthak mūrtiḥ anyā na jīvasya mṛtyau dṛśyati dehinaḥ pañca rūpāt paraḥ devaḥ sūkṣmāt sūkṣmataraḥ mataḥ na asau paśyati na ghrāti na śṛṇoti na jalpati na jānāti na ca sparśet jīvaḥ prāṇa samāvṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ nāma mahā vāyuḥ jīvam dhārayate dvija sa prāṇaḥ dhārayati agnim sa ca jīvaḥ iti smṛtaḥ vāyu saṃdhāraṇaḥ hi agniḥ kriyāsu parivartate evam etat śarīram tu pañca bhūta guṇa ātmakam hṛdaye karṇikāyām tu madhya sthaḥ tejasām nidhiḥ ātmā sarva gataḥ nityam varjitaḥ viṣaya ādibhiḥ bhābhiḥ prakāśitaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vikāraiḥ vipramocitaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ bhavati vipra indra muktiḥ ca eva tatas smṛtā ṣaḍviṃśaka parijñānāt layam ādhāya tatra hi sarva prāṇi gatam sūkṣmam ātma dehe ca saṃsthitam yaḥ a abhyupāyaḥ paraḥ tasya vijñānāt īśvarasya tu yoga abhyāsam param tam te pravakṣyāmi dvijottama tṛtīyaḥ ṣaṭsaptati uttara śatatamaḥ antarātmā ca cetovān manaḥ saṃkalpa jam smṛtam mahābhūta pracārāt ca kṣobha agniḥ jīvaḥ ucyate na śarīram vinā cetaḥ tat ced nā asti kutas ca tat cetaḥ na vinā jīvam sa ca api na vinā manaḥ yasya cetaḥ teṣām sa cetovān prakīrtitaḥ cetasā tu vijānāti śubha aśubha nibandhanam śabda ādi viṣaya atītaḥ indriyāṇi nigṛhya tu jīvaḥ bandha ātmakaḥ jñeyaḥ śubha aśubha nibandhanāt udrekāt jāyate duḥkham saukhyam sattvāt prajāyate saukhyasya pariṇāmāt hi duḥkha utpattiḥ śarīriṇām sukha duḥkha ātmakam moham bhūtāni āviśya tiṣṭhati manaḥ cetaḥ samādhānāt viṣayaḥ udvijanāt api tasya nāśaḥ samākhyātaḥ saṃgasya ca vivarjanāt icchā nigrahaṇe saktāḥ krodha ādi parivarjitāḥ ātmā sarva gataḥ hi eṣaḥ sūkṣmaḥ saṃbhoga varjitaḥ atha aiśvaryam param dhyānāt yoga jam prāpnute muniḥ asukhāni api karmāṇi mahā pāpa kṛtāni api prāpya karma kṣayam kṛtsnam dhyāna yuktyā mahā mune kāma roṣau tathā saṃgaḥ dveṣaḥ rāga viniścayaḥ pāruṣyam krūra tā ca eva bhāvāḥ kṣatra nibandhanāḥ moha bhāva antara atītaḥ sama duḥkha sukhaḥ sadā dhyānena kṣīyate karma pāpam vā yadi vā śubham kṣīṇa karmā tatas yogī tat param brahma vindati yoginam puruṣam dṛṣṭvā pāpaiḥ mucyanti tad kṣaṇāt yogam eva param jñātvā sarva aśubha vimocanam dhyānam dhyeyam param ca eva dhātāram ca eva ye viduḥ tāpanāt tapanāt tāpyāt muktāḥ te duḥkha bandhanāt nirguṇaḥ sāṃkhya mukhyānām puruṣaḥ paripaṭhyate dīpa nirvāṇa vat teṣām dehabhede gatiḥ smṛtā īśvaraḥ sarva nirmuktaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ yoginām mataḥ dhāraṇābhiḥ samam tābhiḥ prāṇāyāmaiḥ tathā eva ca bhikṣā upātta rasa āhāraḥ mumukṣuḥ iti śabdyate karma mārgāt atikrāntaḥ dhyānī iti parikīrtyate na hṛṣyati sukhe ca eva dhyānī iti sa viśabditaḥ pūrvaḥ saṃketanaḥ proktaḥ paścāt saṃkathanaḥ smṛtaḥ saṃsaktaḥ ca tṛtīyaḥ tu teṣām bhedam imam śṛṇu pratirūpam vibhoḥ kṛtvā daśabhiḥ niyamaiḥ yutaḥ veda ādṛta sukha āsaṃgaḥ sattva karmā tu abāndhavān sarva ārambha parityāgāt kapila ādi niṣevitaḥ smṛtaḥ saṃkathanaḥ panthāḥ yoga agni paridīpakaḥ samyak etān muniḥ jñātvā nirmamaḥ śritaḥ sarvān dhyāna vidhān tu etān ucyamānān imān mayā śṛṇu vyāsa mahābuddhe yoga aiśvarya phala pradān pañcaviṃśatimam tattvam kṣaram tat prakṛteḥ param akṣaram ca param brahma ṣaḍviṃśakam iti smṛtam manaḥ eka gatam kṛtvā dhāraṇābhiḥ punar punar vāyu nigrahaṇam kuryāt pratyāhāra puraḥsaram muhūrta ardham kṣaṇam vā api pratyāhāram samācaret talāt triṃśat śatam ca ūrdhvam prāṇāyāma nibandhanam tat baddhvā vijane deśe dhyāna abhyāsam samācaret kṣudhā ārtaḥ vā atibhuktaḥ vā rujā duḥkha anvitaḥ vā yoga hastam tatas kṛtvā vāmasya upari dakṣiṇam a spṛśan daśanaiḥ dantān oṃkāram brahma saṃsmaran dhyāyīta nirmamaḥ vidvān prāṇāyāma puraḥsaram ātmānam ātmanā yojya sarva aṅgāni tu saṃharet nirīhaḥ pihita akṣaḥ ca nikṣipya hṛdi dhāraṇām pāṣāṇaḥ iva niṣpandaḥ muniḥ dhyānam samācaret ekatra aspanda saṃdhānam manasaḥ dhāraṇā smṛtā vikārāḥ guṇa jāḥ sarve naśyante vighna hetavaḥ anveṣṭi ca param brahma sva śarīram samāsthitam kṛtvā aikyam prāṇa manasām indriyāṇām vinigrahāt sarva bhāva parityāgāt mokṣam āpnoti asaṃśayam atha aiśvarya gatām siddhim dhyāyan aṣṭavidhām yadā paśyate yoga saṃsiddhyā tadā yogī prakīrtyate brahma soma ādikān devān yadā yuktaḥ prapaśyati manasā yoginām siddhiḥ sāṃkhyāḥ tattva viniścayāt na viśeṣaḥ yogānām muktvā māheśvaram vidhim yoginaḥ dhyāna saṃsiddhim sāṃkhyāḥ tattva viniścayam śabda ādīn viṣayān yuktaḥ na dhyāyan vetti vai yadā araṇye maunam ādhāya dhyāyet oṃkāram akṣaram veda ādau yaḥ svaraḥ proktaḥ veda ante ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ tasya prakṛti līnasya yaḥ paraḥ sa mahān smṛtaḥ tri saṃsthānam tri mātram ca tri brahma tri akṣaram tathā mātrā hīnam sa mātram ca yaḥ vidyāt sa vimucyate oṃkāraḥ paramam tattvam ātmā brahma ca kīrtyate kṣetrajñaiḥ ātma saṃbodhāt yogibhiḥ sūkṣma darśanāt īśvaram prāpnute yogī yam avāpya vimucyate indriyāṇi tu sarvāṇi śabda rūpa ādi nigrahāt viditvā karma jān hanti yogī doṣān aśeṣatas dhyāna śaktyā tatas śuddhaḥ sarvajit mokṣam āpnute yuñjan pratidinam vyāsa ṣaṣ māsāt yogam āpnute tam ātmānam param jñātvā yoga śaktyā mahā muniḥ parama aiśvarya saṃyuktaḥ amṛtam padam āpnuyāt pañcamaḥ aṣṭasaptati uttara śatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ūnāśīti uttara śatatamaḥ pañca karmendriyāṇi atra pañca buddhīndriyāṇi ca pañcabhūtam manaḥ ca atra vikārāḥ ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ mahān buddhiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tanmātrāṇi ca pañca hi imāḥ prakṛtayaḥ vyāsa deham aṣṭau samāśritāḥ nābhi madhye tu nāḍīnām śatam ekam pratiṣṭhitam sarva aṅgeṣu tu yāḥ tu anyāḥ jala anna rasa vāhikāḥ tāsām triṃśat sahasrāṇi vyāna srotasi saṃsthitāḥ udānasya aparāḥ nāḍyaḥ brahma mūrdhni pratiṣṭhitāḥ cakranābhī samāśritya bhūta saṃghātam āsthitam tad madhye tu guṇa spṛṣṭaḥ karma ātmā bhūta mohanaḥ vighāta jananaḥ sūrya ayuta nibhaḥ sthitaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ a agniḥ iva utpātī giri nīhāra saṃnibhaḥ guṇa sthaḥ bhūtayoniḥ tu puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ nirdhūma aṅgāra saṃkāśaḥ na vijñāta āgama kriyaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ puruṣaḥ sūkṣmaḥ īśvaraḥ paramaḥ vibhuḥ saḥ eṣa kathitaḥ vyāsa pareṣām paratas sthitaḥ mahādevam imam jñātvā mucyate tad kṣaṇāt muniḥ guṇatraya vikāra sthaḥ kathitaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ bhūyas saṃsarate tasmāt ajñānena eva mohitaḥ deva mānuṣa tiryakṣu bhrāmyate rāga mohitaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaka samādhānāt siddhiḥ tasya vikārataḥ kriyā kārya vinirmuktaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvasṛj prabhuḥ parama aiśvarya saṃpūrṇaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ maheśvaraḥ ajaḥ svayambhūḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ kūṭasthaḥ hi acalaḥ dhruvaḥ tatas tattvāni jāyante puruṣaḥ ca guṇaiḥ saha tasmin eva ca līyante ṣaḍviṃśe tu maheśvare yathā agniḥ nirdahet ante bhūta grāmam aśeṣatas ṣaḍviṃśaka padārtha jñaḥ tathā karmāṇi nirdahet sarva vyāpi yathā ākāśam sūkṣmam na eva tu lipyate ṣaḍviṃśaka rataḥ yogī tathā pāpaiḥ na lipyate ṣaḍviṃśāt paratas na asti tasmāt tad paramaḥ bhavet brahma viṣṇu ādikam sarvam bhūta grāmam aśeṣatas īśvarāt jāyate vyāsa tasmin eva pralīyate saḥ eṣa sarvagaḥ devaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ parameśvaraḥ prāṇaḥ samānaḥ ca udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca ye pañca vāyavaḥ dehe teṣām nigrahaṇe yatet apānam ca samāṇam ca kṛtvā eka gatam ādṛtaḥ vyānena sahitam prāṇam udāne saṃniveśayet nāsā agre tu sakṛt prāṇam prāpayet yoga śaktitaḥ bhadrām dṛṣṭim samāsthāya ṣaḍviṃśam cintayet tatas mātrāḥ pañcadaśa proktāḥ prathamam sandhibandhanam mātrāḥ viṃśati vijñeyāḥ pañcamaḥ sandhi vigrahaḥ ekam āsanam āsthāya ṣaḍviṃśam samanusmaran sarva aṅgāni samāhṛtya niṣpandaḥ dhyānam ācaret śanais saṃcārayet vāyum nāḍibhiḥ srotasi sthitam tāvat tiṣṭheta yukta ātmā dhyāna yogāt gata spṛhaḥ soma maṇḍala saṃkāśam yāvat paśyet hṛdi sthitam jyotiḥ deha āśritam dṛṣṭvā yoga aiśvaryam pravartate tri kāla viṣayam jñānam pratyakṣam yoginaḥ bhavet sarva vidyā vidām vyāsa yatīnām vrata cāriṇām tapasvinām ca viprāṇām yogī śreṣṭhaḥ udāhṛtaḥ na anyathā mucyate jantuḥ saṃsārāt tamasaḥ parāt ṣaḍviṃśaka parijñānam muktvā yoga nibandhanam jitvā hi aṣṭa prakāram tu āsanānām nibandhanam mātrā utkarṣeṇa jitvā ca prāṇāyāmam caturvidham tanmātrāṇi indriyaiḥ jitvā viṣayaiḥ indriyāṇi ca yoga āspadam samādhāya pūrva uktam guṇa varjitam dhyāyīta hṛdi tam devam viśvam viśveśvaram vibhum an ādi nidhanam śāntam traiguṇya parivarjitam tālau jihvām samādhāya dantaiḥ dantān na ca spṛśan kṛtvā manasi tat sarvam prāṇa apānau niruddhya ca oṃkāram tu asakṛt dhyāyan saṃhṛtya aṅgāni kūrma vat śarīram sarvam āpūrya vikṣipet sarvam ātmani tat saṃhṛtya muniḥ bhūyas vyāpi bhūtam pravistṛtam nāḍī vāyu pracāreṇa bhūyas bhūyas tathā ārabhet madhya aṅge ca aparāhaṇe ca kṛṣṇam dhyāyīta tāmasam taijasam sarvatas ca api dhyānadevam jayet guṇān yena ṣaḍviṃśakam buddhvā hṛdaya stham maheśvaram paramātmā param brahma kāraṇam puruṣaḥ mahān īśvaraḥ nirguṇaḥ bhoktā ṣaḍviṃśaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ jāgarti svapate bhuṅkte saṃtiṣṭhati dadāti ca sa sraṣṭā sa ca saṃhartā guṇa atītaḥ maheśvaraḥ yogam pāśupatam tubhyam ādyam mokṣa gati pradam sūkṣmam tat paramam jñānam pravakṣyāmi tava anagha yasya samyak parijñānāt vijñeyam na aparam bhavet ṣaṣṭhe ūnāśīti uttara śatatamaḥ aśīti uttara śatatamaḥ brahma ādyāḥ devatāḥ vyāsa dakṣa yajña vadhe purā śaṃkaram śaraṇam jagmuḥ vīrabhadra bhaya arditāḥ gaṇa indreṇa abhiyuktāḥ tu bhasma kūṭāni bhejire yadā bhasma praviṣṭāḥ te tejaḥ śāṃkaram uttamam abhavan te tadā raudrāḥ paśavaḥ dīkṣitāḥ iva bhasma ābhasita gātrāṇām śaṃkara vrata cāriṇām svam yogam pradadau teṣām tadā devaḥ umāpatiḥ sarvāsām mokṣa vidyānām yat tattvam atiricyate yaḥ yogaḥ sakalaḥ vyāsa kṛcchra upāya prasādhanaḥ yaḥ a ayam bhagavatā sākṣāt yogaḥ māheśvaraḥ paraḥ tattvataḥ kalpitaḥ teṣām prapannānām divaukasām vratam pāśupatam prāpya ṣaṣ māsāt jñānam āpnute sarva dharmam bahis kṛtvā niṣakalasya prabhāvataḥ dīkṣām pāśupatīm prāpya tam viśanti maheśvaram sarva jñāna samāyuktam tapaḥ dharma bahiṣkṛtam pāpiṣṭhāḥ dharmavantaḥ vā bhaktāḥ kevalam īśvaram dahet soma kṛtam vahniḥ īśvaram ca analam viduḥ kṛta akṛtam dahati agniḥ bhūyas soma samāgataḥ bhasmanā mocitāḥ sarve brahma ādyāḥ abhimāninaḥ ātmānam uddharet vyāsa yaḥ snānam bhasmanā caret tejasā tasya saṃspṛṣṭaḥ mucyate janmanā dvijaḥ sāṃkhyam visyāḥ tapaḥ ca eva tyaktvā dharmān ca vaidikān ātmānam yaḥ paśum kṛtvā mahādevam hutāśanam dīkṣitaḥ brahma bhasmabhyām śiva yājī muniḥ bhavet evam vratam anuprāpya bhūtvā pāśupataḥ muniḥ idam māheśvaram jñānam guhyam paramam abhyaset jñeyam jñānam tathā jñātā trayam dehe yathā sthitam ātmā yaḥ ca yathā ca asau sthāna traya samāsthitaḥ nāḍīṣu ca yathā hi ātmā ātmani eva anutiṣṭhati sarvatas sarva bhūteṣu nigūḍhaḥ tiṣṭhate yathā payasi iva ghṛtam vyāsa yam viditvā vimucyate na sa vettum vinā jñānam śakyaḥ ātmā kathaṃcana rūpa śabda rasa atītam kaḥ tvam vetti maheśvaram tathā hi aham mahābhāga prāsādāt tryambakasya tu ātma jñāna ṣara upāyam kathayāmi tava anagha śuddham vimalam ābhāti akṣaram parama aiśvaram sarva bhāva guṇa atītam nirvikalpam nirañjanam bahis antar caram dīptam avināśi varam dhruvam yathā tat akṣaram brahma procyamānam tathā śṛṇu om iti eka sa akṣaram pūrvam kṣaram tasmāt vinirgatam tri akṣaraḥ ca tri mātraḥ ca oṃkāraḥ brahma śabdyate akāre tatra viṣṇuḥ tu ukāre tu pitāmahaḥ makāre bhagavān īśaḥ mātrāyām prakṛtiḥ smṛtā prakṛti strī tvam āsthāya nityam tau īśa pārśva gau patnī rūpeṇa sā śambhum bhajate prakṛtiḥ sadā tu prakṛtiḥ khyātā akṣaraḥ tu svayam īśvaraḥ īśvarāt nirgatā sā hi prakṛtiḥ guṇa bandhanā tasyāḥ sraṣṭā mahādevaḥ yatas viṣṇu pitāmahau yena eva dhyāninā vyāsaḥ īśvaraḥ vikalpitaḥ sa tam āviśya mukta ātmā kṛtārthaḥ jāyate muniḥ na enam jānanti amārga sthāḥ tarka hetu parāyaṇāḥ bhoktāram prakṛteḥ īśam param ṣaḍviṃśa saṃjñitam oṃkāraḥ prakṛtiḥ nityam tad madhye ca īśvaraḥ sthitaḥ oṃkāram dhyāyatā yena atītya prakṛtim mune īśvaraḥ a asau mahān vinnaḥ sa muktaḥ paśu bandhanaiḥ īśvarī prakṛtiḥ khyātā guṇa bandhāt vimohanī brahma tvāt bṛṃhaṇī hi eṣā viṣṇu tvāt vibhava āśritā prasādāt īśvarasya eṣā prakṛtiḥ triguṇa ātmikā sa abhimānā bhava sraṣṭrī bhoktā tasyāḥ maheśvaraḥ aṣṭa bāhuḥ tri pādā ca pañca deha mukhī tathā jaganmātā smṛtā hi eṣā guṇatraya vikāra jā ubhe śubha aśubhe tasyāḥ vidyā avidye tathā hi ubhe udbhavaḥ praṇāśaḥ ca kriyā anuṣṭhānam eva ca nimittam ca abhavat yoniḥ bhāvāḥ saṃkṣepataḥ tu amī īśvarāt jātaḥ oṃkāraḥ sa ca tasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ atas kṛtvā mahābhāga yoginaḥ kapila ādayaḥ īśa bhojyau guṇa ātmānau jñātvā viṣṇu pitāmahau mahā mohau tamaḥ niṣṭhau viṣaya asaṅga saṃyutau saṃsāra bhramaṇau mūḍhau sarva anitya samāyutau īśvara īpsuḥ bhavet vidvān dhyāna yoga parāyaṇaḥ yena asau īśvaraḥ vinnaḥ yogena ātmani saṃsthitaḥ ekāśīti uttara śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ātmā sūkṣmaḥ manaḥ buddhiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ guṇāḥ tathā bhūtāni indriya saṃghātaḥ tanmātrāṇi daśa anilāḥ vibhaktāḥ kramaśas dehe vibhāgena yathāśrayam hṛdaye karṇikāyām tu yat padmam sarvatomukham veṣṭitam tantubhiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ tat ūrdhvam sarva dehinām ātmā tatra sa jīvaḥ tu sa manaskaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ tat suṣuptam iti prāhuḥ saṃsiddhāḥ śiva yoginaḥ jvālinī stimitā dhūmrā vidyunmeghā viśālinī mālinī śaṃkarī ca eva sumaitrī bodhanī tathā etāḥ daśa mahānāḍyaḥ jīve tasmin pratiṣṭhitāḥ śayānam pratibuddham vā yāḥ tāḥ bibhrati dehinam śabda ādi viṣayebhyaḥ tu ātmā sarva gataḥ ca yaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ mataḥ buddhiḥ bhāvāḥ cetaḥ ca deha jāḥ saha jīvena tiṣṭhanti dhārayantaḥ śarīriṇam te eva sahitāḥ sarve jīvaḥ ca eva tu pañcamaḥ sthitaḥ manasi sūkṣmaḥ tu śītāṃśuḥ nāma tantukaḥ cetaḥ saḥ eva samproktaḥ saḥ eva puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ manaḥ somaḥ sukham brahmā jñānam dharmaḥ ratiḥ tathā ahaṃkāraḥ hutāśaḥ ca mṛtyuḥ duḥkham atha āmayam kāma roṣau jarā tṛṣṇā adharmaḥ ca iti tāmasāḥ viṣṇuḥ buddhiḥ tathā kāryam kāraṇam bhūmiḥ eva ca jñānam vairāgyam ākāśam rājasaḥ bhāva vistaraḥ jīva madhye sthitā sūkṣmā vidhūmā pāvakī śikhā amṛtam sarva bhūtānām gatiḥ ca eva hi sā parā madhye tasyāḥ sthitam saumyam amṛtam śaśi maṇḍalam madhye tasya agni saṃkāśaḥ jīvaḥ īśaḥ pradṛśyate sarasā lohitā mukhyā prītā rasavatī tathā vidhūmā ca amṛtā ca eva nikuṇṭhā bahu vistarā etāḥ sūkṣmatarāḥ nāḍyaḥ sambhidya daśa pāvakam tarpayanti sadā somam bhūta ādhāram payaḥ saṃchādayati vṛddhaḥ tām jīva madhya gatām śikhām tat eva amṛtam ākhyātam īśvara āspadam uttamam yā amṛtā iti aparā nāḍī sā tu svapne pratiṣṭhitā ubhau etau muniḥ jitvā svapna jāgaraṇa āśrayau mamatva ādyāḥ ca ye bhāvāḥ manasaḥ ca eva yā ghṛṇā yat vā kuryāt ahaṃkāraḥ tad jñānāt sarvam utsṛjet bhoktā vahniḥ smṛtaḥ teṣām tad jñātā kena baddhyate iti jñātvā tyajet cintām bhavet yoga paraḥ sadā vahneḥ yat auṣṇyam tat pāpam tejaḥ dharmaḥ udāhṛtaḥ prakṛtiḥ yā sa jīvaḥ tu yā śikhā sa maheśvaraḥ nirmamāḥ yoga viduṣaḥ śaṃkara vratam āsthitāḥ gacchanti sva tanum tyaktvā hitvā māyām param padam idam anyat param jñānam asmāt sūkṣmataram punar muktvā pāśupatān siddhān yat na bhūteṣu vidyate na spṛśanti tadā ātmānam vikārāḥ tasya te bahis saḥ evam dṛśyate dhyānāt na anya upāyāt kathaṃcana sarva bhāva guṇa atītam su cintyam parameśvaram jñānena ye prapaśyanti yoginaḥ te pare smṛtāḥ chāyā eṣā dṛśyate yā tu cakṣuḥ viṣayam āśritā sa jīvaḥ kīrtitaḥ vyāsa sthiti hetuḥ śarīriṇām mahānāgaḥ smṛtaḥ nāmnā vāyuḥ ākāśa gocaraḥ ākāśe karṇikāyām ca nāḍyām jīve ca saṃsthitaḥ gāndhārī vijayā ca eva saṃjayā tala vartinī nāgaḥ etāsu nāḍīṣu vāyuḥ samparivartate sā jayā vijayā yā ca dve te prāṇa vahe smṛte apāne talagāndhāryau nāḍyau nāgena saṃyute yogāt apāna manasoḥ nāgena samudīritāḥ vṛddham saṃdhārayet deham āyuṣā ca balena ca nāḍī tu anyā suṣumṇā iti soma vahni manaḥ sthitā sā asmin sa dhātuke dehe kūrmāre ca anile sthitā gulphe kara tale saktā nikuñcā sa prasāriṇī samāna vyāna saṃyuktāḥ rakta māṃse hi tarpayet nāḍyām nābhi nibaddhāyām tulāyām pratiṣṭhitau adhas ekaḥ caret nāḍyā vāyuḥ anyaḥ tad ūrdhva gaḥ adhas sthaḥ pāda sambaddhaḥ ūrdhva gaḥ śirasi sthitaḥ devadatta mahānāga kṛta kūrma dhanaṃjayāḥ prāṇāḥ te pañca vikhyātāḥ vahnayaḥ yājinaḥ hutam eṣu yat iṣṭam vā somam tat upatiṣṭhati somam viśanti yajvānaḥ na teṣām mukti lakṣaṇam dīptiḥ agneḥ smṛtā yā tu oṣadhibhyaḥ ca yat rasam tarpaṇam yat ca somasya karṇikāyām tat āsthitam netreṣu dṛśyate yaḥ aayam jyotiḥ chāyā prakāśakaḥ sa jīvaḥ sarva sattvānām ātmā tatra samāsthitaḥ tat ca amṛtam samākhyātam jñāna labhyam tat ucyate tasmāt paratarā na asti jñāna vijñānayoḥ gatiḥ jñātvā evam saṃtyajet moham guṇatraya vikāra jam vimohāḥ tyakta saṃsargāḥ kriyā kārya vivarjitāḥ tam viśanti maheśānam īśvara vrata cāriṇaḥ iti idam yogam ākhyātam vyāsa māheśvaram tava yogavidhau aṣṭame ekāśīti uttara śatatamaḥ dvyaśīti uttara śatatamaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca aho jñānam tvayā ākhyātam ajñāna vinivartanam adya aham gata saṃdehaḥ mahādevam param prati śaṃkarāt prakṛtiḥ jātā brahma viṣṇū tad ātmakau jñātvā ṣaḍviṃśam īśānam mucyate bandhanāt iti niṣkalam sakalam jñānam kaḥ aanyaḥ evam prabhāṣate tvad prasādāt aham tāta prāpta jñānaḥ mahā śubhaḥ visaṃdehaḥ bhavam śāntaḥ praṣṭavyam kiṃcid asti me tat tvām vijñāpayāmi idam niṣṭhām ākhyātum arhasi vinā kleśam tanum tyaktvā yogī yoga bala anvitaḥ īśvara ādhāra samprāpteḥ upāyam mokṣa lambhanam kathayasva muni śreṣṭha praṣṭavyam na anyat asti me evam uktaḥ sa śiṣyeṇa vyāsena su mahātmanā śṛṇu vyāsa param jñānam īśvara ādhāna kāraṇam sva deham ripu vat tyaktvā ṣaḍviṃśe layam āpnuyāt yāḥ nāḍyaḥ vāyu avaṣṭabdhāḥ saṃvaranti śarīriṇam śatam tāsām śatānām tu karṇikā madhyam āśritam tam āśritya āsthitāḥ nāḍyaḥ nābhyām pādeṣu adhas gatāḥ śiraḥ baddhāḥ smṛtāḥ bhūyas tāḥ eva karam āsthitāḥ karam āśritya tāḥ bhūyas karṇikām punar āśritāḥ dvisaptati sahasrāṇi nāḍīnām aparāḥ mune tāsām ekaikaśas bhedāḥ sūkṣma sūkṣmatarāḥ smṛtāḥ tāsu saṃcarate prāṇaḥ karṇikā vyoma sambhavaḥ tatra ātmā sūkṣma saṃlakṣyaḥ prāk uktaḥ tiṣṭhati dvija yā prabhā durdṛśā tasya tām bhajet yoga vid muniḥ tat tejaḥ sarva nāḍīṣu vibhaktam sarva dehinām tena nāḍyaḥ bahis sparśāt manaḥ kurvanti vistṛtam tat tejaḥ cakṣuṣā hṛtvā sarva nāḍī samāśritam vāyuḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ nāmnā yaḥ hṛdi sphurate sadā trīṇi tasya mukhāni āhuḥ śiraḥ nābhi hṛd eva ca ye a anye prāṇāḥ nava ākhyātāḥ vāyavaḥ kīrtitāḥ mayā tad vaśāt utkramanti ete tasmin tiṣṭhanti saṃsthitāḥ nābhībandhanam āsādya nāḍīnām vaktram āsthitam dvitīyam karṇikāyām tu tṛtīyam tālu saṃsthitam kṣurikā paraśuḥ śūlam trividhā utkrāntiḥ ucyate śūlam hṛdi kṣuram nābhyām tālau paraśuḥ āsthitaḥ tāluke hṛdi vā baddham trayam nābhyām pratiṣṭhitam tālau viyojitam sarvam prāṇam eva vimuñcati ākṣiptam tritayam nābhyām karṇikāyām viyojitam yathā jīvaḥ na yoginaḥ tat idam śṛṇu bāhyaḥ śarīra jaḥ ca eva mṛtyuḥ dvividhaḥ ucyate viṣa śastra agni yogaiḥ tu sarpa daṃṣṭri marut jalaiḥ bāhyaḥ mṛtyuḥ iti khyātaḥ śarīram tu nibodha me yoga upāya kṛtaḥ yaḥ ca yaḥ ca kāla kṣaya āgataḥ tayoḥ bheda vikāre tu śṛṇu vyāsa samāsatas yaḥ aayam āghoṣa jaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate śrotra sandhitaḥ śabda sparśa guṇa atītaḥ rūpa yogam vimuñcati evam agnau praṇaṣṭe tu sarve eva anilāḥ tatas udānena āśu saṃyujya karṇikāyām viśanti hi indriyāṇi manaḥ yānti manaḥ prāṇa vinirgamam teṣu sarveṣu līneṣu prāṇān vāyuḥ nipīḍayet pīḍyamānāḥ tatas sarve te bhavanti ekatas śeṣaḥ tatra hi mūrmāraḥ jīvam tyaktvā sa tiṣṭhati niṣkramanti tatas dehāt tvaritam vāyunā īritāḥ prāk upāttaḥ tatas dehaḥ sūkṣmaḥ vijāyate sa tatra sandhitaḥ jīvaḥ bhūyas mūḍhaḥ ca tiṣṭhati evam kāla kṛtā hi eṣā sarva bhūta gaṇa sthitiḥ vinā yogam na jīyeta sūkṣmam māheśvaram padam upaviṣṭaḥ prasuptaḥ vā utkrānti abhyasta saṃyamaḥ sva icchayā mucyate vyāsa jñātvā tam tu maheśvaram kṣurikām paraśum vā atha śūlam vā dhārayet muniḥ tatas sarve līyante vikārāḥ karaṇaiḥ saha vīkṣate ca īśvaram brahma ṣaḍviṃśam sva tanu sthitam sukham ārohati brahma harmya pṛṣṭham talāt iva padārtham pañca vijñāya duḥkhānta pariniṣṭhitaḥ pañcabhiḥ brahmabhiḥ pūtaḥ bhasmanā dīkṣitaḥ dvijaḥ śaṃkara ekamanāḥ yogī jñānam etat avāpnute māheśvaram imam yogam niṣkalam mukti kāraṇam mahādeva paraḥ bhūtvā jñānam etat avāpnuhi mahādevam prapannāḥ ye tān muktvā śiva yoginaḥ evam pāśupatāḥ viprāḥ niṣkalam tam maheśvaram tryaśīti uttara śatatamaḥ bhavya bhūta bhavānām ca saptānām ūrdhvatas sthitaḥ na asau tarka vinirdeśyaḥ lokāḥ tasmin pratiṣṭhitāḥ brahmāṇḍam sakalam tasmin śiva loke pratiṣṭhitam na asau naśyati saṃhāre dhruvaḥ sthāṇuḥ surālayaḥ yatra aham sanaka ādyāḥ ca brahmā ca eva pitāmahaḥ bālakhilya purogāḥ ca siddhāḥ ca kapila ādayaḥ śiva yoga pariprāptyā sattva ādi guṇa varjitāḥ tiṣṭhāmaḥ nirvṛtāḥ vyāsa sevamānāḥ tam īśvaram paramāṇuḥ asau īśaḥ bhāva gamyaḥ manīṣiṇām kṣamā satyam dhṛtiḥ ca eva tapaḥ vairāgyam eva ca sraṣṭṛ tvam jñāna vairāgyāt ātma bodhaḥ maheśa tā aṣṭamam dhruvam adhyeyam akṣaram mukti kāraṇam māyā dhāma tad īśasya jagat saṃhāra hetumat ūrdhvatas brahma lokasya yojanānām mahātmanaḥ viṃśatīnām tu koṭīnām puram sthāṇoḥ samāsthitam etāvān ūrdhva saṃcāraḥ gati antaḥ ca tatas smṛtaḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ pure tasmin nityāḥ sūkṣmāḥ tathā avyayāḥ jñāna adhikāra dharmiṇyaḥ śaivī prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ yābhyaḥ jajñe mahā īśānau brahma viṣṇū prajāpatī tābhyām prakṛti bhūtābhyām sraṣṭṛ tvam paramam dadau akṣayaḥ vimalaḥ sūkṣmaḥ niṣkalaḥ sakalaḥ ca yadā āsīt haimam aṇḍam tu laukikam tu āpavargikam tasmāt bījasya nirbhedaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ sa vibhuḥ smṛtaḥ prakṛtiḥ vaiṣṇavī proktā sā ca tasmāt vinirgatā sura asura ādi sṛṣṭi artham brahma tvam punar āsthitā aṇḍasya bhedataḥ padmabrahmaṇaḥ śaṃkara ātmanaḥ yat sthānam vigraha īśasya īśvarasya parātmanaḥ nāmnā śivapuram vyāsa gatiḥ īśvara yoginām śatam śata sahasrāṇām yojanānām tat ucyate mahī maṇḍala saṃsthānam tat madhye vistṛtam smṛtam mahatā haima jātena prākāreṇa su veṣṭitam jarā mṛtyu śrama vyādhi kopa moha mada ādayaḥ śatam śata sahasrāṇām yojanānām yathādiśam tat puram vṛṣabhāṅkasya sarva vyāpi samṛddhimat divyā mārakatī bhūmiḥ sparśa mātra sukha āvahā vaidūrya maṇi kalpāni bāla arka sadṛśāni ca mahā hrada pramāṇāni nālaiḥ vaidūrya sannibhaiḥ indranīla nikāśāni mahā maṇi nibhāni ca pure bhagavataḥ śambhoḥ pārāśarya nibodha tāḥ varadā ca vareṇyā ca vareśā varavarṇinī vārāhī vāribhadrā ca varā ca eva mahāpagāḥ nānā kusuma saṃmiśram tāḥ vahanti jala amṛtam na devāḥ na muni indrāḥ ca na asurāḥ pitaraḥ na ca meru śṛṅga pratīkāśaḥ diś bhadraḥ tapana prabhaḥ prāsādaḥ lakṣapādaḥ tu kāmagaḥ kanaka āmayaḥ vaidūryaiḥ vyoma saṃkāśaiḥ sphāṭikaiḥ candra saprabhaiḥ prabālaiḥ arka saṃkāśaiḥ indranīla mayaiḥ paraiḥ śaśi raśmi prakāśābhiḥ kvacid arka aṃśu rūpibhiḥ śobhitam tat patākābhiḥ virarāja sukha anilam śuśubhe tat puram kīrṇam pādapaiḥ giri sannibhaiḥ mahīdhrāṇām yathā meruḥ sarveṣām pravaraḥ mahān tatra viśveśvaraḥ sākṣāt mahā bhūtapatiḥ haraḥ sadā āste sahitaḥ patnyā ṣaḍviṃśaḥ parameśvaraḥ lakṣmīḥ meghā dhṛtiḥ ca eva hrīḥ śrīḥ kīrtiḥ sarasvatī śiva bhāva arpita ātmānaḥ ye narāḥ rudra tatparāḥ yatra tatra mṛtāḥ vatsa teṣām tatra āspadam smṛtam ye ca māheśvarāḥ vyāsa tiṣṭhante śaṃkara ālaye munayaḥ śaṃkaram bhaktāḥ tān śṛṇuṣva samāhitaḥ ṛbhuḥ brahmā surajyeṣṭhaḥ nara nārāyaṇau api śiṣyaḥ siddhaḥ pañcaśikhaḥ tathā muniḥ hayaśirāḥ yaḥ ca yajñavalka ādayaḥ tathā tri akṣāḥ śaṃkara varṣmāṇaḥ parama aiśvarya saṃyutāḥ tiṣṭhanti īśvara mūla sthāḥ guṇa atītāḥ mumukṣavaḥ īśvaram te samāviśya prāpnuvanti apavargikam yaiḥ ca dṛṣṭāni vipra indra śiva liṅgāni tāni tu kedāraḥ madhyamaḥ ca eva girīśaḥ ca mahālaye catuḥśṛṅgeśvaraḥ devaḥ śrīgirau ca maheśvaraḥ kārohaṇaḥ ca deveśaḥ gaṅgādvāre ca śaṃkaraḥ bhadreśaḥ ca mahādevaḥ śaṅkukarṇa īśvaraḥ tathā mahākāleśvaraḥ ca eva gokarṇe ca tathā hi ubhau avimukteśvaraḥ ca eva yāni ca anyāni bhū tale te a api yānti mṛtāḥ vyāsa tat puram girijāpateḥ yogaḥ pāśupataḥ yaḥ ca mayā te parikīrtitaḥ bhaktiḥ yeṣām bhave nityam kṛtārthāḥ te nara uttamāḥ mṛtāḥ śiva pure vyāsa tri akṣāḥ paṭṭiśa pāṇayaḥ nandīśa skanda saṃkāśāḥ yoga aiśvarya bala anvitāḥ rudrāḥ bhavanti te vyāsa sadā śaṃkara pārśva gāḥ eṣa te kathitaḥ sarvaḥ yogaḥ māheśvaraḥ paraḥ sakalam niṣkalam ca eva jñātvā evam param īśvaram bhaviṣyasi ca yoga ātmā jñānasya asya prabhāvataḥ yajña dharma pracāra artham vedam svāyambhuva smṛtam vijñānāt tvam anusmṛtya caturdhā vikariṣyasi tvad kṛtāḥ pracariṣyanti tīrthakṛt tvam bhaviṣyasi śāṃkara jñāna sampannaḥ īśvare layam āpsyasi evam uktaḥ sa vipra indraḥ hṛṣṭa sarva tanūruhaḥ upasadya muni indram tam bhasma saṃskāram āptavān tad kṣaṇāt ca asya yogaḥ a asau prādurbhūtaḥ mahā muneḥ śarva āyatana vīkṣā artham vicacāra mahī tale vāyuḥ uvāca evam sanatkumāraḥ tu pṛṣṭaḥ vyāsena dhīmatā muni indraḥ kathayāmāsa purāṇam skanda sambhavam śiva yoga udbhavam dhyānam sarva jñāna arṇvamvam mahat tasmāt yūyam api jñātvā vratam pāśupatam dvijāḥ abhyasya śāṃkaram yogam īśvare layam āpnuta veda artha smṛti sambaddhāḥ vidyāḥ cakre mahā muniḥ purāṇam prathamam prāhuḥ ādyam nandīśvaraḥ dvijāḥ kṛtsnasya jagataḥ viprāḥ ādikartā yathā haraḥ tathā sarva purāṇānām purāṇaḥ a ayam paraḥ smṛtaḥ sāyujyam śṛṇuyāt vibhoḥ ādyam puṇyam umāpateḥ dvija vṛṣāḥ stotra anuvādam param sarve te jvalat arka vahni vapuṣaḥ tri akṣāḥ śaśāṅka tviṣaḥ iti skandapurāṇe tryaśīti adhika śatatamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ ārṣam skandapurāṇam sa yoga vidhi samāptam ālaṣka caitra śukla dvādaśyām samāptam śubham mārgaḥ aṣṭāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ aryamā bahubhiḥ bāṇaiḥ prahlādam daitya puṅgavam ājaghāna ratham ghoram dhvajam ca asya vyaśātayat jaghāna bahubhiḥ bāṇaiḥ vṛṣṭyā meghaḥ yathā acalam śarān a gaṇayan eva hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ gṛhītvā kūbare tasya ratham hema pariṣkṛtam nirjitāḥ tarjitāḥ ca eva yuddhāya ca punar sthitāḥ tatas saṃkulam eva abhūt devānām dānavaiḥ saha paraspara jigīṣūṇām yuddham bhīru bhaya āvaham tatas bheryaḥ ca śaṅkhāḥ ca paṭaha āsekya puṣkalāḥ jharjharyaḥ pepukāḥ ca eva ḍiḍṇimāḥ goviṣāṇakāḥ avādyanta bale vyāse ubhayeṣām sahasraśas keśa śaivāla bahulā dhanuḥ jyā kṛta tantukā niṣṭanat śastra maṇḍūkā dukūla chatra phenilā uṣṇīṣa vara haṃsā ca kara pāda śira upalā hāra keyūra sikatā mukuṭa utphulla paṅkajā medaḥ usra kapha paṅkā ca prāṇa jīvita nāśinī prāvartata nadī ghorā hasti aśva ratha vāhinī tasyām snāyanti rakṣāṃsi pibanti ca ramanti ca nṛtyanti ca api bhaya dāḥ tathā gṛdhrāḥ gomāyavaḥ ca eva śvānaḥ mārjāra vāyasāḥ cakṣūṃṣi kara pāda antram bhakṣayantaḥ mama ayam hastinaḥ pādaḥ mama ayam meda paṭṭakaḥ mama ayam ca karaḥ śukraḥ bāhuḥ ca rudhirasya daḥ mama ayam tava na ayam ca gṛhṇa paśya iti ca eva hi kalaham cakrire tatra krūrāḥ piśita bhojanāḥ tyaktvā anye ca hatān tatra sva dehān su mahā rathāḥ vimānaiḥ strī jana ākīrṇaiḥ prayayuḥ brahmaṇaḥ sadaḥ apare pāpa karmāṇaḥ hanyamānāḥ ruṣā andhitaiḥ kecid ārtta svaram kṛtvā ṣa arditāḥ mriyante puruṣāḥ yuddhe śataśas aatha sahasraśas daśantaḥ ca tṛṇāni anye bhrātar putra iti ca apare krandamānāḥ janāḥ bhītāḥ prāṇān kṛcchreṇa tatyajuḥ saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭāḥ kecid deva asura mahā rathāḥ śara sannata marmāṇaḥ patanti urvyām drumāḥ iva aśivāni śivāḥ neduḥ aṭṭahāsān ca rākṣasāḥ ārtta nādān ca puruṣāḥ tathā eva gaja vājinaḥ siṃhanādāḥ ca śūrāṇām bāhu śabdāḥ ca puṣkalāḥ dhanuṣām kṛṣyamāṇānām śabdāḥ vādya ravāḥ tathā atha indraḥ ca dhaneśaḥ ca yamaḥ kālaḥ ca vīryavān varuṇaḥ marutaḥ ca eva viśvedevāḥ ca sarvaśas mitraḥ ca eva jayantaḥ ca bhagaḥ pūṣā aryamā tathā kāpālī ca api yaḥ rudraḥ vasavaḥ ca mahā balāḥ nāsatyaḥ ca eva dasraḥ ca pṛśnayaḥ ca sura uttamāḥ ete ca anye ca devānām pravarāḥ bāhu śālinaḥ prabhañjanāḥ iva akāle mahāntaḥ iva ca acalāḥ vṛṣabhāḥ iva nardantaḥ bṛṃhantaḥ iva kuñjarāḥ grasantaḥ ca yathā grāhāḥ chindantaḥ makarāḥ iva varṣamāṇāḥ iva ghanāḥ siṃḍāḥ iva ca nardinaḥ dānavānām balam sarve vegena eva abhyavārayan yuddhe aṣṭāśītitamaḥ a adhyāyaḥ
